du/ 'phan yul yur ma'i mda'i rnor bzang su lo gsum/ yer par lo gsum/ bla ma sgom pa go bteg mdzad nas/ sems 'grel skor gsum man ngag phran dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs
pa dang / gsang 'dus 'phags skor sogs bum pa gang byo'i tshul du zhus/ de rjes bla ma mya ngan 'das pa'i sku mdang mdzad/ rnor bzang nyid du thugs dam las mi g.yel bar
bzhugs pa na/ phyis paN chen bod du phebs dus slob ma rnams kyi lha rje sgom pas gdams

ngag thams cad sgrol byin nas khong rang gshegs so zhes zhus pas/ sgro ston gyi paN chen mjal du 'ongs pa'i dus su/ ngas chos gang 'dod sbyin no gsungs pa la/ gzhon dus su
ni gnad du ma bzhed nga rgas pas mi zhu byas pas/ khyod dkon mchog srungs kyi chos kyis ngoms 'dug ste/ de nga las ma byung na su las byung gsungs nas phyag byugs/ bla ma
chen po'i bka' drin lags zhus pas/ gang gang byin gsungs/ 'di dang 'di rnams gnang lags zhus pas/ de las nga la yang med thams cad rdzogs par byin 'dug de gzhan la ster
ri mna' skyol gsungs nas mgul la phreng ba bcug der bla mas ni rdzogs par ma gnang bla ma sgom pa la zhus pa lags mod/ zhus pas phreng ba phud de ngan pa 'di gsung nas dbu
la bye ma sbar gang rgyab/ re shig na da 'o na khyod kyis gzhan la ston la mgo lus tshang bar byin cig ces rjes su gnang ba yang thob/ sgro ston gyis rang gi yo byad yod
do cog phul bas paN chen mnyes te/ dbang rnams rdzogs par bskur/ rgyud 'grel gyi dka' gnas rnams dri gtugs mdzad cing gsan/ de ltar pan chen dang bla ma sgom pa las sems
'grel skor gsum/ gsung gdams ngag cha lag dang bcas pa ma lus par gsan nas/ chos phran

bag re gsung zhing slob ma thams cad la sor bsam gnang nas sgom pa kho na la btsud de/ gzhung bshad mi mdzad pa las/ dgung lo bdun cu rtsa gnyis bzhes pa na grub chen yu mo
la chos skor rdzogs par gnang ste/ dgung lo brgya bcu la chos kyi dbyings su snyoms par zhugs so// 'di'i phyi rten sgro ris gnas sgang na bzhugs pa zhig pa'i sa 'bur tsam
las ring bsrel du ma rnyed cing tsha tsha'i nang bzhugs gzungs kyi sham bur bla ma gnam la rtsegs kyi thugs dgongs rdzogs par gyur cig ces pa yod pa/ phyis kun spangs chos
grags dpal bzang pos mjal bas ring bsrel brgya phrag mang po rnyed/ khang bu brtsegs pa'i mchod rten bsos te bzhugs so// //4 grub chen yu mo mi bskyod rdo rje/bla ma
de'i thugs kyi sras gcig pu grub chen yu mo ni/ gangs ti se'i rtsar yab rngam khro bo zhes pa la/ sras shAkya rgyal mtshan/ rdor byang / tshul she/ grub chen ste bzhi 'khrungs
so// 'di nyid kyis rim gyis la stod lhor byon nas dgung lo bcu pa la lto 'cher gyi gnas su mkhan po stag lo tsA ba gzhon brtson las rab tu byung ste/ mtshan 'dogs pa'i
tshe gdung rus rngam du 'dug dad pa shin tu che ba cig 'dug pas/ rngam btsun dad pa rgyal po zhes par 'dogs so

zhes mtshan de ltar btags/ mkhan po la chos gsan zhing lo gnyis bzhugs/ de nas don mo rir se ston sgra gcan 'dzin dang / dge gnas su ba reg thos pa dga'i drung du/ mngon pa
dang phar phyin gsan/ mi rnams dbu ba yu mo'i mgo 'dra zhes gleng bas rang nyid kyis yu mo zhes mtshan bla dwags su btags so// rma dge mthong dang / snyegs la dbu tshad
dang / sog 'dul ba 'dzin pa la 'dul ba dang spyod phyogs gsan/ mdo rtsa la zhal ton mdzad/ kye rdor sogs sngags skor yang gsan/ der grogs cig gis dgun ci byed 'dri pa la
mtshams byas sngags kyi dpe 'dra 'di gsungs pas/ 'o na byon la ga tshad na rdo rje snying 'grel 'dug zer bas de 'dri'am zhes zer ma thag sngon gyi bag chags sad nas dad pas
spu zing du gyur te/ dpe de g.yar nas 'dri zhir gzigs pas shin tu dad de sus shes dris pas/ so ma nA thas shes zer ba la/ de sngon gyi mi zhig yin snyam nas/ dbus su khams
pa lde'u pa la spyod phyogs gsan cing bzhugs pa'i dus su/ paN chen zla mgon skar chur bzhugs zer ba gsan te/ rdo rje snying 'grel shes sam byas pas/ de los mkhyen der
ma zad/ spyir gsang sngags

tsam la mkhas/ khyad par du dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel pa chen mo yang mkhyen zer/ zhus na gnang ngam dris pas/ spyir bka' dog ste da lta bal yul du gshegs pa'i zhabs tog
pa med pas 'gro nus na gnang 'ong zer/ sum pa rdo rje gzhon nus zhu sna byas nas/ pan chen dang / bla ma gnam brtsegs gnyis/ kyai rdo rtsa sngags dang / de bzhin gshegs
pa'i yi ge brgya pa la zhu tig mdzad pa'i skabs su mjal te chos 'brel zhus pas/ sngags gnyis po la bshad pa mdzad nas gsungs/ chang dkar yol gang gnang / paN chen gyis gser
thig po dang / gla rtsi'i rkyal pa mang po bstan nas/ 'di rnams khyod kyis bal yul thug khur nus shing mgo thon na/ sang res nga bod du 'ong dus chos sbyin no gsungs
pas/ sgom pa tshul grags la dpe cha bcol pa len du byon pas/ khyod gar 'gro zer ba la sngar gyi lo rgyus bsnyad pas/ paNDi ta la chos mi khugs/ sngar yang mang pos ma khugs
pa yin/ de bas paNDi ta'i chos ma lus pa mkhyen pa nged kyi bla ma rnor bzang na bzhugs byas pas/ blo 'gyur te ston pa rgyal pa 'od/ sgom pa dbang ba song / sgom pa tshul
khrims grags rnams kyis zhu sna byas/ sgro ston la zhu rten gser zho 'ga' zhig dang / dung

chos legs pa cig ka pa li cig phul pas/ khyod kyi 'di tsho la nye bcad sogs 'dul pa 'dzin pa de btsun pa zas za mi shes gos gon mi shes pa thams cad la zhal 'chol pha ltar
byed pa yin zer/ de'i thugs zin khyod yin par 'dug pas/ yon tan cig yod pa yin te 'ong gsung nas chos gnang bar zhal gyis bzhes/ bla ma dgung lo bdun cu rtsa gnyis pa la
zhal mjal te/ lo bzhi bar med du bsten nas 'grel pa skor gsum gyi gzhung man ngag cha lag dang bcas pa dang / mtshan brjod man ngag gi bshad pa dang / gsang 'dus sgron gsal
la sogs pa gsan pa'i dus su/ bla ma bag tsam bsnyung ba na/ gtsang ston 'di la chos ma phogs kyi bar du nga ma bshad ces mkha' 'gro ma la gsol ba btab nas gdams pa thams
cad rdzogs par gnang ngo // mthar yang dbang bzhi pa gnang / bdag po chen po'i dbang bskur mdzad nas 'dis rgyud kyi bka' gnad khrol ba yin/ skal ldan ma gtogs pa la ma
bshad gsung ste/ rdo rje lag tu gtad/ rgyud 'di khrid dang bdag po'i dbang ma thob pa la mi 'chad pa yin/ dpe tsam gyis mi khrol bas lan gsum yan chad thos nas tshig zin
cing don go bas bla ma la tshur bzlas shing gtan la dbab dgos pa yin gsung /

dgung lo lnga bcu pa la 'u yug tu byon nas nub ma'i mda' rgyal khab zhes par gzhi phab ste/ phur dben gnas kyang mdzad/ gag tshangs kyi phu'i brag tu'ang thugs dam yun ring
du mdzad pas grub pa thob ste/ dbang rgyud bshad man ngag mang du gsungs/ gsal sgron bzhi dang gces bsdus la sogs pa'i gdams pa'i bstan bcos kyang mang du mdzad nas dgung
lo brgyad bcu'i bar du bzhugs te/ bstan pa la bya ba rgya cher mdzad pa yin no//slob ma yang sras mchog dharme shwA ra/ wa brag dkar ba/ gnyal pa gro/ gnyos kyi khung ba/
grub thob dharma bo dhi/ mkhas pa tre bo mgon po/ se chos kyi mnga' bdag la sogs pa mang du byon te/ wa brag dkar ba dang / gnyal pa gro chen po gnyis kyis bka' gdams
la 'dag 'byar yun ring du byas pas/ rtogs pa'i khyad par ci yang ma byung ba las/ phyis bla ma yu mo'i drung du 'ongs nas gdams ngag bsgoms pa'i zhag dang po la rtags rnams
rdzogs te/ lam gyi mchog tu nges pa rnyed/ bsgoms pas mngon par shes pa rgya chen po dang ldan no// bla ma yu mos skya ka'i gzugs su bsgyur te/ wa brag dkar ba brag thog
cig na nyin mo'i rnal 'byor sgom pa'i sar byon nas/ khyi lud kyi phung bo la mchu bdar te skad phyung ba dang / des ngo shes te

bla ma rin po che bdag la de 'dra'i kyal ka mi mdzad par zhu zer nas phyag phul bas/ bla ma mnyes nas sgyu 'phrul sku'i bkod pa mtha' yas pa bstan to//wa brag dkar ba/khyad
par du wa brag dkar ba ni/ rdzogs rim gyi lha grub pas sprul bsgyur nus pa ste/ dpal chen rgwa los gnam rtse ldang gi phu'i ngang tshang brag phug nas bya rog gi gzugs kyis
phyin nas/ wa brag dkar ba'i nye logs na sha 'dug pa la 'then pa dang / des ngo shes nas/ rgwa chung ba khyod de 'dras ci bya tshur shog la sha zo zer te/ dpal chen po
dang phan tshun stag rnam par rtse ba'i sgyu ma'i bkod pa ci yang ston res byas so//gnyos kyi khud pa/gnyos kyi khud pa ni/ ra sgreng du lo bdun cu'i bar du bka' gdams
la sbyangs pas yon tan ma skyes pa las/ bu yug tu yu mo dang mjal man ngag bsgoms ma thag rlung dbu mar tshud zhi ba can grub cing 'dzin pa'i yon tan thob po// des ngor rje
ston pa/ des dol pa 'gar ston dbang phyug grub sogs la rim par brgyud pa byung ngo // tre bo rdo rje mgon po ni/ yu mo la gzhung gdams pa mtha' dag mnos shing / rwa chos
rab la yang gsan nas bshad pa'i gra yun ring du btsugs pas/ glan bang so ba chos dbang dang / ldum ra sgang pa gnyan rdo rje seng ge sogs

slob ma mang du thon/ gnyan la snye mdo thams cad mkhyen pas gsan to//5 sras dharme shwa ra/yu mo'i sku sras dharme shwa ra ni/ yab dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa lnga pa'i tshe 'u
yug rgyal khab tu 'khrungs/ skyes stobs kyis thugs rab shin tu che zhing / mtshan chos kyi dbang phyug tu btags/ chos 'di sngon gyi bag chags sad de/ yab la legs par gsan
nas/ dgung lo bcu gnyis pa la dbang mdor bstan gsungs/ bcu drug pa la mi chen mang po la sems 'grel gsum ka gsungs/ bcu bdun pa nas lo ra la rgyud 'grel dus chos su gnang
/ nyer lnga tshun la yab kyi yon tan bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mkhyen/ spyir yab kyi zhal slob dge bshes che dgu mtha' dag la gtugs nas/ spyod phyogs dbu tshad/ lam rim/
rgyud sde mang po dgung lo sum cu'i bar du gsan cing sbyangs/ dpyal kun dga' rdo rje/ sa chen/ rgya gling pa sogs mkhas pa mang po rtsod pas zil gyis gnan te mkhas pa'i
grags pas sa steng thams cad khyab/ gtsang g.yas ru shangs rtse gdong gi shar phyogs smon mkhar gyi grong chung dgon par phal cher bzhugs nas spyod phyogs dang / tshad
ma dang / 'phags skor sogs kyang gsung zhing gtso bor chos 'di'i sgo nas bstan pa'i sgron me 'bar bar mdzad do//khang gsar pa nam mkha' 'od/'di'i slob ma

khang gsar pa nam mkha' 'od ni/ 'gos dbang btsan la rigs tshogs gsan pas/ sde snod mtha' dag la mkhas pa/ sras mchog dharme shwa ra las sems 'grel skor gsum gyi gzhung gdams
ngag ma lus par gsan te/ rgyud 'grel chen mo'i bshad pa byang ba/ yan lag drug gi nyams rtogs khyad par can 'khrungs pa zhig go/ //6 ma cig sprul sku jo 'bum/bla ma dharme
shwa ra las sras lcam sring gnyis kyi dang po ma cig sprul sku jo 'bum ni/ byad gzugs mdzes pa/ DA ki'i mtshan dang ldan zhing gzhon dus spyod pa sna tshogs mdzad/ skyes
stobs che bas yab la chos rnams gsan cing mkhyen/ yab grongs dus yum gyis bskul bas mthu bsgrubs te dgra mang po brlag par byas/ tshe bdag gi zhal gzigs/ nus mthu'i pha
rol tu son/ de dus byang chub kyi lam sna cig ma zin na cis kyang mi phan zhes nges 'byung bcos min du 'khrungs te/ sngar yab las gsan pa'i rdo rje'i rnal 'byor rtse gcig
tu bsgoms pas de ma thag rlung dbu mar tshud de mngon shes lnga thob/ brag ri la yang thogs pa med par rgyu zhing / kham zas la mi ltos/ tshe de nyid la rang bzhin gyis
grub pa'i rnal 'byor ma rnams dang skal ba mnyam pa'i 'phags mar gyur te/

kho mo o rgyan du 'gro zhes sgra 'od dang / sa g.yo ba la sogs pa'i ltas dang bcas te mkha' spyod du gshegs/ lcam lakShmIM ka ra'i sprul par grags so// //7 grub thob se mo
che ba/gnyis pa sras grub thob se mo che ba ni/ ljags mi bde yang chung ngu'i dus nas klog ma bslabs par mkhyen/ yab la dbang rgyud bshad gdams ngag dang bcas pa thob cing
/ sprul sku jo 'bum las kyang 'grel chung padma can dang / sgrub thabs man ngag phran mang po thob/ slar yang mkhas pa nam mkha' 'od las rgyud 'grel gyi gzab bshad dang
/ yu mo'i bstan bcos 'ga' zhig dang / yab kyis mdzad pa'i ro bcud stong thun la sogs pa dang / 'bro lugs kyi gsung sgros 'od zer phreng ba dang / jo btsun khyung gis mdzad
pa'i dri med rgyan rnams gsan cing / de dag kyang lan re la thugs su chud la/ mi brjed pa'i gzungs thob/ rab tu byung ba'i mtshan nam mkha' rgyal mtshan zhes btags/ bla
ma gye ra ba dang rtse gdong ba sogs la chos drug phyag chen bde mchog sogs gsan/ rdo rje'i rnal 'byor la thugs dam snying por mdzad pas gang snang stong gzugs kho nar
shar la/ mngon par mkhyen pa thogs med du mnga'/ gzhan gyi sems shes pa'i mngon shes 'dzem med du gsungs

pas 'ga' zhig mos kyang phal cher skrag cing bag tsha bar gyur pas/ bla ma rtse gdong pas bka' rgya btab nas phyis snod ldan re re tsam las gnang du mi bzhed/ gtsang gi 'o
lung se mo cher bzhugs pas grub thob se mo che bar grags/ lcam jo 'bum mkha' spyod la gshegs pa'i dus mchod kyi skabs su/ zla ba phyed kyi bar du mi g.yo bar ting nge 'dzin
gyi sgo mang po la mnyam par bzhag ste/ de las bzhengs nas 'di skad gsungs pa/ bdag gis phag gi lo gsar la// 'od gsal chen por mnyam gzhag dus// sngon gyi skye ba dran
zhing gsal// dper na gnyid sad rmi lam bzhin// sngon 'das dus na 'jig rten khams// 'od zer kun nas 'gro zhes par// bskal pa chen po bzang ldan la// bcom ldan bde gshegs
rdzogs sangs rgyas// dri med sgron ma zhes pa byon/ rgyal sras zla ba dri med dang // nyi ma'i snying po zhes pa byung // bdag ni 'dzam gling sa yi bdag/ 'khor los bsgyur
ba stobs po che// gtsug gi nor bu zhes byar skyes// lha mdzes 'od mdzes nyi mdzes gsum// btsun mo'i mchog yin gzhan nyis brgya// dpal 'bar zla 'od snying rje sogs// sras
ni gzhon nu sum brgya yod// blo

gros snying po la sogs pa'i// blon po dam pa nyi khri yod// rgyal phran 'bangs bcas brgyad khri yod// pho brang 'tsho ba bzang po zhes// mchu zheng dpag tshad bzhi bcu pa//
de na rgyal srid 'dod yon la// kun nas spyod cing gnas pa na// sems dpa' gnyis po der byon nas// sangs rgyas 'khor bcas mchod pa dang // chos ni nyan par bskul gyur kyang
// bdag ni rgyal po'i dregs pa yis// sems dpa' gnyis kyi bka' bcag cing // brnyas te dus su ma nyan to// phyi zhig rgyal po 'gyod gyur nas// sems dpa' gnyis la mdongs gsol
te// sangs rgyas 'khor bcas rtag mchod cing // dam pa'i chos kyang nyan cing bsgoms// de nas bdag ni tshe 'phos te// byang chub sems dpa'i ngag bcag cing // brnyas pa'i
sdig pas lhung gyur te// phug ron skye ba brgya blangs shing // de nas bya rgod lus nyi shu// bye'u sum cu skya ka bcu// ne tso bzhi bcu khrung khrung gi// skye ba lnga
bcu lha yul du// shang shang te'u'i lus bcu gsum// de nas pu shud lus drug cu// chu bya lnga bcu rma bya bcu// sbrang bu nyi shu sbur bcu gsum// de nas mir skyes dmus long
la// tshe lo drug bcur sdug bsngal myong // de nas rigs ngan lkugs shing dbul// nad kyi lo ni lnga bcur gtses// slar

yang grog ma'i skye ba gsum// ra lnga khyi gsum rta lnga dang // mtha' mar lug ni dkar por skyes// rdzi bos 'ur rdo 'phangs bas shi// ro de rnal 'byor pa bzhis 'khyer// brag
phug dben par tshogs 'khor byas// de yis mir skyes bdag rang yin// ngan 'gro zad mod sdig lhag gis// mig mi gsal zhing lce mi bde// rna ba 'on pa 'di lags so// rdzogs sangs
rgyas la bsnyen bkur zhing // theg pa chen po'i chos thos pas// da lta dam pa'i rigs su skyes// bla ma grub thob mchog dang mjal// zab lam rnal 'byor yan lag drug/ nyams
su len 'di byung ba yin// khyad par ma gcig 'das mchod dus// phyag rgya chen po'i rang nyams la// ye shes mkha' 'gro rnam lnga byon// de rjes bde mchog dkyil 'khor mthong
// mi skyod snang ba mtha' yas dang // 'jam dpal sgrol ma spyan ras gzigs// phyag na rdo rje stobs po che// mi g.yo ba dang byams pa mgon// de rnams kyi ni sku mthong
gsal// de rjes dam pa'i sangs rgyas kyi// brgyud pa'i bla ma rnams byon te// phyag na yid bzhin nor bu bsnams// zhal nas gdams pa'i bdud rtsi stsal// khyod ni skye 'di'i
'og rol tu// rab tu dga' ba'i sa grub nas//

gtsang ma'i gnas su nyer 'gro zhing // sems can ther 'bum mang po yi// don yang 'grub par 'gyur ces gsung // zhes sogs mang du gsungs shing / da ni kho bo skye ba bcu drug
na sangs rgyas nas sems can thams cad sgrol bar byed de/ skye ba dang po mi gdung ba'i lha/ gnyis pa 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po gdugs kyi nor bu/ gsum pa rgyal po dbang
bskur chen po/ bzhi pa rgyal po don yod nor bu/ lnga ba rgyal po 'khor lo nor bu/ drug pa rgyal po rdo rje 'chang / bdun pa rma bya'i rgyal po gser du snang ba/ brgyad pa
nam mkha' lding gi rgyal po/ dgu pa rgyal po lag na padma/ bcu pa rgyal po dge ba bkod pa/ bcu gcig pa rgyal po lag na rin po che'i phyag rgya/ bu gnyis pa rgyal po pho
brang ral gri can/ bcu gsum pa rgyal po grags pa mtha' yas/ bcu bzhi pa lha'i bu dbang bsgyur rgyal po/ bco lnga pa 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po padma can/ bcu drug pa rgyal
po padma'i nor bu rnams su skyes nas sa bcu bgrod pas smon lam rdzogs shing / sems can thams cad smin par byas te sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su sbyang pa mthar thug
nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams padma can zhes bya ba bai DUrya las grub pa'i sa gzhi lag mthil ltar mnyam pa/ ngam grong

dang lung khung med pa/ gser gyi bye ma bdal ba/ der skyes pa'i sems can thams cad kyang dug gsum med cing longs spyod lhun gyis grub pa/ bud med dang nyan rang med pa theg
pa dman pa'i sgra yang mi grag pa/ der skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyang skye ba gcig gis thogs pa sha stag go/ der bdag de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang
dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas padma'i nor bu zhes bya bar 'tshang rgya ste/ 'khor byang chub sems dpa' 'ba' zhig la theg pa chen po'i chos ston to// ston pa de'i phyag
zhabs kyi sor mo re re las padma re re 'byung la de re re las kyang padma bye ba phrag ther 'bum 'byung zhing / de re re'i nang na sangs rgyas sprul pa'i sku bye ba phrag
ther 'bum byung nas sems can dpag tu med pa la theg pa chen po'i chos bstan te grol bar mdzad do// zhes rang gzhan gyi skye ba 'das ma 'ongs mang po lung bstan/ pho ba
lung phug tu bsnyung ba mi mnga' bar dbyu gu zla ba'i tshes brgyad la sku gdung ring bsrel gyi phung po can bzhag ste chos kyi skur thim mo//khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa
dpal/bla ma 'di la slob ma yang mchog tu gyur pa ni/ khro phu lo tsA ba/ dge bshes rma bya ba/ chos rje 'jam gsar ba/ bo dong rin rtse/ lho pa chos ldan dang lnga las/ bla
ma khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa dpal

ni/ sngar paN grub mang du bsten pas chos kyi mnga' bdag tu gyur nas/ chos 'di la lhag par mos pas/ se mo che ba smon mkhar gnas su gdan drangs te/ sbyor drug gi khrid phran
dang bcas pa gsan/ lo tsA ba'i sku tshe'i tshad dang khro phu'i dar rgud la sogs pa lung bstan pas mchog tu gus shing bsngags pa che bar mdzad do// //8 chos rje 'jam dbyangs
gsar ma/chos rje 'jam gsar ba ni yul nyad ro'i skyur bor/ yab slob dpon dpal chen zhes pa la sras gnyis 'khrungs pa'i chung shos yin/ mtshan jo sras blo bde zhes pa
mig 'khrul dang lugs kyi bstan bcos mtha' dag la mkhas shing / skyes stobs phul du byung bas byis pa'i dus nas/ gtsang nag pa'i 'grel pa la thun nyan byas te phar phyin
la slob gnyer byas/ yab dang mched 'das pa la brten nas 'khor ba las yid byung ste/ chu mig lung du sangs rgyas lam pa'i drung du rab tu byung / mtshan shes rab 'od zer du
btags/ chos dus su slob dpon bse dmar pa la phar phyin gsan cing / chos bar la mkhan po la bslab bya dang / bde mchog phag mo/ phyag chen gsan/ dka' thub la rgyun du gnas
pas lus sbyangs/ skabs der shig nad drag po byung ba la bzlog sgom mdzad cing sku lus sbyin par btang bas zug rngu la brten nas thugs

dam 'khrungs/ de nas yang mdze nad drag pos mnyel ba na slob dpon la phyag rdor mdo lugs zhus te/ mtshams dam par bcad nas tho rengs yud tsam re ma gtogs mnal ye ma log par
bzlas pa mdzad pas bskyed rim brtan par byung ste/ mthong ba tsam gyis gdon bgegs thams cad dngangs nas 'gro snyam pa byung / lo gcig dang zla ba drug na yi dam gyi zhal
gzigs te/ bsnyungs rtsa ba nas grol zhing / gzhan la 'dre gdon gnod pa na/ thugs gtad pa tsam gyis 'phral du 'gro ba byung / de nas phar phyin gyi tshig don gsung sgros
thams cad ma bsnyel bar bton pas slob dpon las kyang mkhas zhes grags/ zhang 'bri mtshams pa la mngon pa byang bar bslabs/ de nas gsang phur byon te/ gnyal zhig la dbu tshad
phar phyin rnams gsan/ chos bar la paNDi ta dA na shi la la bde mchog dang gshed dmar gyi dbang dang sngags chos mang du gsan/ paNDi tas kyang rje 'di la phar phyin gsan/
de nas sa skya pa rnams dang bgro gleng mdzad pas thams cad las rgyal yang thugs ma tshim ste/ lan cig gnyal zhig la rnam nges kyi chos thon pa'i rjes su khyed de ltar
bzhed pa lags sam zhus pas/ thugs rgyal bzhengs te/ 'di ma

skyong na gnyal zhig min gsungs nas dam bca' khas blangs/ rje 'dis 'di ma khegs na gtsang ston min zhus te/ phyogs chos dpe la 'gro mi 'gro la nyi ma gsum du mun sros sros
kyi bar du bgro gleng mdzad pas rje 'di rgyal/ gnyal zhig gis de'i nub mo ja bzang po zho nyi shu'i mang bskol byas/ dar yug cig btang ste/ 'di la nga 'jam dpal dang mnyam
pa yin snyam pa yod de/ nga bas kyang khyed shes rab che bar 'dug pas 'jam dpal rang du gda'o// gsungs pas 'jam dpal gsar mar mtshan grags te/ snyan pa'i ba dan gyis kun
tu khyab/ gnyal zhig bu dgu'i ya gyal du grags/ der tshad ma rdo rje phreng ba mdzad nas gtsang du byon pa dang / slob dpon bse dmar ba grongs 'dug pas thugs skyo ste/
yul zhing rnams phag tu btsongs nas slob dpon gyi dgongs rdzogs la btang / sa lam gyi rnam gzhag me tog phreng ba mdzad/ thar ba gling du byon nas dpyal chos bzang las lo
tsA bslabs/ de nas 'dol chung dang / rkyang 'dur du bzhugs nas grwa ba phyed dang nyi brgya la phar tshad kyi TI ka mdzad nas gsungs/ khro phu lo tsA ba dang / dpyal kun
dga' snying bo dang / snar thang pa gro chen po dang / zhang chos bla dang bya mo khung pa rnams la'ang dbang rgyud gdams ngag mang po dang sa sde

sogs gsan/ kha che paNDi ta shAkya shrI la dbang dang gdams pa mang po gsan zhing / lo tsA mdzad de/ u rgyan sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs sogs bsgyur/ ko brag pa la lam 'bras gsan
pas thugs snang 'gyur te/ sku mtshams dam po la bzhugs dus rdo rje lus kyi rtsa gnas mngon sum du gzigs/ 'jam dpal ngag gi dbang phyug mjal ba la/ bdag gi bla ma dang gdams
ngag sgom pa gang legs zhus pas/ se mo che ba la dus 'khor dang sbyor drug zhus nas lam myur du bgrod par 'gyur zhes lung bstan thob ste/ se mo che ba de g.yas ru grong
chung na sprul sku jo 'bum mkha' spyod du byon pa'i chos 'khor mdzad pa'i skabs su der 'byon par brtsams pa na/ gnod sbyin chen po bdun gyis gtsos pa'i snang srid kyi
lha 'dre mang pos me 'od dang 'jigs pa'i gzugs ston pa dang sgra drag po sgrog pa dang / rdo char 'bebs pa sogs cho 'phrul mang po bstan pas/ dngos grub ster ba'i yi dam
lha// gnod par sems pa'i 'dre gdon gnyis// mi bdag la ro mnyam khyad par med// lha 'dre gang dga' ma dgar shog/ gnyen po thos bsam sgom gsum dang // spang bya nyon mongs
rnam rtog rnams// mi bdag la ro mnyam khyad par med// nyams bzang ngan gang 'ga' ma dgar shog/ 'khor brgya

dang stong gis bskor ba dang // rang gcig pu gang bder nyal ba gnyis// mi bdag la ro mnyam khyad par med// 'khor mang nyung gang gis bskor ba dang // tshe ring nad med phun
tshogs dang // dus da lta nyid du 'chi ba gnyis// mi bdag la ro mnyam khyad par med// tshe ring thung gang gis bskor ba dang // ces sogs chos brgyad ro snyoms pa'i mgur
gsungs pas zhi/ gtsang gzhung la yar byon tsa na/ nam mkha' thams cad sangs rgyas byang sems kyis gang ba'i snang ba byung / se mo che pa dang mjal ma thag bla ma de nyid
phyag na rdo rje dngos su gzigs te snang ba 'gyur ba'i mos gus tshud 'bul nod rgya chen po mdzad de/ sbyor drug zhus pas sngon 'gro'i khrid tshar ba dang mchog dbang gong
ma bskur nas sor bsam gnang ste bsgoms pas/ sngar gyi chos kyi go ba tsho spun skogs bzhin du bud/ zhag gcig na bsam gtan gyi drod dang rtags rnams byung ste yid ches gsungs
thob nas/ slar yang rkyang 'dur du byon dbyar chos grol nas/ bo dong rin rtse sogs slob ma bcu dang lhan cig dus 'khor gsan du byon te/ zhag bcu gsum la dbang rdzogs
par thob nas/ zla ba bzhi'i bar du rgyud 'grel man ngag dang bcas pa ma lus par mnos/ de nas rkyang 'dur du/ thub pa'i dbang po 'khor dang bcas pa zhal gzigs pa la/ yan
lag bdun pa zhig phul/ sangs rgya ba'i rgyu lam

'bras bu thams cad bla ma sangs rgyas kyi drung du sgro 'dogs bcad zin pas chos ni ma zhus gsungs/ rdo rje theg pa mchog gi lam zhugs kyang // las dang ye shes phyag rgya rtsa
rlung dang // phra mo thig le la sogs bsgom pa yang // thun mong dngos grub 'grub kyis mchog min gsungs// paN chen rnams dang grub chen grangs med dang // bod yul gsang
sngags spyod pa 'bum gyis kyang // sangs rgyas rnams kyi rdo rje'i nye lam mchog/ rgyud kun la sbas bltas pas rnyed ma yin// bla med rgyud bstan rdo rje rtse bstan gyi//
rgyal po'i pho brang mtha' drug tshul bzhi'i sgo// legs bsdams rdo rje tshig gi sgo lcags bcug/ gsang 'dzin chen po rnams kyis lde mig sbas// rigs gsum mgon dang de rnams
rjes 'brangs pa'i// 'grel pa rdo rje'i sgo 'byed lde mig gis// dus 'khor rin chen bang mdzod sgro glegs phye// rgyud kun dgongs pa sbyor drug nyid yin par// skal ldan
bla ma rnams kyis rtogs par gyur// dngos grub kun 'byung rin chen sna tshogs dang // sbyor drug yid bzhin nor bu dngos su gnang // rtsod ldan shin tu myur bar sangs rgya
ba'i// zab lam 'di ni bla ma'i man ngag dang // rgyal sras 'phags pa rnams kyi rgyud 'grel las// bsod

nams shes rab stobs kyis kho bos rnyed// yid bzhin nor bu gos hrul gyis bstums nas// gter du sbas te 'dzam gling 'di nyid na// nga nyid nor che smras kyang su yid ches// gang
zhig la yang phan 'dogs nus par 'gyur// de bas bdag rang 'tshe med 'cho sla ba'i// gnas der sgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan rtser btags nas// rtse gcig mi rtog sems kyis gsol
btab na// rang gzhan dgos 'dod 'byung bar the tshom med// de phyir kho bo dben par bsdod la dka'// 'chi med bdud rtsi rnyed nas zas ngan spong // nor bu rin chen rnyed nas
gser yang 'dor// mchog thob dman pa 'dor ba ji ltar 'khrul// sngon chad gdams ngag brgya phrag du ma bslabs// 'on kyang da dung gzhan dag tshol bar 'dod// da ni sangs rgyas
thams cad byon lags kyang // myur du 'tshang rgya'i lam gzhan zhu bsam med// kho bo yon tan gyi khyad par 'ga' zhig ma rnyed kyi bar du mgo la me shor ba gsod pa la
brtson pa ltar 'bad nas bsgom pa'i ched du dben par mchis pa la mi mnyes pa ma dad na bzod par 'tshal zhes sogs spring yig bai DUrya'i phreng ba zhes pa dang / rnal 'byor
bdag gi dka' spyad tshig 'ga' bshad// sngon yang bstan 'dir mi lus lan 'ga' thob// kha che'i yul

du rgyal bu dpal ming can// za hor yul du bram ze dga' ba'i blo// ko sa la ru khyim bdag grags pa'i ming // sum cu gsum du nor bu dri ma med// de nas 'phos nas da lta 'dir
skyes so// longs spyod rgya chen mnga' ris phun tshogs kyang // mkhas pas sgyu ma brdzun du shes pa ltar// ma chags spangs nas dad pas rab tu byung // byis pa'i dus nas chos
spyod las la brtson// skye 'chis 'jigs pas mtshan ldan bla ma btsal// dam pa rnyed tshe rtse gcig gsol ba btab// byang chub 'dod min yid la gzhan ma bsam// dam pa'i chos
phyir lus srog thed la bor// 'bol ba'i stan spangs spen ma'i gdan la 'dug/ chos brgyad dpa' brjid bzang po'i gos spangs nas// phyags dar khrod pa dman pa'i gos la brten//
de tshe dad pas sdug bsngal lam du khyer// las ngan dbang gi lus la shig nad byung // snying rje bzlog sgom bdag lus sbyin par btang // chos nyid rtogs pas zug rngu
rang sar grol// byams pa'i dbang gis gnod byed pha mar shes// mdze nad 'byung bo'i gdon gyis btab pa'i tshe// so dang sen mo'i mdog shor smin ma byi// lo gcig zla drug 'dod
lha'i bsnyen pa bskyal// de tshe gdon grol rkyen

ngan dpal du shar// spros bral rnam dag gdod nas gnas pa'i don// khrid dang ngo sprod gdams ngag ma bstan par// lo brgyad byis pa'i dus nas gsal bar mthong // gnas lugs don
gyi sgro 'dogs legs par bcad// chu 'thung rde 'cha' bdud rtsi'i bcud len la// lo brgyad bar du dka' spyad sna tshogs byas// byang chub 'dod pas lus srog thed la bor// zab
mo'i gdams pas bde sdug lam du khyer// sa gzhi'i khri steng nam mkha'i bla res brgyan// byin pa'i stan gting lag ngar rngas su bcug/ 'dod yon kun spangs sprang bo'i cha
bzung ste// lang tsho'i gzi 'od dka' spyad drag pos bcom// pha yul nye drung bde skyid blos spangs te// byang chub bsgrub phyir bkres skom sna tshogs myong // sdug bsngal
bshad na dgra yang mchi ma 'chor// gzhon pa'i me tog rgas pa'i sad kyis bcom// srod kyi kha ton 'don dang gsol ba gdab// nyin phyed sde snod rgyud sde kun la bltas// phyi
dro phyag dang gtor ma la sogs byas// 'khor ba'i gnas 'dir kho bos

nom pa spyad// sngon 'gro skyabs 'gro sems bskyed maNDal phul// dngos gzhi sems dpa' gsum gyi nyams len byas// rjes la dmigs med zab dang rgya cher bsngos// tshe thung 'di
la stong log ma byas so// chos pa'i so nam yin pas thos bsam byas// chos kyi rtsa ba yin pas gnas lugs bsgoms// chos la 'bras bu dgos pas smon lam btab// sgo gsum tha mal
nam yang ma bzhag go/ thog mar 'chi bas 'jigs pas bla ma btsal// bar du 'chi phrod dgos pas nyams len byas// tha mar 'chi rgyu med pas nyal nas bsdad// mi rgan nga yi nyams
len rnam thar yin// bdag la bsgoms dang ma bsgoms khyad med cing // bde sdug skye 'chi'i 'du shes zad gyur kyang // gzhan rnams blo sna brtung phyir dben par 'gro/ bdag
la soms la sgrub pa mdzad par zhu// zhes sogs bslab bya zhal thems kyi yi ge rkyang 'dur dang 'bob chung gi ka ba la sbyar nas/ dpon slob gnyis nam la bzhud de/ rgya nag
ri bo rtse lngar thegs nas thugs dam la rtse gcig tu bzhugs/ slob ma rnams kyis phyogs kun tu tshol du phyin pas lo mang rab na rnyed de/ slob ma dbu chen dang dpon che
bas/ gdan 'dren rta ba mang po rgya nag la brdzangs te/ ri bo rtse lngar phyin/ khyed bod yul du mi 'byon na/ nged rnams

dus gcig la lceb pa'i mna' phul bas/ thugs rjes dgongs nas bod du byon/ lam rnams su'ang 'gro ba dpag tu med pa'i don mdzad/ slar rkyang 'dur du phebs pa na/ dbus gtsang khams
gsum gyi bu slob dpag tu med pa 'dus te/ klog pa ba rnams la dus 'khor gtso bor gyur pa'i gzhung bshad dang / spong ba pa rnams la sbyor drug gi gdams pa lo drug gi bar
du gnang ba'i mthar/ dus 'khor da res las mi bshad pas/ su nyan 'dod pa shog gsung pa'i skad phyogs kun la btang bas/ tshogs pa rgya mtsho lta bu 'dus pa la dbang rgyud
'grel man ngag dang bcas pa rgyas par gnang ste rdzogs ma thag da 'di nas bde ba can du skyes nas sangs rgyas kyi zhing sbyong zhing sems can smin par byed gsung zhing
/ sa ga zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi'i tho rangs 'ja' 'od dang me tog gi char 'bab pa sogs cho 'phrul sna tshogs dang bcas pas mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan te/ gdung la
'jam dpal dang / phyag rdor dang / dus 'khor gyi sku dang ring bsrel yungs 'bru lta bu mang du byon to// //9 kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/rje 'di'i sras kyi thu bo ni rje
btsun rgwa lo dang / kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer gnyis yin la/ chos sku ba ni yul myang stod kyi gnas utpa la kha phye ba lta bu'i gser sdings su/ gdung sum pa/ yab grub

thob kyi rgyal po gser sdings pa gzhon nu 'od dang / yum 'gar btsun ma shes rab rgyan gyi sras su sku'i skye ba bzung / g.ya' ma ri'i gtsug lag khang gi 'dabs su yum gyi ming
po 'gar grags pa dbang phyug dang / sbrum ma skyong du bcug nas/ shing pho khyi lo'i stong 'bring nyi ma sgra gcan gyis bzung ba dang dus mtshungs par sku bltams/ yum
gyis mtshan bdag med rdo rjer btags/ yum gyi lad mo byas pas yi ge 'dri klog dang / chos spyod kyi kha ton rnams tshegs med par mkhyen/ de nas gser sdings su bla ma dge 'dun
la bsnyen bkur te/ bzod pa gsol nas gser sdings pa chen po'i drung du zhang po dang lhan cig chos nyan pa na/ shin tu gzhon pas rtse thabs 'ba' zhig gis dus 'da' pa gzigs
te/ bdag med rdo rje khyod kyi rtsed mgo dang / nga'i chos mgo 'dzugs pa dus mnyam du byed pas/ nga dang chos la ma gus pa zhig gam/ zhes bka' bskyon pas chos rna bas
nyan cing rtse thabs rkang lag gis byed pa la 'gal ba ci mchi/ chos gsungs pa rnams 'di dang 'di'o zhes lhag chad med par skyang bas/ kun gyis 'di ni sprul pa zhig go zhes
ya mtshan du sgrog cing sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa'i tshul brjod pas paN chen shAkya shrI'i sprul par kun gyis shes so// bla ma yang dgyes

te yab tu zhal gyis bzhes nas/ de phyin gyi bstan bcos rnams kyi sbyar byang du rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po zhes mdzad do// bcu gsum pa la gnas snying pa chos kyi rin
chen gyis mkhan po/ glang pa phang thang pa shAkya dar gyis slob dpon mdzad nas rab tu byung / mtshan yang chos kyi 'od zer du btags/ yab gser sdings pa chen po'i drung
du smon 'jug gi sdom pa dang / thog mar dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob/ gdams pa mang po zhig gsan pa'i skabs su/ rdo rje 'chang chen byin brlabs
kyis// byang chub sems la brtan pa thob// snang sems srid pa hrul bor song // 'gyu ba sems kyi de nyid mthong // thams cad rtsol med lhun grub rdzogs// zhes zhus pas/
'o de tsug 'ong ba yin/ ngas ji ltar ngo sprad pa bzhin du khyod la par btab pa bzhin rtsol med du 'byung ba 'di rang brod gsungs nas/ 'dus pa dang / dgyes rdor gyi dbang
/ rim lnga/ chos drug lam 'bras sogs gnang ba ni/ gnas pa rtsa yi de nyid shes// g.yo ba rlung la rang dbang thob// bkod pa byang chub sems kyis brgyan// lus ngag sems
ni bde gsal stong // rgyu lam 'bras bu'i bzhugs tshul shes// zhes zhus pas/ 'o cag pha bu la de tsam re ste re sar byung / ngas snying po'i lde

mig gtad zin gyis/ gzhon dus bshes gnyen phyogs med grangs med bsten la/ theg pa mtha' dag gi lung nod cig sde snod dang rgyud sde thams cad kyi sgo phye la/ 'dod dgu 'byung
ba'i nor bu rnams gdul bya'i sems can ris med pa la rang rang gi skal ba dang 'tsham par brims shig snying bo bsdus pa'i lde mig gis// sgo lcags btsan yang phyed de mchi//
thog mar nges shes skyes na yang // da dung rgyu mtshan phye nas soms// de ltar byas na thub bstan dang // sems can kun la phan pa byas// nga yis 'bad pa'ang don dang
bcas// de ring kho bo'i bsam pa rdzogs// zhes gsungs// dgung lo bco lnga pa nas lo bcu'i bar du gsan sbyong mdzad pas bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mkhyen/ de nas yab kyi zhal
nas/ chos rje 'jam gsar ba dang skye ba snga ma nas las 'brel yod pas de'i drung du song zhig ces brdzangs te/ 'jam gsar ba gru khang na bzhugs pa'i drung du byon nas/
gshed dmar gyii dbang gsan pa'i tshe bla ma gshin rje gshed du gzigs/ gzhan yang dbang byin brlabs/ phar tshad sogs gzhung gdams ngag mang du gsan/ chos rje'i zhal nas/
gzhan blo bum nang nam mkha' tsam// 'di blo phyi rol nam mkha' 'dra// de phyir

'di blo mtshungs med de// ma byung 'byung ba shin tu dkon// zhes tshogs su bsngags par mdzad do// grub thob se mo che ba la dus 'khor gsan du byon pas/ chos 'di la ngas dam
du byas pa yin zhing / gdams ngag dang rgyud rdzogs par zhu ba la bla ma lo mang du bsten dgos pa yin te/ de bas 'jam gsar brgyud mtho bar 'dug khong 'jam dpal dngos su
mthong bas ngas thams cad dus gcig la byin nas/ chos 'di'i bdag po khong la gtad pa yin pas/ khyod rang yang chos 'di 'dod na khong la zhus/ khyed gnyis skye ba mang po'i
dpon slob yin gsungs nas chos 'brel dang byin brlabs gnang / de nas gru khang du 'jam gsar ba la dus 'khor gyi dbang gsan pa'i tshe/ bla ma rdo rje shugs dngos su gzigs/
'di ltar gda' zhus pas/ rdo rje shugs dngos yin snyam pa'i dpa' yod pa yin/ 'o skol dpon slob la gegs kyis mi tshugs gsung / ye shes phab dus saM skr-i ta'i skad mang po
byung bas kha che paN chen gsang 'dus la mkhas pa'i bag chags sad par 'dug gsung / dkyil 'khor du zhugs pa'i tshe ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor mngon sum du gzigs/ dbang bzhi
pa'i skabs su nga bzhin du lus gnad 'chos la mi rtog par zhog gsungs pa tsam

gyis 'gyu ba phra rags chad de bde stong chen po'i ting nge 'dzin mngon du gyur/ phyis sgom khang du bsgoms pas nyams rtogs 'ur langs te/ chos rje'i gsung gis gsal ba rab kyi
mthar phyin gda'/ gzhan ma'i sgom chen gyi sgom sran la 'o skol gyi gdams ngag 'di yod na lung pa grub thob kyi dgang du yod de gsung / chos rje de thub pa dang 'jam dpal
sogs su gzigs pas/ ngas lha gang bsgoms pa ltar khyed kyis mthong bar 'dug pa gzhan la ma gleng gsung / phyis rgya nag nas phebs nas kyang rgyud 'grel man ngag dang bcas
pa mang du gsan/ dang po mjal ba nas sangs rgyas kyi 'du shes las tha mal du nam du'ang ma mthong gsung / mtshan gsan pa tsam la'ang spyan chab 'byin/ grang po lung du
'jam rgyal ba la bsnyung gnas kyi lung zhus pas spyan ras gzigs kyi phyag gis dbu la nyul ba'i snang ba byung / khro phur bzang rings la mngon pa dang / stag thog tu sa
skya paNDi ta la sgra tshad snyan ngag sdebs sbyor bde dgyes sogs chos mang po dang / pan chen bi bhU ti tsandra la phreng ba skor gsum/ bde mchog sbyor drug kha che sangghA
shrI la phreng ba'i dbang dang ka tsan gyi sgra mdo/ dpyal chos bzang la dpyal ba'i chos skor/ dpyal padmo can la sbyor drug

rnams gsan/ nyer lnga pa la sngar gyi mkhan slob dge 'dun dang bcas pa las bsnyen par rdzogs/ sre'u chung pa lce mdo sde seng ge la yo ga sogs chos skor mang po gsan/ so brgyad
pa la mang mkhar dril chen du/ sa skya paNDi ta la dgyes rdor gyi dbang sems bskyed rigs gter gsan/ khong hor yul du thegs pa'i skyel gdung gzhu kun dga' ra ba'i bar
du mdzad/ lha sar jo bo'i drung du mchod pa'i sprin gtibs te gsol ba btab pas jo bo'i sku las 'od zer 'phro ba byung / bdag gis tshogs bskyangs chos bshad dang // dben par
tshogs spangs sgom pa gnyis// tshe 'dir dge stobs gang che lags// sgom pa'i gnas mchog gang zhig legs// zhes zhus pas/ jo bo nyid ston pa dngos su gsal ba'i gsung snyan
pos/ khyod kyis dang por brtsams pa nas// brtson pas bsgrubs pas lus 'di yis// sangs rgyas mchog 'thob 'gyur ba la// brtson pa dor ba ma legs so// 'on kyang nga yi theg
chen chos// ston par 'dod na 'di rnams bsgrubs// lhag pa'i lha ni grub pa'i phyir// sbyin sreg lan brgya rtsa brgyad kyis// sku gzugs 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud bzhin// skye bo
mang po'i tshogs sar bzhengs// gsang sngags gzhung gdams ma lus pa// bshes

gnyen bzang la lung thob byos// rga nad dbul bas sdug bsngal ba'i// mi rnams kyi ni mgon skyabs kyis// de ltar khyod kyis bsgrubs gyur na// yon tan gegs kyi las sgrib sel//
rten 'brel 'grig nas tshe 'di la// yon tan rgya chen skye 'gyur te// 'jig rtan gsum gyi mgon po dang // 'gro ba'i yid bzhin nor bur 'gyur// brag gnas rdo rje'i rtse 'dras
rgyan// mtho ba'i dgon par skye bo rnams// byang chub sems mchog la bkod na// sdig spyod rgyal pos gnod mi 'gyur// blo ldan gong nas gong du 'gro// zhes lung bstan thob/
der chos rgyal rigs ldan sogs bka' rgyud kyi bla ma rnams kyang byon nas thugs dam dbu thog tu bzhag ste/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i chos skor gyis 'gro ba la phan thogs par lung
bstan/ de nas gser sdings su zhi ba'i sbyin bsreg brgya rtsa mdzad/ go dgu ba pa hor dmag bod du lhags dus sems can mang po'i srog bskyabs/ bzang sman grub gling gi dgon
pa btab/ 'gro mgon 'phags pa dang mchims chen po nas/ rdza chung ma la chu rde'u dka' thub zhub pa yan la bla ma grangs med pa bsten/ bod du 'gyur ro 'tshal gyi chos ji
snyed pa gsan zhing lan re gzigs pa tsam gyis

mkhyen pas kun mkhyen du grags la/ nyin mtshan gyi snang ba mtha' dag 'od gsal kho nar 'char bas/ 'gro mgon 'phags pas chos sku 'od zer du mtshan gsol/ 'dol chung chos 'khor
chen mo'i dus sde snod 'dzin pa rgya mtsho'i dbus su sna ba'i seng ger gyur cing snyan pas sa thams cad khyab/ rnam rgyal 'khor chen bde dgyes 'dus pa dus 'khor sogs thugs
dam gyi lha dpag tu med pa'i zhal gzigs/ phar phyin spyod 'jug gsungs tshe/ gang 'dir ston pa chos kyi char 'bebs kyis// gang dag nyan par 'dod pa 'dir shog cig/ ces
gsungs pa na/ sku'i sgo thams cad nas 'od zer sna tshogs 'gyed cing bsdud/ gzhan gyis bltas na gti mug gi bag zhad che ba cig 'dug na'ang kho bo la dge sbyor gyi bogs su
'gyur ba cig gda' gsungs nas mnal bar mdzad/ kho bo rmi lam rang rgyud pa// rmi ba yong ye ma dran zhing // bshad nyan sgom la sgrib pa lngas// sgrib pa nam yang 'byung ma
lags// zhes gsungs/ mnyam rjes kyi dbye ba med par mnyam gzhag 'ba' zhig gis dus gda'/ myang chu la ma bying bar zhabs chu la reg tsam mdzad de byon/ gser sdings su gtsug
lag khang brtsigs pa'i tshe sa skam po las chu rdol/ bsams na shes pa tsam las

'das pa'i mngon par mkhyen pa thogs med du mnga'/ rang nyid kyis gsan pa'i chos rnams slob ma'i tshogs la so sor gtad/ slob dpon 'od zer mgon gdan sar bskos te dben gnas bya
btang du thegs nas/ don dgu pa chu pho 'brug lo hor zla gsum pa'i nyer dgu la nam mkhar zla ba lta bu la tshom bu so gnyis 'od lngas bskor ba thal byung du gyen la 'gro
ba dang / lha'i spos dang rol mo'i sgra dang bcas te sku'i bkod pa bsdus so// sku gdung zhu bas thugs ljags rang byon te thugs dge sdings dang / ljags gser sdings kyi gdung
khang na bzhugs shing / gdung phal che ba bya btang gi phyi rten mchod rten na bzhugs/ kun spangs chen pos kyang dge sdings su nang rten ston pa'i gser sku dang / phyi
rten rnam rgyal mchod rten bzhengs so//10 kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus/bdag nyid chen po de'i sras kyi thu bo zhang kun spangs chen po ni/ yul g.yas ru byang gi ngab
phyar spang skang du/ yab 'bro rje dbang phyug yum gnyag mo lcam me'i sras su chu mo yos la sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo lnga pa la gnyag tshar sa skya paNDi ta sems bskyed
gsungs pa la ma'i pang nas gsan/ bdun pa la 'khyog dpon rdzong ba'i drung du dge bsnyen mnos/ dgu pa la 'khyog zhang gis mkhan po/ rdzong pas slob dpon mdzad nas rab tu byung
/ mtshan

thugs rje brtson 'grus su btags/ nyi shu ba la g.yas ru phyi 'brum dgon gsar du lha btsun bsod nams snying pos mkhan po/ mdog lhod pa shAkya byang chub kyis las slob/ bsod
blo bas gsang ston mdzad nas dad pa'i dge slong lnga bcu'i dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ 'gro mgon 'phags pa/ sangs rgyas 'bum/ shangs pa dkon brtsegs/
lha btsun dgon gsar pa/ rdo rje 'jam dbyangs pa/ rigs pa'i seng ge mdog lhod pa/ mkhan chen mchis pa/ mkhas pa gnyan ston la sogs pa bla ma dam pa rnams bsten/ mdo
mangs/ byams pa dang 'brel ba'i chos sde nyi shu/ mngon pa gong 'og tshad ma sde bdun/ rigs gter/ ka lA pa/ smra sgo mtshon cha/ 'dul ba mdo rtsa/ lung sde bzhi/ 'bum nyi
khri/ brgyad stong ba/ sdud pa/ de dag gi rgya 'grel/ spyod 'jug bslab btus rnams gsan zhing mkhas par sbyangs/ khro phu ba la/ bde chen ral gcig sogs khro phu ba'i chos
rnams gsan/ ma 'ongs pa na jo nang du yun ring du bzhugs na bstan pa la phan zhes lung bstan/ 'gro mgon phyag na gshegs pa'i chos 'khor gyi tshe lung rigs smra ba'i mchog
tu grags/ de'i dus na rtog ge la chu mig pa seng ge dpal mkhas

par grags pas/ khong gis dpal chos kyi grags pa la lan med kyi thal 'gyur bcu gsum yod ces gsan pas/ khong snar thang na bzhugs pa'i drung du byon nas/ khong gi grub mtha'
la zhag mang po'i bar du rtsod nas/ dpal chos kyi grags pa'i lan du ngas kyang khyed la lan med kyi thal 'gyur 'di rnams song ba yin no// zhes grangs 'dzin cing / phyag la
ri mo mdzad/ 'jam sgeg la sogs pa'i mkhas pa chen po rnams lung rigs kyis btul/ chu mig gi chos 'khor snga ma la phar 'dri ba dang / phyi ma la lan 'debs pa la 'gran zla
dang bral bar gyur to// don mo ri dang 'dar chos sdings su phar mngon dbu tshad kyi 'chad nyan dang 'khyog po che'i gdan sa mang du mdzad/ de'i tshe rkyang 'dur du chos
bar la byon nas kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer ba la/ sbyor drug rigs mi 'dra ba mang po gsan dus/ rnam pa thams cad pa'i sku rags pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / phra ba chen
mo'i steng na bzhugs pa'i dzambu'i gling du mi shong snyam pa dang / nang gi dbang po drug ting nge 'dzin gyi yul drug la 'byams nas 'gro ba byung / de nas dus 'khor
rgyud 'grel/ gsang 'dus 'phags skor/ bde mchog rtsa sdom/ kyai rdor sa lugs/ rngog lugs/

gdan bzhi/ mA yA/ yo ga bya spyod kyi dbang rjes gnang rgyud 'grel gzhung bshad man ngag dang / lam 'bras/ rim lnga/ nA ro ni gu grub snying sogs chos rnams bum pa gang byor
gsan/ gsang mtshan mi bskyod rdo rjer btags/ de nas rkyang 'dur du 'jam gsar ba'i gdan sar bzhugs nas chos rje'i chos dung btang ste 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis bstan pa
rgyas par mdzad/ dol po ba ye shes mgon po la srog rtsol gsan te/ rkyang 'dur du 'dag 'byar mdzad nas sbyor drug bsgoms pas nyams snang 'ur langs shing mngon shes lnga
grub/ gegs kyi rnam pa mang du byung ste/ bde ba can du gdan 'dren pa yin zer nas bsu ba'i bkod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / de'i dus su bud med cig gis lde mig cig khyer
byung nas/ sgo zhig la sgo lcags rgyab 'dug pa de la bkal song / de sgo phye cig pa'i brdar dgongs nas sgo phye ste/ de nas lus sbyongs kyi man ngag byung ba bzhin mdzad
pas/ rlung lnga stobs su gyur te/ res phyag ya re la mi bdun bdun gyis gzung ba phyogs gcig tu 'phangs kyang gnod pa mi 'byung / res mi mang bos dgul bskyol mi nus/
res bsil bas mi rnams 'dar zhing 'khyag res tsha gdung gis lung ba 'gengs pa byung zhing / de thams cad kun mkhyen chos

sku 'od zer gyis dge sdings nas gzigs te byon pa na/ rje 'dis kyang mkhyen nas slob ma rnams la bla ma mjal bar 'dug gis gsol ba thob gsung / sang bla ma byon te da res khyed
sku gshegs na sku bzhi la 'byor bar 'dug ste gdul bya mang po'i don du bzhugs dgos so gsung nas srog gegs de bsal bas/ bde ba can du bsu ba de rnams da res gdan mi 'grongs
par 'dug zer nas gyes pa'i snang ba byung / dus 'khor ba shar pa ye shes rin chen pa dang rnal 'byor seng 'bum sogs bod na sbyor drug mi 'dra ba yod zer tshad la yang
gsan pa mdzad/ mang mkhar gnas gsar du bla ma 'jam dpal ba la/ mdo sgyu sems gsum gsan pas/ mnal lam du mkhar bdun rim skas bdun btsugs pa la 'dzegs pas rtse mor phyin
te/ ting nge 'dzin gyi snang ba rgya chen gzigs/ nyid phug pa sangs rgyas 'bum la rdzogs chen gsan/ de nas 'chad nyan gyi spros pa bcad de kha rag tu byon nas dbyar bzhugs
mdzad/ de nas ri khrod rnams su sbyor drug dang dmar khrid bskyangs pas kun spangs pa chen por grags/ se mkhar chung gi gtsug lag khang bsos shing 'brog mi'i sku 'bum la
gser gsol bas/ mi ma yin rnams kyis se mkhar chung ba de da

'dir byung zhes sgrog pa gsan/ der jo mo nags rgyal ma byung ste/ khyed la gnas legs pa cig 'bul zhes zhu ba la lo gsum na 'byon par zhal gyis bzhes/ sbyor drug rdzogs par
ston pa bka' gnyan par byung bas lha sar byon nas/ jo bo rnam gnyis khyad par du bcu gcig zhal gyi drung du nyin mtshan du gsol ba drag tu btab pas/ khrid yig bri ba dang
/ khrid rdzogs par bstan pas 'gro phan rgya chen po 'byung ba'i gnang ba thob/ de nas lhun po rtse sogs g.yas ru ri khrod du sgrub pa mdzad/ de nas jo mo nang du phebs ma
thag gdul bya 'ur te/ gtso bor dus 'khor rgyud 'grel gyi dus chos gsung zhing slob ma brgya stong mang po la sbyor drug gi khrid tshan lnga drug dus mnyam du gnang / khyad
par du mkha' spyod bde ldan du byon pa'i tshe/ chos rgyal rigs ldan sogs bka' rgyud kyi bla ma rnams byon nas byin brlabs dang lung bstan mdzad/ se mkhar chung du thog
ma dang / seng ge rdzong du bar dang / gnas der mtha' mar dge ba'i mtshan ma thob nas dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud kyi snying po rtsa 'grel dang / thog mtha' bar dge'i khrid
yig mdzad/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen dpag tu med pa 'dus pa la dus kyi 'khor lo gtso bor gyur ba'i gsang sngags gsar rnying gi dbang bskur/ rgyud 'grel gyi bshad

pa/ man ngag gi khrid rim rnams rgya cher stsal/ sa skya dpon slob sogs skye bo'i tshogs mang po la'ang so so'i skal ba dang 'tsham par chos kyis tshim par mdzad pas jo nang
ba chen po zhes phyogs kun tu grags par gyur/ chu pho byi ba lo la mar me 'chi khar gsal bya ba yin gsung sku khams bzang ba'i ngang nas slob ma rnams la chos rnams rdzogs
par gtad/ de nas dgun smad sku tshe'i 'du byed btang yang byang sems rgyal ba ye shes pa gdan sa la bsko ba'i ched du/ srog rtsol la brten nas 'tsho ba'i 'du byed byin
gyis brlabs te/ zla ba phyed tsam na byang sems pa la mgur cham byung yod pa la phan na myur du shog gsungs pas byon pa na/ nga da lo me tog khra chil ba'i dus la 'chi
rtsis yin pa la mdang zhag glo bur du rtsa bsdus pa cig byung / nged 'chi dus khyed dang 'phrad dgos pa la ma bslebs pas/ nga dus kyi 'khor lo'i rnal 'byor ba yin/ khyed
kyis brtungs na ngas bsrings pa chog snyam du rlung sbyor 'ga' byas pas rtsa sor chud de 'chi ba blus bdog gsung / sku khams bzang zhing phyag rtsa bden gshegs pa'i rtags
ci lags zhus pas/ rlung sems la dbang thob pa 'gro ba la rtags ci dgos/ do zhag ngas bar dor phyin

nas 'jig rten gyi khams mang po'i bar do'i sems can tshad med pa bsgral/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing mang po bltas shing / bde ba can dang / dga' ldan dang / shambha lar yang phyin/
bde ba can na rin po che'i padmo kha bye ba sogs skye sgo mang po gda' yang / mtshan nyid kyi dus nas byams pa'i drung du sgro 'dogs gcad snyam nas 'dug pa drag pos rten
'brel bsgrigs shing / khro phu ba dang dpon slob thams cad rten 'brel 'grig pa cig byung bas/ nga 'di nas bar do rigs mthun du byas nas sems can dpag tu med pa bsgral/
de nas dga' ldan du 'gro gsung nas byang sems pa gdan sar bskos/ byang sems sku khams 'khrugs pa na/ nga 'gro ba'i tshes yin te/ nga song na de'i rkyen gyis khyed kyang
'grongs par 'dug pas/ khams sos kyi bar du ngas bsdad do// gsung nas zhag nyi shu lhag tu nyin re bzhin chos zab mo'i 'bel gtam mdzad/ don gcig pa chu glang dpyid 'bring
nyi shu lnga'i tho rangs byang sems pa la rdo rje slob dpon du dbang bsgyur ba'i cho gas rdo rje dril bu gnang nas/ khyed kyi khams ni sor chud 'dug da nga 'gro ba yin/
ro 'di shi ma thag bsregs kyang chog nga ro'i nang du 'od gsal bsgoms zhing bsdod bya ba'i lugs min/ kun spangs kyi bya ba mthar phyin/

dga' spro dang bcas pas gsol ba thob gsung ste mya ngan las 'das so//de nas zhag bdun na sku gdung zhu bas dus 'khor la sogs pa'i rten mang po dang / ring bsrel yungs 'bru
lta bu'i phung bor gyur/ dge 'dun khri phrag gcig 'dus te sgrub pa byas/ skyid phug tu sku 'bum dang / dga' ldan du sku 'bum che ba dang sku gdung rin po che bzhengs so//la
stod pa dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/rje 'di la slob ma'i tshogs rgya mtsho lta bu las yongs su grags pa ni/ khro phu rin po che bsod nams seng ge 'jam dbyangs bzhi thog pa/
kun spangs grags rgyal ba/ 'jam dbyangs 'khon ston thugs rje rin chen sogs sa skya ba'i chen po rnams dang / byang sems rgyal ba ye shes/ la stod pa dbang rgyal/ mun me
brag kha ba/ sron pa kun rgyal rnams la kun spangs bu bzhir grags pa dang / shes rab 'bum/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu chen rin chen dpal
bzang rnams las/la stod pa dbang phyug rgyal mtshan ni/ bsgoms pas 'dzin pa'i yan lag man chad grub/ bar dge dang mthar dge la bla ma'i zhal shes kho na las 'byung ba'i khrid
yig khyad par can mdzad/ mang po'i bogs 'don pa dang gegs sel ba la shin tu mkhas/

de'i man ngag gi yig 'jog kyang mang du mdzad/ grub thob kyi slob ma yang mang du byung ba las/ mkhan chen rin tshul ba/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ 'khrul zhig pa/ bdag gi bla
ma dus 'khor zhabs pa ste la stod lugs kyi brgyud pa'o//mun me brag kha ba grags pa seng gemun me brag kha ba grags pa seng ge ni/ g.yas ru byang gi rgyal sde thang mkhar
du brgya dpon 'od ldan gyi sras su/ shing mo los la 'khrungs/ gdung rus glan/ khro phu rin po che las rab tu byung / mkhan po de nyid dang / las slob dbu ma ba sher 'bum/
gsang ston bu ston seng ge 'od kyis mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ sa skyar phya ru ba seng ge dpal las sde snod mang du gsan cing sbyangs/ kun spangs chen po dang / byang
sems rgyal ye la sbyor drug gi khrid dbang dang bcas pa gsan/ rgyud gsung bar zhus pas rong du song gsung ba bzhin byon te/ rgwa lo'i sras skye med grub pa la rgyud 'grel
cha lag dang bcas pa gsan nas/ g.ya' lung gi ri khrod du sgrub pa gtso bor mdzad/ 'di la rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa dang / khrid kyis slob ma mang po rjes su bzung / phyis
lo spe ba dkon bzang gis sbyin bdag byas nas/ mun me brag khar phebs te/ brag rtse na spe'u cig yod pa'i sgo brtsigs nas/ dkyus gcig la dus 'khor gyi bsnyen pa dang /

sbyin bsreg 'bum phrag bcu mdzad pas me lce rin po che'i rnam par 'bar ba sogs mtshan ma khyad par can byung / zhag re la lus sbyongs lan drug re mdzad/ sbyor drug dmar khrid/
gcod/ gzer lnga rnams la khrid chen bzhir ming btags nas gtso bor skyong / dbyar mtshams dus rgyun gcod la bzhugs/ mngon par shes pa mnga' bas sa skya ba'i bde dog thams
cad lung bstan pa bzhin babs/ phyag tu yo byad byung tshad jo mo nang / rong / khro phu rnams su 'bul/ khrid yig ngo sprod dang bcas pa mdzad/ gya dgu pa chu mo lug gi
lo la gshegs te gdung sbyangs pas ring bsrel gyi phung bor gyur to// des bang mo zhu ba gzhon nu dpal la khrid skor mtha' dag gnang zhing / de gnyi ga dpal ldan bla ma
dam pas dbang dang khrid gsan no// //sron pa kun rgyal ba/sron pa kun rgyal ba ni hor rgyal bo'i bu gur che yin pa/ chos rgyal 'phags pas dbang yon la 'di phul gsungs nas
bzhes/ rab tu phyung nas phyag phyir khrid de sde snod kyi slob gnyer la bcug chos dang gdams pa mang du gnang / 'phags pa zhi bar gshegs pa dang / kun spangs chen po'i
zhabs la gtugs zab lam zhus te bsgoms pas ting nge 'dzin phul du byung ba 'khrungs/ ra sa rin

chen gling du sha wa ra la bsam gtan gyi khrid dang / stong gzugs kyi spyan ras gzigs la gegs sel gsan pas man ngag la mnga' brnyes/ rlung sems la dbang thob/ sbyor drug kyang
sron lugs zhes gzhan dang cung zad mi 'dra bas gzhan don mdzad de mkha' spyod du gshegs so//sron pa chos dpal bzang po/de'i slob ma sron pa chos dpal bzang po ni/ sha
ba snyan dkar seng ge rdzong du bsgoms pas sor bsams 'byongs/ srog rtsol btsan thabs ma gtso bor bton pas srog thur 'dres rtsa dral te/ 'dzin pa'i yan lag grub nas/ khrid
'dri'i sgo nas gzhan phan rgya che ba mdzad/ ri bo rtse lngar mkha' spyod du gshegs so//mkhan chen bsod grags pa/de la mkhan chen bsod grags pas gsan te/ de ni snye mo
phu gsum du chu mo bya la 'khrungs/ bcu dgu pa la mkhan po dkon mchog skyabs las rab tu byung / nyi shu pa la mkhan po bde ba dpal bzang po/ las slob dka' bzhi ba grags pa
gzhon nu/ gsang ston gzhon nu dar gyis mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan slob las phar mngon 'dul ba spyod 'jug sogs mang du gsan/ khyad par du rong ba shes seng la dus
'khor gyi dbang / sron pa chos dpal bzang po la sbyor drug gi khrid/ mkhan chen rgyal mtshan dpal la sems 'grel gsum dbang mdor bstan sbyor drug phran dang bcas pa

gsan/ mkhan chen dka' bzhi ba las thugs bskyed cing blo sbyong gsan pas phyis mtshan nas brjod pa'i tshe spyan chab 'byin/ nga'i sems bzang bo khong gi bka' drin yin gsung
/ kun gyis kyang byang chub sems dpa' zhes gsol/ zhe gsum pa la chos lung tshogs pa'i mkhan po mdzad de bslab pa gsum gyi bstan pa rgyas par spel/ bla ma grags pa dpal la
bsnyen sgrub/ kun mkhyen chen po la dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud bshad man ngag dang bcas pa gsan/ khang ba'i ka ba 'gyel yang thog mi lhung ba dang zhal chab btab pa tsam
gyis lkugs bye ba sogs byin brlabs kyi rnam 'phrul mang po bstan/ bdun bcu pa la mkhan po bsod bzang ba gdan sar bskos te chos lung nyid du thugs dam la rtse gcig tu bzhugs
pas spyan ras gzigs dang sgrol ma zhal gzigs/ lha klu gnod sbyin gyi khrom chen po la sems bskyed gnang / gya gcig pa chu mo sbrul la me tog gi char dang bcas te bde bar
gshegs so// de gnyi ga la dpal ldan bla ma dam pas gsan to// //kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/kun mkhyen 'phags 'od ni myang stod thu gu dang nye ba'i la ber/ yab rje bo rdo rje/
yum rje mo rgyal mtshan 'bum la sras brgyad yod pa'i tha chung sa pho 'brug la 'khrungs/ byis pa'i [81b"/>dus su nam mkha' la sangs rgyas byang sems mang po gzigs rlung
dbu mar chud par 'dug gsung / bco lnga ba la yab dang mched thams cad 'das nas/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer las rab tu byung / mtshan 'phags pa 'od du btags/ brtag gnyis
dang phar phyin la sbyangs shing / yi ge lha bris kyang mkhas par mkhyen/ nyi shu pa nas nyer lnga'i bar la chos sku ba las dus 'khor 'bro lugs kyi dbang rgyud bshad khrid
dang bcas pa/ gsang 'dus/ bde dgyes/ sgyu thod gdan bzhi/ mnyam sbyor/ yo ga la sogs pa zab chos rab 'byams gsan/ chos kyi gtad sar dgongs nas zhib tu gnang / nyer lnga'i
mjug la snar thang du mkhan po sgro ston smon tshul/ las slob rin bzang / gsang ston sangs rgyas rgyal po rnams las bsnyen par rdzogs shing 'dul ba gsan/ mu ge byung
dus lce chung gi bdud rtsi'i bcud len kho nas sku 'tsho/ mdzo pho lhas pa/ grang po lung pa dkon gzhon/ thugs she/ lce blo ldan seng ge rnams las chos mang du gsan/ dben
gnas bya btang du sku mtshams la bzhugs pa'i tshe/ kun spangs chen pos 'dir rgyud 'grel cig dang dus 'khor gyi thang ka zhig 'bri ba la shog gsung pas jo mo nang du byon
pa dang / rgyud kyi snying po gsung dbu tshugs

'dug pas sngon la 'di nyon cig gsung / thugs la btags pa yin snyam te nyan pa dang de'i 'phro cung ma tshar ba la khyed yi ge 'dri ba kho na la bos pa min da res khrid 'di
la zhugs shig gsung pas khrid la zhugs/ bka'i 'phro la rgyun 'thung nas lo gsum la khrid rdzogs par mdzad/ khyed rang 'dod cing mi bde ba byung na zhu ba su byung gi zla
la shog gsung nas snga phyir khrid tshar ba lan bdun zhus/ phyag len thams cad legs par sbyangs/ gsung sgros rnams zin bris su mdzad/ 'khrul 'khor dgos pa rnams dpe chung
du bris te legs par gtan la phab nas bla ma nyid la bzhugs pa'i sbyor drug gi skor drug gi skor thams cad ma lus par gsan/ de'i dus su da dung bdag dus 'khor 'di la slob
gnyer cig byed/ sgra tshad la mkhas par grags che bas der 'gro bar zhu zhus pas/ de kun shes rab che yang shes rab kyi rtsal gyis bshad pa yin brgyud pa'i man ngag dang
mi ldan/ rwa 'bro gnyi ga'i man ngag gi gtugs sa yin pas rong du rgyug cig gsung pas bla ma shes rab seng ge'i drung du byon te/ dbang zhus nas rgyud 'grel la sbyangs pa
mdzad/ dka' gnas la bshad pa gzab pa byung tsa na 'phral du glegs shing la yi ger bris/ de'i 'phro rnams

chos thon pa'i rjes su zhus/ de nas yi ger btab nas chos thog phyi ma la de rnams mthun mi mthun pa bltas shing mthun pa bris/ dpe chung dgos pa thams cad zhib par bkod/ phyag
len dka' ba 'gag thams cad dang / tha na rdor dril 'jog lugs dang phreng ba khyer lugs tshun chad la dri gtug zhib par mdzad nas/ bla ma'i gsung gis khyod 'phags rgod
yag ma bya ba rtsa ba ldum bu bzhin ma bcad par ye mi nyan pa'i mi yin gyis/ dris shig gsungs nas lan legs par btab/ chos rdo rus thug pa zhig bslab na dri ba de lta bu
dgos pa yin/ gzhan nga rang las mkhas pa ka nga'i rtsar yong gi 'dug dri ba de lta bu byed pa rang ma byung gsungs nas mnyes tshor chen po yang mdzad/ sham 'bar/ khro dgon/
shar dgon/ gnam rtse ldang / gnas mo che la sogs gang du bzhugs par phyag phyir 'brangs nas rgyud 'grel man ngag dang bcas pa'i don la zhu gtug mdzad/ khrid zhus pas nyams
rtogs la bogs thon/ gzhan yang dbang mdor bstan/ sgrom lde/ man lungs pa'i sbyor drug sogs gsan/ kun spangs pa gshegs rjes jo mo nang du byon pas/ byang sems rgyal yes
kyis dbon po rnams sprad nas dus 'khor gyi slob gnyer khrid du bcug der dus 'khor la mkhas pa'i dge bshes mang du

thon/ byang sems pa la'ang dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud snying / mtshan brjod 'grel pa sogs mang du gsan/ gzhan yang grags chen pa/ grags dpal ba/ bsod mgon pa/ snur chos 'phags
rgyal mtshan rnams la'ang chos mang du gsan/ stod phyogs kyi dge bshes rnams la nyin rang bshad pa dang / mtshan rangs dbang mdzad kyang / 'jig rten blos btang nas sgrub
pa mthar 'don pa dang / po ti rkang btsugs nas slob gnyer rdo rus thug pa byed pa mang po ma byung bas thugs phyung ste/ myang stod skyil mkhar lte gud kyi phur spe'u
chung gcig pa zhig tu sku mtshams dam po la bzhugs so// de'i tshe de la bu ston thams cad mkhyen pas gsan te de'i rnam par thar pa ni rwa ba'i skabs su brjod par 'gyur ro//
//bla chen rin chen dpal bzang /bla chen rin chen dpal bzang po ni/ g.ya' lung dpe lngar byi ba la 'khrungs/ gdung phyar/ gzhon nu la chos rgyal 'phags pa la thugs bskyed
gsan/ spyi bo lhas pa'i mkhan po shes rab rgyal mtshan las rab tu byung / mkhan po de nyid dang / las slob bsod nams 'bum/ gsang ston thub pas mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/
brag ram du dbus pa shes rab 'bum la phar tshad dbu ma rigs gter rnams

gsan/ spyi bo lhas su 'chad nyan mdzad/ jo mo nang du kun spangs chen po la sbyor drug gsan te sang dngos gzhi la 'jug pa'i nub mo gnas po dang gsung gleng mdzad cing / phar
phyin dang sbyor drug sa mtshams dang sgom tshul 'dra bar 'dug gsungs pas/ sang chos la byon dus khyed gnyis phar phyin dang sbyor drug mtshams sbyor ba las bsgoms na rang
khe che ba yin te gsung du byung / bsgoms pas rtags rnams rdzogs par 'khrungs/ de nas sgro smon can gyi gdan sar bzhugs/ lhag pa'i tshul khrims gtsang / byang chub kyi
thugs 'byongs/ yi dam gyi bskyed rim brtan/ bla ma don yod rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po sogs mi chen po mang po'i bla ma mdzad/ phag lo hor zla bzhi pa'i nyer gnyis la gshegs

du gnang / mngon shes lnga grub/ nga bdun pa la jo mo nang gi gdan sar bzhugs nas chos 'di gtso bor bton pa'i 'phrin las rgyas par mdzad/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod la sogs pa
dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po mang po dang / dpon chen

byang rdor la sogs pa'i mi chen po rnams kyis kyang zhabs la gtugs/ mdo sde lung sbyor che chung / rgyud sde lung sbyor che chung rdo rje theg pa'i bcud len sogs bstan bcos
yang mang du mdzad/ mthar gtsang bo brgal ste chos dbyings phug mo'i gnas su rtse gcig tu sgrub pa la bzhugs/ re bzhi pa lcags po spre'u la mkhas btsun pa gdan sar bskos
nas/ dpyid zla ra ba'i tshes bcu la gshegs/ steng phyogs 'og min gyi lha gnas na bzhugs so zhes karma pa rang byung rdo rje gsung ngo // rje 'di nyid la rgyud 'chad pa la
mkhas pa dang / sbyor drug la myong rtogs thob pa'i slob ma grangs med cing phyir mi ldog pa'i sa thob pa yang brgya phrag mang du byung ba las/ mchog tu gyur pa ni/ stag
lung pa ratna ka ra/ sha grags seng ba/ grub thob dar yul ba/ mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho dang bzhi las/ stag lung pa ratna ka ra ni/ jo mo nang du byon nas byang sems
pa la sbyor drug dang rgyud 'grel rdzogs par gsan pas/ ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo dpag med bye/ slob ma mang po sbyor drug gis khrid par mdzad do// //zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin
pa sha grags seng /zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa sha grags seng ba ni/ spom por gyi sa'i char/ pha tshan sha 'bu gnyis las sha/ gdung dbrad gu yab stag chung / yum a rgod
kyi sras su chu mo lug la 'khrungs/ kheng ye shes seng ge las rab tu byung zhing

dang / gzhan la ston cig pa'i bka' gtad kyang thob/ sgrol mas kyang ayon du mi bgrod pa'i lung bstan byung bas/ 'byon pa'i sgros pa bcad/ de nas mi la'i rdzong drug la thegs

mar 'khrungs/ byang sems pa las gdams pa mnos te rgya nag ri bo rtse lngar bsgoms pas grub pa brnyes nas byang phyogs su bstan pa spel lo//12 mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho/mkhas

gdung lhing / mched lnga'i tha chung / bcu gsum pa

la shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan la dge bsnyen mnos/ mtshan yang thugs rje dpal du btags/ bco lnga pa la mdar du mdar byang skyabs kyi gra sar byon/ sbyang ston rdo rje rgyal
mtshan gyis mkhan po/ yon tan dpal gyis slob dpon mdzad de rab tu byung / mtshan thugs rje rgyal mtshan du btags/ mngon pa kun las btus/ rnam nges/ rigs gter rnams mkhas
par sbyangs/ de nas sa skyar byon te 'jam dbyangs bzhi thog pa la gtugs/ khong gis bu ston kun bzang dpal la sprad/ phar phyin 'jam gsar lugs slob tu bcug pas 'phral du
mkhyen/ bzhi thog pa mnyes te/ de ring chos khri khar 'bul ba gang byung yang khyed la ster bas nga'i chos khri'i steng du bsdod/ 'bul ba che chung khyed rang gi bsod nams
la rag las so gsung pa la/ der khams pa gcig gis dbu zhwa/ gsol zhal sder/ ber thul/ ja sdum/ gos phyi nang / par thang khra bo/ mdzo sogs 'bul ba byung bas sku bsod che
bar grags so// bzhi thog pa'i drung du phyi nang gi rgyud sde mang du gsan/ dus 'khor ba ye shes rin chen rgya yul la 'byon pa'i phyag phyir byon te/ lo ngo bzhi la sa
skyar phebs/ bzhi thog pa la dus 'khor rgyud 'grel dbang dang bcas pa dang / brtag gnyis phran dang bcas pa gsan/ grub pa dpal

bzang po las kyang phyag len rnams bslabs/ de nas sum cu ba la jo mo nang du kun spangs chen po'i zhabs la gtugs te/ sbyor drug gi chos tshan brgya lhag pa gsan/ rgyud 'grel
sogs kun spangs pa dang / byang sems pa la mnga' ba'i chos rnams bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mkhyen/ mang du gsan pas yon tan rgya mtshor btags/ so bdun pa la bla brang
bzhi thog tu 'jam dbyangs chen pos mkhan po/ zhang kun spangs chen pos las slob/ shar ba ye shes rgyal mtshan pas gsang ste ston pa mdzad nas bsnyen par rdzogs/ re gcig pa
la jo nang gi gdan sa mdzad de/ sde snod 'dzin pa'i tshogs chen po la/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang rgyud 'grel man ngag gnang ba sogs phrin las rgya cher bskyangs/ mngon par
shes pa sogs mngon par rtogs pa'i yon tan mang po mnga'/ re bdun pa la kun mkhyen chen po gdan sar bskos te/ spyir lo sum cu rtsa brgyad kyi bar du jo mo nang nyid du
bzhugs nas/ re brgyad pa me mo yos tha skar zla ba'i tshes brgyad la ma nyel ba med par sa g.yo ba dang / me tog gi char 'bab pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dang bcas te bde
bar gshegs/ gdung zhugs la gzhen dus 'od kyi gong bu rdza ma tsam pa mang po thon te nam mkha' la 'gro ba byung / ring bsrel rnams sku 'dra

dang / phyi rten rnam rgyal mchod rten bzhugs so//13 kun mkhyen dus gsum sangs rgyas/de'i sras kyi thu bo kun mkhyen chen po ni/ dol po ban tshang du yab nam ston ye shes dbang

du btags/ bcu pa la mkhan chen byang chub seng ge la yang dag sogs rnying ma'i skor gsan/ bcu gsum pa la skyi stengs su mkhan po tshul khrims snying po dang slob dpon ze

ba'i gar thig bslabs pa tshegs med par mkhyen pas mkhas pa chen po cig 'ong bar 'dug gsungs nas shin tu dgyes/ skyi ston pa ya tshe rgyal po'i bla ma la byon nas slar glo
bor phebs pa gsan pas/ bco brgyad pa la rang gcig pur dar yug 'ga' zhig dang zangs che ba cig bsnams nas glo bor byon/ skyi ston pa la tshad ma bsdus pa gsan/ skyi ston

spyod

'jug rdo rje phreng rnams kyi slob gnyer dus gcig la mdzad/ skyi ston shAg 'bum/ bdag nyid bzang po dpal/ ti shri kun blo/ nam legs pa/ shar ba seng ge dpal rnams la phar tshad

kun bsod

la bde mchog gsan/ de nas sa skyar phebs te dus chos su dka' chen bzhi sogs po ti lnga drug re sgrel nas gsungs/ dung lung dga' ldan du kye rdor gyi mchod mdzad pas bum chu
khol/ yi dam gyi lha mang po'i zhal gzigs/ jo mo nang du shrI rin seng ba'i dar 'gyed skyel du byon pas sgrub pa ba rnams kyi sgrub tshugs la dad pa skyes te da bzod 'dir

bstan/ seng ge dpal ba gong du bzhud pa'i phyag phyir 'byon dgos gsung pa la zhu ba nan gyis phul nas/ so gcig pa la jo mo nang du mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho'i zhabs

phyag len/ byams pa'i chos lnga sogs gsungs/ de nas kun spangs pas zhu ba po mdzad nas mkhas btsun pa la dus 'khor gyi dbang gsan dus/ thig 'debs pa la kun spangs mchog mkhas

su dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs dang phyogs mtshams su thab thib rnams btab/ 'jim pas dkyil 'khor dang thab bslar/ phyi 'jig rten dang nang rtsa thig rlung gsum gyi bkod pa

/ de nas mkha' spyod bde ldan du thugs dam la rtse gcig tu bzhugs pas/ mngon par mkhyen pa thogs med du mnga' ba dang / srog 'thur 'dres pa'i bde nyams 'ur langs pa sogs

pa/ gdugs kyi lha khang na rin po che sna tshogs las grub pa'i dus 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi dkyil 'khor blos bslang bzhugs pa lo phyed dang bzhi la grub ste/ rab gnas mdzad

ba

can du bzhugs nas ri chos nges don rgya mtsho/ mngon rtogs rgyan dang rgyud bla'i TI kA sogs mdzad/ gong ma tho gan thi mur gyis gdan 'dren du mngags pa'i gser yig pa byung
dus/ gsang dam pos na thung ngu gnyis sngags pa'i cha lugs mdzad nas rta mgrin gyi thugs dam la rtse gcig tu bzhugs pas gser yig pa bzlogs/ sa skya/ ngam rings/ bzang ldan/

lung dang gnang sbyin bzang po phul/ de nas khu lung mda'i gnas/ bde gnas/ ngur mig bye ma/ tsa dbye/ tsha mig dge 'dun sgang / gzhu ku na ra/ gnam khri tshang / dbu ri/

mgur mo/ snar thang / khro phu/ bo dong e la sogs pa rnams su/ bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang / mi chen po rnams la dus 'khor gyi dbang khrid gnang / skye bo stong phrag

nas bskor ba byed// zla gdan gyi steng nas me tog 'bul// khyams khra'i nang du gsung rab blta// so so'i sgo nas phyag mchod byed// e ma skal ldan kun dga' bar byos//

chos kyi lhag ma ma lus par stsal/ lo mtshams pa rnams la bug sgo so sor yud kyis phebs nas/ gegs sel dang gdams pa gnang ste bden pa mthong bar mdzad/ phal che bas ni
'phral du grub pa'i mtshan ma bstan pas chos rje yang mnyes/ bdun cu pa lcags mo glang gi lo hor zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes lnga'i nyin khrid gsar ba rnams la/ bla ma'i rnal
'byor rgyas pa cig gnang nas 'di la rten 'brel thams cad bsgrig

dgos/ gal po che yin pas bsgoms shig de nas gdan sa pas gnang ngo gsung / tshogs pa la nges don rgya mtsho'i chos 'phro re nyin ches thugs gsal zhing / gzi mdangs che ba'i
rnam pas lhag par gsung che bar gsungs te/ 'u cag gi chos bshad mtshams de ka la byed pa yin no gsungs nas chos 'phror bzhag tshes drug gi nam langs ma thag 'od gsal la mnyam
par gzhag nas dgong mo mya ngan las 'das te/ mkha' khyab mkha'i rdo rje can yin mod na'ang / sprul pa'i sku ni zhing bde ba can du 'byon par zhal gyis mches so// zhag
bdun gyi bar du gzi mdangs je cher song zhing zhal 'dzum ston/ gsang ba sbubs su nub/ dbu'i gtsug tor 'phags pa la zla ba bdud rtsi lud/ phyi nang rten 'brel gnad gcig
pas gtsang bo gyen la log te gram pa'i mthil gyi rdo mthong ba byung / gdung zhugs la gzhen pas ring bsrel yungs 'bru lta bu'i phung por gyur cing spyan ras gzigs kyi sku
byon/ bde ba can du tshe dpag med jo bo'i sku tshad ma dang / sku 'bum chen mor sku 'dra mthong ba don ldan bzhengs pa'i nang du ring bsrel phal che ba bzhugs so// //kun
mkhyen chen po'i thugs sras bu chen rnams/

bdag nyid chen po rigs ldan sprul pa'i sku 'di'i slob ma'i thu bo ni/ kun spangs chos grags dpal bzang po/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ lo tsA ba blo gros dpal/ chos rje phyogs
las rnam rgyal/ dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ chos dpal mgon po/ chos rje rin tshul ba/ zhang ston rgya bo bsod nams grags pa/ g.yag sde paN chen/ la dong sman chu kha ba blo
gros rgyal mtshan/ lo chen byang rtse/ se sdings pa blo gros dpal/ bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ chos grags gsar ma/ nya dpon kun dga'/ bla brang pa bzang po dpal/ thang chen
pa kun dga' 'bum/ sa skya mkhan po yan ye ba/ shangs pa rdo rje/ gnas drug pa blo gros mtshungs med/ 'jam sngon/ 'jam sgeg mkhas pa rin chen mchog khams pa ngag dbang /
snar thar pa mchims blo bzang grags pa/ chos lung mkhan po bsod nams bzang po dang grags pa rgyal mtshan/ byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i blo gros/ ri ston blo chen 'od/ mkhan
chen don grub dpal dang yon tan rgyal mtshan/ chos lung mkhan chen grags tshul ba dang grags pa dpal/ mkhan chen byang chub 'od zer/ nubs gnas gsar ba seng ge dpal/ lo
pa

gzhon nu sangs rgyas/ snye thang pa bkras seng / gra dgon pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ chos 'khor gling pa byams pa/ bde ba can pa 'jam rin/ tsha mig pa yon tan seng ge gsang
phu ba blo gros seng ge/ tshal pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ khra phu ba nam mkha' bzang po/ e pa nam mkha' grags/ myang stod sgo mo ba sangs rgyas dpal/ ngam rings pa brtson
rgyal/ spang 'dab rin po che/ ri khrod pa dbang rin/ mdzod ma ba ston rin/ dus 'khor ba dge 'dun dpal/ bla ma rtse mo ba/ bde lung ba/ mkhan po lha btsun/ slob dpon dar
dbang / gsang phu ba grags bzang / slob dpon bsod nams dpal/ so stod pa rdor rgyal/ rta nag pa rdor rgyal/ rta nag pa nyi rgyal/ bla ma rgyal 'byung / snye thang pa rdor
rgyal/ shes rdor ba/ mkhan chen bkras tshul ba/ brag ram pa bsod nams seng ge nags phug pa/ dpal rgyal/ bcom ldan rdo rje snying po sogs dus kyi 'khor lo la mkhas shing
yongs su grags pa'i slob ma mang du byung la/ ti shri kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bzhi thogs pa la sogs pa sa skya'i gdung rgyud
pa rnams dang / rtogs ldan dar rgyal pa/ grub thob dbus pa/ bla ma mkha' spyod pa/ sgom khang pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan la sogs pa'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug mang du byon

to// //kun spangs chos grags dpal bzang po/kun spangs chos grags dpal bzang po ni/ 'jam dbyangs 'khon ston pa la dus 'khor 'bro lugs kyi dbang dang rgyud kyi lung zhus/ mkhas
btsun yon tan rgya mtsho lo lnga'i bar du 'bral med du bsten nas/ dbang dang sems 'grel skor gsum man ngag dang bcas pa gsan/ dpang lo la sgra sna sdebs sbyor mngon brjod
sogs tha snyad kyi gtsug lag mang po dang bka' bstan bcos mang po gsan rjes/ dbang gis rgyud 'brel rgya dpe'i steng nas gsungs/ rje 'dis shod 'gyur bkram nas 'gyur mi
bcos su mi rung ba rnams la zhu chen zhu zhing bod dpe la mchan du yang btab/ bskul ba po mdzad nas dbang gis rdo rje snying 'grel dang / nA ro 'grel chen gnyis dang / dpe
med 'tsho'i sbyor drug rtse 'grel gyi 'gyur bcos grub cing gsan/ kun mkhyen chen po la dbang man ngag rgyud bshad tshar bzhi/ gzhan yang chos mang du gsan pas/ nges pa'i
don gyi bka' dang bstan bcos kyi don tshul bzhin du rtogs pa ni 'di nyid kyi bka' drin kho na yin gsung / bu ston rin po che la yang gsan pa rgya cher mdzad/ lo tsA yang
mkhas par mkhyen pas/ 'jam dpal lta 'dod mdor bstan bzhi 'gyur yang mdzad do// //sa bzang ma ti paN chen/sa bzang ma ti paN chen ni/ mtshan blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po zhes pa mkhas grub chen po zhig go/

'di la sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros dang / rin rgyal ba sogs slob ma mang du byung ba las/ rin rgyal ba nas chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ 'khrul zhig pa/ bdag gi bla ma dus
zhabs pa'o// // lo tsA ba blo gros dpal ni/ lcags pho byi ba la sku 'khrungs/ kun mkhyen chen po/ dpang lo tsA ba/ bu ston rin po che sogs mkhas pa mang du bsten nas/ rig
pa'i gnas ji snyed pa dang sde snod mtha' dag la legs par sbyangs/ khyad par dus 'khor la mchog tu mkhas par gyur nas/ so lnga pa khyi lo la ma ti paN chen dang rnam pa
gnyis la kun mkhyen chen pos bka' gnang nas/ rgyud 'grel shong 'gyur la bu mchan 'gyur bcos yod pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du bris/ dpang lo'i 'gyur bcos la yang brten nas
'gyur bcos dag par bcos/ so dgu pa sa pho stag la jo mo nang gi gdan sar bzhugs te gzhan phan rgya che bar mdzad cing / bstan bcos kyang mang du brtsams lo bcu bdun gyi
bar du gdan sa bskyangs nas nga lnga pa shing pho rta la zhi bar gshegs so// //zhang ston bsod nams grags pa/zhang ston rgya bo ni mtshan bsod nams grags pa/ kun mkhyen
chen po la dbang rgyud bshad man ngag mtha' dag mnos/ yongs su rdzogs pa'i mkhas grub chen por gyur nas/ yar 'brog

do'i kha ba lung du bzhugs te gzhan phan rgya chen po mdzad do// de la dka' bzhi ba chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ 'khrul zhig pa/ bdag gi bla ma dus zhabs pa ste/ dbang khrid kyi
brgyud pa'o// //thang chen pa kun dga' 'bum/thang chen pa kun dga' 'bum ni/ bu dol gnyi ga las dus 'khor cha lag dang bcas pa gsan/ khyad par kun mkhyen chen po la rtsa ba'i
bla ma mchog tu 'dzin zhing 'bul mo che yang mdzad/ tshal dbus gling du 'phrin las bskyangs/ ta si chen po'i bkas rang gi grwa sar byon te lha ri dgon par bzhugs nas
bstan pa la phan par mdzad do// //14 nya dbon kun dga' dpal/nya dbon po kun dga' dpal ni/ nya ston dar rin gyi dbon po yin te gdon gyis mnyel ba la kun mkhyen chen po'i drung
du byin brlabs zhus ma thag nad las grol/ kun mkhyen chen po'i zhal nas lo sgrub lo gsum gyis dang spyan ras gzigs dang mngon sum du mjal nas mdo rgyud kyi dgongs pa
phyin ci ma log pa'i don thams cad shes pa ngas khag theg ngas kyang mdo rgyud kyi tshig don ma shes pa thams cad bla ma dkon mchog dang thugs rje chen po la gsol ba btab
pas rgyal pa'i dgongs pa phyin ci ma log pa shes pa yin/ ma shes pa than thun byung yang thugs rje chen po la zhus pas chog pa yin gsungs pas/ bka' bzhin

bsgrubs pas yi dam gyis zhal gzigs/ dus kyi 'khor lo sogs bka' dang bstan bcos rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son/ 'chad nyan yun ring du mdzad pas slob ma mkhas pa mang du thon pa
nyid do//mkhas pa rin chen mchogmkhas pa rin chen mchog ni/ de bzhin du lo gsum bsgrubs pas thugs rje chen po'i zhal gzigs te sde snod rab 'byams mkhyen nas bstan pa gsal
bar mdzad pa nyid do//khams pa ngag dbang /khams pa ngag dbang ni/ kun mkhyen chen po'i zhabs la thug nas zab chos rnams gsan/ bdag 'jam dbyangs dang mjal ba cig drung
nas mkhyen zhus pas/ slob ma'i rmi lam du bla mas rdor dril mgo thog tu bzhag nas lag tu gtad pa dang / sngags kyi rjes gnang mdzad pa rmis na/ bla ma de byang chub sems
dpa'i rnam 'phrul yin zhing slob ma yang snod dang ldan pa yin/ khyed rang mos gus byas shing sgrub pa lo gsum byas na don de 'grub pa yin/ gzhan don rgya chen po byed pa'i
bla ma cig 'tshal gsung bas/ bka' bzhin sa skya zur khang du mtshams dam po byas pa'i skabs shig tu rmi lam na kun mkhyen chen po tshogs kyi 'khor lo mdzad pa'i drung
du phyin pas/ phyag gis rdor dril mgo thog tu bzhag a ra pa tsa na'i rjes gnang mdzad pa rmis/ mahA kA la la gtor ma ma brjed par thong zer ba'i sgra cig kyang byung ba

dang / sngar gyi lung bstan dran nas bla ma la sangs rgyas dngos kyi 'du shes kyis gsol ba drag tu btab pas/ sgo gsum la ye shes phebs pa'i rnam 'gyur mang po byung ba la grogs
rnams kyis smyo 'dug zer ba yang byung / 'jam dpal gyi zhal mthong / dus 'khor dang nges don gyi bstan bcos mtha' dag la mkhas shing 'gro phan che bar byung ngo // //shangs
pa rdo rje pa/shangs pa rdo rje pa ni/ kun mkhyen chen po'i zhabs la btugs te/ dus 'khor dang nges don gyi bstan bcos la mkhas shing / thugs dam nyams rtogs shin
tu mtho/ shangs su dgon pa btab nas kun mkhyen chen po rab gnas la gdan drangs pas/ ming dus 'khor bde chen gling du btags 'gro phan yang che bar byung ngo //grub thob dbus
pa/grub thob dbus pa ni/ jo mo nang nyid du 'dag 'byar la rtse gcig tu bzhugs pa las/ skabs 'gar bug sgo las dog pa med par thon te nam mkha' la 'phags nas sku 'bum chen
mo la bskor ba byed pa dang / ji tsam gsol kyang yog cing zag pa mi 'byung la grub pa'i mtshan ma mang du ston pa zhig go/ bla ma mkha' spyod pa ni/ 'dag 'byar kho na
la bzhugs pa las/ nam zhig med par shes nas bug sgo bshig pas na bza' tsam lus pa zhig byung ngo // //khams pa thugs brtson/yang khams pa thugs brtson zhes pa sa skya ba'i
dge

bshes phar tshad mngon sum la mkhas pa zhig gis/ dbus phyogs su gra bskor la phyin pa'i lam zhor la/ jo mo nang du phyin lo tsA ba dang mjal nas chos 'brel zhus/ kun mkhyen
chen po dang mjal dogs nas sku 'bum chen mo'i bskor log la phyin pas gtug gis mjal nas rang dbang med par phyag 'bul dgos byung / dus phyis mtshur phu gnas nang du/ zhwa
dmar cod pan 'dzin pa sha grags seng ba'i drung du/ drung nas mngon shes thogs pa med pa mnga' ba lags pas/ kun mkhyen jo nang ba 'di bdud gang gi sprul pa lags zhus pas/
dbu hril gyis gtums nas khyod kyis labs tshar ram gsung / de ci labs zhus pas/ khyod de 'dra ma zer de ni rigs ldan gyi sprul pa yin/ 'di'i rgyu mtshan mang du smras na
sgom chen pa'i zog yin zer du 'ong / nga'i ngag la nyan na/ kun mkhyen pa nyid la mtsher ba ma byed par bshags pa gyis khong gis rjes su 'dzin par 'dug gsungs pas/ de ma
thag kun mkhyen chen po chu bzang na bzhugs 'dug pa'i drung du phyin/ gser gyi maNDal phul/ bshags pa byas/ zhabs bkrus pa'i khu ba 'thungs nas khrid zhus pas nyams rtogs
bzang po skyes so//g.yag sde paN chen/g.yag sde paN chen ni/ g.yag sde bye mar

yab dkon mchog dpal dang yum skya rgyal chos skyid kyi sras su sa mo phag la 'khrungs/ mkhan chen 'od 'byung las bsnyen par rdzogs/ blo gros mtshungs med la phar tshad sogs
gsan/ karma pa rang byung rdo rje/ sha grags seng ba/ la stod pa dbang rgyal rnams la sbyor drug kun spangs chos grags dpal bzang po la rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa/ g.yung
ston pa la tsa mi lugs kyi rgyud 'grel gyi lung dbang dang bcas pa/ bu ston pa la yongs rdzogs kyi dbang rgyud bshad/ kun mkhyen chen po la brgyud bshad mchog dbang / sbyor
drug gi khrid/ nges don rgya mtsho sogs gsan/ spyir bla ma brgya dang rtsa brgyad bsten/ sku tshe'i stod yo byad srab pa la skyes mchog bsam gtan dpal bas longs spyod
kyi rten 'brel bsgrigs pas legs par 'grig ste/ na ning bar nga'i khas skyo ma ma rnyed/ da ni skyo mas nga'i kha mi rnyed par 'dug gsungs/ de nas a waM gyi dgon pa btab nas

pa/ ri khrod pa mgon po ye shes dang / 'jam dbyangs chos mgon pa dang / mkhas grub

byang chub rgyal mtshan dang / mkhan chen sangs rgyas blo gros la sogs pa mang du byon no// //ri khrod pa mgon po ye shes/ri khrod pa mgon po ye shes kyis paN chen gshegs rjes/
lo shas e waM gyi gdan sar bzhugs nas wa sna'i dgon pa btab te gzhan phan rgya che bar mdzad do// 'jam dbyangs chos mgon pa ni/ kun mkhyen chen po/ bu ston rin po che/

gsung zhing gzhan phan mdzad do//'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/de'i gdan sa 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan ni/ zhang ston rgya bo/ chos mgon pa/ rtogs ldan sngon

gshegs so//rkyang chen pa shAkya shrI/

chos mgon pa'i slob ma rkyang chen pa shAkya shrI ni/ gtso bo chos mgon pa las rgyud 'grel byang bar bslabs/ mkhan chen rgyal bzang pa dang / tshal min pa las kyang gsan/ bu

du byon pa na/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor shin tu bkra ba cig gi 'gram na/ kun mkhyen chen po bzhugs pa dang mjal te byin gyis brlabs pa'i snang ba byung bas chos mang
po la nges pa rnyed gsung / brgyad cu pa sa pho 'brug la bde ba can du gshegs so// de la thams cad mkhyen pa 'gos lo tsA bas gsan to// //15 chos rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/chos
rje phyogs las rnam rgyal ba ni/ mtshan gzhan chos kyi rgyal po zhes pa 'khrungs yul mnga' ris pa/ me pho rta la 'khrungs/ gzhon pa'i dus nas dbus su byon nas chos
'khor gling du phar tshad la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid kyi sde snod la sbyangs pas mkhas pa chen po gyur te/ dbus gtsang gnyis kar gra bskor yang mdzad/ gra bskor gyi nang
la kun mkhyen chen po dang mjal bas shin tu dad pas jo nang nyid du phyag phab ste/ kun mkhyen chen po'i drung du dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang

rgyud bshad man ngag dang bcas pa dang chos gzhan yang mang du gsan/ man ngag thugs nyams su bzhes pas ting nge 'dzin bzang po 'khrungs te/ bla ma la yid ches bas rang gi bla
ma thams cad kyi gtso bor 'dzin/ kun mkhyen chen po'i slob ma byang pa ta dben pas kun mkhyen chen po dpon slob la zhal ta zhus te ngam rings kyi chos sde btab/ der kun

ring du mdzad/ slob ma blo gsal ba yang mang du 'dus/ phyis bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan pa la gdan sa gtad nas zhe dgu pa la jo mo nang gi gdan sa mdzad/ lo lnga na gdan sa de
yang gtad nas dbus su phebs/ tshal dbus gling du dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang rgyud bshad man ngag gi khrid rnams slob ma'i sde chen po la gsungs/ de nas yar klungs phyogs
la phebs/ rdor lo chen byang rtse la mchog dbang gong ma gnang / khra 'brug la sogs par bzhugs te gdul bya dpag tu med pa legs pa'i lam la bkod/ de nas gtsang la thegs te
