ba'i rtags dang rten 'brel 'dzom// zhes gsungs/ dgu bcu pa la phar phyin TI ka mdzad/ go gnyis pa la sems 'grel gsum la gzabs bshad mdzad/ go gsum pa chu mo glang la gshegs
so//dka' bcu pa padma bzang po/de'i slob ma'i thu bo gsum las/ dka' bcu pa padma bzang pos rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa lan mang du gsungs shing TIka chen yang mdzad do//chos

sogs bka' gter gyi chos mang po gsan/ de nas rtse thang du chen po chos seng ba dang slob dpon 'od zer dpal ba la phar tshad lo chen byang rtse la rgyud bshad tshar phyed
dang gnyis/ lo tsA ba nam mkha' bzang bo la tshar gnyis/ chos rje phyogs pa la dbang yongs su rdzogs pa/ rgyud bshad tshar gnyis/ sbyor drug dang bsnyen sgrub rtogs ldan
sngo nyal ma la rgyud 'grel phyogs mchan/ chos 'khor gling pa 'jam dkar la don dam bsnyen pa dang lta 'dod mdor bstan/ zhang ston rgya bo la rgyud 'grel kun mkhyen chen
po'i mchan dang bcas pa/ ri ston blo chen 'od la rgyud 'grel lo grags pa'i 'gyur dang / nA ro pa'i dbang mdor bstan gyi 'grel pa gsan/ kun mkhyen chen po lha sar phebs dus
bsnyen par rdzogs/ chos phran 'ga' yang gsan/ de rnams las phyogs las rnam rgyal ba'i lugs nyid gtso bor mdzad/ de nas sgrub pa la zhugs te yan lag drug gi rnal 'byor
lhur blangs pa'i tshe sku lus mes bsregs pa 'dra ba'i bsnyun gyis lo dgur bsnyung yang thugs dam ma chag

de nas bsnyun las grol zhing grub pa brnyes nas rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa yang gnang / rgyun ldan du skya ser pho mo la sogs pa'i gdul bya mang po la sbyor drug gi khrid btab
ste/ gzhan gyi don yun ring du mdzad nas/ gya drug pa shing pho 'brug la sku'i skye ba snga ma'i gnas dga' ldan du byon to// //'gos lo tsA ba chen po gzhon nu dpal/de'i
slob ma'i thu bo thams cad mkhyen pa 'gos lo tsA ba chen po gzhon nu dpal ni/ yul rgya sman lha khang gi mda' ngam pa ra'i grong nag mo dbus khyim du/ yab 'gos ston 'byung
gnas rdo rje dang yum sri thar skyid la sras lnga 'khrungs pa'i gsum pa yin/ chu pho spre'u la 'khrungs/ dgung lo dgu la spyan g.yas mkhan chen sangs rgyas bstan pa las
rab tu byung / slob dpon shes rab dar las spyod 'jug gsan/ khong gi zhal nas dka' bzhi dus 'khor dang bcas pa cig ci nas kyang slobs gsung bas dus 'khor slob pa la khyad
che bar byung gsung / bcu gnyis pa la rtses thang du byon te bsam bzang pa las rnam 'grel dang ston shAka pa las phar phyin rgyud bla gsan/ rgyud bla thugs la zin pa dang
mkhyen pa dus mnyam du byung / thang sag tu ye rgyal pa la rtsa 'jug tshig gsal bzhi brgya pa gsan pas zla ba shar ba'i mtshan ma brnyes/ nyer

gnyis pa la skyor mo lung du bsam gtan don grub pa la 'dul mngon gsan/ de'i tshe ra tshag jo mo mjal te gsol ba mang du btab/ thang sag tu ye rgyal ba la na bza' 'bul du thegs
pas kha ba bab ste yab kyi la thog tu nub gcig bzhugs pa'i tshe/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma dngos su gzigs/ ra tshag jo mos byin gyis brlabs par 'dug gsung / chos rje de bzhin
gshegs pa rtses thang du phebs pa la thugs bskyed dang chos drug gsan/ zhi byed kyi dpe cig phyag tu byung dus/ byang phyogs kyi nam mkha' la 'jam dbyangs sprin gseb
tu bzhugs pa gzigs/ gung snang pa la bde mchog lus dkyil gyi dbang zhus nas/ 'on gyi bkra shis do khar rje rin po che blo bzang grags pa la nA ro chos drug lam rim dbu ma
gsan/ rkyang chen pa shAkya shri la dus 'khor rgyud 'grel gsan cing rkyang chen pa dang lhan cig lha khang stengs su sangs rin pa la dus 'khor gyi dbang zhus/ phyis rgyud
bshad man ngag dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs par gsan/ gnas der zhing blon gyis zhal dngos su bstan/ mal gro rgya stengs kyi spyan snga rin chen 'phel la bka' gdams kyi
chos skor mang du gsan/ nyer lnga pa la shangs ri bo dge 'phel du

shangs pa kun mkhyen pa la zla ba lnga'i bar du thugs bskyed dang dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud 'grel bu lugs kyi bshad pa/ dpal ldan bla ma'i TIka chen/ 'khor lo sdom chen dang
gshed dmar la sogs pa'i dbang rjes gnang sum cu lhag gsan/ kun mkhyen pa'i gsung nas khyed kyis dus 'khor legs par shod/ thog mar rtsis bzhin bslabs la de rjes rgyud 'grel
la sbyor zhes bka' gtad/ nyer bdun pa la snang thang du lo tsA ba sanggha shri la ka lA pa dang / mkhan chen grub she ba la bslab btus skye rabs ched du brjod pa'i tshom
bya ba mdo sde rgyan gsan/ bstan 'gyur gyi gzigs rtogs kyang grub/ khyad par byang chen du dus 'khor rgyud 'grel la legs par sbyangs pas thugs kyi dpyad pa mthar phyin/
grub chen bsod blo ba la mdo sde rgyan 'byed gnyis gsan/ nyer brgyad pa la rta nag tu chos rje sgrol ma pa las sgyu 'phrul sogs rnying ma'i skor po ti lnga bcu tsam gsan
cing sbyangs/ de dus mnal lam du jo mo nang gsal bar gzigs pa phyis mjal du thegs pas de nyid ji lta ba bzhin du 'dug gsungs/ chos rje rong chen pa la snga phyir phar
phyin rtsa 'jug rnam nges rim lnga sogs gsan/ rab brtan gling du mkhan chen rgyal bzang pa la sbyor drug dang / sbe zhing du byang chub dpal ba la rngog chos sogs mang du
gsan/ so bzhi pa la stag rtse bas

rgya dur gyi mkhan sar bzhugs par gsol bas lo drug bzhugs/ de'i tshe slob dpon nam legs pa la dus 'khor rgyud 'grel gnang / so dgu pa la bzang pa blo rgyam la mngon pa gsan/
rgya dur bskyar nas lha pa rin po che rdo rje bla ma la ye shes zhabs lugs/ spyan snga nyer gnyis pa la do ha dang phyag chen gsan/ bzhi bcu pa la grar sems dpa' chen po
la sgron gsal dang / gong dkar du zhwa lu ba grags pa rgyal mtshan la yo ga rab 'byams phyis sne gdong rtser grub pa sde bdun gsan/ yongs rdzogs kyi paNDi ta chen por gyur
nas rtses thang du chos rje nam pa sogs sde snod 'dzin pa mang po la dus 'khor rgyud 'grel gsungs/ zhe gnyis pa la/ paN chen nags kyi rin chen rtses thang du phebs pa
la brtag cing dpyad pas mkhyen pa'i gting mi mngon par dgongs nas lu yi pa'i dbang gsan/ zhe bzhi pa la bsam gtan gling du thugs dam la bzhugs pas slongs che bar byung te
bsnyun drag pos btab pa na chos brgyad mgo snyoms shing thugs las byon pa'i man ngag nyams su bzhes pas khro gnyer ba'i sgra byung ma thag bsnyun dwangs/ slar yang paN
chen la sbyor drug gi khrid dang mi g.yo ba'i dbang gsan/ mchim phur dbang mdor bstan gyi bka' 'grel sogs

'gyur mang po mdzad/ 'gos lo tsA ba zhes mtshan gsol/ rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang / bde dgyes/ mi g.yo ba/ gra lnga rnams kyi dbang / dbang mdor bstan/ dpe med 'tsho'i sbyor
drug rtsa 'grel/ mtshan brjod dpyid thig 'grel pa/ man snye/ mi g.yo bla med kyi rgyud rnams gsan/ de'i tshe rje 'di spyir rig pa'i gnas ji snyed pa la mkhas/ khyad par rgyal
ba'i gsung rab mtha' dag gi tshig don drang nges ma lus pa dpyis phyin du mkhyen cing smra ba'i spobs pa mchog tu dge bas/ paN chen gyi zhal nas paNDi ta mi'i nyi ma'i
shes rab lta bu ma mthong / mi'i nyi ma ni gshegs/ da ni 'dzam bu'i gling na ku ma ra shri las mkhas pa mi snang gsung te mchog tu bsngags par mdzad do// sa pho rta'i
lo la chos rgyal grags pa 'byung gnas pas sbyin bdag mdzad de btsan thang du dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer ba la rje 'di nyid sogs sde snod 'dzin pa mang pos kri ya sa mutstsha
sogs dbang rjes gnang rgya mtsho lta bu gsan/ 'on chos sdings su rgod phrug chos rje la phag mo gzhung drug gsan nas dwags phyogs su thegs/ ku rab pa dang 'brum mda'
bas bsnyen bskur te smyon phug tu thugs dam mdzad cing sher phyin dgu ba sogs kyi 'gyur mdzad/ de nas tsa rir thegs te sdong bo mkhar ngang zil chen dang skyo go tshal
dang /

g.yag phug rnams su zla ba drug thugs dam mdzad/ slar dwags por phebs te sprul sku chos dpa' ye shes pa la chos drug gsan/ sgam por thegs dus sku 'dra rin po che de sgam po
pa dngos su mjal zhing / de'u shar mar chos nyid kyi bden pa gzigs te der nga la go ba skyes pa yin gsung / dwags po la bar du ri mi 'babs pa bsod nams rin chen la phyag
chen spyod yul do ha gsan/ zhe dgu pa la yar klungs su phebs rgod phrug pa la ayon bsnyen sgrub gsan/ gzhan la bstan na phan pa rgya chen po 'byung zhes lung bstan/ lnga
bcu pa la yid bzang rtser bzhugs te dmar ston pa dang / chos rje nam pa dang / dpal kun bzang rtse pa la sbyor drug gnang / de'i phyi lo chu pho khyi'i nag zla la/ chos
rgyal grags pa 'byung gnas kyi bkas dpon slob rnams la phogs dang chos ja gnang nas slob dpon rin po che ye shes rgyal mtshos gtsos pa'i sde snod 'dzin pa'i dpe 'grims dgu
bcu lhag la rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa rgyas par gnang / ye shes rgya mtsho bas zhus nas rgyud gsum gsang ba rnam phye mdzad/ chu mo phag la rtsis la 'khrul sel yang mdzad/
skyam 'chad pa stengs su sgron gsal la 'gyur bcos mdzad nas rje nam pa sogs la gsungs/ 'ju lha khang

stengs su yang / gdan sa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ bla ma bkras bsod pa/ ston nyi sogs la rgyud 'grel gsung / bkras bsod pas zhus nas bskyed rim yan lag bzhi pa mdzad/ nga
bdun pa la ljang pho brang du chos rje lo chen la rgyud 'grel gsungs/ de'i phyi lo la chos rje nam pa dang lo chen la sgron gsal nges don gyi bshad pa rtsal du bton nas gsungs/
sbrul lo la dpal kun bzang rtse pas zhus te lha khang stengs su sde snod 'dzin pa mang po la rgyud 'grel gsungs/ rta lo la rdo'i mthong smon dgon par chen po dpal
'byor ba sogs sde snod 'dzin pa mang po la rgyud 'grel gsungs/ lug lo la chos sdings g.yu lo bkod par sku mtshams mdzad/ re gcig pa la paN chen gdan 'dren pa la thegs te/
ngur mig gi sgrol ma la gsol ba btab pas/ mnal lam du sgrol ma'i utpa la'i sdong po'i 'og la dpon slob rnams byon pa'i mtshan ma byung / lam rnams su'ang sde snod 'dzin
pa mang po la chos gsungs/ chos rje nyid la stod du bzhugs nas slob ma rnams bal bor paN chen gdan 'dren du brdzangs/ paN chen ding ri ste dmar du phebs pa la mjal te sna
len bzang po bshams/ paN chen gyi mdzad pa'i sha wa ri'i bstod pa bsgyur/ paN chen chos gsung pa dang dbang

bskur ba'i lo tsA yang mdzad/si tu rnam rgyal grags pas dus 'khor skor gyi dri ba mang du mdzad pa la the tshom rtsa ba nas bsal bas mchog tu gus par 'dzin/ seng ge rtse nas
phebs pa'i nyin phyi bas thog nyid du lce rtse skan sbyar gyi 'gyur mdzad/ re lngar phebs dus bcu gsum ma'i mchod chog dang tsarba Ti'i bstod pa'i 'gyur mdzad/ rim gyis
sne gdong rtser phebs/ paN chen la snang ba'i phreng ba dang dril bu rim lnga gsan/ glang thang spyan snga kun rdor ba la sgron gsal snang / re bzhi pa la paN chen bal por
thegs rjes skyam 'chad pa stengs su dpal kun bzang rtse pa sogs la sgron gsal gsungs/ de nas smin rir chos rje bstan pa bas gdan drangs smin ri ba'i dge bshes mang po
dang khrid thob brgya lhag la rgyud 'grel gsungs/ re lnga pa la sman cig pa shes rab bzang po la zhi byed gsan/ de rjes chos rje sman cig pa dpon slob la zhi khro'i dbang
sogs gnang / de nas yar klungs su phebs nas zhi byed kyi thugs dam sku mtshams mdzad/ de nas zhal snga pa kun rgyal ba la phur ba'i dbang gnang / rdor bzang pa sogs dge
bshes mang po la/ sgron gsal brtag gnyis sgyu 'phrul sogs gnang / rgyal dbang chos rje kun dga' dpal 'byor ba dang / dpal

kun bzang rtse ba la rgyud 'grel gnang / don gcig pa la/ stag lung par gdan drangs te/ phan yul gyi de'u gong du phebs pa'i nyin bdun gyi brag logs la shAkya thub pa'i sku
sku chos ser po mnabs pa gzigs/ chos rje ngag gi dbang phyug la dus 'khor sogs gnang / rong po chen po/ kong po thang mgon pa/ 'ba' rom pa sogs dge bshes mang po la chos
gsungs/ rwa sgreng du thegs pas 'jam rdor gyi sku de ye shes kyi sku dngos su gzigs/ don gsum pa la ljang phu bkra shis dgon par lo gcig gi bar du sku mtshams la bzhugs pas
da ltar gyi snang ba 'di thams cad 'od gsal 'ba' zhig tu 'char bar 'dug gsung / stag lung pas zhus te dus 'khor bka' 'grel/ 'khrul 'khor bcu gcig gi nang bshad/ red mda'
ba'i rtsod lan rnams mdzad/ don bdun pa la yid bzang rtser sku mtshams dam po la bzhugs pa'i khongs su mchod rten chen mo grub nas/ tshong 'dus yangs pa can du phebs te/
chos kyi rje spyan snga rin po che la sems 'brel skor phran dang bcas pa gnang / smon thang du sku mtshams dam po la bzhugs pa'i khong nas chos mang du gnang / go lung
par 'khrungs pa sogs sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa dang / lha'i mig dang / gzhan gyi sems

shes pa sogs mngon par mkhyen pa mnga'/ rgyud bla'i 'grel bshad chen mo mdzad pa na/ sa g.yo ba dang rje btsun gyi byin gyis brlabs pa'i mtshan ma byung / gya gsum pa la mngon
dga' chos rdzong du phebs chos rnams lhug par rtsol bzhin pa'i ngang nas me pho spre'u la tshong 'dus yangs pa can du thegs te/ sprul sku rin po che zhwa dmar cod pan
'dzin pa bzhi pa phebs pa la dpal mkha' spyod pa'i lugs kyi rim lnga/ phyag chen/ rlung sems/ gnyis med sbyor drug ber nag can gsan cing phyis mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang
rgyud 'grel phag mo snying thig rnams gsan/ spyir bla ma drug cu rtsa drug mnga'/ sprul sku rin po che la sha wa ra'i sbyor drug rgyud gsum gsang ba gnang / bsnyen par
rdzogs pa'i mkhan po mdzad/ de nas mngon dga' chos rdzong du sprul sku rin po che la sems 'brel bskor sogs chos rnams bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gnang / sbyor drug gi khrid
yig dang phar phyin TIka chen mdzad/ gya bdun pa la yang dgon pho brang du bzhugs te chos rje lo chen la rdo rje snying 'grel gyi bshad pa gnang / dgu bcu pa me mo glang
gi lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nyer brgyad la sku'i bkod pa bsdus so//

dpal ldan bla ma mchog 'dis dus kyi 'khor lo'i dka' ba'i gnas rnams legs par dkrol zhing / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dbang bzhi pa sbyor ba yan lag drug gi gsang mdzod la nges
pa'i spobs pa thob par mdzad pas bdag la bka' drin lhag par che'o//chos rje dmar ston pa/bdag nyid chen po 'di'i slob ma'i mchog ni/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ slob
dpon rin po che ye shes rgya mtsho/ stag lung rin po che ngag gi dbang phyug sprul sku rin po che zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa/ chos rje rin po che nam mkha' blo gros/ spyan
snga rin po che ngag gi dbang phyug chen po dpal 'byor rgya mtsho/ lo chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ rgyal dbang chos rje kun dga' dpal 'byor/ chos rje bstan pa rgyal mtshan/
glang thang spyan snga ba kun dga' rdo rje/ dpal kun bzang rtse pa chen po/ rgyal sras gzhon nu dbang phyug lhun sde rab 'byams pa/ chos rje lha lung pa nam mkha' rgyal
mtshan/ dka' bcu pa grags pa mtha' yas sogs sde snod 'dzin pa chen po khyad par dus kyi 'khor lo la mkhas pa mang du byon pa las/chos rje dmar ston pa ni/ dmar khams
pa grags bzang dang / ngor pa kun dga' bzang po sogs bla ma dam pa mang du bsnyen nas dka' chen bzhi sogs sde snod mtha' dag la

thugs sbyangs/ gsang sngags rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son/ chos rgyal grags pa 'byung gnas pa'i gtsug rgyan du bzhugs nas sa pho rta la btsan thang du dbus phyogs kyi sde snod
'dzin pa phal mo che la bod du byung ngo 'tshal gyi dbang dang / rgyud bshad sgrub skor dang bcas pa gnang bas btsan thang dbang mangs su grags/ yon du gser gyi phung po
chen po byung bas gcig kyang ma god par dmar khams pa dang ngor chen pa la phul nas/ rje 'di'i zhabs la gtugs te gangs can na mchog gi bla ma khyed nyid las lhag pa ma
rnyed pas tshe gcig la sangs rgya bas man ngag sbyor ba yan lag drug rdzogs pa cig zhu zhes gsung ba la man ngag mtha' dag rdzogs par gnang / gsan ma thag khams su byon te
bug sgo 'dag sbyar can zhig tu ji srid 'tsho'i bar du sgrub pa snying por mdzad pa la thugs thag bcad nas gzhan la chos gsung ba sogs ye ma gnang bar thugs dam la rtse
gcig tu bzhugs so//stag lung pa/stag lung pa ni/ sa pho khyi la 'khrungs/ bla ma mang du bsten nas mdo sngags kyi gzhung lugs rgya mtsho lta bu gsan/ sgrub rgyud kyi gdams
pas phyug khyad par du 'gos lo tsA ba gdan drangs te/ sbyor drug gi khrid/ rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa sogs sems 'grel gyi skor phran dang bcas pa/ 'phags skor/ ye shes zhabs
lugs/ mtshan brjod/

rnam snang mngon byang / zhi byed/ spyod yul/ rgyud bla ma rnams gsan/ rgyal ba'i gsung rab mtha' dag la mchog tu mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang phyug tu gyur/ phyogs kun tu snyan
par grags/ ljang gi rgyal khams yan phrin las kyis khyab/ sde snod 'dzin pa phal mo che zhabs drung du lhags pa na mkhyen pa'i gting mi dpogs par zhum/ dgung lo don
dgu'i bar du bstan pa dang 'gro ba la phan pa che bar mdzad do// //chos rje rin po che nam mkha' blo gros/chos rje rin po che nam mkha' blo gros ni/ yul yar klungs dge ra
sar yab rdo rje padma rgyal po dang yum lha mo skyid kyi sras su chu mo lug la 'khrungs/ g.ye ba'i rkun mas gdan drangs tshe nyi zhur gyi steng du spyan ras gzigs bzhugs
pa zhal gzigs/ dgung lo dgu pa la rtse thang du chen po tshul blo ba las rab tu byung / ston shAka pa dang blo rgyal ba las phar tshad la sbyangs/ bcu pa la karma pa de
bzhin gshegs pa la chos drug gsan/ 'bras spungs su chos rje bkra shis dpal ldan pa dang rab mchog pa las dka' bzhi dang dbu ma gsan cing sbyangs/

rgyal tshab dar ma rin chen dang bzang skyong ba dang shar pa ye rgyal ba la chos mang du gsan/ gtsang phyogs su jo mo nang gi bar du byon nas kun mkhyen chen po'i slob ma
sgrub pa mo 'od gsal 'bum dang 'u lu gnyis la chos 'brel gsan/ snar thang du grub chen bsod blo ba dang / chos rje a mo ba la chos 'brel gsan/ nyer dgu pa la sna mo chos
rdzong du mtshan sgrog pa'i mkhan po legs rin pa/ dge blo pa dpal rin pa rnams la mkhan slob bzhus te bsnyen par rdzogs/ rtse thang du 'gos lo tsA ba la dus 'khor rgyud 'grel
dang phar phyin gsan/ rgyal bzang rgyud 'bum zhus dag gi phyag phyir thegs te rgyud 'grel skyar chos

su gsan/ lha khang stengs su yang gdan sa ba dang lhan cig rgyud 'grel dang rgyud bla gsan/ rtses thang du chen po blo rgyal ba'i 'chad nyan pa mdzad de dge bshes mang du thon/
de dus gtsang phyogs su chos bar la thegs pa'i tshe 'u yug dka' bzhi pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la rdo rje phreng ba dang mi tra brgya rtsa'i dbang gsan/ so drug pa
la dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer la kr-i ya sa mu tstsha sogs dbang rjes gnang brgya lhag dang bde dgyes kyi rgyud lam 'bras lam skor/ paN chen nags kyi rin chen la mi
g.yo bla med kyi dbang / paNDi ta shA ri 'u tral mtshan brjod/ chos rgyal grags pa 'byung gnas la khams sum rnam rgyal sogs kyi dbang / byang chub dpal ba la rngog chos/
slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho la dus 'khor dang dpal mchog gi dbang / mkhan chen bsod nams mchog grub pa la dbang rjes gnang lung mang po yar 'brog tu skyes mchog smon lam
ba la bde mchog sogs mang du gsan/ 'gos lo tsA ba la phar tshad gsan cing sbyor drug gi gdams pa mnos pas rtogs pa 'khrungs/ rtses thang sgrub mchod chen mo thog mar 'dzugs
pa'i sgrub las dang / dus 'khor sgrub mchod kyang mdzad/ spyan snga rin po che

yum gyi lhums su zhugs pa'i tshe gong mas bka' gnang ste lha sar smon lam 'debs pa la thegs/ rtses thang gi 'chad nyan chen po bsod yes pa la gtad nas 'on bu bla mkhar sogs
dben gnas rnams su thugs dam la rtse gcig tu bzhugs/ lhag tu mkhan chen shAkya grags pa la sems khrid/ sbyor drug phyag chen/ chos drug sogs gsan/ zhal snga nas kun rgyal
ba la dbang mang po dang grub snying gsan/ dga' ldan dgon par sku mtshams la bzhugs pas bar do la bogs thon/ zhe lnga ba la 'on bu bla mkhar du bla sgrub mdzad nas ljang
pho brang du 'gos lo tsA bas chos kyi gsang mdzod brtol te 'phags skor ye shes zhabs lugs/ mdo sgyu sems phyogs sogs chos rnams gtad/ 'o khar chos rje chos grags pa la
rgyud 'bum gsan/ zhe brgyad pa la kong por thegs te/ sprul sku chos dpal ye shes dang mkhan chen lhag ru ba la bsnyen sgrub sogs zab chos mang po gsan/ de nas tsa rir sdong
po mkhar du bla sgrub mdzad/ klu rgyal dbang po lha lhag gis slob bu brgya 'bul bar khas blangs/ zhing skyong dam la btags/ lnga bcu pa la 'on gyi dpal rir phebs te 'gos
lo tsA ba la gang snang stong gzugs kho nar

'char zhing brtan pa'i rtogs pa phul bde drod rang 'bar/ de na skyam 'chad pa stengs su 'dul ba dang sbyor drug sogs chos mang du gsungs/ de'i gzhi bdag gis sems bskyed zhus
pas yul mi rnams mchog tu gus par gyur/  nam mkha'i bya la'ang sgom thebs pa'i grags pa byung / rwa khrid lug khrid thub pa'i slob ma zhig byung na ngo sprod 'debs pa la
gnas 'gyu la khyad med gsung / re gnyis pa la spyan snga rin po che'i bla ma mdzad/ re bzhi pa la lha sar thegs nas smon lam btab ste gung thang / dol gyi gangs khrod/
zhu la'i rdza rnams su sbyor drug sogs chos mang du gsungs/ sa pho byi ba la rje nyid kyis las dpon mdzad de/ rtses thang du mchod rten chen mo bzhengs/ yang dben du yang
rnam rgyal mchod rten bzhengs/ don gsum pa la g.ya' bzang su sbyor drug sogs khrid mang du bstsal/ sprul sku rin po che bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i slob dpon mdzad/ don lnga
pa me mo bya'i lo hor zla bzhi pa'i nyi shu brgyad la byams pa gling du 'ja' 'od dang me tog gi char dang / pi wang gi sgra dang bcas te sku'i bkod pa bsdus pa'i tshe dbu'i
gtsug

tor 'phags pa las 'o ma lta bu'i byang chub kyi sems phyur ba byung ngo // dam pa 'di la bdag gis 'khor lo sdom chen gyi dbang / sha wa ra dang dpe med 'tsho'i sbyor drug yu
mo'i gsal sgron/ dus 'khor dka' 'grel rnams mnos so//chos kyi rje spyan snga pa/chos kyi rje spyan snga rin po che ni/ yab chos rgyal grags pa 'byung gnas dang / yum skyo
bza' dbang 'dzoms ma'i sras su sa mo lug la bltams/ jo gdan nyi ma ba la gshed dmar gyi dbang lan mang po dang / dmar ston pa la mnyan mgon gyi rjes gnang zhus/ chos skyong
'dis 'phrin las sgrub par 'dug ces lung bstan/ dgung lo bzhi pa la rgod phrug chos rje la dge bsnyen mnos shing rab tu byung / mtshan ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa phyogs
thams cad las rnam par rgyal ba'i lha zhes gsol/ rgyal bzang smon mkhar du yab sras mjal/ yab kyi drung du ye shes mgon po'i dbang sogs gsan/ slob dpon mnga' ris bka'
bcu ba las phar tshad 'dul mngon la sbyangs bas/ skyes stobs kyis tshegs med par mkhyen/ paN chen nags kyi rin chen la dril bu rim sngags gsan/ bcu bzhi pa la rtses thang
gi

gdan sar bzhugs te/ sde snod 'dzin pa rgya mtsho lta bu la/ dka' chen bzhi rgyas par gsungs pas 'dus pa thams cad ngo mtshar du 'dzin/ bcu drug pa la dpal kun tu bzang po'i
nags khrod du 'jigs pa med pa sengge'i khri la lha dang bcas pa yongs kyis bzhugs su gsol te/ bka' rgyud kyi bla khab kyis phyogs kun tu khyab par mdzad/ nyer lnga pa la
slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho ba la/ dus 'khor yo ga sogs kyi dbang mnos/ dpal kun bzang rtse bas phyag len rnams phul/ nyer drug pa la chos rje na ma pa la sbyor drug rgyud
'grel rdo rje phreng ba mi tra brgya rtsa sogs dbang rjes gnang / gzhung khrid man ngag rje de nyid la mnga' ba phal che ba gsan/ so gcig pa la thams cad mkhyen pa 'gos
lo tsA ba la sems 'grel skor phran dang bcas pa sogs gsang sngags gsar rnying gi dbang khrid gzhung bshad mang po dang / sde snod kyi bshad pa mang du gsan/ sgra snyan
rtsis sogs rig pa'i gnas phra mo rnams la yang rab tu byang bar gyur/ so bzhi pa la 'gos lo tsA ba/ chos rje nam pa/ mkhan chen 'gro bzang rnams la mkhan slob zhus te bsnyen
par rdzogs/ 'gro bzang

pa la lung sde bzhi gsan/ so brgyad pa la zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa la karma pa'i chos skor mtha' dag gsan/ mngon par rtogs pa'i yon tan dang ldan/ ye shes kyi mgon po rnams
kyis bka' bzhin sgrub/ zhe gnyis pa la sne sdong rtser phebs te khrims gnyis kyi sgo nas bstan pa gsal bar mdzad nas/ nga gsum pa lcags mo phag gi zla ba drug pa'i tshes
gnyis la me tog gi char dang bcas te dga' ldan du gshegs so//rgyal dbang chos rje kun dga' dpal 'byor/rgyal dbang chos rje kun dga' dpal 'byor ni/ gtsang ba rgyal sras
kyi sku skyer grags/ 'brug dang ra lung du bzhugs nas sgrub rgyud kyi bdag po mdzad/ sne gdong rtser paN chen nags kyi rin chen la sbyor drug dang / yid bzang rtser 'gos
lo tsA ba la rgyud 'grel gsan cing sbyangs/ slad du sgam po'i gdan sar bzhugs pa'i tshe/ 'on smon thang du phebs te 'gos lo tsA ba la dbang mdor bstan/ sgron gsal/ rgyud
bla rnams gsan/ sa stod smad thams cad du byon te 'gro phan rgya cher mdzad do//dpal kun bzang rtse ba/dpal kun bzang rtse ba ni/ sngags 'chang rin chen rnam rgyal gyi sras
su me mo bya la 'khrungs/ gdung zi

na/ skyes stobs kyi thugs rab che zhing sku mchog tu mdzes/ yab dang lha khang stengs pa sangs rin pa la rnying ma'i dbang po gsan/ dgung lo dgu la dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan
gyi zhabs la gtugs/ slob dpon thang chen pa tshul khrims rgyal mtshan las dge bsnyen mnos mtshan bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang por gsol/ bcu drug pa la rtses thang
du gong ma grags pa 'byung gnas pa'i gzims dpon mdzad/ bcu dgu pa la gong mas sne gdong ka bzhi bar bskos/ de'i tshe dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer la kr-i ya sa mu tstsha
sogs dbang rgya mtsho dang / zhwa lu ba grags pa rgyal mtshan la dus 'khor yo ga rab 'byams sogs dbang mang po dang / paN chen nags kyi rin chen la dus 'khor gyi dbang
dang sbyor drug gi khrid rdo rje phreng ba sogs dang / bla brang ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dang bsod nams dpal 'byor la gshed dmar gsang 'dus rdo rje phreng ba sogs dang rje
'gos lo tsA ba la sbyor drug gi khrid sems 'grel skor phran dang bcas pa dang / byang chub dpal ba la rngog chos dang / rgod phrug pa/ sgo mo ba bzang po dpal/ mkhan chen
byang bzang pa/

rgyal ba phyag na rnams la yang chos mang du gsan/ so gcig pa la ka bzhi bzhag ste kun bzang rtser bzhugs nas rdo rje phreng ba dang yo ga rab 'byams kyi dbang dang bshad pa
phyag khrid kyi dus chos btsugs pas phyag len mkhas pa mang du thon/ 'ol khar chos rje chos grags pa la dus 'khor rgyud 'grel gsan/ sne gdong bzang lcog tu yang bzhugs
te chos rje nam pa la mi tra brgya rtsa sogs dbang man ngag mang po dang / ye shes rgya mtsho ba la dus 'khor gyi dbang / bka' 'gyur ba la lung sde bzhi phal dkon mdo mangs
sher phyin gyi lung / chos nyi ba la gsang 'dus gnyis med rnam rgyal/ zhal snga nas la dbang rgyud bshad mang po dang ayon bsnyen sgrub sogs khrid mang po dang bka' rgyud
bka' 'bum/ byams pa gling pa la tshad ma dang snyan ngag me long / lhag ru pa la sems khrid phyag chen chos drug rdzogs chen a ro snying thig sogs khrid dang / dpal mkha'
spyod pa'i bka' 'bum gsan/ gong ma kun dga' legs pa'i bla ma mdzad de dbang man ngag dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i phyag khrid

mang du bstsal/ zhe gsum pa tsa rir thegs te tshogs 'khor mdzad pas mtshan ldan thod pa'i steng du rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ e yig gi rnam par gzigs/ sgam po mjal nas slar tshong
'dus yangs pa can du phebs/ spyan snga rin po che la rgyud sde bzhi'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga phal mo che'i phyag khrid phul/ slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho ba/ chos rje
nam pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa 'gos lo tsA ba/ zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa rnams spyan snga rin po che'i bla mar spyan drangs pa la chos mang po gsan/ drug cu pa la thams cad
mkhyen pa 'gos lo tsA ba/ chos rje nam pa/ mkhan chen 'gro bzang snying po rnams la mkhan slob zhus nas bsnyen par rdzogs/ re lnga pa la sne gdong rtser byon nas mgon khang
stengs su bzhugs/ gsang sngags rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son/ thugs dam rtogs pa mngon du gyur/ gang dang gang du bzhugs pa de dang der mngon par dbang bskur ba rgya mtsho
lta bu dang zab rgyas kyi chos lhug par bstsal bas sde snod 'dzin pa mang po dbang gi chu bos smin pa dang grol bar mdzad/ re bdun pa la chos rje rdo rje gdan pa kun
dga' rnam rgyal bas gdan drangs

pa la spyod rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis dang / kr-i ya sa mu tstsha dang / mdo dbang chen mo/ sgyu 'phrul zhi khro sogs gsar rnying gi dbang mang po dang / dpal ldan bla ma'i
dus 'khor TIka chen dang mdo sgyu sems gsum gyi rgyud bshad dang khrid sogs gnang / rje btsun ma sgrol ma rdo rje dang bcas pa'i skyabs sbyin gyi phyag rgya can sogs yi
dam gyi lha mang po'i zhal gzigs/ rje karma pa chos grags rgya mtsho la yang chos mang du gsan/ dpal ye shes dbang po'i sde la chos rnams gtad de/ don gcig pa me mo lug
gi zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bco brgyad la sku'i bkod pa bsdus so//dam pa 'di la bdag gis 'jam dpal gyi lta 'dod mdor bstan dang dbang mdor bstan gyi dka' 'grel sAdhu pu tras
mdzad pa sogs dang / paN chen nags kyi rin chen nas brgyud pa'i dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang mnos so//rgyal sras gzhon dbang bas yid bzang rtser bzhugs te/ rgyud bshad dang
khrid kyis gzhan don cher mdzad/ rtses thang bsam gtan gling du sgrub grwa yang btsugs so// chos rje lha lung bas lha lung du dbang rgyud bshad khrid kyis gdul bya mang
bo rjes su

gzung ngo //spyang lung chos sding pa/yang mkhan chen rgyal bzang pa'i slob ma spyang lung chos sding pa ni/ 'phan yul dmar zhogs su yab dmar dge bsnyen mgon po/ yum rdo rje
bu 'dren gyi sras su chu pho byi ba la 'khrungs/ dmar ston rgyam rin pa'i gcen po yin/ sengge dpal ba las dge bsnyen mnos/ mtshan gzhon nu blo gros su btags/ byang chub
tu thugs bskyed rdor dbyings kyi dbang gsan/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal slob spyang lung ba bsod nams sengge las dge tshul thob/
mchog dbang zhus nas sbyor drug sron lugs gsan cing / phyis mkhan chen yon tan blo gros la yang sbyor drug gsan pas nyams rtogs 'khrungs/ gro pa mkhan chen kun rgyal bas
mkhan po/ dmar ston dpal rin pas las kyi slob dpon shAkya rin chen gyis gsang ston pa mdzad nas bsnyen par rdzogs/ rtses thang du phebs te mkhan chen rgyal bzang pa las
dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud 'grel phran dang bcas pa gsan/ bla ma de rnams dang / byang ngam rings pa zla mgon shes rab pa/ bla brang pa nyi ma rgyal mtshan/

red mda' ba/ lo tsA ba skyabs mchog dpal/ mkhas btsun gzhon nu 'od/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ spyan snga nyer gnyis pa/ gnyag phu ba/ rje tsong kha pa/ shar pa ye shes rgyal
mtshan sogs mkhas btsun mang po bsten nas mdo sngags kyi gzhung lugs phal mo che la sbyangs shing / sbyor drug gi rtogs pa mngon du gyur pas gzhon nu nyid nas rtogs
ldan dka' bzhi ba zhes grags/ dgung lo bcu gsum nas sku rdo rje'i dkyil dkrung / gsung rdo rje'i bzlas pa/ thugs zung 'jug phyag rgya chen po las mi g.yel bar rgyun du bzhugs/
lta stangs grub pas spyan 'byed 'dzum mi mnga'/ stong gzugs kyi sha wa ra zhal gzigs/ sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa dang / gzhan gyi sems shes pa la sogs pa'i mngon
par shes pa mnga' spyang lung ri khrod du bzhugs nas khrid 'di'i sgo nas 'gro ba grangs las 'das pa grol ba mdzad de/ dgung lo brgya dang lnga bzhes pa me pho spre'u'i
lo la chos kyi dbyings su gshegs so// de la lhun sde rab 'byams pas gsan te khrid kyis 'phrin las

bskyangs so//stag pa chos kyi rdo rje/yang chos rje phyogs pas mkhas grub nam mkha' rgyal mtshan la dbang rgyud bshad man ngag dang bcas pa gnang / des stag pa chos kyi rdo
rje la gnang / de ni sde snod spyi dang khyad par du dus 'khor la shin tu mkhas shing / mngon shes dang ldan/ srog thur 'dres pas rlung la dbang thob pa'i mkhas grub zhig
go/skungs lungs pa sangs rgyas dpal/des skungs lungs pa sangs rgyas dpal/ des bdag gi bla ma rje dus 'khor zhabs pa la dbang rdzogs pa/ rgyud 'grel dbang mdor bstan/ sems
'grel gzhan gnyis/ sbyor drug gi khrid legs par gnang ngo //sman chu kha ba blo gros rgyal mtshan/sman chu kha ba blo gros rgyal mtshan ni/ kun mkhyen chen po la dus kyi
'khor lo'i dbang rgyud bshad man ngag dang bcas pa gsan nas/ la dong sman chu kha dang / byang 'bab rong rdza de'u rin chen spung par thugs dam rtse gcig tu mdzad cing
bshad sgrub kyi 'phrin las yun ring du bskyangs/ khrid yig ngo sprod dang bcas pa'ang mdzad mar me rong ba la sogs pa'i grub thob kyi slob ma mang du byung ngo // de'i dbon
pos sangs rgyas blo gros pa ni/ khu bos chos rje phyogs rgyal ba'i drung du btang / thog mar sde snod gsum la sbyangs/ khyad par sems 'grel

bskor la mkhas par gyur nas/ phyogs rgyal bas lo bcu gnyis kyi bar du 'dag 'byar la bzhag ste rtse gcig tu sgom du bcug pas grub pa brnyes nas/ la dong sman chu kha nyid du
bzhugs nas bshad sgrub kyi 'phrin las bskyangs so//'khrul zhig gzhon nu 'od/de'i slob ma 'khrul zhig gzhon nu 'od ni/ yul g.ye rong rlung 'gags kyi skam lung zhes par/ mes
po 'gar padma bzang po/ yab grags pa bzang po/ yum bde chen skyid kyi sras su sa pho spre'u la 'khrungs/ mes pos smi ri'i gzhi bdag la mna' zos pas/ yum ma gtogs nye du
thams cad 'das/ dgung lo lnga pa la bla ma tshul 'od pa las dge bsnyen mnos/ brgyad pa la khrab la kar mkhan chen sangs rgyas bzang po dang / mtshungs med gzhon nu grags
pa las rab tu byung / mtshan gzhon nu 'od du btags/ mkhan po dang slob dpon gzhon seng ba'i drung du 'dul mdzod la sbyangs/ bco brgyad pa la mkhan slob de gsum dang dge
'dun las bsnyen par rdzogs/ dbus g.yor gyi 'dul mdzod kyi grwa ba rnams su grwa bskor yang mdzad/ khrab la kar

'chad nyan mdzad dus chags sdang la thugs skyo nas/ mtshungs med pa'i drung du blo sbyong gsan pas byang chub kyi sems bcos ma ma yin pa 'khrungs/ snying rje'i gzhan dbang
gis rgyun du spyan chab 'byin pas/ mtshungs med pa'i zhal nas khyed kyi dbu 'di chu las byas pa 'dra zhes gsung / de nas gcod skor gsan te gnyan khrod 'ba' zhig brten nas
dur khrod gcig tu bzhugs pa'i thugs nyams la/ glo gnyis nas mi dkar dmar 'jigs su rung ba dbyug pa thogs pa re byung nas/ khyed kyis nged gnyis ma bcom na mi 'ong zer bas/
ro rkyang gi bgrod pa 'joms dgos pa'i brdar go gsung / de nas mtshungs med pa'i drung du zab lam gyi khrid dpal ldan bla ma'i lugs gsan pas/ rab kyi dang po rtogs pa ste/
zhes pa ltar rtags bcu rdzogs shing sku dang zhing khams mtha' yas pa gzigs/ 'phar g.yo 'dar sprug la sogs pa rdo rje'i nyams ci yang rdol/ gzhan yang rgyud bla rtsa
'grel sogs mang du gsan/ nyer lnga pa la bsam yas su 'od gsal dpal gyi dgon par thegs te/ dka' bzhi ba chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa la/ dus 'khor gyi dbang khrid/ phar phyin
rgyud bla rnams gsan/

bu lugs kyi khrid snga phyir tshar sum cu lhag pa gsan no// de nas khrab kar 'dar 'byar la lo gsum bzhugs pas sku lus kyi rtsa gnas gzigs/ der la ka ba nang ma mthun pas thugs
skyo ste skyi shod du thegs nas/ la dong sman chu kha'i dgon par sangs rgyas blo gros pa la sbyor drug phran dang bcas pa gsan/ slar yang bsam yas su chos kyi rgyal mtshan
pa las bsnyen sgrub/ spros med/ shangs chos rdzogs pa dmar khrid rnams zla ba bco brgyad kyi bar du mtshams khongs nas gsan/ mchod rten dkar po ba sangs rgyas skyabs
la gshed skor gsan/ zhabs kyi byin pa'i nang du rlung 'dzin pa'i thugs nyams byung ba'i tho rangs zhabs gnyis nag hrul song ste cig char gum/ dpon tshal pa na re 'di klu
gdol pa nag pos zin pas bcos su med zer/ de nas 'do li la btegs nas khrab la kar byon sku mtshams bsdams te mnyam par bzhag pas/ zla ba bzhi na be bum chung ngu zhig gdung
mtshams na yod pa len pa'i thugs nyams kyis har bzhengs pas bsnyung las grol te/ bsnyung zug thugs dam gyi bogs su thon pa 'di bla ma'i bka' drin yin

gsungs nas/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa khrab la kar gdan drangs te gser srang bzhi bcu phul bas shin tu mnyes/ de res dbang rjes gnang bzhi brgya lhag dang / bu rin po che dang
kun mkhyen chen po'i gsan yig na gang bzhugs kyi dus 'khor skor mtha' dag dang / lam 'bras lam skor dgu dang bcas pa/ yang dgon pa'i ri chos skor gsan/ snga phyir sku
mtshams 'dag 'byar lo bcu gcig mdzad/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi zhal gzigs/ smin ri'i gzhi bdag gis kyang drung du 'ongs nas dge bsnyen mnos te gdan drangs pas/ zhe lnga pa
la smin ri'i phug tu phebs sgrub sde yang btab/ slob ma'i tshogs mang du 'dus te 'dag 'byar la rtse gcig tu gnas pa'i lo mtshams pa brgyad cu lhag tsam 'khor mar byung /
g.ye gnyal yar klungs rnams su'ang thegs te khrid kyis 'gro don rgya chen po mdzad/ khyad par du chas dgon gsar bas sbyin bdag mdzad de khra 'brug tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor
zhing slob ma'i tshogs khyams khra gang ba la sor bsam gyi khrid thabs gcig tu gnang ba na phal cher nyams rtogs mngon du gyur/ rdo rje'i tshig grub pas yon bdag

cig 'chi ba'i mgor phyag reg ste/ oM the gong gong zhes gsungs pas theg sgra dang bcas te gong du 'phos/ lta stangs grub pas spyan la 'byed 'dzum mi mnga' zhing mngon par mkhyen
pa mnga'/ chos brgyad mgo snyoms pas 'khrul zhig par grags/ gsang chab la gla rtsi'i dri bro zhing gzhan gyi nad thams cad sel ba'i sman gcig po mdzad tshems byon pa
rnams mu tig tu gyur/ lan cig chos grwar thog babs pa la rnal 'byor ma'i zhabs dran par byos shig gsung ma thag grwa pa rnams la stangs pa tsam yang med par thog de sku
drung de nas shar phyogs kyi wa chu'i bug pa la dmar hril li li song ste lung pa gzhan zhig tu song ba byung / don drug pa chu mo phag gi mchu'i zla ba'i nyer gnyis la chos
kyi dbyings su gshegs so// slob ma'i mchog kyang rgyal tshab blo gros dbang phyug chos rje bstan pa ba/ rje dus 'khor zhabs la sogs mang du byung ba las/rgyal tshab pa/rgyal
tshab pa ni/ chos lung mkhan chen rin rgyal ba dang / chu mig dgon gsar ba slob dpon byang rgyal ba la gtugs te mkhas pa

chen por gyur nas/ lha lung byang sems pa'i phyag phyir smin rir byon/ nyin cig 'khrul zhig pa'i/ ma hA kA la nga yin pas// nga yi bka' las ma 'da' zhig/ ces gsung drag po
gzhan gnang ba gzigs ma thag sgo gsum la ye shes phebs/ rje de phyag drug pa dngos su gzigs/ de nas sangs rgyas dngos kyi 'du shes kyis legs par bsten nas zab lam gyi khrid
sogs gdams pa mtha' dag nod de/ bsgoms pas mngon par rtogs pa'i yon tan dang ldan/ 'khrul zhig pa nyid kyi gdan sar bskos pas rgyal tshab par grags/ phyis paN chen nags
kyi rin chen la yang sbyor drug gsan/ yar klungs lha lung du'ang 'gro don rgya cher mdzad do//chos rje bstan pa ba/chos rje bstan pa ba ni/ yar klungs sprul sku'i rgyud
du 'khrungs/ khu bo sangs rgyas dbon du grags pa des khong rang gi bka' 'bum dbu la bzhag nas byin gyis brlabs/ g.ye rte'u rar rtse mo ba las rab tu byung / mtshan bstan
pa rgyal mtshan du btags/ 'khrul zhig pa dang/ sku zhang chos rje dang / yon bkras pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa 'gos lo tsA ba rnams bsten nas/ dbang rgyud bshad

man ngag mtha' dag mnos te grub pa brnyes nas rgyud 'grel par du bzhengs/ smin ri ltar dga' lha lung du dbang khrid kyis gzhan phan mdzad do//rje dus 'khor zhabs pa/rje dus
'khor zhabs pa ni/ yar klungs lha lung du yab 'brug sgra dbon po dang / yum ston ma bde ba'i sras su me mo phag la 'khrungs gdung ngo rje/ dgung lo bdun la sman char dgon
par chen po tshul blo ba las dge bsnyen mnos te mtshan blo gros rgyal mtshan du btags/ smin rir 'khrul zhig pa'i drung du blo sbyong gsan/ rtses thang du dwags po 'od zer
sengge dang / 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' grags las rab tu byung / rnam 'grel la sbyangs te bcu drug pa la bshad ston mdzad/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' grags la dus 'khor gyi dbang
gsan/ 'khrul zhig pa la sbyor drug gsan pas rdo rje gsum gyi nyams dang mtshan ma bcu rdzogs par grub/ nyer gsum pa la smin rir mgon po phyag drug pa la bsnyen pa mdzad
pas mtshan ma brtan po brnyed/ mgon po la tshal min pa dang / rin rgyal ba dang / rkyang chen pa gsum po gang gi drung du phyin na dus 'khor gyi rgyud nyan pa la bzang
zhes lung ston par gsol bas

rin rgyal ba bzang pa'i lung bstan thob/ mnal lam la sngar gzigs ma myong bas lung pa zhig tu 'phur nas byon pas/ ri'i ngos kyi phug pa zhig na yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po
che 'od zer gyi phung po bar 'brel bas phyogs thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa yid 'phrod pa cig 'dug pa phyag tu lon te/ slar yang nam mkha' la 'phur bas phyag gi nor bu'i
'od kyis gnam sa thams cad khyab pa gcig rmis te/ mnal sad pa'i skabs su yang thugs la dga' ba khyad par can 'char ba zhig byung gsung / nyer bzhi pa la lha sar jo bo la
byin brlabs nan tan du zhus nas e waM du byon te 'jam dbyangs rin rgyal ba la rtsis dang sgrub dkyil gyi mdzub khrid legs par gsan/ de nas dpon slob rnams mal gro'i dgon
pa cig tu thegs nas slob ma nyi shu rtsa lnga dang stabs gcig tu rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa gsan cing dri gtug gi sgo nas kyang dka' ba'i gnas mtha' dag bkral/ mal gro lung
ba de snga mnal lam du byung ba'i lung pa'i bkod pa de ji bzhin tu snang zhing / dgon pa'i sa cha de nor bu lon pa'i ri'i ngos de kar 'dug pas/ yid bzhin gyi nor bu lon
pa de rgyud 'grel

thob pa la lta bar 'dug gsung / de nas smin rir phebs dus 'phrul zhig pas dus 'khor gyi glegs bam gtad de bla ma dus 'khor ba zhes su mtshan gsol/ sbyor drug gi man ngag ma
lus pa dang kun mkhyen chen po'i bka' 'bum gnang / rgyal tshab pa la yang rgyud bla dang rgyud 'bum gyi lung gsan/ dus 'khor gyi rgyud la zhal ston 'khor mor mdzad/ nyer
bdun pa la gsang phur chos rje dpal seng ba'i drung du phar phyin dang dbu ma la sbyangs/ nyer dgu ba la snye mo ru dgon gsar du sku zhang chos rje rin chen bkra shis pa
la dus gsang bde dgyes mA yA gdan bzhi gshed dmar rdor dbyings sogs kyi dbang sgrub bskor/ dbang mdor bstan/ sbyor drug/ rim lnga/ spros med sogs gsan/ chos rje yon bkras
pa la rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa tshar gsum dri gtug dang bcas pa'i sgo nas rgyas par gsan cing mkhas par sbyangs/ so gcig pa la sku zhang chos rje'i mkhan po/ yon bkras
pas las slob/ bkras rin pas gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ mtshan 'phags pa rin chen du btags/ so gnyis pa la shangs skungs lungs su sangs rgyas

dpal ba la bu dol gnyi ga'i lugs kyi dbang dang rgyud 'grel gyi zab bshad gsan/ rdo rje slob dpon bdag po'i dbang gi skabs su/ chos rje de nyid kyi bzhugs khri la bzhugs su
bcug nas bka' mi nus pa'i bka' gtad dang bcas te gnang / de nas smin rir lo gsum phyogs gsum gyi sku mtshams bcad de 'khrul zhig pa la ayon bsnyen sgrub/ lam 'bras/ ni gu/
yang dgon pa'i ri chos/ spyod yul/ dmar khrid sogs gsan/ thugs dam gyi rtsal thon/ bdag las gzhan gces kyi thugs bcos min 'khrungs/ der lo ltar gyi nag nya sgrub mchod
btsugs/ kong por byon te zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa chos dpal ye shes pa la phyag chen dang / ku cor rtogs ldan pa la grub chen brgyad cu'i glud gsan/ sgam por dge bshes
mang po la rgyud 'grel gsungs/ slar smin rir phebs nas 'khrul zhig pa'i gdung la mchod pa 'bul zhing gdung ba'i gsol 'debs mdzad/ gnyal du byon te pho brang yangs rtser
khri dpon bkra shis dpal bzang po yab sras la dus 'khor gyi dbang gnang /

zhe gnyis pa la gtsang phyogs la thegs te/ dpal 'khor bde chen du chos rje dkon mchog bzang po la byams chos lnga gsan/ khro phu'i byams chen mjal nas sa skyar byon te/ chos
rje ngor pa'i gcung po gzhon nu pa la lam 'bras lam skor dang bcas pa/ ngor pa nyid la nA ro mkha' spyod dang lam dus kyi dbang / mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan la bde
mchog nyung ngu'i rgyud dang gur brtag sam gsum gyi bshad pa dang sa skya pa'i bka' 'bum gsan/ la stod byang du bdag po rnam rgyal grags pa la 'khor lo sdom chen gyi dbang
gsan/ bdag pos bka' gnang nas dge bshes mang ba zhig la rgyud 'grel tshar gcig gsungs/ jo mo nang mjal dus mthong grol chen mo'i gdugs g.yas bskor du 'khor ba'i nyams
shar ma thag nam mkha' thams cad sangs rgyas kyi sku'i snang bas gang / thugs nyams 'ur langs te ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo mtha' yas pa 'khrungs/ de nas skungs lungs su chos
rje sangs rgyas dpal ba la rdo rje phreng ba la sogs pa'i dbang rjes gnang bzhi brgya lhag dang / rgyud sde du ma'i bshad pa dang sgrub skor/ shangs chos sbyor drug rigs
mi 'dra ba'i khrid rim du ma gsan/

phag mo gzhung drug ma'i dbang khrid gsan pa'i tshe/ rje skungs lungs pa'i drung na ka pA la bdud rtsis gang ba na rje btsun zhal gnyis ma sku mthe bong tsam cig 'dug pa gzigs
ma thag thod pa'i bdud rtsi de hor len mdzad nas gsol bas sku lus la bde ba khyad par can skyes/ chos rjes bka' gnang nas bla ma shambha la pa sogs skungs lungs pa'i
dge 'dun rnams la rgyud 'grel gsungs/ thang pa chos mdzad pa la'ang rgyud bshad gnang / zhe drug pa la yu mo'i dben gnas mjal nas/ byang chub gling du chos rje padma bzang
po la 'jam dbyangs dang mi g.yo ba gsan/ khong dus 'khor gyi DI kA brtsoms pa'i skabs kyis 'bel gtam nyin mtshan 'khor mor mdzad/ de nas rtsa ri mjal bas DA ki 'du ba'i
mtshan ma mang du gzigs/ snga phyir mtshan ldan thod pa'i drung du rnal 'byor ma'i cho ga dang 'brel ba'i tshogs 'khor stong phrag gcig mdzad/ gnyal padma gsal rje gangs
su mtshams dam po'i thugs dam lo gcig gnang / de nas byar padma brag chu dgon par bsam gtan khang bu chung ngu bug sgo can du/ thun 'jug gi spros pa bcad de/ rdo rje skyil
dkrung las mi g.yo

bar gsung bcad kho na mdzad de/ ltos med bzhi la brten nas lo gsum phyogs gsum gyi bar du rdo rje'i rnal 'byor bsgoms pas mnyam rjes 'dres pa'i rtogs pa 'khrungs/ nga gcig
pa lha sar bcu gcig zhal gyi drung du bsnyung gnas stong phrag gnyis kyi dam bca' phul nas/ sa ga nas brtsams te bsnyung gnas chun dril brgya rtsa re lo re bzhin mdzad/ rkong
por karma pa mjal ba la thegs te bla ma'i rnal 'byor gsan/ gu shri dpal 'byor don grub pa la nA ro chos drug dang rlung sems gnyis med gsan/ gtso bor ko ro brag tu thugs
dam nyid la bzhugs/ nga drug pa la 'grongs ltas mang du byung bas bdag tu 'dzin pa'i khri ba bcad/ gtso bor sems can rnams sdug bsngal ba la mi bzod pa'i thugs rjes
gtong len kho na mdzad pas/ mnal lam du chos rje sangs rgyas dpal ba byon nas tshe dpag med kyi khrid mdzad pa'i dus kyi tshe'i bdud rtsi de 'di yin no// 'di gzhan la ma
byin par 'thung cig gsung nas ka pA la bdud rtsis gang ba gnang ba bzhes pas ltas rnams bzlog tshe bsring ba la yang blo sbyong rang zab

par 'dug gsung / nga brgyad pa la smin rir bzhugs te/ sku mtshams dam po bug sgo can mdzad nas thugs dam kho na la gtso bor bzhugs shing / skabs 'gar dus chos kyi sbyor drug
dang / bsnyen sgrub/ ni gu/ lam 'bras spros med/ dmar khrid gcod yul/ blo sbyong la sogs pa'i khrid dang / dus 'khor/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ mi tra brgya rtsa la sogs pa'i
dbang dang / dbang mdor bstan la sogs pa'i rgyud bshad bag re gnang / snga phyir mnyal du thegs nas bsgrub pa'i mar khal khri drug stong gi dkar me dang / gser zho sum
brgya lhag pa'i gser chab dang bcas pas lha sar jo bo la mchod de/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gang bzhugs dang // gang dag 'das dang ma byon pa// de dag rjes su bdag slob
cing // byang chub spyod pa spyod gyur cig/ ces pas smon lam stong phrag mang po mdzad/ yar klungs su/ karma pa la sku gsum ngo sprod dang / zhwa dmar cod can 'dzin pa la
phyag chen gsan/ rab 'byams pa rin rgyal la byang chub sems dpa'i 'grel pa la sgyed mkhar btsugasanas gsung rabs

gzhan la gzigs na bstan pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i bdag sogs 'gyur nges pas de kho na ltar mdzad dgos/ gzhan phyogs ris su chad pa'i mkhas par rlom pa cig las mi 'ong / rdo rje'i
rnal 'byor gyi myong rtogs bzang po cig byung na grub mtha' 'dra blos byas pa yin pas rang zhig la 'gro/ grub mtha' la phyogs ma mdzad ces gsung / nga'i bsnyung gnas
'dis zas kyi rnam g.yeng med pa dang / ngag bcad kyis yengs ma lam la mi 'gro bar dge sbyor shin tu 'phel ba'i mtshams gcod chen por byung gsung zhing / bsnyung gnas ma yin
pa'i skabs su'ang phal cher gsung bcad mdzad/ nyin zhag phrugs gcig la thugs dam gyi khrigs chu bo'i nyer ma lta bus dus 'da'/ de lta bu'i mtshan nyid yongs su rdzogs
pa'i dpal ldan bla ma dam pa de ni dgongs pa yongs su rdzoigs nas gya lnga pa lcags mo phag la mnyel zhi ni nam yang mi mnga' ba'i ngang nas phyag pad dkor dang bcas te/
nyams bsam dga' la blo bsam bde// thar pa'i btsan sa zin pa yin// bde chen gyi thang la 'gro ba yin// byang chub kyi lam la bzhugs pa yin// 'gro ba'i 'dren pa byed pa

yin// mi kho bo'i 'dun ma rtse la song // zhes gsungs shing bde ba can du gshegs te sku gdung las kyang lha sku dang ring bsrel mang du byon no//bdag gis lo bcu bdun pa la
rje 'di'i zhabs kyi padmor btugs te lo sum cu'i bar du gus pas bsten nas/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang rgyud man ngag dang bcas pa legs par mnos so//chos rje rin tshul ba/chos
rje rin tshul ba ni/ yul tsha rag dbus sde'i khang gsar du/ yab dpon don yod bzang po dang yum byang chub ldan gyi sras su yos lo la 'khrungs mtshan gzhon nu bzang por
btags/ bcu gsum pa la chu bzang dgon par mkhan sengge rin chen dang slob dpon rin bsam pa las rab tu byung ste mtshan rin chen tshul khrims su btags/ lhun grub sgang du bla
ma sengge dpal la gur brtag sam gsum gsan/ slob dpon rin bkras pa las phar phyin byang bar bslabs/ bco brgyad pa la mkhan chen sangs rgyas gzhon nu ba/ las slob dar ma
bzang po/ gsang ston pa rin bkras pas mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ bu ston rin po che'i drung du phar mngon/ spyod 'jug yo ga rab 'byams gsan/ de nas yar klungs lhung mor
chos dpal mgon po'i drung du dus

'khor gyi dbang sbyor drug gsan te bsgoms pas lus ngag gi nyams rdol/ myang stod du la stod pa dbang rgyal la sbyor drug rdzogs par gsan pas rtogs pa 'khrungs shing mngon shes
dang ldan/ shangs su bla ma rin seng ba la lam 'bras gsan/ de nas bzang ldan du kun mkhyen chen po rgyud 'brel gsung ba'i drung du byon pas/ e waM gzugs bsgrub kyi skabs
su phebs/ de nyin rang bshad pa'i 'phro la zhugs chog pa byung / dbang rgyud bshad man ngag phran dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs pa/ byams pa'i chos sde nyi shu sogs mang
du gsan cing dpyis phyin par mkhyen/ lo tsA ba blo gros dpal ba la sems 'grel gnyis sogs mang du gsan/ der cig shes kun grol gyi gnad go bas/ 'jam gsar ba'i gsung las/
da ni rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas byon gyur kyang // myur du sangs rgyas lam ni zhu bsam med// gsung ba de bden par 'dug gsung / sgrub pa la rtse gcig tu gzhol nas grub chen
man lungs pa lta bu cig mdzad dgongs pa na/ kun mkhyen chen pos nges don gyi chos ston pa la gtso bor

'don pa zhu gsung pa la brten nas/ slob ma mtho dman ris med pa khrid kyi myong rtogs la sbyor bar mdzad/ mnyal phyogs su yang 'gro don mang du mdzad/ phyis yar klungs lhung
mon bzhugs dus g.ya' bzang khri dpon tshul 'bum 'od mchog tu gus par yod pa de 'das pa'i gtam gsan pas/ khong la res nga ma gtogs med gsung nas de ma thag thugs dam zab
mos rjes su gzung bas tho rang shig nam mkha' las/ e ma sangs rgyas e sangs rgyas// zhes sogs ched du brjod pa'i sgra grags gsan/ de nas mkhan chen bsod nams 'od zer bas
stod lung gter mdzod du gdan drangs nas byi rdzong tshogs pa'i mkhan por bskos/ gzhon rgyal du wen sha bas sbyin bdag gi rtsa ba byas te yo byad mtha' dag gis bstabs/ tshogs
pa dang sbyin bdag rnams la zab lam gyi khrid stsal/ lo gcig tshogs bskyangs nas mkhan chen bsod she ba gdan sar bskos te/ dar kha che ba sangs rgyas 'od zer gyis dkyil
'khor sdings kyi dben gnas btab nas phul bar gtso bor

bzhugs/ phyis dar kha che ba gong du bzhud dus/ khong 'das pa mkhyen nas rtsa rig 'bum gter bzlas pas dga' ldan du skyes pa'i mtshan ma byung / kun mkhyen chen po su la yang
phyag lan mi mdzad pa yin pa la/ rje 'di la nges don gyi mnga' bdag la phyag 'tshal lo zhes phyag lan mdzad/ kun mkhyen chen po dbus phyogs su gdan drangs/ lha sar de'i
sku 'dra bzhengs/ nges don gyi bstan pa 'phel bar mdzad nas bde ba can du gshegs so// de'i slob ma zho lung mtsho kha ba yon tan 'phel dang / gnyal pa dpal ldan 'od dang
/ rtogs ldan ye rgyal ba gsum ga la/ la phyi ba sangs rgyas dpal gyis gsan/ de la chos rje ye shes dpal bzang pos sbyor drug phran dang bcas pa gsan to// yang rin tshul
ba'i slob ma chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ 'khrul zhig pa/ bdag gi bla ma dus 'khor zhabs so//bo dong rin chen rtse mo/grub thob se mo che ba'i slob ma bo dong rin chen rtse mo
ni/ bo dong rog tshor 'khrungs/ e'i bla chos pa gsan rong gnyis kyi drung du mngon pa bslabs/

gnyal zhig pa dang 'jam gsar ba las phar tshad sogs mkhas par sbyangs/ se mo che ba'i drung du/ 'jam gsar ba'i phyag phyir byon te/ dus 'khor rgyud 'grel dbang gdams ngag dang
bcas pa ma lus par gsan/ slad du 'jam gsar ba la yang dri gtug mdzad cing gsan pas mkhas par mkhyen/ bo dong e'i bla chos pa mdzad/ brag ram du bshad grwa btsugs pas
slob ma mkhas pa mang du byung / khyad par du rgyud gsungs pas gdugs thogs pa'i slob ma bco brgyad tshar/ khrid phog pas kyang grub pa thob pa'i slob ma mang du byung / gung
thang gi lha chen dpal 'bar/ khrod phu byams chen/ bo dong rin rtse'i lha mo che zhes mnyam por grags pa'i dus 'khor gyi thang ka chen mo bzhengs/ stan thog gcig tu bzlas
bsnyen bye ba rdzogs/ sbyin bsreg mdzad dus me lce la dpal be'u dang bkra shis 'khyil pa sogs byung / se mo che pa la long du thub/ gar skye zhus pas/ lo lnga bcu rtsa
gcig thub/ shambha lar skye zhes lung bstan pa ltar/ nga gcig pa nag zla'i nya'i zla ba cung zad 'phags pa la gshegs/ der byon pa mkhan chen gser

khang pas chos gsung ba'i grwa nas kyang gzigs so//stag sde ba sengge rgyal mtshan/de la slob ma stag sde ba dang / 'jims pa rin she dang / grub chen oTyan pa sogs mang du
byung ba las/ stag sde ba sengge rgyal mtshan chu pho spre'u la pha ri lung du sku 'khrungs/ la stod byang gi stag sde ba yin/ bo dong rin rtse la phar tshad mngon sum/ khyad
par dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud bshad man ngag mtha' dag gsan pas mkhas pa chen por gyur nas er zur chos pa yun ring du mdzad/ rin rtse gshegs nas long grong sogs chos
gzhi rnams su bshad nyan mdzad pas/ snga tshar la shong sku mched/ dkon gzhon che chung / thugs she che chung sogs mkhas pa mang po tshar te gdugs theg pa'i slob ma bcu
gsum byung / phyis la stod byang gi tsha snar bshad pa mdzad pas/ rong pa shes seng / stag sde brtson rgyal/ bla ma dge 'dun brtan/ mkhan po yon tan mgon/ dpang lo la sogs
pa'i mkhas pa mang du thon te slob dpon las slob ma mkhas shes grags pa byung / gya gsum pa shing pho rta lo rgyal zla'i ches brgyad la sku gshegs so//shong lo tsA ba rdo
rje rgyal mtshan/shong lo tsA ba rdo rje rgyal

mtshan ni/ la stod lho'i spyad lung shar kha'i bor ra zhes par sku 'khrungs/ gzhon nu la rab tu byung / go lung pa mdo sde dpal rgyal mtshan gyi drung du/ dus 'khor chag lugs/
bde dgyes phreng bskor gsum sogs mang du gsan cing gar thig rtsis la byang bar bslabs te/ gza' gsal bar byed pa'i sgron ma sogs rtsis kyis bstan bcos du ma mdzad/ de
nas tsha snar stag sde ba'i drung du phar tshad mngon sum la mkhas par sbyangs/ dus 'khor gyi skor shog sdeb bzhi bcu tsam phyag ris su bris nas yon du phul te 'bro lugs
kyi dbang rgyud bshad man ngag dang bcas pa gsan/ 'phags pa rin po chos sna res sa skyar byon pa na bstod pa'i tshigs su bcad pa spel legs phul nas lo tsA slob tu 'gro bas
rdzogs par zhu zhus pas/ de lta bu'i blo skye ba bzang / gzhung lugs gsar ba bsgyur ba'i nus pa 'ong ba bka' ste/ paNDi ta la slob gnyer dang dri gtugs legs par gyis shig
kho bos kyang chos kyi rje bsten yun thung bas sdebs sbyor me tog gi chun bu dang / tshig gter sogs tshul bzhin du mi shod par snang bas 'di dag shes pa zhig ci nas kyang
gyis la shog cig gsungs nas/ de dag gi

dpe dang gser srang lnga dar yug bcu rnams gnang ste/ rten 'brel yod pas do nub rje btsun gong ma'i gzims khang dpe khang du nyol la song zhes gsungs nas brdzangs song / shong
gi thugs dgongs la skyes stobs kyi blo gros ni phun sum tshogs/ sbyor byung gi nan tan ni mchog tu gyur na/ legs bshad gsar ba mang du bsgyur bar ci ste mi nus snyam
du dgongs te/ 'phags pa'i gzim g.yog pa mdo smad pa blo gros rgyal po dang 'grogs nas bal yul du byon te/ paNDi ta ma hIntra bha dras dbang bzang po'i drung du sgra snyan
ngag sdebs sbyor zlos gar mngon brjod la bya bar mdzad nas sa skyar byon/ 'phags pa rin po che'i bka' bzhin rgyud 'grel shong 'gyur mdzad/ slar yang rdo rje gdan du byon
nas ma hA bo dhi la mchod pa dang bskor ba mdzad/ paNDi ta lakShmIM ka ra spyan drangs nas/ dpag bsam khri shing / klu kun tu dga' ba'i zlos gar/ snyan ngag me long / 'jig
rten dbang phyug gi bstod pa brgya pa/ 'jam dpal gyi bstod pa pr-itta mA la/ tsandra pa'i mdo la sogs pa sngon ma 'gyur ba bsgyur/

'chi med mdzod la 'gyur mchan mdzad nas/ sgra snyan ngag gi srol legs par btsugs/ 'phags pa rin po ches kyang / sde snod 'dzin pa shong lo tsA ba'i snyan du gsol ba/ zhes pa'i
phrin yig mdzad pa na/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel par bcas pa rgya che la zab cing gting dpag par dka' la tshig brling zhing / sdeb sbyor dbyings che bas chen
po rnams kyang nyams su lon dka' bas/ sngon byung ba'i lo tsA ba dag gis kyang ma 'gyur ba dang / log pa dang / rnam grangs gzhan dang / phyogs re ba dang / thal bar bsgyur
ba la sogs pa de dag khyed kyi legs par khong du chud cing mtha' gcig tu nges te/ zhu chen mdzad pa'i glegs bam dang / klu rnams rab tu dga' bar byed pa'i zlos gar mthong
bas/ dge ba dang rjes su yi rang ba khyad par can skyes/ zhes rab tu bsngags/ sgra bsgyur rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bur gyur to// de la de nyid kyi dbon po shong lo tsA
ba blo gros brtan pas gsan te/ de ni 'phags pa rin po che'i slob ma'i thu bor gyur cing / se chen rgyal pos kyang bla mar bkur ba/ gzhi 'gyur

dang 'gyur bcos mang du mdzad/ gcen gyi yon tan bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mkhyen zhing / dus 'khor la mkhas pa'i slob ma mang du thon to//lo mchog pa legs pa'i blo gros/de
la lo tsA ba mchog ldan dang sgra tshad pa rin rgyal gnyis kyis gsan pas/ lo mchog pa ni/ mang mkhar khra tshang du sku 'khrungs 'phags pa rin po che las rab tu byung /
mtshan mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros dpung rgyan mdzes pa'i tog ces rang nyid kyis 'dog par zhus pa bzhin btags la/ phyis lo mchog pa zhes grags/ shong lo sku mched las dbang
rgyud bshad man ngag dang bcas pa gsan/ bod du 'gyur ro 'tshal gyi dbang gdams ngag bka' bstan bcos phal mo che'i bka' lung mnga' bas dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po'i
bla mar gyur to// de la sde bdun pa chen po dpal ldan sengge dang / skyi ston 'jam dbyangs grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis shong lugs gsan la/ de gnyi gas rong pa shes rab sengge
la rwa lugs yang gsan te/ dpal ldan sengge la/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa dang / ti shri kun dga' rgyal mtshan dang / kun spangs chos grags dpal bzang pos gsan

zhing / skyi ston pa la/ kun mkhyen chen pos gsan to// yang lo mchog pa mnyam gung snang gi bcom ldan lha mo mdzes pas kyang gsan to//dpang lo tsA ba/stag sde pa'i slob ma
dpang lo tsA ba ni/ la stod lho'i spyang lungs kyi 'um bu gyam du me pho byi ba la 'khrungs/ gdung dpang / yum snga mo nas grongs te lug gi 'o mas bsos pas lu gu zhes par
grags/ kho bo ba'i 'o mas bsos na legs pa la blun pa rnams kyis lug gi 'o ma byin pas blo gros kyi phyed 'grib tu bcug gsung / grub chen o rgyan pas bu chung de la dge bshes
chen po cig 'ong bas 'di byin gsung nas ja gsol 'phro gsol zhal dang bcas pa bskur/ lo lnga pa la rgod tshang ba'i gdan sa ba byang gling pa las dge bsnyen mnos/ mtshan
blo gros brtan par btags/ bdun pa la mkhan chen gser khang pa dang me ston 'dul 'dzin las rab tu byung / yab kyis kyang dge slong byas te byang chub sengge zhes btsun
par grags so// bcu pa la mdo rtsa bya TI ka dang bcas pa khyi bdun gyis bdas kyang thon pa byung / sngon tshe sbyangs pas skye ba 'dir// gzhung rnams

rtsed mo'i zhor la shes// gsungs/ grogs zhig gis chu la khur bas khyed stobs che sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rangs po khur bas theg 'gro bar 'dug gsungs pas des 'thabs skad do//
bcu gsum pa la tsha snar stag sde ba'i drung du byon/ lo drug bar ma chad du bsten nas phar tshad mngon sum/ dbu ma/ khyad par dus 'khor la sbyangs pas bum pa gang byo'i
tshul du mkhas par mkhyen nas phyi nang gzhan gsum don ston pa'i rgyud 'grel tshig don rab bshad nas/ rdo rje theg par blo phyogs mdzad// gsang ba'i don ston bla mar 'dud//
bsam shing yang bla ma 'di bka' drin che/ stag sde pa 'di bka' drin che/ sengge rgyal mtshan ni bka' drin che/ bka' drin can gyi bla ma la// gus par phyag 'tshal skyabs
su mchi// zhes sogs kyi gsol 'debs yang mdzad/ bcu dgu pa la stag sde ba sku gshegs nas mang mkhar khra tshang du lo mchog pa la dus 'khor shod lugs/ ka tsan/ me long
/ rong pa shes rab sengge la dus 'khor rwa lugs/ sa skyar 'jam skya ba la brtag gnyis rnam 'grel rigs gter gsan/ nyi shu

pa la gser khang pas mkhan po/ me ston pas las slob/ byang stobs pas gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ a tsa ra byung tshad la phral skad bslabs/ 'jam dbyangs bzhi thog
pa dang paNDi ta'i bar gyi lo tsA mdzad pas lo tsA bar grags/ nyer gcig pa la bal bor byon/ ra ma A tsarya la tsantra pa gsan/ sa skyar byon te ka lA pa 'grel pa gnyis
dang bcas pa bsgyur/ shong ston legs bshad lde mig blang/// legs sbyar skad kyi gter kha phye// sna tshogs gzhung lugs rin chen blangs// legs bshad dga' ston 'gyed la dbang
// zhes gsungs/ dgo shing pa la bstod pa rgyan phreng mdzad nas bskur bas ngang de dngul bre chen phul ba bsnam nas yang bal bor byon/ paNDi ta snga ma gnyis dang rgya
gar shar phyogs kyi tsu Ta paNDi ta rnams bsten nas/ dgongs rgyan sogs bsgyur/ slar sa skyar phebs dus 'jam skya pas gtso mdzad kyis ser phreng dang bkur cha chen po mdzad/
bal bor lan bdun du byon/ bal po'i paNDi ta phal che bas man snye dang dgongs rgyan sogs bzhus/

sa skyar bzhi thog pa dang 'jam skya pa la lam 'bras sogs mang du gsan/ so gnyis pa la gung thang gnas po cher chos gzhis btsugs te/ gung thang pa bde blo sogs slob ma'i tshogs
rgya mtsho lta bu 'dus pa la/ dbyar dus 'khor/ dgun phar tshad mngon gsum gyi dus chos gsungs/ de'i tshe yang bla ma dge 'dun brtan dang ri 'dabs pa la dbang lung /
sbyor drug gsan/ snyan pas grags pas rgya gar hor yul tshun khyab/ yang tshe dang hor rgyal pos gdan 'dren rim par byung ba la/ bar chad du gzigs nas spring yig gong 'og
can gyis ya tshe ba bzlogs shing / spyad phu dgon gsar la sengge gling du btags te der bzhugs pas hor bzlogs/ sdig pa'i grogs po'i yo ba ring du spangs// bdud kyi zhags pa'i
'ching ba che las grol// 'jigs pa med pa sengge'i gling du sleb// dpal ldan blo gros brtan pa'i bsam pa 'grub// ces gsung / skabs der sa skyar byon nas lo mchog ba la
mnga' ba'i bka' lung mtha' dag lo nyi shu rtsa lnga'i bar bsten te bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan/ shas cher gnas po cher bzhugs/

bshad bsgyur rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas bstan pa gsal bar mdzad/ shin tu sdig la 'dzems pa'i blos// chos spyod bcu bo 'bad pas bsgrub// de yis gzhan phan ci nus byed// rnal 'byor
bdag gi las ka lags// zhes gsungs/ slar yang sa skyar byon chos mang du gsungs/ gyam dang e'i gdan sa thegs tsam mdzad/ de nas dbus su byon pa'i lam du glegs bam mang
po slob ma la bkye ba'i mnal lam byung bas zla ba bcu drug gi bar dbus su bzhugs nas/ lha sa/ bsam yas/ gung thang / stag lung / ra sgreng / gnang ne'u thog rnams su dus
'khor/ dgongs rgyan/ phar tshad mngon sum/ dbu ma rgyan/ sgra snyan ngag zab mo'i mdo snga sogs chos mang du gsungs pa dbus kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen phal mo ches gsan/ da
ni shi yang mi 'gyod do// zhes gsungs/ de nas snar thang du mchims blo bzang pa sogs la dus 'khor dgongs rgyan sgra snyan sogs gnang / de nas e dang sa skya'i bar du byon/
gzhi 'gyur dang zhu chen mang du mdzad cing / dus 'khor

'grel chen gyi stod 'grel sogs bstan bcos mang du mdzad nas/ re bdun pa chu pho rta'i nag zla'i tshes bcu gsum la bde ba can du gshegs so//lo chen byang chub rtse mo/dam pa
'di la bla ma don yod rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ lo chen byang rtse sogs mkhas grub kyi slob ma mang du byung ba las/ lo chen ni/ la stod zur
tsho zhes par yab gzhon nu dpal bzang / yum dpang lo'i lcam mo ye shes sman ne'i sras su shing mo yos la 'khrungs/ dgung lo bdun pa la dpang lo las dge bsnyen mnos mtshan
dpal ldan byang chub rtse mor btags/ shong gi dbon po chos skyong dpal las rab tu byung / bcu drug pa la gung thang gnas po cher dpang lo las mngon tshad gsan cing sbyangs/
dpang lo bo dong e'i gdan sar bzhugs dus lo bzhi'i bar rig pa'i gnas phal mo che la sbyangs/ nyer gsum pa la 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan gyis mkhan po/ dpang lo'i
las slob/ chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis gsang ston mdzad

de sa skyar bsnyen par rdzogs/ nyer lnga pa la lo tsA mkhas par mkhyen/ dpang lo zhi bar gshegs kyi bar phyi bzhin 'brangs pas dus 'khor sogs de nyid la mnga' ba'i yon tan
ma lus pa thugs su chud/ de nas bu ston rin po che/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ rgyal sras thogs med pa rnams las rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i dbang rgyud man ngag dang bcas pa gsan
zhing thugs nyams su bzhes pas rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen por gyur nas kun gyis grub chen du mnga' gsol/ rgyal sras thogs med pas lo chen 'di la zhal zas kyis bsnyen
bkur na mu ge'i skal ba las nges par thar bar 'dug gsung pa thos pa gang du bzhugs kyang bsnyen bkur gyi mtsho brdol ba byung / chu la mi bying / bug pa chung ngu la'ang
sku bde bar shong / dbang bskur mdzad dus khang bu chung ngur mi mang po dog pa med par shong ba sogs rdzu 'phrul du ma bstan/ mngon par mkhyen pa thogs med du mnga'/
dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i bkas bo dong e'i gdan sa yang mdzad/ dpal ldan bla ma'i phyag phyir stag lung du byon pas/ stag lung par ratnA ka ras lo chen 'di nged kyi dbon
po'i slob dpon du

'jog par zhus pas gnang ste/ stag lung pa nam mkha' dpal bzang po la dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud man ngag dang bcas pa gnang nas/ slar dwags por dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i drung
du phebs te ka lA pa'i sa ris phul/ gtsang phyogs su bzhugs nas dgung lo mthon por gyur ba na spyan snga grags byang bas gdan drangs nas/ yar klungs gdan sa thel gung
thang rnams su dus 'khor gtso bor gton pa'i chos kyi char gyis mkhas pa mang po tshim par mdzad/ g.ye'i chab tshan la byon dus thugs mkhyen mang du gsungs/ stag tshang /
shangs/ 'u yug myang stod rnams su dus 'khor la sogs pa'i dbang rgyud bshad dang / sbyor drug sogs khrid mang du gnang / gsang chab 'thung pa tsam gyis lkugs pa mang po bye/
zhal mthong ba'am/ gsung thos pa'am/ gsol ras zos pa tsam gyis nang thon pa dang byin brlabs zhugs pa mang du byung / gdul bya mang po smin grol la bkod nas/ don brgyad
pa lcags pho spre'u mchu zla'i nyer gcig la gzims khang 'od

kyis gang / lha'i spos kyi ngad ldang / me tog gi char dang bcas te u rgyan du gshegs shing / gdung la rnal 'byor ma'i sku dang / ring bsrel mang du byon to//lo tsA ba nam
mkha' bzang po/slob ma'i mchog lo tsA ba nam mkha' bzang po nyid dbon po lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga grags pa byang chub/ stag lung pa nam mkha' dpal bzang
/ lha khang stengs pa sangs rgyas rin chen sogs mang du byung la/ lo tsA ba nam mkha' bzang po ni sgra tshad dus 'khor la mkhas par gyur nas lo chen gyi phyag phyi dang
/ sa gzhan du'ang dus 'khor gyi bshad pa mang du mdzad do//lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan/lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan ni/ lo chen nyid kyi chos rnams bum pa gang byor
mkhyen/ dus 'khor gyi bshad srol ma nyams par gzung ngo //dpal 'jigs med grags pa/de'i dbon po dpal 'jigs med grags pa ni/ bstan pa'i bdag por gyur nas/ de nyid 'dus chen
bcas pa'ibastan bcos chen po mdzad/ bskal bzang kyi sangs rgyas stong gi mtha' ma mos pa yin par rang nyid kyis zhal gyis bzhes so//byams pa gling pa chen po/de'i slob
ma byams pa gling pa chen po ni/

sde snod mang po la sbyangs shing mkhas pa chen por gyur nas/ phyis par 'brog tu paN chen 'jigs med grags pa'i drung du gsan pa rgya cher mdzad de/ 'di lugs kyi gsang sngags
kyi snying po kho na la thugs rton cing / paN chen nags kyi rin chen la zab lam gyi khrid mnos/ dus 'khor la ring du sbyangs pa'i mkhas pa don grub kun dga' la rgyud 'grel
gyi bshad pa gsan nas TI kA po ti bdun pa zhig dang / sngags 'dul la sogs la mkhas par gyur nas dkyil 'khor blo slongs dngul las bzhengs shing / chos 'di dar bar mdzad
do//bdag po rnam rgyal grags pa/dpal 'jigs med grags pa'i slob ma bdag po rnam rgyal grags pa ni/ sde snod mang po dang / khyad par dus 'khor la mkhas par gyur nas dkyil
'khor blo slongs dngul las bzhengs shing / chos 'di dar bar mdzad do//spyan snga grags pa byang chub/spyan snga grags pa byang chub ni/ lo chen la sbyor drug gsan nas/
lo chen 'di'i thugs dam mdzad tshul mthong ba na/ rang re kun la dge sbyor mi byed pa'i dbang mi 'ong bar 'dug gsung nas gzims chung du mun mtshams bsdams te thugs dam rtse
gcig tu mdzad do//stag lung pa nam mkha' dpal bzang /

stag lung pa nam mkha' dpal bzang po ni/ lo chen byang rtse las dus 'khor gsan nas/ sbyor drug bsgoms dus mnal lam du 'o ma phor gang gsol phro la las pa gcig byung bas/ lo
gcig bsgoms na mchog 'grub pa 'dug ste gsung / bskyed rim bde mchog dang / rdzogs rim sbyor drug la mdzad/ 'phags pa'i yul du bdag cag sngon// log par lta bas sems 'khrid
kyang // dus kyi 'khor lo dang mjal bas// phyis nas gsang ri khrod 'di ru// yan lag drug ldan nyams su blangs// zhes gsungs/ sbyor drug gi khrid yig dang / rtsis yig sogs
mdzad/ zab lam gyi gdams pas gdul bya rnams bskyangs/ sras dharmAe shwa ra yin par zhal gyis bzhes so// yang mngon grwa ba'i slob ma 'jims pa rin shes bo dong rin rtse
dang / lho pa grub seng gnyi ga la gsan/ de nyid dang rje btsun rgwa lo gnyi ga la dbus pa dge slong tshul khrims dar gyis rwa 'bro'i skor tshad bar gsan/ de la dus 'khor
ba shar pa ye shes rin chen gyis gsan/ de la byang sems rgyal ye dang mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtshos

gsan no// yang mngon grwa ba rin rtse/ zhang rdo rje rin nas/ 'jam dbyangs 'khon ston/ kun spangs chos grags dpal bzang po sogs byung te 'bro lugs so// //3)rwa lugs/rwa lo
tsA ba chos rab/gsum pa rwa lugs ni/ snya nam snang yul du sku 'khrungs pa'i rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags kyi dbon po rwa lo tsA ba chos rab kyis/ rwa lugs kyi gshin rje gshed
nag po skor gsum/ mngon 'byung rnam gsum/ a bhi dhA na/ sampu Ti rogs rgyud mang po dang / chos chung drug la sogs pa mkhyen nas/ dus 'khor gsan pa'i ched du bal por
byon te/ ye rang du paNDi ta sa manta shrI lo lnga zla ba bcu zhag lnga bar ma chad du bsten nas/ dbang rgyud bshad man ngag gi bka' rnams zhus shing / paNDi ta bod du spyan
drangs nas rgyud 'grel man ngag dang bcas pa bshad bsgyur gtan la phab/ thams cad kyis bsnyen bkur cher byas te nyin gcig la gser srang sum brgya phul/ gshegs skyel
yang skyi rong gi bar du mdzad pas/ bla ma yang shin tu mnyes te/ paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa'i srog zhu

dang phyag lham/ paNDi ta nyid kyi phyag dril dus 'khor lugs kyi phyag tshad ma rnams gnang / lo tsA bas kyang ne'u me tog ldan gyi bsti gnas su bzhugs te/ gzhan phan rgya
cher mdzad do//rwa ye shes sengges/de la de nyid kyi sras bla ma rwa ye shes sengges gsan te bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mkhyen/rwa 'bum seng gede la de nyid kyi sras rwa
'bum seng gis gsan no//rje btsun rgwa lo/de la rje btsun rgwa los gsan te/ de nas sngon chos rgyal khri srong lde btsan gyi mchod gnas me nyag ha shang du gyur pa'i sras
rgyud theg pa chen po'i gzhung lugs ma nyams par spyod pa'i sngags 'chang sha stag byung ba las/ me nyag rdo rje sengges gtsang rong mkhar phug bzung / de'i sras grub thob
ye shes rdo rjes rong dben dmar du bzhugs/ de dang ma gcig skyid mo'i sras su chu mo phag la 'khrungs/ yab kyi mtshan ltas las dpal rgwa lo'i skye bar dgongs te mtshan
rgwa lor btags/ lo gsum pa na paN chen shAkya shrI ngur mig du byon pa'i tshe yum gyis bsnams nas chos dang byin brlabs zhus pa na/ gzhan las mchog tu 'gyur bar saM skr-i
ta'i skad kyis lung bstan/ nyid kyi gsung gi

kyang / byis pa'i dus na kha che ba'i// bla ma paN chen nyid dang mjal// mgo la phyag gi byugs mdzad nas// legs sbyar skad kyis dbugs dbyung mdzad// ces so// yab kyi drung
du 'bri klog dang / 'jig rten bstan pa/ phung po lnga'i rab byed/ spyod 'jug sogs la sbyangs/ dgung lo bcu gsum pa la lcags lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po'i drung du byon/ lo
gsum gyi bar du rgya yig 'dri klog dang / khyad par du dgyes phag gnyis la sbyangs nas bcu drug pa la ngur mig du legs par gsungs/ de'i tshe rmi lam du btsun rgan lham
mthil rdol gyi khres po khur ba zhig 'ongs te/ 'di tsam zad zad btsal kyang ma rnyed pa'i grogs po de ga ngo rnyed pa la a re dga' zer zhing / dga' dga' mgu mgu ltar drung
na 'khod pa nas brtsams te phyi bzhin 'brang zhing phan pa sgrub pa ltar tshul 'chos so// de nas dben dmar du byon pa'i tshe yab kyi gsungs gis/ mdang ni 'byung po'i cho
'phrul che ba la de ring dge bshes pa byon/ bgegs kyi bar chad 'ong nyan yod pas 'byung po'i phan

pa la ma gtad par thugs dam la gtso bor mdzod cig gsungs ba dang / thugs kyi dam pa bskyed de bzlas pa dang / 'thab pa dang / bskrad pa lta bu byas kyang zhum pa med do// de
nas 'dol chung na bzhugs pa'i tshe cung zad bsnyung ba na/ mgron btsun rgya dpe kong rtse gang gyur ba cig gi po ti bstan te/ khyod mkhas na 'di dag gi don smra bar gyis
shig zer bas nga ni na bas khams zi ba'i phyir re shig sdod cig gsungs pa na/ mig sngar du dpe ris yag yug shad shud byed cing / yi ge la ni ma brten par// dam pa'i don
ni rtogs mi 'gyur // zhes rgol ba dang / mtshan mo gcer bur byas nas lha khang gi rdza'i dum bu mgor bzhag nas/ nga ni rdza khyung mgo zhes bsdigs pa sogs byed do// res
'ga' ni bshes gnyen gyi tshul lta bur bsgyur te/ skye ba mang po nas grogs su gyur pa yin la/ skye ba 'di dang 'dir yang legs pa 'di lta bu bsgrubs so// zhes skye rgyud sna
tshogs kyi gleng gzhi ston/ res 'ga' ni gtsug lag khang gi bdag po bcol te/ bdag gi

gtsug lag khang 'di'o// sngon gyi rabs ni 'di 'dra'o// phyis kyi rgyud ni 'di 'dra'o zhes gtam sna tshogs ston cing / khyod kyang bdag dang mthun par byas te 'di 'dra ba'i
bdag po bya bar rigs so zhes ston to// res 'ga' ni mkhas pa'i gzugs su bsgyur te/ gzhung lugs ni 'di 'dra'o// sngon ni 'di 'drar gyur to// phyis ni 'di 'drar 'gyur ro// khyod
kyang 'di ltar bya bar rigs so zhes ston to// res 'ga' ni grub pa ltar bcos te rdzas dang sman dang sngags ni 'di 'dra'o// 'di lta bu bsten na 'di 'drar 'gyur ro// zhes
'chad cing / res 'ga' ni bya'i gzugs se bo chen po mi'i skad du smra bar gyur te brtse brtse ltar 'bram du 'dug nas/ tho rangs kyi tshe 'dab shog rdeb pa'i sgra dang
bcas pas/ zla 'od gzhon nu/ sengge rgyan mtshan/ 'od kyi snye ma zhes 'bod cing / yar la long cig lta rtog mdzod cig thugs dam mdzod cig gzhung shod cig ces chos la bskul
ba ltar 'chos pa las/ thar bar gshed dmar

gyi dmar zhu bar brtsams pa na/ nga ni yul du 'gro bar rigs so// yab dang yum ni na bas blta bar bya'o// dbang bskur ni phyis zhu bar 'thad do zhes smra'o// phyis zhu ba dka'
bas da lta zhu'o zhes smras pas/ ngas de tsam du khyod la bsam nas khyod 'di ltar byed pa ni shin tu mi rigs/ da lta 'deng zhes smra zhing 'brang dang khres pa 'ong bsdog
par byed do// de ltar byas kyang gshegs par chas pa na/ 'brang dang khres po skas 'og tu bsgyur/ yun ring 'grogs pa'i grogs pos bslus so// da ni nga 'gro bas khyed kyis
skyel thung gyis shig ces smra ba la/ thar pa gling gi mo dben sgang khar bskyal pas/ de na 'dug pa'i rta la bzhon nas nam mkha' la 'phags te/ rta de sengge'i rnam par
bsgyur nas dpon gu ru ba ces pa'i gnas brtan gyi rnam pas/ lag pas 'gram pa bskyor te glu len cing mgo se ye re la rgan brgal nas song ngo // de nas dbyal la gshed dmar
gyi dbang zhus/ mtshan yang rnam rgyal rdo rjer btags/ de phyin chad bdud kyi bar chad kyis ma tshugs so// gzhan yang brtag gnyis nA ro

'grel chen man ngag dang bcas pa/ bde mchog gzhung phran dang bcas pa gsan/ bde mchog gi dbang zhus pa'i tshe dkyil 'khor gyi dbus nas ngo mtshar ba'i sgra thos/ shangs khrag
zags pas nad dang sdig sgrib byang te sku lus bde zhing shes rab gsal bar gyur/ sa skya paNDi ta gan byang thang du chos grwa la byon pa'i tshe mjal bas/ rigs bzang lan
po gzhon zhing shes rab che bas kun mkhyen lta bu cig bslab par bya'o zhes zhal gyis bzhes/ gzhu o rgyan du nag po pa'i dbang sgrub skor/ rnam 'joms/ a ra pa tsa na gsan/
rkyang 'dur du chos rje 'jam gsar ba'i drung du phar tshad sogs mtshan nyid phyogs kyi bka' bstan bcos du ma dang / khyad par du dus 'khor 'bro lugs kyi dbang rgyud bshad
man ngag gi bka' ma lus par mnos pas mkhas pa'i mchog tu gyur/ gshed dmar dang sgrol ma yang gsan/ chu zhing du rwa 'bum seng gi drung du dus 'khor sogs chos skor ma
lus pa gsan/ lce mdo sde seng ge la/ yo ga dang gsang 'dus/ paN chen bi bhU ti tsantra la sha wa ra'i sbyor drug khro phu

lo tsA ba la man ngag zab chos mang po/ chos rgyal 'phags pa la bde dgyes/ mA yA gur mgon rigs gter rnams gsan/ gzhan yang lcags a mo gha dang / srin po ri pa mkhan po 'jam
dang / sengge zil gnon la sogs pa bsten nas zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi phyug par gyur/ sbyor drug la thugs dam rtse gcig tu mdzad pas/ rdo rje'i tshig grub cing
mngon par shes pa thogs med du mnga'/ sras rgya gar grags pa dang slob ma gzhon nu rgyal mtshan gnyis hor dmag gi khyer ba la/ sgrol ma btson 'don gyi cho ga mdzad pas sgrol
ma'i sku nam mkha'i khyon gang ba zhig gi lte ba'i khung na byis pa gnyis po mgu rug ge 'dug pa gzigs/ zhag gsum nas sras thar la zla ba gcig nas slob mas kyang thar
ro// snar phu'i dgon pa mdzo sgang gi bu gcig po sogs lkugs phye mang po la gso brjes ming btags pas de ma thag 'gro 'dug smra brjod shes par gyur/ thar pa gling du ston
pa gzhon brtson zhes pa rma 'bras kyi snag khrag zags pas glo snying mthong ba zhig la ston pa rwa rtser ming btags nas/ ston pa gzhon brtson pa rwa rtser reng / ston pa
rwa rtses mi khar tho bsad

ces sgo gong la bris pas nad sos/ so na ba thabs kyi sar ka bsubs pas phan pa dang / glang zer na ba la sgo'i gzer phyung bas phan pa dang / rkang pa na ba la 'o dod bod cing
dbyug brdungs byas pas phan pa dang / bu tsha ma lon pa la thang ka'i gyeng la bug pa phug pas phan pa dang / smyo btul ba sogs gzhan phan mtha' yas pa mdzad/ khyad par
du dus 'khor rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa dus chos su mdzad cing / sbyor drug gi khrid bskyangs pas dus 'khor la mkhas pa'i slob ma/ sras rnams dang / man lung gu ru/ chos
rgyal 'phags pa/ khro phu rin po che bsod nams sengge/ dpyal a mo gha'i sras nyi ma dpal/ la stod pa chos ldan dang / dbus pa tshul dar/ lho pa grub seng / thang ston lo
tsA ba la sogs pa mang bo byung / bsam yas nas rgod dkar la byon pa'i tshe chom rkun mang bo byung ba la/ lta stangs dang sdigs mdzub mdzad pas rengs pa sogs grub pa'i mtshan
ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan nas/ brgyad cu chu pho rta'i lo cho 'phrul chen po'i tshes gsum la sku gshegs

so// de'i sras che ba rgya gar grags pa rab tu byung ba'i mtshan nam mkha' dpal zhes pas dus 'khor la sogs pa yab kyi yon tan rnams thugs su chud nas dben dmar gyi gdan sa
bzung / gtsug lag khang brtsigs chos kyi bya ba rgya chen po mdzad nas mya ngan las 'das so//bla ma shes rab sengge/sras gnyis pa bla ma shes rab sengge ni lcags mo phag
la 'khrungs/ yab kyi drung du dus 'khor la slob gnyer mdzad de/ dgung lo bcu dgu pa la gsungs/ nyi shu pa la thar par byon nas dpyal ba'i chos rnams zhus/ nyer gnyis pa la
stag sde seng rgyal gyi drung du byon te lo lnga'i bar du phar tshad la sbyangs/ khyad par du tshad ma la mkhas par gyur te dbus gtsang du grwa bskor yang mdzad/ sum cu
pa la chos rgyal 'phags pa dang mkhan po mchims kyi drung du rab tu byung ste bsnyen par rdzogs nas chos mang du zhus/ man lungs pa la dus 'khor gyi zab gnad mang po gsan/
lo grags pa gdan drangs nas rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang dang / 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud la sogs pa'i rgyud dang / sman dpyad yan lag brgyad pa gsan/ dben dmar gyi gdan sa bzung
nas

dus 'khor gyi bshad pa yun ring du mdzad/ gzhan yang thar pa/ khro phu/ bsam yas/ stag lung / gzhu kun dra/ shangs rtse gdong / ston mo lung / g.yus dga' ldan rnams su chos
mang po gsungs/ zhe gcig pa la dben dmar gyi gdan sa bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan pa la gtad nas/ dmu ru phyag phab ste shangs 'bar btab nas gzhan phan rgya cher mdzad/ ti
shri kun blo sogs sa skya ba'i gdung rgyud mang bo dang / gzhan yang mi che ba dang mkhas btsun gyi slob ma mang du byung zhing khyad par du lo tsA ba/ yar/ thar/ dpang
gsum/ dpal ldan sengge/ skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ dpyal Arya sogs dus 'khor la mkhas pa'i slob ma mang po byung ngo // de ltar rang gzhan gyi
don mthar phyin par mdzad nas shing mo yos kyi lo la shangs 'bar du sku gshegs so// sras gsum pa slob dpon rnal 'byor gyis yul 'khor bskyangs/a kA ra sa dhi skye med grub
pa/sras bzhi pa bla ma a kA ra sa dhi zhes pa skye med grub pa ni/ rten dge bsnyen/ yab las dus 'khor rwa 'bro'i lugs gsan pas mkhar par mkhyen/

dpyal pa dang sa skya ba'i chos skor ma lus pa mnos/ 'phar sprel du gtso bor bzhugs te sbyor drug la thugs dam rtse gcig mdzad pas grub pa brnyes te mngon par mkhyen pa mnga'
ba zhig go/rdo rje rgyal mtshan/de'i sras bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni chu mo lug la 'khrungs/ 'jam dbyangs rin rgyal ba dang / slob dpon shes rgyal la
mkhan slob zhus nas dge tshul mdzad/ bla ma shes rab sengge'i drung du/ dus 'khor sogs rong lugs kyi chos 'khor skor thams cad zhus pas bum pa gang byor mkhyen cing khyad
par dus 'khor la mchog tu mkhas par gyur/ bcu drug pa nas dben dmar gyi gdan sa bzung / dus 'khor gyi bshad grwa bskyangs/ chos lung mkhan chen dka' bzhi ba dang / bsod
grags pa la mkhan slob zhus nas bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ thar lo las tsantra pa bslabs/ rgya gar/ siM gha gling / kha che'i yi ge'i rigs thams cad mkhyen/ mngon pa dang / sbyor
drug dang sgrub thabs mang po gsan/ las slob la 'dul mdzod gsan/ mdzo bo lhas pa sangs rgyas sgom pa la sgang lo tsA ba nas brgyud pa'i rdor 'phreng gi dbang / gsang
'dus

bde mchog lam 'bras gsan/ sri'u chung ba blo ldan sengge la yo ga gsang 'dus gsang ldan gdan bzhi sogs rgyud mang po gsan/ bla ma shes rab sengge sku gshegs nas shangs 'bar
yang bzung ste dus 'khor gyi bshad yun ring po mdzad/ bzhi bcu pa la rgya nag tu byon nas rgyal blon rnams la dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang bskur/ 'gro phan rgya chen po mdzad
nas zhe gsum pa shing mo glang la zhi bar gshegs so// de la bu ston rin po ches rgyud 'grel yan lag dang bcas pa gsan to// bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan gong du thegs rjes
de dang gdung gcig pa'i bla ma rong pa bsod nams lhun 'grub kyis gdan sa gnyi ga bzung ste/ de ni bla ma shes rab sengge dang skye med grub pa dang rdo rje rgyal mtshan
rnams la rgyud 'grel yan lag dang bcas pa'i dbang bshad man ngag gi bka' legs par gsan/ mkhas shing grub pa brnyes so//rong pa dpal ldan dbang phyugde'i slob ma rong pa
dpal ldan dbang phyug grags pa ni/ bla ma 'di la sems 'grel skor cha lag dang bcas pa gsan/ bu rin po che dang / dpal ldan bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan

la yang / dbang rgyud man ngag mtha' dag gsan/ kun mkhyen chen po la sbyor drug gsan/ drang ba'i don dang nges pa'i don gnyi ga la mkhas pa/ gar dbyangs la sogs pa'i phyag
len gyis kyang gzhan gyi yid 'phrog pas/ dpal ldan bla mas ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa zhes mtshan btags/ gsang phu brag nag tu bzhugs pas brag nag par grags/ rtsis la yang
shin tu byang sngags gar sogs dkyil 'khor gyi phyag len gyi rgyun yang phyogs kun tu shin tu dar/ dbang rgyud man ngag mtha' dag gi sgo nas slob ma dus 'khor la mkhas
pa mang po thon/ rgod phrug chos rjes sbyor drug gsan dus sha wa ra dbang phyug dngos su gzigs/ dus 'khor skor gyi brtsams chos mang du mdzad/ mngon par mkhyen pa mnga'
zhing grub pa brnyes/ zhal nas kyang / gnyid tham thum log pa'i rmi lam na// byang shambha la der phyin pa rmis// rgyal po 'jam dbyangs grags pa dang mjal ba rmis// rgyud
