dus kyi 'khor lo de thos pa rmis// lho dpal gyi ri bo der phyin pa rmis// grub chen ri khrod dbang phyug dang mjal ba rmis// sbyor ba yan lag drug ldan

de zhus pa rmis// rmi lam bag chags cig yin kyang ngo mtshar che// zhes gsungs/ bsam yas su sku gshegs pa'i tshe gtsug tor mngon par 'phags pa las byang chub kyi sems dkar
po bum pa gang ba tsam lhud kyi byung zhes grag go/yar klungs pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa/de'i slob ma yar klungs pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa ni/ dge slong byang sems rdo
rje 'dzin pa chen po/ dka' chen bzhi sogs sde snod mtha' dag la legs par sbyangs/ rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son/ khyad par du dbang chen chos kyi dpal ba/ ngag dbang
grags pa/ zhang ston rgya bo gsum ga la dbang rgyud bshad man ngag mtha' dag dang / rin tshul ba la sbyor drug gsan cing grub nas/ bsam yas kyi dben gsan 'od gsal dpal
gyi bde chen du 'phrin las bskyangs pas chos rje bsam yas par grags/ de'i slob ma 'khrul zhig pa ste rong lugs so//grub chen man lung gu ru/grub chen man lung gu ru ni/
man lungs pa dran ston mtha' gral zhes pa gzhung lugs du ma la sbyangs pa mngon shes can des dran ston shes rab sengge la gsungs pa/ nub phyogs nas bud med

padma can zhig 'ong bas de rjes su zungs shig de la brten nas ma 'ongs pa'i dus su sems can gyi don rgya chen po 'grub pa yin/ zhes dang / tshe gzhug rgya gar du skyel snying
'dod// 'khyol na 'khor 'dab ci dga' gyis// zhes dang / po ta la'i lam yig khro phu lo tsA ba'i phyag nas byung ba de ma 'ongs pa na kho bo la dgos pas dpe sgam du sbos
shig ces gsungs nas/ yab dran ston shes rab sengge dang / yum ma cig padma rin chen zhes pa lung bstan pa'i mtshan nyid tshang ba de'i sras su dran ston mtha' bral nyid
sku skye ba bzhes te/ rong yung gi stag lung dgon par sa mo phag gi lo la sa g.yo ba dang bcas te sku bltams/ yab kyi shes rab bskyed pa'i cho ga dang dbang gi smin par byas
te/ mtshan mar me mdzod du btags/ lo dgu nas yab gshegs te/ gye re nas lha rin chen rgyal po gdan drangs/ lug lo dpyid tha'i tshes drug gi nyin snga dro yab kyi gshegs
rdzongs byas/ phyi dro lha sa'i drung du mkhan po gam nyag pa bkra shis sengge / slob dpon rin chen rgyal mtshan

las rab tu byung / mtshan bsod nams dpal du btags/ lha sa'i phyag phyir gye rer byon nas lha de nyid dang / 'bri gung gcung dang / slob dpon mkhas pa las/ gnyos lugs dang 'bri
khung pa'i chos ma lus par gsan/ de nas lha rin po ches lam lungs pa'i gdan sar bskos/ dkar lung pa dpal bzang po la dran ston chen po'i zhal gdams sogs man lungs pa'i
yab chos thams cad dang / gnyan ras la karma pa'i chos skor gsan/ da lta bde mchog su mkhas dris pas/ dbu na dkon yon dang / gtsang na dran ston jo dbang mkhas zer bas/
de gnyis ga la bde mchog gsan pas/ stod 'grel gyi rdzogs rim kyi bshad pa la thugs ma tshim ste/ 'di'i don su mkhas dris pas/ rong dben dmar na rje btsun rgwa lo mkhas zer
bas der byon nas dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud 'grel cha lag dang bcas pa dang / rgyud sde mang po'i dbang rjes gnang / rgyud 'grel sgrub thabs/ byams pa'i chos lnga / spyod
'jug 'jam gsar

ba'i phar tshad la sogs pa mang du gsan cing / khyad par du sbyor drug 'chi med kyi rtsa ba lag len dang bcas pa zab lam gyi gnad ma lus pa gsan pas thugs legs par tshim/ snye
mor skyes pa don grub la dgyes rdor gsan/ bla ma thams cad mnyes pa gsum gyis mnyes par mdzad/ mdo rgyud bstan bcos mtha' dag la mkhas shing / rgyud kyi nges don la mchog
tu mkhas par gyur te/ man lungs su dus 'khor gtso bor bsam gtan pa'i 'dus pa dang byams pa'i chos lnga sogs gzhung chen mo rnams dge 'dun mang po la gsungs/ bod byon
dus mi bde bas thugs phyung ste phag ri rin chen sgang du byon/ lha rin chen rgyal po la man lung phul nas sgrub pa byed par zhus pas bla mas shol btab kyang rlung sems
las su rung dgos par 'dug gsungs nas sdings bo cher lo bzhi dang zla ba phyed dang brgyad ltos med bzhis sbyor drug la/ thugs dam rtse gcig tu mdzad pas rdo rje'i tshig grub
ste/ rgyal khams than pas bsregs pa na/ char phob cig gsungs ma thag char chen po bab pa dang / gangs la me sbar ba dang / a ru ra rlon pa 'phral la phyag du 'byung ba
mdzad/ de nas tshe gcig

la byang chub sgrub par rgya gar du 'byon par thugs thag bcad nas/ lam gyi bar chod bzlog pa'i ched du zhi ba'i sbyin bsreg mang po mdzad/ nyer drug pa me byi la lugs smad
lcang gsar ba byang chub dpal/ rong g.yung gi mdo mkhar ba rin bsod/ la stod pa 'od zer snying bo/ myang stod pa bsod nams mgon sogs phyag phyir khrid nas rgya gar la byon
pas tshol mis sa skyar zin nas ldog par zhus kyang ma gnang bar skyi rong du 'phags pa wa ti'i drung du byon/ 'phags pa'i dbu nas me tog gi phreng ba 'phar te nyid kyi
dbu la phog zhabs la gser gyi me tog gi tsher ma zug ste khrag mang po zags pas nga'i sgrib pa rags pa zad pa yin gsungs/ bong tsog khab kyi rgyal po yang dag pa'i lam la
bkod/ de nas bal bor phebs te ye rang du gnas po a ma ra tsinta la babs/ 'phags pa shing kun tu byon pa'i tshe spre'u rnams kyis su shing me tog phul/ der mchod pa mdzad
pas sa g.yos/ 'jam lir byon pas mar me rang 'bar/ bhuggaM du byon pas 'phags pa gom pa gang tsam nur te bsus/ hUM ka ra'i lha khang du byon pa

na nam mkha' la hUM gi sgra che la yun ring ba cig byung bas drung na gnas pa thams cad rnam par mi rtog pa'i ting nge 'dzin la yun ring du gnas pa byung / de dus ti ra hU
ti ba dang tu rukSha 'khrugs nas lam mi bde bas ya tse la byon/ rgyal po a sog ldes bla mar bkur/ der 'dzal ba nam yes sku tshab la bzhag nas rdo rje gdan du byon/ byang
chub chen po la mchod cing sgrub pa mdzad/ bdud 'jom pa'i lha khang bsos/ de'i dus su dus 'khor bsdus rgyud mtshan brjod sems 'grel gsum la don khyad par can gsar du rtogs/
de dang mthun pa'i yi ge rnams kyang mdzad/ slar yang yos lo la bal bor phebs/ bong tsog pa'i sa'i cha dben gnas lcam pa skor du thugs dam mdzad/ de dus rgwa lo'i sras
nam mkha' dpal sogs dpon g.yog sum cu tsam gyis gdan dran la skyi rong du sleb/ rgan po rnams nyen 'gro bas nged skyi rong du 'gro gsung nas byon/ de rnams kyis zhu ba zhu
rten dang bcas pa phul bas lo gcig gi khongs su phebs par zhal gyis bzhes/ bka' shog mdzad nas man lungs kyi gdan slob dpon bsod nams rgyal

mtshan bskos/ de nas lcags pho 'brug la phug rdzong dang dkar lung du byon te bla ma dpal bzang po mjal/ man lungs dang sdings po cher yang byon/ lha sar byon nas mchod pa
mdzad/ de dus lam du tshur phu'i dkon gnyer cig gis gzhan la bskor nas bsnyen bkur lan brgyad zhus kyang thugs mkhyen gyi ma gsol/ lha rin chen rgyal po dang rje btsun rgwa
lo sogs bla ma rnams mjal/ de nas phug rdzong du lo ngo gsum bzhugs nas thugs dam mdzad/ de dus man lung pa rnams kyi chos skal byed pa yin gsung nas/ rgyud 'grel gyi
bshad pa dang sbyor drug gi khrid mang po gnang / zhe bzhi pa chu pho rta la rje btsun rgwa lo gshegs pas kyang thugs bskur te/ khyed rnams mtshan brjod mang du thon/ su
shi snga ba nga dang 'phrad pa snga ba yin yan par mi 'gro zhes dang / nga don chen po sgrub dgos par yod gsungs nas/ ya tser byon te rgyal po a sog lde dang / de'i mchod
gnas paNDi ta ratna kakShi ta la chos mang du gsan/ rong snar pa byang yes

sku tshab tu bzhag nas/ byang chub dpal/ rin bsod/ stag tshal lo tsA ba grags pa byang chub/ 'od zer snying po/ dpal le rnams phyag phyir khrid nas rdo rje gdan du byon/ mchod
pa dang sgrub pa la nan tan du mdzad/ nga 'dir sdod khyed rang rnams byang chub gling gi ri'i rgyab tu lo bcu gnyis bsgoms gsung / bla ma dang nam mjal zhus pas/ dpyid
'bring nag pa'i nya/ 'di dus khyad par can yin pas mchod pa bshoms la gsol ba thob/ dag pa'i dbyings su nges par phrad 'ong gsung / bla ma gcig po der bzhugs/ gzhan rnams
tshad pa ma thub nas tshur la 'ongs/ de'i phyi lo spre'u'i lo la/ yar klungs lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan/ stag tshal lo tsA ba grags pa byang chub/ zhang bsod nams
dar sogs mi dgus rdo rje gdan du byon/ zab lam gyi khrid cha lag dang bcas pa zhus/ bod la 'byon par zhus pas/ da shrI dhA nya ka Ta ka ra 'gro ba yin gsungs nas ma gnang
/ bya lo'i dgun tshun bzhugs par zhus nas khong rnams bod la byon/ zhang der gum/

gzhan rnams kyis slob dpon byang chub dpon dpal la lan rnams sprad/ khong gis slob dpon rin bsod man lungs su btang / man lungs pa rnams kyis gser srang nyi shu rtsa bdun rin
bsod la bskur nas brdzangs/ byang chub dpal ba slob dpon dang bcas pas rgya gar du byon/ de'i bar la grub chen nyid kyis byang chub chen po'i drung du thugs dam la rtse
gcig tu bzhugs shing khyad par zhag bcu bdun gyi bar du sa sde btsugs te/ 'bras nyag ma gcig dang / btung ba thigs pa gcig yang ma gsol bar bdag la lung ston na legs/ mi
ston na 'chi ba'i dus byed kyang bla'o zhes dam bca' brtan po mdzad/ zhag bco lnga na ma ga dha'i paNDi ta mu kha ti mai tri dang / gnas po ra ma sogs kyis dbu la chu blug
pa tshor ba tsam byung / zhag bcu bdun na byang chub chen po'i zhal nas/ po ta la na spyan ras gzigs 'khor byang sems mang po la theg pa chen po'i chos sgra rgyun chad
med par sgrog pa'i drung du tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod du song cig ces lung bstan

don du ni sor bsam gyis rlung dbu mar zhugs pa'i mthus lung bstan thob ste/ ma ga dha'i rgyal po buddha se na dang / paNDi ta mu kha ti mai tri sogs mang pos shol btab kyang
ma thebs par/ bka' shog cig bzhag ste/ paNDi ta mu kha ti mai tra'i dpon po gau ta ma bha tra dang / rgya gar shar phyogs tsandra DI pa zhes pa zla ba'i gling gi btsun
pa dze tA ri bha dra gnyis phyag phyir khrid nas shing mo bya'i lo'i smin drug gi zla ba'i tshes brgyad lho phyogs su gshegs so// der bla ma byang chub dpal la sogs pa rnams
kyis zla ba de'i nyer drug la rdo rje gdan du slebs/ bka' shog gi lugs bzhin gser rnams la rdo rje gdan du mchod pa rgyas pa mdzad/ byang chub dpal ba dang / lo tsA ba
grags pa byang chub sogs kyis bka' bzhin bal bod mtshams kyi byang chub gling gi ri la thar pa gling zhes pa'i dgon pa btab nas lo bcu gnyis 'dag 'byar la bzhugs nas thugs
dam mdzad pas grub pa brnyes/ byang chub gling pa zhes grags te grub thob kyi bu slob mang du thon to/ 'od zer snying po ni dben gnas lcam pa bskor du bzhugs te grub
pa brnyes so// grub chen dpon slob gsum gyis ri bya rkang dang / dzambU'i gling

gi gnas chen po bzhi dang brgyad dang bcu gnyis sogs gzigs nas/ dpal 'bras spungs kyi mchod rten chen por bzhugs te phyag mchod bskor ba dang bsgrub pa la nan tan du mdzad
pas/skye ba'i las zad pa'i rtags su zhabs las khrag mang po zags/ de chad pa dang da nga la 'chi ba mi 'ong gsungs/ bza' btung bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsol yang zag pa mi 'dzag
gcig kyang ma gsol yang mi bkres/ stag la sogs pa'i gdug pa can rnams kyis gus 'dud byed/ tshad pa la sogs pa'i nad kyis mi rdzi/ sku la grib ma med/ gzhan gyi dbugs
phyi nang du rgyu ba mi tshor/ chu la mi 'bying / sku lus yang bas nam mkha' la yang thegs/ grub pa thob pa'i snyan pas sa thams cad du khyab/ paNDi ta bi ma la shrIs chos
'byung rab gzigs zhes pa la sogs pa'i bstod pa mdzad/ de'i tshe gau ta ma bha dra la khyod bod du song la sher phyin stong phrag brgya ba'i lung long / bod kyi dpe las
rgya dper bsgyur/ dza ya pu rir dge 'dun gyi sde tshugs des kyang bka' bzhin sa pho byi ba lo la man lungs su phebs/ man

lungs pa dang / sa skya pa rnams kyis brdzangs pa'i gser gyis rten so byas nas/ rgyal po'i khab kyi dza ya pu rir theg pa chen po'i dge 'dun gyi sde btsugs/ rab tu byung ba
sum cu rtsa gsum re bzhugs te/ ma ga dhar chos tshugs bzang shos su grags so// grub chen nyid dze tA ri bha dra dang lhan cig 'bras spungs nas lho phyogs su bimba kA ya
zhes pa reg pa med pa'i gdugs can du grags pa der byon/ de nas kyang lho ra dznyA na kA ya zhes pa rten chu nang du bzhugs pa de'i gnas su byon/ slar yang 'bras spungs kyi
mchod rten du byon te/ paNDi ta su tsa ri bha dra sogs skal ba dang ldan pa mang po la/ dus 'khor gsang 'dus bde dgyes la sogs pa'i dbang bskur rgyud bshad/ zab lam gyi
khrid mang du gnang ste/ rgya gar lho phyogs su slob ma grub thob mang du byung zhing rdo rje theg pa dar bar mdzad do// de'i tshe sa ma brtan gyi bde ba gyen du kha bltas
te/ rnam smin gyi lus ma bor bar mi 'gyur ba'i bde bas rig pa 'dzin pa'i sku brnyes/ sa thob 'jigs pa lnga dang bral zhes pa'i yon tan thams cad rdzogs/

byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rlabs po ches rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs pa 'gyed/ dze tA ri bha dra la khyod dzambU'i gling gi gnas chen po bzhi dang brgyad du grags pa rnams ltos
la rgya nag ri bo rtse lnga la song / sngon gyi 'brel bas 'jam dpal gyis rjes su 'dzin par 'dug kho bo ni rje btsun spyan ras gzigs kyi drung du tshangs pa mtshungs par
spyod du 'gro gsungs nas po ta lar gshegs so// de tshun ni je tA ri la sogs pa phal cher gyis mthong la/ phan chad ni so sos skye bo dang 'grogs pa'i skal ba mi mnyam
pas blo'i yul las 'das te 'phags pa rnams kyi spyad yul kho na'o// dze tA ris bka' bzhin ston pa bltams pa'i sa lumbi nI la sogs pa gnas rnams bskor nas lo re lnga lon pa
gcig sa mo phag gi lo la bod du byon/ thar los sngar gyi lo rgyus rnams bsgyur/ man lungs su zla ba gnyis bzhugs/ de nas ri bo rtse lnga la thegs nas lo shas cig de nas
bzhugs pa der gnas pa rnams kyis mthong la mthar ye shes kyi sku grub bo//slob dpon bsod nams mgon/slob dpon bsod nams mgon ni/ sbyor drug bsgoms pas tshad pas mi rdzi bar
gyur nas rgya gar du byon

te/ rdo rje'i gdan du mchod pa phul/ de nas dpal ldan 'bras spungs su byon/ de nas kyang grub chen la gtad de lho phyogs la gshegs so// yar klungs lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal
mtshan ni/ chu pho stag la gser ba sar 'khrungs/ rgya gar du thegs te/ kIrti tsantra sogs paN grub du ma bsten nas rgyud sde mang du gsan/ man lungs pa la dus kyi 'khor lo'i
dbang rgyud man ngag mtha' dag mnos/ spyir lho bal du lo sum cu bzhugs/ bod du phebs nas sa skyar 'jam dbyangs bzhi thog pa/ bcom ldan rig ral/ rong pa sher seng rnams
kyis yon sbyar nas 'gyur mang bo mdzad de/ skad gnyis gzhung lugs nyi shu drug/ bod skad rkyang pa sum cu gnyis/ mngon (sngon )chad ma bsgyur nyi shu bzhi// bsdoms na lnga
bcu rtsa brgyad do// zhes pa ltar ro// rdo rje phreng ba sogs kyi dbang mang po mdzad/ phyis yar klungs su g.ya' bzang pa dang / jo bo grags pa rin chen sogs kyis btegs
nas gser thang brag khar bzhugs te/ dus 'khor gtso bor gsungs pas/ dus 'khor ba bsod she sogs rab tu byung ba'i

dpe 'grems brgya lhag re 'dus/ 'gro phan dang sku shin tu che/ mngon par shes pa thogs med du mnga'/ dgung lo brgya dang lnga bzhugs te gshegs so// grub chen man lungs pa nyid
kyis rong ba sher seng / des kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ des bu ston rin po che la/ dbang mdor bstan dang / man lungs pa'i sbyor drug phran dang bcas pa gnang ngo // yang
lo grags pa/ bla ma grub pa dpal bzang po/ yon tan rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen chen po rnams las brgyud de man lungs pa nas brgyud pa'i rgyud 'grel gyi bshad bka' dang / sbyor
drug gi man ngag dang lo grags pa'i 'gyur gyi rgyud 'grel dang / lo grags pas paNDi ta mang po la gsan pa'i gtam rgyud/ zhal gdams rnams kyang byung ngo // yang lo grags
pa/ 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan/ ri ston blo chen 'od/ sangs rin pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa 'gos lo tsA ba rnams brgyud de rgyud 'grel man ngag dang bcas pa byung ngo //chos rgyal
'phags pa/chos rgyal 'phags pa ni/ rgya yul nas yar phebs dus ngur mig tu

rje btsun rgwa lo gdan drangs nas dbang rgyud bshad man ngag rnams gsan te dus 'khor la mkhas pas bstan pa'i bdag por gyur to//bu ston rin chen grub/gangs can 'dir thub pa'i
bstan pa yongs rdzogs pa'i mnga' bdag thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che ni/ yab brag ston rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes pa gdung rabs bcu bdun du sngags rnying ma'i
grub thob zam ma chad pa'i mkhas grub zhig dang / yum slob dpon ma bsod nams 'bum zhes pa gsang sngags rnying ma'i chos la mnga' brnyes pa zhig gi sras su lcags pho stag
la shab smad sgom gnas su sku bltams/ kha che paNDi ta shAkya shrI'i sku skyer grags/ 'jam dpal bsgrubs pas zhal gzigs/ dus phyis kyang gzigs rtog ma grub par chos gsung
ba'i tshe/ yon tan ye shes bzang po'i bstod sgrub/ re sngon du btang na tshig don thams cad gsal lam mer thugs la 'char/ dgung lo lnga drug nas yum gyis klog slob par
brtsams pa na 'da' ka ye shes dang sa'i snying po 'khor lo bcu pa la sbyar klog mdzad pas klog mkhyen pa dang thugs la zin pa mnyam du byung / mos bla chen tshul khrims
dpal bzang po'i phyag dpe gzigs pas 'di bstan bcos

rnam dag go/ 'di ni min no zhes so sor phye bas mes po'ang shin tu dgyes/ yig rtsis bslabs pas slob dpon las mkhas par 'gyur/ bdun pa la khro phu rin po che'i drung du sems
bskyed zhus pas bdag pas gzhan gces kyi thugs bcos min du 'khrungs/ brgyad pa la khro phu rje de'i drung du bde mchog dril bu ba'i dbang zhus dus 'di'i dbu la phyag bzhag
nas 'o 'di la nga'i ngal gso sa byed pa lags so gsungs/ khro phu ba'i zab chos rnams kyang gnang / mes po'i drung du gsang sngags rnying ma mang du gsan/ bzo sman mkhyud
dpyad mkhas par mkhyen/ bco brgyad pa la lo tsho'i mkhan rgyud mkhan po rin chen sengge dang / slob dpon tshad ma'i skyes bu bsod nams mgon las rab tu byung ste mtshan
rin chen grub tu btags/ slob dpon de'i drung du phar phyin gyi slob gnyer la zhugs te 'di'i phyogs su shi na'ang shi snyam du dgongs te/ nyin mtshan du gsol dang mnal gyi
long med par gsan sbyang la 'bad pas sku seng seng por song ste kun gyis snying rje'i gnas su byed/ gzhung TI ka nag 'byams thugs su chub cing / nyi snang / brgya stong
'grel chen

byams pa dang 'brel ba'i chos sde nyi shu la mkhas par gyur nas/ khro phur bshad gsar mdzad de sde snod 'dzin pa rnams rigs pas zil gyis mnan/ bod na ka ba mi 'grems pa cig
la shes rab che bar grags/ de nas mdo rtsa dang me tog phreng rgyud gsan cing gtso bor rnam nges la sbyangs pas sde bdun mdo dang bcas pa tshegs med du mkhyen/ de nas mngon
pa kun las btus la sbyangs te/ snga dro gzhung mda' tshad shog bu bdun dang TI kA shog bu lnga thugs su 'dzin pa dang / phyi dro bshad pa rtsal bshad du gsan pas zla
ba gcig la mkhas pa'i phul du phyin/ spyod 'jug dang rigs tshogs sogs dbu ma'i skor rnams kyang gsan yang rtse ba rin chen sengge la bde mchog sogs sngags chos mang po gsan/
nyer gcig pa la yab dang lhan cig dbus gtsang gi chos sde phal che bar grwa bskor la byon/ dbus nas shAka gzhon/ btsan dgon pa ba/ kha rag byang gzhon/ gtsang nas dpal
ldan sengge/ 'jam skya sogs lung rigs kyis btul bas pha ston bu ston du grags shing khyad par du rje 'di grub mtha' rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son pas mkhas pa'i grags pas

sa thams cad du khyab/ de nas rnam snang ba yon tan rgya mtsho la spyod yul/ don grub dpal la brtag gnyis/ yab la phyag rdor/ grang bo lung ba la don zhags/ 'jam skya nam mkha'
dpal la rnam 'grel gsan/ de nas khro phur 'chad nyan mdzad de phar tshad mngon sum la bshad pa'i rkang btsugs/ nyer gsum pa la tshong 'dus 'gur mo'i bla brang du/ dka'
bzhi ba grags pa gzhon nu/ byang sems bsod nams grags/ bsod nams bzang po ste chos lung mkhan po gsum gyis mkhan slob mdzad/ dad pa'i dge 'dun nyer gnyis kyi dbus su bsnyen
par rdzogs/ mkhan slob la mdo rtsa/ so thar gyi mdo/ karma sha taM/ blo sbyong rnams gsan/ de nas thar pa gling du thar lo'i drung du zla ba bcu bar ma chad dang lar
lo bzhi bzhugs nas/ ka tsan gyi mdo byings nye bsgyur u Na dang / a ma ra ko Sha rnams saM skri ta'i skad du thugs 'dzin mdzad nas/ de rnams 'grel pa dang bcas pa la legs
par sbyangs/ rgya gar shar nub/ kha che/ singgha la/ sindhu/ rgya mtsho mtha' la sogs pa'i yi

ge rigs mang po mkhyen/ lo tsA byang bar gyur/ de nas gser gyi maNDal phul nas zab lam gyi khrid zhus pas/ chos 'di'i bdag po khyed rang yin pas bgyi'o gsungs nas/ dpe med
mtsho dang sha wa ri'i gdams pa gnang ste/ 'dag sbyar bug sgo can du bzhugs pa na/ rtsa rlung thig lei'i gnas tshul mngon sum du gzigs/ gzung 'dzin dbyings su dag nas ye
shes chen po'i rtsal rdzogs/ rin chen snang ba dang rin chen sgron ma sogs ting nge 'dzin sgo du ma mngon du gyur te/ nyams rtogs mngon par shes pa thogs pa med pa 'khrungs/
bla ma la sangs rgyas dngos kyi 'du shes las tha mal du nam yang ma mthong gsung / dbang mdor bstan/ rgyud phyi ma/ sems 'grel gnyis/ don dam bsnyen pa/ nA ro pa/ a bha
ya/ brtson 'grus dpal gyi sbyor drug dbang rab byed kyi 'grel pa/ snying po rgyan/ sA dhu pu tra'i sgrub dkyil/ nyi zla sgrub pa/ ye shes spyan sgrub/ sbas pa mig 'byed/
thar lo nyid kyis mdzad pa'i sbyor drug gi skor sogs mang du gsan/

de nas dpal ldan sengge'i drung du/ rwa 'bro'i dgongs pa gcig tu dril ba las/ khyad par phyag len rwa lugs gtso bor bton pa'i dbang zhus pa'i tshe/ bla ma rdo rje shugs dngos
su gzigs/ gzhan yang bde dgyes sgyu thod rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang sogs gsan/ de nas rong dben dmar du bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan pa'i drung du byon/ zla ba dgu bar ma
chad par bsten nas/ dus 'khor rgyud 'grel rwa 'bro'i bzhed tshul so sor phye ba'i rgyud bshad mdzub khrid tshar gnyis cha lag dang bcas pa gsan te tshig don gnyis la mkhas
par gyur/ bla mas kyang 'o chos bdag po la 'phrod da blo bde'o gsungs/ dus phyis kyang dus 'khor kho na la thugs rtsis che zhing / gsung ba'i dus na'ang 'di dpal dus
kyi 'khor lo bya ba gzhan gyi rgyud 'grel pas 'di'i dkyil chog dka'/ rgyud gzhan gyi dkyil chog pas 'di'i bsrung 'khor yang tshan che/ 'di 'dra ba'i chos slob pa la 'o yangs
zhor sham la shes pa mi 'chi/ 'dir byon cig gsung nas sa ris la sogs pa rnams dpon slob chos khri'i kha ru bsgrigs nas mdzad/ brjed

tho'i dpe chung dang 'khrul 'khor gyi gnad la sogs pa rnams rgyud 'grel dang btun gyin phyag len mdzad/ 'o skol sngags pa kun la phra mo'i lag len tshun chad la dri gtug byed
pa cig rang ma byung na/ oM sob sob re'i dge bshes la gsha' ma mi 'chi/ des na 'di lta bu'i rgyud la slob gnyer byed na/ khol thon du dka' dka' la nan tan chen po 'tshal/
ma bde ba byung na dris shig chos zab la rgya che ba sangs rgyas rnams kyis gsungs/ sdud byed rnams kyis bsdus/ paN grub rnams kyis bsgyur/ mkhas pa rnams kyis gtan la
phab/ bshad pa'i srol ma chag dbang gi chu bo ma nub/ lhad ma zhugs/ 'dres ma khyer/ dam ma nyams/ bka' rgyud grub thob kyi zam ma chad/ byin brlabs kyi na bun ma yal/
mdo rgyud 'grel ba zab mo rnams kyi lde mig sangs rgyas sras bcas thams cad kyi spyi lam 'di lta bu'i chos bshad nyan byar yod pa tshogs bsags pa yin pas da chud ma gsan/
rang gzhan gyi don rgya chen po mdzod ces nan tan chen po'i sgo nas gsung zhing / dka' ba'i gnad rnams la dri ba zhus pa la shin tu dgyes/ dzA landha ri pa'i dngos slob
bi bhU ti dA la

la gtum mo dang gegs gsel dang / bar phug rong ba gzhon nu grub la bka' gdams pa'i lugs mang po gsan/ so gcig pa la sku zhang grags pa rgyal mtshan pas gdan drangs/ zhwa lu
gser khang gi gtsug lag khang du phyag phab nas dka' chen bzhi la bshad pa'i rkang mdzad nas 'chad nyan gyi grwa btsugs pa na/ grwa pa 'ga' zhig gis chags sdang gi rnam
'gyur mi bzad pa bstan pa zhi ba'i ched du dbu mdzad bkra shis bzang po la phar phyin gsan/ 'on kyang da dung ma bzlogs par spyan la rde'u 'phen pa sogs byas pas/ rang la
mi phan gzhan la gnod pa yi// bdag gi 'chad nyan 'di 'dras ci bgyi lags// za 'dug 'gro 'chag la sogs ci byas kyang // gzhan gyi khong khro'i rgyu ru 'gyur la skyo// da ni
tshe yang ring du mi gnas shing // nang gi dbang po yongs su mi gsal la// skye 'chi'i sdug bsngal shin tu bzod par dka'// cung zad shes pa nyams len dus la bab// gsungs
nas re shig thugs las chung ngu la gzhol pa na/ sku zhang chen po tab tab sogs

gyur nas ma rungs pa rnams srog gi chad pa la gtugs pa na/ de rnams kyang 'gyod pas nongs pa chags shing rje 'di kho na skyabs su bsten te mgrin gcig tu gsol ba btab pas/ de
rnams kyi 'jigs skyob dang bstan pa la dgongs nas slar yang chos kyi 'khor lo zla med pa bskor/ de dus grub thob ze dmar ba la bde mchog gsan/ de nas sngon jo bo rjes byin
gyis brlabs pa'i bsti gnas/ de'i mchod rten yang bzhugs pa'i zhwa lu ri phug tu gtsug lag khang dge 'dun gyi sde dang bcas pa bzhengs/ sngar rong pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan
la dus 'khor gsan pa'i dus su gsang 'dus shes pa zhig byung na slob zhus pas/ nged kyi mched grogs slob dpon 'phags pa bya ba 'phags yog dus gsum la mkhas pa zhig ma
dag phyogs na yong gsungs ste rtsad bcad pas/ phyis skyi mkhar na bzhugs pa gsan nas gdan 'dren btang ba na/ mnal lam du bud med gcig gis bum pa chu'i cung ma gang ba gcig
dang / rnal 'byor ba gcig gi rdo rje dril bu gcig khyer byung nas/ 'di pa sngar khyed rang gi yin pa na ning nas brag ram na yar la 'phyin da khyed rang la gtod pa yin
zer nas

gtod du byung ba rmis/ thugs dgyes tshor dang bcas pas kun mkhyen 'phags 'od zhwa lu ri phug tu gdan drangs pas/ khyed la rgya ba'i rgya lugs dang gar ba'i gar lugs sogs nas
dgos pa de min/ 'gag 'dra bshad/ gzhan shar rtse bklags nas thob che ba gcig bgyi'o gsungs/ bshad pa rdo rus thug pa cig zhu zhus pas/ a ba snying nas rang slob na sngon
la rim lnga'i dmar khrid bgyi gsung nas dbang dang khrid gnang / de'i tshe sangs rgyas byang sems mang po ting nge 'dzin gyi rtsed mo sna tshogs mdzad pa dang / bskyed
rim kyi dus su lha so gnyis kyi zhal gzigs/ rdor bzlas kyi dus su rtags lnga dang rlung lnga so sor gsal ba gzigs/ sku lus 'ja' 'od du gyur pa la lha so gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor
du gzigs/ mnal 'od gsal du zin/ u rgyan du byon nas ye shes mkha' 'gro ma dang mjal/ mngon dgar byon nas rin po che'i zhal med khang na sangs rgyas stong gral bsgrigs
su bzhugs pa gzigs/ zhing khams dag pa blta na nyi zla la zhon pa'am 'od zer la 'jug pa'am/ mkha' lding la zhon pa sogs byas nas gang 'gro 'dod

pa'i yul du bslebs pa snyam byas na mthong gi 'dug gsungs/ mtshan mo mnal lam du gsung rabs gang bzhed la gzigs rtog mdzad nas sang de tshogs su gsungs/ de nas gsang 'dus 'phags
skor/ ye shes zhabs lugs/ dus 'khor rwa 'bro'i dbang rgyud bshad man ngag gi bka'/ nA ro pa/ jo bo rje/ shAkya shrI/ sha ba ri/ dpyal a mo gha/ gyi jo/ tsa mi/ rgwa
lo/ zhang tshal pa/ sreg pa lung pa/ mar pa bya ze rnams kyi sbyor drug o rgyan bsnyen sgrub sogs sbyor drug rigs mi 'dra ba mang po/ bde dgyes/ gshin rje gshed/ sgyu dra/
gdan gzhi/ mA yA/ grub snying / yo ga bya spyod phal mo che'i dbang bshad man ngag gi bka' thams cad do// bla ma 'di la rdo rje 'chang gi 'du shes las skad cig kyang mi
g.yel/ bla mas kyang chos re re gsung pa'i sham du chos bdag po la 'phrod do gsungs/ spyir bla ma nyi shu rtsa brgyad mnga'/ mang du thos pa rgya mtsho'i mthar son nas/
dbyar dgun gyi dus chos la/ dka' chen bzhi spyod 'jug 'phags yog dus gsum zhes pa'i tha snyad mdzad nas ston dpyid dus 'khor

dang gsang 'dus rgyud 'grel/ rdo rje 'byung ba/ sam pu Ti rnams rgyun du gtso bor gsungs/ gzhan mdo rgyud kyi bshad lung dbang man ngag dag thug pa med par zhar chos su gsung
/ bstan bcos mang du mdzad pa las dus 'khor gyi skor la/ rgyud 'grel gyi mchan/ sa bcad/ chos 'byung / mkhas pa dga' byed/ lag len gyi rtsis/ myur rtsis kyi lhan thabs/
sgra rig mkhas rgyan/ mdor bsdus dang po'i TI kA nges don snye ma/ lhan skyes dang / thugs dkyil dang / yongs rdzogs kyi sgrub thabs/ bstod pa/ dkyil chog de'i lhan thabs/
mchod gar/ sngags gar/ stangs stabs bdun pa/ rgyud mchod/ brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ rab gnas/ dus tha ma'i cho ga mchod phreng / go la'i rnam gzhag zhi ba dang las bzhi'i
sbyin bsreg thig rtsa khor yug gi lha 'god tshul/ dbang mdor bstan gyi TI kA/ khrid yig ngo sprod/ 'gal spong rnams mdzad/ sa skya pa don yod rgyal mtshan sku mched kyis
brtag gnyis la TI kA mdzad

par bskul ba na/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan dang lan gnyis mjal/ rje btsun gyi zhal nas 'di'i 'grel pa byed pa de legs/ spyir bka' bstan bcos rnams dang / khyad par gsang
sngags kyi bstan bcos la zhus dag dang yang sgos su de'i bstan bcos la/ nga rang gi zhus dag cig bya snyam na'ang ma grub/ da nyid kyis zhus dag gyis shig ces lung bstan
pas/ ga re bla ma rje btsun chen po dang mjal/ sa skya pa'i chos rnams dang khyad par brtag gnyis la nga bas rgyud thag nye ba deng sang med snyam du dgongs/ 'grel pa
bya bar lung bstan gong ma'i yig cha rnams la dgag sgrub bya bar bkas gnang yang btang snyoms su bzhag nas lung 'grel mdzad/ sku zhang chen po'i rjes su sras kun dga' don
grub gyis sbyin bdag byas nas/ zha lur rnal 'byor rgyud kyi gzhal yas khang du lha 'bum mdzad de dkyil 'khor lnga brgya lhag logs bris su bris/ bstan 'gyur bzhengs te dkar
chag mdzad/ dbon chen rgyal ba bzang pos shangs su gdan drangs te/ mchod rten dang lugs ma'i rten mang po'i zhal bskos/ spyod rgyud kyi dkyil 'khor bzhi bzhi bcu lhag

bya rgyud kyi dkyil 'khor sum cu lhag gi lha 'bum mdzad nas ri mor bris/ ri phug tu dus 'khor gyi sku rin po che las grub pa sogs sku mang po dang bka' 'gyur dang / bod kyi
bstan bcos kyang phal mo che bzhengs/ rgya gar/ rgya nag bal po/ hor/ yu gur/ sog po/ 'ga'/ dbus gtsang mnga' ris khams kyi slob ma grangs med pa smin grol du mdzad/ 'jam
dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan sku mched/ bsod nams blo gros sku mched/ chos lung mkhan chen bsod nams grags/ gu shrI chos grags dpal bzang po/ lo tsA ba blo gros dpal sogs
mkhas btsun gyi slob ma mang du 'dus/ dka' chen bzhi/ dbu spyod rnams kyi tshig don la mkhas pa'i ston pa dang / 'phags yog dus gsum/ gur brtag sam gsum/ lo nag dril gsum/
sgyu thod gdan gsum/ dmar nag 'jig gsum sogs la mkhas pa'i phyi nang gi rdo rje slob dpon pher ba dang / bskyed rdzogs la brtan pa thob pa'i rnal 'byor pa dang / ku
sa li la sogs pa'i slob ma grangs kyis mi lang pa

thon/ zhwa ltar tshogs pa sum stong brgyad brgya/ ri phug tu sde snod 'dzin pa sha dag dang / 'dag sbyar bug sgo can la bzhugs pa'i dge 'dun lnga brgya lhag re 'dus/ stag tshal/
'or mo/ tsha mig bre/ 'bras yul/ shangs/ dben dmar la sogs par skye bo khri khrag mang po la sems bskyed gnang / rgya gar gyi rgyal po puNya mal gyis 'phrin yig skyes
dang bcas nas phul/ chos zab mo'i skyes lan gnang bas gus par 'dzin/ rgya nag nas rgyal po tho gan thii mur gan gyis gdan 'dren gyi gser yig pa btang ba dben par bzhugs
pa'i thugs dam gyis bzlog gshed dmar gyi rgyud sogs gsung rabs mang po zhu chen mdzad de gzhi gnas bsgyur/ 'gyur chos dang hor khong bsab pa mang pos bstan pa'i srog shing
mdzad/ re gnyis pa la g.ya' phag gnyis kyi 'khrug sdums la dbus su byon pa'i lam du myang stod chu mig ra lung sogs su chos mang du gsungs/ rtsis kyi mkhan po nam mkha'
rin chen sogs dge slong dge tshul mang po'i mkhan slob mdzad/ ra sogs lha btsun gyi bu'i lkugs

phye/ kha ro dang / yar 'brog sna dkar rtse la sogs par so thar dang sems bskyed mang du gnang / yar 'brog mtsho mo che la byon dus gru nang du 'dul ba'i dus go mdzad/ srin
po ri/ grwa thang / yar klungs rnam rgyal/ sne gdong / do sngon/ khra 'brug pu gu do/ 'ol kha tsha thang rnams su sngags mtshan nyid theg pa che chung gi chos mang du gsungs/
de nas dpal ldan bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan dwags po nas gdan 'dren pa'i ched du stod sde lung ba nas yul ma la brgyud de rtswa de yul du 'byon par brtsams pa na/
yul de'i khrom chen po tshogs pa'i nang du gtsang mo gzugs mi tshad las nyis 'gyur gyis che ba/ gos ne tso kha gyon pa rgyan gyis mdzes pa gsum byung nas/ kye'i grong mi
rnams nang par yul ma rong la skyes bu dam pa khyad par can 'byon gyin khyed rnams kyis zam pa 'dzugs pa dang bsu skyel byas na bsod nams chen po thob bo zer nas mi snang
bar gyur pas/ kun ngo mtshar te thang shing gi zam pa 'dzugs pa dang lam 'phrang bcos tshar ba na/ rje nyid phebs te de rnams kyis zam pa la gdan drangs byin brlabs zhus
de ni sgrol mas

chu'i 'jigs pa las bskyabs pa yin gsungs/ de nas dwags po mkhar lung bzang su phebs/ dpal ldan bla ma gdan 'dren par brtsams pa na/ rong mi kun gyis dmag gis bkag pas dpung
gi khrod du thog babs te star ka'i sdong bo phye mar brlabs pas sa skya pa'i 'dre byung zer nas skrag ste slar dad par gyur/ sgrum pa dang / sgom tshigs pa sogs skye bo
mang po la sems bskyed gnang / sgam po rin po che sogs dam pa mang po'i mkhan slob mdzad/ de nas dpal ldan bla ma gdan drangs nas yar byon/ gdan sa thel dang / bsam yas sogs
su lha btsun bsod nams 'od zer sogs dge bshes skye bo'i tshogs stong phrag mang po la chos gsungs/ yer pa/ gung thang / 'phrul snang / ra mo che/ mtshur phu/ dbu ri/
gzhu kun ra/ snye mo/ tsha mig gya ba mdo phug la sogs pa gnas bshad grwa sgom grwa che chung rnams su sngags mtshan nyid kyi bshad srol sngags med pa rnams srol bstod/ yod
pa rnams dar zhing rgyas par mdzad/ skye dgu'i tshogs 'bum phrag mang po theg pa chen po'i lam du bkod de/ slar ri phug tu phebs nas sngar bzhin dus chos rnams dang

sbyor drug rim lnga/ spros med/ chos drug ngal po/ zhi byed sogs kyi khrid bka' dang / rgyud sde bzhi'i dbang bshad byin brlabs kyi bka' bar ma chad du gnang / re gsum pa la
dbang ldan 'bras spungs kyi chag tshul bsgyur/ ri phug tu byang chub chen po'i mchod rten bzhengs/ dpon chen dbang brtson sogs skye bo mang po byang chub la bkod/ hor rgyal
bu pradznyA cing ze'u tsing dbang 'khor hor brgya phrag dang bcas pa la dus 'khor gyi dbang gnad zab chos la sbyar/ chos yon du btson bsod nges stong phrag mang po'i
srog bskyabs/ khro phur khro lo'i gdan sa mdzad de bshad grwa dang sgom grwa bskyangs/ sa skyar byon nas gdung rgyud pa dang sde snod 'dzin pa gnam gyi skar ma tsam chos
kyis tshim par mdzad/ khru so drug pa'i dpal mchog rigs bsdus kyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs nas chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa la dbang bskur/ lha khang chen mor rdor dbyings kyi dkyil
'khor blo blongs rgyu rin po che las grub pa rtsa thig khru bcu gnyis pa'i bkod pa mdzad de bzhengs/ re bdun pa la zhwa lu'i gdan

sar thugs sras lo tsA ba bskos nas ri phug nyid du bzhugs te/ kha che paNDi ta su man shri byon pa la spyan ras gzigs padma'i dra ba gsan/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa/ gu shri
kun dga' rin chen/ ta'i si tu/'jam dbyangs gu shrI rnams la dus 'khor gyi dbang gnang / ti shri bsod blo ba la rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang gnang / dus 'khor sogs phyi nang
gi dkyil 'khor mang po'i lo dus kyi sgrub mchod chen mo'i srol btsugs/ bo dong er thugs sras lo tsA ba dang / chos kyi dpal ba dang / tshe 'jam sogs sde snod 'dzin pa mang
po la rdo rje phreng ba sogs chos rje nyid la bzhugs pa'i dbang phal mo che gnang / e'i gtsug lag khang gi rab gnas mdzad/ chu mig stag tshal rdzing kha/ rin spungs/ myang
stod lcang ra/ stag tshang rdzong kha/ zhu 'brog gnas/ shangs mthong smon sogs su gdul bya mang po smin grol la bkod/ gdan sa ri phug tu gtsang phyogs kyi dge 'dun mtha'
dag bsags nas/ nga dga' ldan du 'gro ba'i phyi phyag yin gsungs nas spong thag mdzad/ skabs shig tu mdang sum rmi lam shin tu

bzang / dga' ldan nas skas rings gsum byung ba'i dbus ma la byams pa byon/ gcig la ngas 'dzogs/ gcig la sus phyin nam gsungs/ don bzhi pa la/ grwa pa klog pa pa rnams zhwa
lur brdzangs/ spong ba pa rnams nang mtshams bsdams/ chos rje nyid kyang mun khang bsrubs nas thugs dam la rtse gcig tu bzhugs/ 'brug lo'i dpyid sku khams mnyel ba na/ rgyal
sras thogs med pa sogs dge 'dun mang pos gser gyi maNDal phul nas gsol ba btab pas/ mdang gsum nga'i rmi lam na rnam thos kyi bus nang tsho 'gog pa yin zer nas lus la
bse khrab lta bu mang po bkog nas bskyur gtong gin gda' gsung nas sku khams dwangs te gtang rag gi gtor ma mdzad do// slar hor zla lnga ba'i gzhug nas/ cung zad mnyel te
don lnga ba shing pho 'brug gi lo zla ba drug pa'i nyi shu gcig gi tho rangs me tog gi char dang bcas te mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan/ nyi shu bdun la gdung sbyangs
pas ring bsrel yungs 'bru lta bu'i phung bor gyur pas/ rgya gar/ rgya nag bal bod

kyi phyogs thams cad du khyab par byas/ zhwa lur nang rten jo bo'i sku tshad ma/ phyi rten gser 'bum/ dbyen 'dum pa'i mchod rten/ gdan sa ri phug tu sku 'dra rin po che rnams
bzhengs so// bdag nyid chen po 'di la bu slob bsam gyis mi khyab kyang mchog tu gyur pa dus 'khor la mkhas pa ni/ kha che paNDi ta su ma na shrI/ dpal ldan bla ma dam
pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ thugs sras lo tsA ba/ chos kyi dpal ba gnyis/ lo chen byang rtse/ rgyal thang pa/ skyabs mchog pa/ khyung po lhas pa/ chos grags dpal ba/ lo tsA
ba blo gros dpal/ dbang rnon pa/ 'jam dkar ba/ dus 'khor ba shAkya dpal/ tshe 'jam pa/ 'jam rin pa/ grub pa dpal/ gzhon nu grub/ mgon dpal ba/ dbang grags pa/ dpal chen
pa sogs byung la/ kha che paN chen su ma na shrI ni/ yongs su rdzogs pa'i paNDi ta chen po rgyud sde rgya mtsho la mkhas pa des/ rje 'di la 'phags yul du sha lu paNDi ta
zhes grags shing mchog tu dus 'khor la mkhas pa'i snyan pa

gsan nas/ de zhu ba'i ched du zhwa lur phebs pa la dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud bshad sbyor drug gi khrid ma lus par saM skri ta'i skad du gnang bas/ paN chen de mchog tu dgyes
shing gus pa chen pos legs par gsan nas/ slar rgya gar du thegs te de'i rgyun dar bar mdzad do//bsod nams rgyal mtshan/dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po ni yab bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal dang / yum zhwa lu ba gzhon nu 'bum gyi sras su chu pho byi ba lo la sa skyar sku 'khrungs/ zla ba gsum na nyan chen bsod
nams brtan pa la dril bu ba'i dbang dang / dgung lo gsum pa rong pa sher seng la gshed dmar gyi dbang gsan/ brgyad pa la brtag gnyis gsungs/ bcu gcig pa la bla chen kun
blo ba la dge bsnyen mnos/ bcu bdun pa la mkhan chen bsod grags pas mkhan po/ dpal ldan seng ge bas slob dpon mdzad de rab tu byung / nyi shu pa la mkhan slob de gnyis
dang / rin chen dpal bzang pas gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ mnal lam du paN chen shAkya shrI/ sa skya paNDi ta/ pha dam pa rnams dang mjal/ bla ma rin chen

dpal bzang po la sbyor drug gsan pas stong gzugs kyi 'jam dbyangs longs sku'i rnam pa gzigs/ brag kha ba dang / sngon pa chos dpal bzang po dang / mkhan chen bsod grags pa
la sbyor drug gsan pas drung rtsol la dbang 'byor/ bla ma dpal ldan sengge/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ gzhon nu dpal bzang po/ dpang blo gros brtan pa/ gan pa rin chen
rgyal mtshan/ bu ston rin po che/ mkhan chen gzhon nu mgon po/ rgyal sras thogs med pa/ lo chen byang rtse rnams la bsten nas/ phar tshad 'dul mngon dbu ma sogs bde snod
kyi gzhung lugs rab 'byams dang / sgra/ snyan ngag bsdebs sbyor/ mngon brjod la sogs pa tha snyad kyi gzhung lugs mang po dang / khyad par gsang sngags kyi rgyud sde rgya
mtsho'i dbang rgyud bshad man ngag mtha' dag la legs par sbyangs pas/ mkhas pa zla med par gyur/ khyad par du dpang lo la rgyud 'grel gsan dus khyed kyis 'di ci nas kyang
legs par mkhyen par mdzod cig ces do dam cher mdzad nas gsungs pas/ slad mar bu ston rin po che la dus 'khor

gyi dbang rgyud man ngag dang bcas pa dang / rje des chos gsan no cog mtha' dag bum pa gang byor gsan pas mchog tu mkhas par gyur/ nyer bdun pa la gong ma'i gdan 'dren lan
gsum byung na'ang / 'od zer can gyi man ngag gis bzlog so gsum pa la hor rgyal po'i 'ja' dwa dang shel dam bzhi phul nas bzhi thog tu bzhugs su gsol te bstan pa'i mnga' bdag
tu bkur/ phar tshad brtag gnyis la sogs pa'i bshad grwa btsugs/ lam 'bras la sogs pa'i khrid dang dbang gis gdul bya tshim par mdzad/ so drug pa la dbus su phebs te/
thol du spyan snga grags pa rgyal mtshan pa la chos gnang / bsam yas zhig bsos kyi grwa btsugs/ so bdun pa la yang hor gyi gdan 'dren byung bas/ ta dben blo gros rgyal mtshan
bzhi thog tu bskos/ rta la chibs pa spangs te zhabs thang mdzad nas byang 'dam gyi bar du byon/ stag lung pa ratna A ka ra la thugs bskyed gnang / g.yang la la kha ba
chen po bab kyang thang rgyang mdzad de byon pas rlangs phyur re byung bas kun ngo mtshar

du gyur/ rwa sgreng du jo bo'i rgya dpe rnams gzigs pas 'ja'i gur phub/ dge 'dun rnams la chos gsungs pas me tog gi char bab/ dpon slob nyi shu tsam klung shod/ 'ol kha/ dwags
po sman lung / tswa de yul rnams brgyud de rdzam yul gyi mkhar lung bzang su phyag phab/ lo gcig gi bar du thugs dam 'dag 'byar la bzhugs/ bu ston rin po che gdan 'dren
la phebs pas/ gtsang du 'byon pa ni ma gnang bar dbus su bskor cig phebs/ bla chen bsod blo ba gdan sar brdzangs/ slar yang dwags po thegs/ ma gcig dbang ba'i gdan 'dren
byung bas 'gyogs par byon te/ bo dong er yum sras mjal/ ma gcig 'das pa dag pa'i zhing du 'dren par mdzod/ de nas sa skyar mkhas btsun stong phrag mang po la dbang dang
lam 'bras kyi khrid gnang / dbus su phebs te nyan por phar phyin gsung dus/ gros kun mkhyen pas thub pa chen po sher phyin gsung bar mthong / shes rdor bas chos rje nyid
'jam dbyangs su mthong ste/ maNDal gyi rgyan gyi ched du rang nyid kyi lag pa'i gsor

mo lnga bcad pa na/ chos rje nyid tab tab por byon te de'i sor mo rnams bsgrigs zhal chab btab/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin brlabs gnang bas de'i nub mo sor mo sngon bzhin du
sos/ de nas snye thang du bzhugs nas dge 'dun gyi tshogs chen po la bar chad/ brtag gnyis/ lam 'bras sbyor drug rnams gnang / de nas gdan sa thel du spyan snga ba sogs
sde snod 'dzin pa mang po la dus 'khor gyi rgyud bshad lam 'bras sbyor drug sogs gnang / de dus lo gcig gi khongs su bsam yas kyi zhig gsos mtha' dag grub/ rab gnas kyi tshe
dge 'dun khri phrag lhag tsam 'dus lha'i me tog sna lnga pa'i char bab/ de nas sa skyar byon te chos gsung pa'i skabs su/ hor gyi gdan 'dren pa byung bas/ dpon slob bco
brgyad kyis zla ba gnyis kyi bar du nyin mo bzhugs shing mtshan mo 'bros pa'i dka' ba spyad nas/ zhe brgyad pa la yang mkhar lung bzang su byon/ der lo gcig gi bar du
sku mtshams mdzad nas slob ma mang po la lam 'bras dang / sbyor drug gi khrid bka' mang po bug sgo las gnang / dus 'khor TIka chen mdzad par brtsams pa na

mnal lam du bud med sngo bsangs rgyan dang bcas pa gcig gis snag snyug gtad nas nga bris shig zer byung bas mthar phyin pa'i ltas su dgongs/ lnga bcu pa la brag rings zhes
pa'i gnas su sku 'khor bzhi dang bcas pa zla ba drug gi bar du thugs dam kho na la rtse gcig tu bzhugs/ slob dpon manydzu shrI bas sku lus cung zad re ma bcags na skyon mi
mchi lags sam zhus pas ting nge 'dzin gnad du song na de nyid lus sbyongs su'ang 'gro ba yin par 'dug gsungs/ de nas mtha' rgyas su byon nas bla chen bsod blo ba gong du
brdzangs/ rtses thang bsam gtan gling du rgyal sras thogs med pa dang lhan cig zla ba gsum thugs dam la bzhugs/ snye thang chos rdzong btab ste/ der si tu chos rin pas
zhu ba po mdzad nas sde snod 'dzin pa lnga bcu tsam la thugs brtsoms TIka chen gyi steng nas dus 'khor gyi bshad pa rgyas par gnang / khrid rim yang rgyun mi 'chad du gnang
/ de nas yang nga gsum pa la mkhar lung bzang su phebs te/ dus 'khor don du gnyer ba'i dge bshes mang po phyag phyir byon pa rnams la dus 'khor gyi bshad pa rgyas pa dang
khrid rim rnams gnang / de nas lo

gcig na rkong po nas par dus 'khor thugs dkyil gyi dkyil 'khor blos slang bzhengs/ rkong po ral gsum phyag phab nas skye bo'i tshogs chen po la sems skyed gnang / lo gcig gi
bar rgya bsdams/ sbu chu lha khang du 'bum nag dang 'bum dmar gzigs pas me tog gi char bab/ 'o thang mtsho mo'i yul sde ma chu'i gnod pa bsgyur/ nga drug pa la bod klungs
la rgyud de byar bel kha/ pho brang yang rtse rnams su phebs/ gnyal lte'u rar dbyar chos la brtag gnyis dang / lam 'bras gnang / gser phye 'bum pa'i drung du sems skyed
gsungs pas thams cad kyis gzung du btub pa me tog gi char bab/ lha sar jo bo rin po che la khri rgyab phul/ snye thang du dus 'khor gyi bshad pa rgyas par gsungs pas/ rwa
'bro shong 'gyur gyi dpe 'grems brgya lhag byung / dbus phyogs kyi dus 'khor 'chad nyan pa gcig la de nyid sde snod 'dzin pa'i tshogs 'du che bar grags/ rlung ltas la
sku tshe'i bar chad 'ong ba mkhyen nas/ g.ye go ra gdong du rdo rje bzlas pa 'bum phrag gcig mdzad pas lo lnga sku tshe bsrings/ mkhan chen grags rgyal

pa la rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang gnang / 'jam dbyangs gu shrI la sbyor drug gnang / bo dong er dge 'dun bzhi khri lhag 'dus pa la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor te gser zho re'i 'gyed
gnang / de nas sa skyar phebs te tshogs su dus 'khor gyi chos 'byung / mdor bsdus dang po yan gyi bshad pa/ brtag gnyis rnams gsungs/ rten rnams la zhig gsos mdzad/ sku
khams cung zad mnyel dus thub pa chen pa la gnas brtan bcu drug gis bskor ba mngon sum du gzigs ma thag bsnyun las dwangs/ de nas bo dong er lo chen byang rtse sogs gtsang
phyogs kyi bla ma rnams kyis thog drangs sde snod 'dzin pa sha stag dang bskyed rdzogs la brtan pa thob pa'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug mang du 'dus pa la dus 'khor
gyi bshad pa rgyas pa/ lam 'bras/ sbyor drug rim lnga/ spros med la sogs khrid dbang byin brlabs mang du gnang / de nas dpal sdings/ chu mig snar thang / zhwa lu rnams su'ang
chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bzhin par byon te/ dbus phyogs su phebs/ bsam yas su dge 'dun nyi khri 'dus pa la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor/ gser

zho re'i 'gyed gnang / rje 'di'i bka' 'bum la po ti nyi shu rtsa lnga bzhugs pa las khyad par du dus 'khor bskor la bsdus don chos 'byung / stong 'jug gi rtsis/ sbyor drug
gi khrid yig ngo sprod bsrungs 'khor gnyis/ mngon dkyil/ thugs dkyil mngon rtogs/ rnal 'byor ma'i mchod chog rnams so// rje 'dis dge bsnyen dang dge tshul lta zhog bsnyen
rdzogs kyi sdom pa phog pa la stong phrag lnga ldan pa byung / sdom pa 'bog pa dang / dbang bskur ba dang / rab gnas rnams la sla chos gtan mi mdzad/ tshul khrims kyi dri
dang ldan/ kho bo lo bcu bdun pa la rab tu byung nas nga'i bar du tshul khrims gtsang bar bsrungs pas 'di nga'i 'phrin las kyi gtso bo yin gsungs/ dus phyis bod du byung
ba gcig la mkhan chen bu ston pa'i rtson 'grus la sus kyang mi do/ de ma gtogs nga yang brtson 'grus chung rgyu med gsungs/ mnyam par ma bzhag pa'i thugs mi mnga' ste/
gzigs rtog gi skabs su'ang phyag dpe'i steng du stong gzugs dus rgyun du 'byung gsungs/ bdag nyid chen po 'di'i zhabs gnyis la 'khor lo'i mtshan dang ldan/ sku lus la

srin 'bu'i rigs mi 'byung / skye bo gzhan las mchog tu gyur pa'i gzi 'od 'bar/ gsung snyan cing tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang ldan no// re gsum pa la chos rdzong du bla ma bzhon
rgyal ba can na sa chen yab sras kyang bzhugs pas/ snga phyi kun du der skye bar smon lam btab pa yin yang / byams chos 'di rnams la thos bsam byas pa'i mthu yin nam dga'
ldan du 'gro bar 'dug gsungs/ der sde snod 'dzin pa nyer lnga pa tshan pa gsum la dus 'khor gyi dbang rdzogs pa dang / dbang mdor bstan dang / lam 'bras dang / sbyor drug
gnang / de nas bsam yas su phebs/ mkhan chen zhi ba 'tsho'i dbu thod bla brang du gdan drangs/ nyin re bzhin brgya phyag mdzad cing smon lam 'debs/ tho rangs bu ston
rin po che dang rdo rje rnal 'byor ma byon nas/ bu ston pas 'di rang mkha' spyod yin no gsung ba byung / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku mang pos zhing gang ba gzigs/ lo tsA ba
nam mkha' bzang po la chag lo tsA ba de la rnam thar bzang po yod pas ltos shig gsungs/ re bzhi pa yos lo zla ba drug pa'i nyi shu lnga la sa g.yo ba dang / me tog gi char
'bab pa

dang bcas pa'i cho 'phrul bstan te dga' ldan du gshegs so//mtshungs med gzhon nu grags pa/de dus kyi mkhas btsun rnams dang / khyad par du dus 'khor smra ba phal mo che/ rje
de'i slob mar ma gyur pa med pas bgrang bar mi dpyod la/ bye brag tu mtshungs med gzhon nu grags pa ni/ 'phan yul du sku 'khrungs/ gzhung lugs mang po la legs par sbyangs/
khyad par du 'dul mdzod la mchog tu mkhas/ gnas brtan chen po tshul khrims shin tu gtsang ba/ rgyal sras thogs med pa la thugs bskyed dang / blo sbyong gsan pas byang
chub kyi thugs 'byongs/ bu ston rin po che la dbang dang gdams ngag mang du mnos shing / khyad par du dpal ldan bla ma mkhar lungs bzang su bzhugs pa'i drung du/ dus kyi
'khor lo'i dbang dang sbyor drug gsan pas sgyu ma lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin mngon du gyur/ khrab mkhar 'dul mdzod dus chos su gsung zhing / rang nyid zab lam gyi thugs dam
la gtso bor bzhugs te rang gzhan gyi don rgya chen po mdzad do//

de la 'khrul zhig pa yang dpal ldan bla ma/ ngag dbang grags pa/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ 'khrul zhig pa ste/ de la bdag gi bla ma dus zhabs pas dpal ldan bla ma'i sbyor drug
gi khrid yig ngo sprod dang bcas pa dang / sron lugs kyi gdams pa rnams gsan to// yang rgyal ba yon tan 'od kyis dpal ldan bla ma las dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud bshad man
ngag dang bcas pa gsan pas mkhas shing grub pa brnyes/ de la shangs pa kun mkhyen shes rab dpal bzang po/ de la thams cad mkhyen pa 'gos lo tsA bas dpal ldan bla ma'i TIka
chen nges don gsal byed kyi lung gsan to//thugs sras lo tsA ba/thugs sras lo tsA ba ni/ sngags 'chang zhig gi bu mo'i sras su sa pho rta la 'khrungs/ mes po la yang dag
phur pa 'jigs byed kyi dbang thob/ gsang mtshan thugs kyi rdo rje/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge la dge bsnyen mnos/ dgung lo bdun pa la yum 'das nas zhwa lu dpon mos legs
par bskyangs/ bcu pa la bu ston rin po che dang slob dpon

dar byang las rab tu byung ste rin chen rnam rgyal du btags/ phar mngon dang sgra tshad mkhas par mkhyen pas sgra tshad par grags/ rgya gar nub phyogs kyi paNDi ta su ma ti
kI ti mgur mor byon pa la/ bu ston rin po ches dri ba nyi shu 'drir btang ba'i tshe de la dbyangs can ma dang rlung sbyor zab mo gsan/ paNDi ta des bu ston la bstod pa dang
'phrin yig dus 'khor gyi bum sman tshang ma phul/ bstod 'phrin de bsgyur bas lo tsA bar grags/ dbyangs can ma'i pi wang gi sgra gsan/ bslab pa la skyon zhig byung ba
legs par gshegs nas de nyin rang bu ston rin po che/ skyabs mchog dpal bzang po/ dar byang pa la mkhan slob zhus nas tshig rdzogs su bsnyen par rdzogs/ 'dul ba byams chos
dbu ma sogs sde snod kyi gzhung lugs rgya mtsho lta bu la sbyangs/ rgyud sde kun gyi dbang rgyud bshad man ngag dang bcas pa gsan pas bum pa gang byor mkhyen/ khyad par
sbyor drug gsan dus zla ba gsum mun mtshams la bzhugs pas bsam gtan gyi rtogs pa 'khrungs shing mngon par shes pa mnga'/ dgra nag

gi dbang zhus dus nam mkha' la 'phags nas gar mdzad/ phag dkar dang bde mchog gi zhal gzigs/ gshin rje gshed kyi sbyin bsreg mdzad pas me lce las bkra shis pa'i rtags shar/
so dgu pa la bu ston rin po ches zhwa lu'i gdan sar bskos te/ zhal bskos mang po gnang / a ti sha'i gsung bzhin/ sbrul gyi spags pa brjes kyang sbrul mi brjed/ kho bo 'chi
tshul bstan kyang a ti sha/ de bas chags shing zhen pa ma che bar// dga' ldan gnas su kho bo'i drung du shog/ ces gsungs rjes bka' bzhi/ 'phags yog dus gsum/ bde mchog
sampu Ta'i rgyud dus chos su gsungs/ rgyud rnams la le'u mtshams ma gtogs chos thun ring thung med pa dang / gdan bzhi gsung pa la dpon slob la blta phyogs tshun sngan ma
las ma 'gyur bar mdzad/ lan cig slob dpon 'jam dpal ba la bsam yas rgyal po dngos su 'ongs te bar chad brtsams pas khong la grwa lnga'i dbang dang bsrung ba gnang ba tsam
gyis rgyal pos khong ji tsam btsal yang mi mthong ba byung / de ma gtogs lo dgu'i ring bu ston nyid la chos gsan pa dang /

dus chos bshad pa kho na las dbang rjes gnang mi mdzad/ bu ston dga' ldan du thegs nas ni dbang khrid man ngag rnams kyang lhug par stsol/ bkra shis sgo mang dang / bu ston
rin po che'i bka' 'bum po ti so gsum bzhengs/ mnga' ris pa bde ldan la padma dra ba'i dbang gnang dus/ de nam mkha' 'phags te gar bsgyur zhing rta skad tsher ba sogs byung
/ bzhi thog pa / nya btsan lha sbyin/ g.yag gzhon gnyis/ byams chos pa/ skyabs mchog dpal/ tsong kha pa blo bzang grags pa/ karma pa dkon gzhon/ lo tsA ba grags rgyal/
tshogs sde bzhi'i mkhan po/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ dbus pa blo gsal/ snar thang pa rgyal mtshan grags sogs mkhas btsun mang po la mdo sngags kyi char phab/ rtogs ldan chos
'byung la nam mkha'i rlung gegs bsal/ grub chen chos grub las rlung log pa'i gegs bsal/ gnas rnying pa rgyal dbang gi thig le'i gegs bsal/ slob dpon rtsed po'i stong nyams
kyi gegs bsal/ hor rgyal bu phing chang gi snying

rlung bsal/ hor bi ma la gu shrI la bdud gzher pa nag po phog pa'i dug bsal/ bdun bcu pa sa pho 'brug la/ dbon po grags rgyal 'di la chos bum pa gang byor gtad yod pas gdan
sar bskos shig ces gsungs te zhwa lu ri phug tu dbu'i da tsug nas glangs pa lta bu'i 'od dkar dmar ba thag tsam pa thon nas bla re la zug pa'i cho 'phrul dang bcas te dga'
ldan du gshegs so// rje 'di'i thugs sras mchog rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan dang / mkhas btsun bsod nams don grub gnyis kyi/ snga ma ni zhwa lu'i gdan sar bzhugs nas
'gro don rgya cher mdzad cing / sne gdong rtser chos rgyal grags pa 'byung gnas pas bla mar gdan drangs/ dbus phyogs kyi mkhas btsun mang po 'phags yog dus gsum sogs chos
kyis tshim par mdzad/ rtses thang gi yo ga dang dus 'khor sogs kyi sgrub mchod rnams kyang rje 'di'i 'phrin las las byung ba yin no//rdo rje 'dzin pa ye shes rgya mtsho/de'i
slob ma rdo rje 'dzin ye shes rgya mtsho ba ni/ de dus chog g.yog tu phebs pa slad mar dbus su gdan drangs te/ chos

kyi rje spyan snga rin po che dang / dpal kun bzang rtse pas dus 'khor dang yo ga'i dbang bka' phyag len gsan cing sbyangs/ dpal kun bzang rtse pa la bdag gis dus 'khor gyi
dbang yongs su rdzogs pa mnos so// mkhas btsun bsod nams don grub pa ni/ thugs sras lo tsA ba las dbang rgyud man ngag ma lus pa gsan cing sbyangs pas dus 'khor la mchog
tu mkhas shing grub pa zhig go/ de'i slob ma sku zhang chos rje rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni/ thog mar thugs sras lo tsA ba las rab tu byung
zhing / dge slong byang sems rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po/ khyad par du bsod nams don grub pa las dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud bshad man ngag ma lus par gsan nas sbyangs pas mkhas
shing grub pa brnyes te/ ru dgon gsar du dus 'khor gyi bshad grwa dang phyag len gyi srol btsugs pas deng sangs gi bar du'ang grwa bzang shos su byung / mngon par mkhyen
pa dang / mtshan mo mun nang du'ang zhal ras zla ba ltar dkar sgor gsal ba dang / rA hu la mkha' la rgyu ba la sdigs mdzub mdzad pas

sa la lhung ba sogs grub pa'i mtshan la mang po dang ldan pa zhig go/ de'i slob ma chos rje yon bkras pa ni/ rgyud 'grel dbang mdor bstan gsum/ bu ston pa'i gsung sgros dang
/ bu mchan phyogs mchan thugs la bzhugs pa dus 'khor la mchog tu mkhas pa zhig go/ de la bdag gi bla ma dus 'khor bas rgyud bshad gsan cing sku zhang chos rje la dbang
khrid gsan to//dharma shrI pa/dharma shrI pa ni/ dge slong byang sems rdo rje'i 'dzin pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i mkhas pa chen po mngon par rtogs pa'i yon tan phul du byung
ba/ jo gdan tshogs pa'i mkhan por bskos pas ma mdzad kyang mkhan chen dharma shrI zhes grags/ khyad par bu ston rin po che la dus 'khor rgyud 'grel tshar mang ba zhig gsan
pas mchog tu mkhas par gyur nas/ dka' chen bzhi/ 'phags yog dus gsum/ lhag par du dus 'khor la dus chos kyi sgo nas 'phrin las rgya cher bskyangs so// gong gsum bde chen
chos kyi dpal ba ni/ bu ston rin po che la rgyud 'grel tshar bcu bdun gsan pas/ dus 'khor la mchog tu mkhas par gyur nas/ chos 'di'i 'phrin las rgya cher bskyangs so//shangs
pa kun mkhyen shes rab dpal bzang po/de'i slob ma shangs pa kun mkhyen

shes rab dpal bzang po ni/ chos kyi dpal ba la dus 'khor gsan pas legs par mkhyen cing mdo sngags ma lus pa la mkhas pas kun mkhyen du grags la/ shangs ri bo dge 'phel du tar
chags pa'i dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyun dang / dus chos gsungs pas sems 'grel gyi phrin las rgyas par mdzad do// de la rje thams cad mkhyen pa 'gos lo tsA bas dbang dang
rgyud bshad gsan to// yang bde chen chos kyi dpal ba la/ rje rin po che tsong kha pa blo bzang grags pas gsan du thegs pa'i tshe mjal dar la dar ser po dang / phyis 'bul
ba la go ne tso yug phul bas/ dang por 'byung ba sdud rim dang slad mar skyed rim du gda' bas rten 'brel bzang gsung nas dgyes/ nang le gsung ba'i thog ma nas gsan chog byung
bas/ gang zhig chen po'i mi rnams smin par bya ba'i slad ces pa tshig mtshams pra legs par dgongs te/ rgyud bshad phran dang bcas pa gsan nas/ sa pho khyi la slob ma'i
tshogs chen po la rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa rdzogs par gnang ngo //'jam rin pa/'jam rin

pa ni/ bu ston rin po che la dbang rgyud bshad man ngag ma lus par mnos/ de la shangs dkar pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ de la skungs lungs pa sangs rgyas dpal bas gsan te/ de
ni me pho stag la 'khrungs/mdo sngags kyi gzhung lugs phal mo che mkhyen cing / khyad par stag pa chos rdor dang shangs dkar ba las dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang rgyud bshad man
ngag mtha' dag mnos/ rmog cog pa rin chen brtson 'grus kyi sprul par grags/ bskyed rim shin tu brtan pas gzhan la yi dam lha'i skur gsal bar ston/ dbang gi skabs su ye
shes nges par phebs/ thugs gtad pa tsam dang dmigs pa'i mde'u kha cung zad res rlung sems dbu mar chud nas nyams myong mtha' yas pa 'char/ mnal lam 'byongs pas shambha la'i
rigs ldan la chos gsan/ mngon par mkhyen pa mnga'/ gsang chab 'thungs pa tsam gyis gtum mo'i bde drod 'phral du skye/ lkog tu slob ma na ba la rmi lam du chos rje nyid
kyis dus 'khor gyi lha so so'i sngags brjod cing byin gyis rlobs pa'i snang ba bstan pas de ma thag grol ba sogs byin brlabs kyi rnam 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga'/
bu slob

rnams la mkha' khyab mkha'i rdo rje can yin pas gsol ba gar btab tu 'ong / dus 'khor smon lam re thob ces gsungs te/ re brgyad pa chu mo bya la 'ja' 'od du pi wang gling bu'i
sgra dang bcas te sku'i bkod pa bsdus/ dbu thod la a yig 'bur du dod pa byon to// de la bdag gi bla ma dus zhabs pas dbang rgyud man ngag mnos so//rje btsun dpal chen
bzang po/rje btsun dpal chen bzang po ni/ yul gnyal stod g.yu rbe phye'u grong du/ yab rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po grub ston bsod nams bzang po dang / yum snyi ba mo rgyal ma
skyid kyi sras su me pho 'brug la 'khrungs/ dgung lo bdun pa la ste'u rar byon te/ mkhan po chag rin chen 'byung gnas dpal bzang po dang / slob dpon thang chen pa tshul
khrims dpal las rab tu byung mtshan dpal chen bzang por btags/ mkhan po la gsang 'dus rgyud 'grel dang / dus 'khor rgyud 'grel chag lugs gsan te legs par sbyangs/ bla brang
pa blo gros dpal ba la gsang 'dus rgyud 'grel sbyong rgyud/ phreng bskor

gsum gyi bshad pa gsan/ bla brang ba shAkya dpal la gshed dmar bde dgyes gsang 'dus sogs chag pa'i chos skor gsan/ rje de gshin rje gshed dngos su gzigs/ grub chen mangga la
shrI zhes pa bde mchog gi grub thob dgung lo brgya bzhes kyang sku lus gzhon nu dang mtshungs pa las las chen bcu gnyis 'phral du sgrub pa la tshegs med pa/ rA hu la bzhugs
gdan gyi 'og tu 'dzud nus pa de lte'u ra'i zur khang du bzhugs pa la/ bde gsang dus gsum/ kun rig sogs gsan/ bla ma de dbang mdzad pa'i dbang g.yog mdzad de phyag len
shin tu byang / chag dar ma rdo rje la gnas kyi bla ma bcol te 'dul ba'i bslab bya la byang bar gyur/ skrags phug tu khu bo grub thob legs ldan 'od la gsang dus kyi dbang
zhus/ dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo dngos su gzigs/ de nas brtsams te rdo rje 'chang dngos kyi 'du shes kho na las tha mal gyi rtog pa mi mnga'/ grub chen de la chag lugs kyi
sbyor drug dang rim lnga dang dbang rgyud man ngag mtha' dag gsan/ mi g.yo sngon po gsan pas/ khyod dang

'brel ba yod pas bcom ldan 'das 'dis rjes su 'dzin par 'gyur ro gsungs/ bra gor du mon khra ba la/ mdo rtsa spyod 'jug lam rim dang / lte'u rar dbu ma pa rin chen rgyal po
la rigs tshogs gsan/ nyer brgyad pa la lte'u rar chag lo'i mkhan rgyud 'dzin pa byar rje sgo ba mgon po dpal gyis mkhan po/ bla brang pa bzang po dpal gyis las slob/ tshogs
chen mo'i dbu mdzad seng ge rin chen gyis gsang ston mdzad nas bsnyen par rdzogs/ bla brang pa de la rdo rje phreng ba sogs dbang mang po dang / phar phyin dbu ma/ spyod
'jug skyes rabs/ ting 'dzin rgyal po/ gsang 'dus/ kye rdor/ spyod rgyad/ mtshan brjod/ sdom 'byung / gshed dmar/ 'jigs byed/ 'khor chen sogs gsan/ so bzhi pa la thang
po cher rje bla brang pa'i drung du byon pa na/ dpal ldan bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa dwags po nas gdan 'dren par/ bu ston rin po che dang / rgyal sras thogs med pa
dang / gnas drug pa sogs phebs pa la chos 'brel re gsan/ khyad par du bu

ston rin po che yar klungs do sngon du brag kha'i jo bo sogs mi chen nyer lnga la dus 'khor gyi dbang gnang ba'i tshe mjal du byon pas/ nyi ma shar ba dang dus mtshungs par
zhal mjal/ khyed rnams bcom ldan 'das dpal dus kyi 'khor lor 'gyur ro zhes gsungs pa dang 'grig pas/ rten 'brel bzang bar dgongs/ chos 'brel dang byin brlabs zhus pas myur
du phrad par byed do gsungs pas/ zhabs drung du slebs pa'i smon lam mang du btab nas gnyal du byon/ yab kyi zhal nas dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang mjal ba la yi dam la gsol
ba 'debs dgos pa yin gsungs pas/ phye'u grog gi mchod khang chung ngu zhig tu mtshams bcad de/ mi g.yo sngon po pus btsugs kyi bsnyen pa 'bum phrag lnga bcu rtsa drug kha
skongs kyi sbyin sreg dang bcas pa mdzad pas/ zla ba bcu bdun/ yi dam gyi thang sku las 'od 'phro ba dang / lho phyogs kyi bu ga nas khyi nag pos gtor ma len pa byung
zhing / mthar khyi nag po de yi dam dngos su gzigs te/ bstod pa gsol 'debs dang bcas pa mdzad/ de nas rim gyis bsam yas su byon/ dpal ldan

bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan las/ dus 'khor rgyud 'grel/ rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i TI kA dang bcas pa/ dbang mdor bstan/ brtag gnyis/ mtshan brjod rnams kyi bshad pa/
shin tu spros med kyi khrid gsan/ de nas snye thang chos rdzong du zhabs phyir 'brangs nas lam 'bras/ zhi byed/ yang dgon pa'i ri chos rnams gsan/ lha sar jo bo la gser
phul nas gsol ba btab/ mtshur phur karma pa rol ba'i rdo rje la chos 'brel gsan/ zhwa lu ri phug tu bu ston rin po che dang mjal nas/ sa skyar thegs te gnas drug pa la mngon
pa/ mdo sde rgyan/ rnam nges man ngag phran mang po gsan cing / zla ba bcu gcig bzhugs/ de nas jo mo nang du kun mkhyen chen po la sbyor drug dang / dkon mchog rgyal
mtshan pa la thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid gsan/ de nas zhwa lur phebs te/ bu ston rin po che'i drung du lo bcu'i bar du bzhugs nas/ dka' chen bzhi la nyid kyi TI ka dang
bcas pa'i bshad pa tshar mang du gsan/ dus kyi

'khor lo'i dbang gsan dus bla ma dus 'khor dngos su gzigs/ gzhan yang gsang 'dus/ bde dgyes gshed dmar/ rdor dbyings/ dpal mchog rtse mo sogs kyi dbang thob/ dus 'khor rgyud
'grel dang / gsang 'dus rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa tshar bdun bdun gsan/ bde mchog rtsa sdom/ rnal 'byor ma kun spyod/ dus 'khor gyi rgyud phyi ma/ don dam bsnyen pa/ phyag
rdor dang rdo rje snying po'i bstod 'grel/ mtshan brjod rnams kyi bshad pa/ rim lnga/ sbyor drug shin tu spros med kyi nyams khrid rdzogs pa dang / sbyor drug lugs mi
'dra ba bcu gnyis/ gshed dmar/ lo nag dril gsum/ bde chen ral gcig gdan bzhi/ yo ga skor sogs mang du gsan/ bu ston pas mkhan chen dharma shrI la bka' gnang nas sgos kyi
yongs 'dzin du bskos pa la/ mngon pa kun las btus dang dus 'khor rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa tshar mang du gsan/ bu ston rin po che'i bka' 'bum dang khro phu ba'i man ngag brgya
rtsa yang gsan/ sgra tshad pa la yo ga rab 'byams gsan/ kha che

paNDi ta su ma na shrI la thugs rje chen po dang sgrol ma gsan/ lo chen byang rtse la ka lA pa snyan ngag me long sdeb sbyor rin chen 'byung gnas gsan cing sbyangs/ dngul chu'i
chos rdzong du rgyal sras thogs med pa la smon 'jug sems bskyed dang / blo sbyong gsan pas byang chub kyi thugs 'byongs/ gzhan yang chos lung mkhan chen pa bsod nams
bzang po sogs bla ma mang du bsten nas/ mang du thos pa rgya mtsho lta bu'i mthar son cing / khyad par du dus 'khor la mkhas par gyur nas/ zhe brgyad pa la gnyal du 'byon
dus/ bu ston rin po ches thugs dam thang ka ston pa'i sku/ rje nyid kyi na bza' dbu zhwa rnams gnang nas/ bstan pa'i bya ba 'chad nyan dang / dbang man ngag gi bka' legs
par skyongs/ rang gi dge sbyong la 'bod pa thon/ rang re ba spad skye ba phyi ma dga' ldan du nges par 'phrad gsung ba la/ zhabs zung spyi bor bkod nas bdag skye ba thams
cad du rjes su gzung du gsol zhes gsol bas/ de kho na bgyi'o gsung / de nas rim kyis mnyal du phebs/ lte'u ra dang skrags

phug tu chos gzhi mdzad de/ spyir na chos kyi bka' drin legs thob pa'i// bshes gnyen dam pa bzhi bcu lhag pa rnams// gus pas bsten te mang du thos gyur cing // thos pa ji bzhin
gzhan la bstan bsam dang // sbyor ba yis kyang 'phags yog dus gsum dang // bde dgyes gnyis dang dka' ba bzhi po dang // 'grel bcas dbu ma rtsa 'jug spyod 'jug dang //
skyes pa'i rab dang gzhan yang sngags phran mang // lan mang bshad pas rigs zugs 'byor ldan gyur// dad blo brtson 'grus ldan rnams dga' bar byos// shes kyang gdams ste/
bla brang ba chos dpal bzang po sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang du 'dus pa la/ dka' chen bzhi/ dbu ma rtsa she/ tshig gsal/ rin chen phreng ba/ spyod 'jug skyes rabs ting
'dzin rgyal po rnams dang / gsang 'dus 'phags skor/ dus 'khor rgyud 'grel phran dang bcas pa/ bde dgyes gshed dmar yo ga phreng ba skor gsum rnams kyi bshad grwa btsugs
te dbyar dgun gyi zla ba drug dus chos su mdzad/ bsam gtan

sgang chung du rtogs ldan rin chen lhun po sogs sgrub pa ba mang po la sbyor drug dang rim lnga'i gdams ngag gnang nas sgrub grwa btsugs/ ston dpyid zla ba gnyis sku mtshams
bsdams nas sbyor drug sogs kyi rdzogs rim la thugs dam mdzad/ de ltar bshad sgrub kyi sgo nas thub pa'i bstan pa rgyas par spel te/ don dgu pa shing pho khyi lo la dga'
ldan du gshegs so//chos rje rin po che ye shes dpal bzang po/de'i sras kyi thu bo chos rje rin po che ye shes dpal bzang po ni/ chag lo tsA ba chos rje dpal gyi gcung dar
ma dbang phyug gi sras mnga' bdag dpal/ de'i sras khra dpal/ de'i sras chag 'phags pa dang / yum dpal dar skyid kyi sras su me mo lug la gnyal smad chag grong du bltams/
bla brang ba bzang po dpal la sems bskyed dang a ra pa tsa na gsan/ dgung lo bdun pa la rje btsun dpal chen pa las dge bsnyen mnos/ bcu gcig pa la gshed dmar gyi bsnyen
pa mdzad pas mnal lam du hrIHNdi'i sngags lcags bsregs pa lta bu zhal du gsol ba'i snang ba byung / gsang 'dus kyi dbang zhus dus bla ma dkyil 'khor

gyi gtso bo dngos su gzigs/ bcu gsum pa la bla brang ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dang / rje btsun dpal chen pa las rab tu byung / bcu pa nas nyer gcig gi bar rje btsun dpal chen
pa nyid 'bral ba med par bsten nas/ dka' chen bzhi/ rtsa she/ tshig gsal/ 'jug pa/ spyod 'jug byams chos sogs sde snod kyi gzhung lugs mang bo dang / dus gsang bde dgyes
sogs rgyud sde mang bo'i bshad pa/ rdo rje phreng ba la sogs pa'i dbang / sbyor drug dang rim lnga la sogs pa'i khrid/ yi dam so so'i sgrub skor phran dang bcas pa gsan
cing legs par sbyangs pas mkhas par mkhyen/ bcu bzhi pa la lte 'u rar/ sdom 'byung / brtag gnyis/ dbang mdor bstan/ sbyong rgyud/ skyes rab rnams bshad/ nyi shu pa la rje
dpal chen pa/ chag shAkya dpal/ g.yag nag pa shes rab dpal rnams la mkhan slob zhus te bsnyen par rdzogs/ nyer gnyis pa la rtses thang du chen po byang rin pa la rnam 'grel

rgya ma ba yon tan dpal la phar phyin/ 'phan yul ba bsam grub ye shes la phar tshad gnyis/ thang bo cher chos rje nyi ma ba la gsang 'dus kye rdor gur mgon gsan/ zla ba gzas
bzung ba'i tshe ma sha'i sgrub pa mdzad pas myu gu me tog dang bcas pa skyes/ gsang phu sogs skyi shod kyi chos grwa rnams su grwa bskor mdzad/ lha sar jo bo'i drung du
gsol ba btab pas nam mkha'i snying pos rjes su bzung zhing / lung bstan pa'i mtshan brnyes/ nyer lnga pa la lte'u ra'i gdan sar bzhugs te gnyal lor byar rnams kyi gnas gzhi
phal mo cher chos gzhi mdzad cing phar tshad spyod 'jug dang / 'dus pa bde dgyes dus 'khor rnams kyi rgyud 'grel dus chos su gsungs/ rje btsun dpal chen pa la chos lhag
ma ma lus par gsan/ bum pa gang byor mkhyen/ lte'u ra'i gdan sa ba de lo bcu gsum la grongs 'gro ba'i sri cig yod pas/ so bdun pa la bla brang nyid du sku mtshams dam
par bcad de thugs dam la rtse gcig tu bzhugs pas/ mi nag po bzhis bzhugs gdan gyi zur nas khyer te nam mkha' la 'phags

nas mgo rting bsgyur ba sogs cho 'phrul mi bzad pa byung kyang thugs dam las ma g.yos pas gshin rje gshed dmar po'i zhal gzigs te bar chad las grol/ ye shes kyi mgon po rnams
kyis bka' bzhin 'phrin las sgrub pas nus mthu'i pha rol tu son/ zhe gnyis pa la bsam 'grub dpal mgon pa gdan sar bskos te/ gsal rje gangs su thugs dam la rtse gcig tu
bzhugs pas/ ye shes kyi rtsa dbu ma dang / rlung rgyuu ba'i srog gzugs mngon du gyur te chos thams cad kyi de kho na nyid gzigs/ 'chi 'pho ba dang skye ba dang mngon gyi
gnas rjes su dran pa'i mngon par shes pa shar/ chag grong du thugs dam gyi lha mang bo dang / khyad par dus 'khor gyi bsnyen pa bye ba mdzad/ dpal rir phyag na rdo rje'i
skus nam mkha' khyab pa gzigs/ de nas snang dgon par thugs dam la snying por mdzad nas bzhugs/ de'i tshe bdud dang srin po'i dmag 'jigs su rung bas bskor ba na/ nam mkha'
nas rdo rje shugs la gsol ba thob ces grag pa dang / rkang ba bcu drug pa lan gcig brjod pas dpal rdo rje shugs

mig gis blta mi bzod pa'i 'od zer 'bar ba dngos su gzigs ma thag dmag rnams byer te bar chad zhi/ bla brang ba bsod nams dpal 'byor la rim lnga'i khrid gnang ba'i tshe gsang
ba 'dus pa dngos su bstan/ gser phye 'bum pa'i drung du/ glang paNDi ta dang / bra gor mkhan chen pa chos dpal rgyal ba sogs sde snod 'dzin pa mang bo la dus 'khor gyi

mdzad pas sel/ chos rjer ston pa dang / mkhan chen nam mkha' dpal 'byor pa la mngon par mkhyen pa mang du gsungs pas mchog tu gus pa thob/ ngang rgyal ba rin chen blo

pa thob cing rgyal ba'i sras po 'di nyid kyi zhal sngar dbang rgyud lung man ngag dang bcas pa legs par mnos so//4)tsa mi lugs/dpal chen rgwa lo/bzhi pa tsa mi lugs ni/

byon nas/ rgyal po ra ma pA la la babs pas/ de na re khyed ci 'dod pa yin chos tshol na dpal na landa nas paNDi ta mang bo bzhugs/ de'i nang nas kyang tsa mi paNDi ta bya

rnams la byin brlabs bzhus/ de ltar yul kun bskor te/ a bha ya ma gtogs pa rgya gar na su che dris pas/ u rgyan na paNDi ta wA kI shwa ra ngag gi dbang phyug bya ba yod zer
bas der bzhud par dgongs te lam du zhugs kha tsam na/ paNDi ta gdugs spu re ba zhig na landar byon pa la su yin dris pas/ tsa mi'i slob ma u rgyan gyi paNDi ta wA gi shwa
ra yin/ sngon tsa mi la zhus pa'i dus 'khor gyi man ngag rnams phyogs gcig tu sdebs pa'i yi ge zhig zhur byon pa yin zer/ de la tsa mis sbyor ba'i phreng ba mdzad de gnang
/ da ni tsa mi dang a bha ya las che ba dzambU'i gling na ma rnyed ngo mtshar che snyam nas gser srang zhe bdun yod pa'i bcu bzhag so bdun la maNDal byas nas tsa mi la
phul te/ bdag la tshe 'di nyid la sangs rgyas pa'i gdams ngag dmigs pa spo mi dgos pa zhig zhu byas pas/ sbyor drug gi gdams ngag gnang ste/ na landa'i mtha' zhig na bod
kyi gnas go sa la kra ma zhes par 'dar 'byar dang smra bcad byas bsgom pa'i tshe/ grogs shig gis bos pas lan ma byung ba la/ khyed

kha rog par 'dug ste tu ru kSha'i dmag byung ngo byas pas/ khams 'dus nas 'dag sgo bshig te rdo rje gdan gyi gandho la'i steng du shor/ mkhas 'dus sol ba dang / slar yang 'dag
'byar byas nas sgrub pa lo phyed dang gsum mdzad pas/ rtags mang bo byung ba tsa mi la zhus pa dang / des a bha ya la bshad pas/ de bug sgor byon nas khyod la yon tan
'di 'dra ba byung ba bden nam gsung ba la/ de bden bzhus pas rtags kyi 'phro chad do// de tsa mi la zhus pas/ da dung yang bsgoms dang mi 'ong ba'i dgos med kyi rtags byung
ba na nga la yang ma smra gsung / slar yang lo drug bsgoms pas rtags dang yon tan sngar bas ches lhag pa 'khrungs/ sgrol ma byon nas bu bsil ba'i tshal du song la tshogs
kyi 'khor lo gyis dang dngos grub thob par 'gyur ro gsungs nas mi snang bar gyur/ de nas bla ma gnyis la bsil ba'i tshal du 'gro bar zhus pas ye ma gnang bas/ slar yang
lo gcig dang zla ba lngar bsgoms nas/ lhas lung bstan pa dang drod thob pa'i rtags rnams tsa mi la zhus nas dur khrod du 'gro ba'i bka' gnang

bar zhu byas pas/ 'o na srod la phyin na bzang gsungs gri gug bskur g.yog po nyams rtogs rtsal can cig btang nas tshogs dang gtor ma bzang po shom du bcug go/ de nas srod la
phyin te lam kha na dur khrod kyi bdag po zhing skyong gi rten shing nya gro dha'i sdong bo cig yod pa'i drung du bzhugs pas/ shing las tsheg sgra dang bcas te me 'bar
ba'i khrod nas/ khyod shing 'di dang lhan cig bcing ngo zer ba dang yar gzigs pas mi'i lus la phag gi mgo bo can cig snang ba la/ sprul pa'i gzugs ma ston par rang gzugs
ston gcig gsungs pas/ sdong bo'i rtsa ba nas sbrul ljang khu sbo dmar ba gdung tsam zhig byung ba shing de la 'khrigs nas song / nang par gyi dus su mdang gi g.yog po de
byung nas/ bar chad ma byung ngam zer ba la/ nga 'dra ba'i dpal he ru ka la sus bar chad byed pa gsungs/ de nas dus khrod kyi dkyil na nya gro dha'i phug ces pa shin tu 'jigs
pa zhig gi nang du byon te tshogs dang gtor ma bshams nas bzhugs pa'i dus su/ de'i phyi mtha' na ro langs sha za lce spyang thams cad

nga ro di ri ri sgrog cing mdun na lce spyang gsum nyal nas 'dug go/ der bsgoms pas ting nge 'dzin mi gsal zhing rgyang na nag yor yor zhig je cher song nas mdun du byung snyam
pa'i mod la/ nam mkha' la stug chom gyi sgra chen po grag/ yar gzigs pas mgo brnyan sna tshogs 'jigs su rung ba dag gis nam mkha' gang nas/ ha ha dang / phaT phaT dang
/ rgyob sod zer zhing mtshon cha sna tshogs 'phang bas skyi bud du song ngo // der 'jigs pa de rnams gang nas byung / gang na gnas gzigs pas ting nge 'dzin du lhan gyis
song ste tho rangs cho 'phrul rnams sangs pa na/ tshogs gtor rnams mi snang bar bdun (mdun )na dkar me re ba zhig 'dug pa la gzigs pa dang / thod pa chang gi gang ba zhig
tu song bas nged phan chad chang mi bzhes pa la/ de ni dpal chen po'i dngos grub tu dgongs nas gsol lo// de ma thag dpal 'khor lo sdom pa lha drug cu rtsa gnyis pa'i dkyil
'khor dur khrod dang bcas pa dngos su gzigs/ skad cig de nyid la de kho na

nyid mngon sum du rtogs/ sku lus kyi zag pa yang chad/ mes mi tshig chu la mi jing ba la sogs pa'i yon tan mang du brnyes/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma tsa muNDi byon te gtum
mo'i gdams ngag kyang gnang / nam langs pa dang lce spyangs sha za dug sbrul la sogs pas phyag dang mchod pa'i rnam 'gyur byed/ sngar gyi g.yog pos ma grongs par mthong nas
myur du log ste bla ma la zhus pas/ bla ma rnam gnyis der byon nas/ gos kyi khri la rgwa lo bzhugs su bcug ste/ a bha yas ni mgul nas 'khyud/ tsa mi ni spyi bos btugs
te dgyes pa'i gsungs bstsal/ de'i tshe khams pa me jo sras phrag dog skyes te/ ha ha rgwa chung bas kyang bsil ba'i tshal du bsgom na/ nga mi tshe sgom bzlas la bskyal bas
kho dang ci ma mnyam zhes zer nas der byung ba la/ dur khrod 'di ni shin tu gnyan pa zhig 'dug pas khyed 'dir bsdad na mi legs so gsungs pa de khros te log go/ de nas sangs
rgyas gdan bzhi zhes pa'i lha khang stong ba zhig tu bzhugs pas/ dbyug tho dang gri thod

thogs pa'i keng rus kyi mi bdun byung nas rna bar mda' 'dzugs pa la sogs pa'i cho 'phrul bstan yang / nyam nga ba ma skyes pas rus par spungs kyis song ngo // der gser 'od
dam pa nas bshad pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa bzhi'i zhal gzigs/ skabs shig na me jo sras gsang nas nya gro dha'i phug na 'dug pa tshor nas de shi dogs te byon tsa na kha bub
tu shi nas 'dug g.yog po cig rtse'u chung phrig phrig shi la shad 'dug pa la chos gos kyi thu ba rgyab pas sos te yul du bskyal lo// de nas nya gro dha'i phug gi g.yon na
rdo'i dbang phyug rang byung zhig yod pa'i steng du bzhugs pas/ nga yul 'di nas ma 'bud bya ba'i sgra zhig grag pa dang / rgyal po ra ma pA la dbang che ste ngas yul nas
phud do gsungs pas/ cung zhig na nam mkha' las 'ur sgra chen po dang / mu stegs pa'i lha dang mi'i dmag dpag tu med pas bskor byung ba la/ he ru ka spyan gsum par bstan
pas bros so// yang phug de'i g.yon na spyan ras gzigs kyi sku rang byon gcig yod pa'i drung du bsgoms pas/ spyan ras gzigs

dang / 'od zer can byon nas gdams ngag gnang / chos skyong gi rdo sku rang byon gyi drung du bzhugs pa na/ las mgon bya rog gdong can nam mkha' la byon pa la bstod pa mdzad/
sa la ye shes mgon po phyag bzhi pa byon pa la srog snying dang sgrub thabs la sogs pa zhus/ phyis tsa mi'i sgrub thabs dang zhus dag byas pas rtsa sngags dang srog snying
la khyad ma byung / de ltar bsil ba'i tshal du zla ba dgu bzhugs pas/ ma ga dha/ shar bhaM ga la/ lho ko sa la/ nub kha che dang u rgyan/ byang wa ra Na sI sogs rgya
gar bod rgya nag 'dzam bu gling thams cad du snyan pa'i grags pas khyab/ rgyal po ra ma pA las grub pa'i mtshan ma ston par zhus nas/ dur khrod kyi mtsho gnyan po zhig yod
pa'i 'gram du rgyal po dpung tshogs dang bcas pa dang / phyi nang gi paNDi ta mang bo dang / bltad mo ba mang po tshogs pa na/ mtsho'i steng du skyil dkrung bcas nas bzhugs
pas/ mu stegs pa rnams chu la mi 'bying ba rlung bsgoms pas 'od 'di la ngo mtshar ci che zer ba la/ rang 'dra'i sku bdun sprul te mu stegs pa sun phyung bas thams cad
'dud par gyur cing / rgyal pos

gdan drangs sku bkrus pa'i chus khrus 'thung byas pho brang la gtor/ glang bo che 'char byed la blud ma thag nges tu rukSha'i dmag pham par byas pas rgyal po mchog tu dad/
rdo rje gdan du shAkya thub pa'i zhal gzigs/ bya rgod phung bo'i ri bor zla ba gsum bzhugs dus u rgyan nas paNDi ta mang bo rgwa lo'i rdzu 'phrul blta ba la byon pa na/ bya
chen po zhig phur byung ba la lta stangs mdzad pas sa la lhung ste shi bas/ de rnams ma rangs pa dang se gol gcig togs pas 'phur nas song / der yang thub pa nyan thos
kyi dge 'dun dang bcas pa gzigs/ de nas na landar byon pa'i lam du mi thams cad kyis me tog gtor ba'i gseb tu ma thar te phyag dgos pa byung bas paNDi ta rnams sngan chad
'di 'dra ba'i mi thams cad dad cing 'dun pa 'ong ma myong zer/ grub thob 'gas kyang zhabs la btud do// ko sa la kra mar bzhugs dus rgya gar shar phyogs nas grub thob gsum
sogs rnal 'byor pa lnga brgya mjal du byung zhing / singgha la dang / gsang gling dang / zangs gling la sogs pa'i gling phran drug gi tshong ba

mang pos kyang nor bu phul te/ de rnams su yang grags pas khyab/ de nas bod du byon te la stod dge phug tu lo gsum bzhugs dus/ ma jo lha gcig ma zhes pa srog chags gso ba'i
chos log spyod pa zhig 'dul ba'i ched du dge phug gi brag logs kyi sna ba cig la sdigs mdzub mdzad pas thang la lhung ste shi/ slar se gol togs pas gsos pa sogs rdzu 'phrul
gyis de yang dag pa'i lam la bcud der khams pa a seng la sbyor drug gnang / ma la yer bab la bde mchog gnang / sa skyar rje sa chen la ma rgyud kyai rdo rje'i sbyor drug
gnang / gang du byon par khrom ches pas mi shogs pa tsam byung / de nas dbus su byon dus gtsang bo la mnyen pas gru ma btang bas chu'i steng du skyil mo dkrung mdzad
nas byon/ byang se mo do la lo lnga bzhugs/ der rmon 'dor ba khu sgom dang / byang chub sems dpa' stag ston rnams sbyor drug gi gdams pas grol bar mdzad/ don grub kyi zhal
gzigs/ klu'i yul du'ang byon te klu rnams la'ang chos bstan/ gnam rtse ldang du gser brdzangs pa'i

drin bzor lo gnyis bzhugs/ rgwa ston dang / dpal phag mo grub pa la gdams pa gnang / 'phan yul rgyal du dus gsum mkhyen pa la gdams pa gnang / byang gi 'bab rong du lo gcig
mdo khams skam po gangs rar lo bdun bzhugs/ mdo smad du byon nas yab yum ni mi bzhugs/ mkhan po la gdams ngag phog ste nyams rtogs la bkod/ sbyor drug gi gdams pas 'bri
lung du slob ma grub pa thob pa bdun byung / rgya nag rgyal pos gdan 'dren byung bas de la bros nas yar byon/ mdo khams sgang du mi nag pos chos bsnubs pa rnams btul te thams
cad chos la bkod/ stong tshar lha khang dang rab sgang sba mda'i gtsug lag khang sogs lha khang bshig pa thams cad bsos/ khams kyi nag chu la skyil dkrung gis phar chod
tshur chod mdzad pas/ phrang de la phyin chad 'dul ba la dgra med par mdzad/ nag shod du zhang la sbyor drug gnang / de nas yang 'bab rom dang mgor 'dzong brag sogs su
bzhugs te/ sku'i bkod pa gsum ston pa/ zhal gyi dkyil 'khor nam mkha' ltar che ba/ sku bgres gzhon sna tshogs su ston pa la

sogs pa'i cho 'phrul sna tshogs pa stan nas 'gro ba mang po rdo rje'i theg pa la bkod pas/ slob ma'i tshogs grub pa thob pa mang du byung / gya dgu pa la rtse shod rangs rdzong
mgor rdo rje'i skyil dkrung las mi g.yo bar shing bal ltar yang ba'i sku gdung bzhag ste mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan to// gdung bzhugs la phul ba'i du ba la ngo
mtshar ba'i ltas du ma byung ngo // rje sa skya pa chen pos dpal rgwa lo la sbyor drug gsan nas/ ma rgyud kyai rdo rje'i sbyor drug ces pa'i yi ge yang mdzad de/ slob
dpon bsod nams rtse mo dang / rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan la gnang / khyad par du rje btsun la bu ngas khyod la chos bstan pa thams cad 'dir 'dus pa yin te/ byang chub
sems kyi bdag nyid dngos/ dngos po'i chos nyid gdan du bya/ 'byung ba rlung la sbar zin bya/ gtum mo'i drod rab tu bskyed/ byang chub chu rgyun dbu mar bzhugs/ sa sogs
'byung ba dbang du bsdus/ ye shes lnga ni sngon gyur nas/ 'chi ba med pa'i gnas thob po/ zhes gsungs te/ rkang ba dang po gnyis kyis sor bsam/ gsum pas

srog rtsol/ bzhi pa'i 'dzin pa/ lnga bas rjes dran/ drug pas ting nge 'dzin/ tha ma gnyis kyis grub pa ye shes kyi sku bstan to// de nas sa skya paNDi ta/ rgyus pa gzhon nu
seng ge/ dol po ye shes mgon po/ kun spangs chen po rnams rim par brgyud de sbyor drug sa lugs zhes grags so//grub thob khams pa a seng /grub thob khams pa a seng ni/ mang
du thos pa'i mkhas pa phyis rgwa lo la gdams pa gsan nas sgrub pa la rtse gcig tu bzhugs te/ lo re la zla gcig zhag bcu gsum gzhan la chos gsungs/ gzhan du sgom 'ba' zhig
mdzad pas grub pa brnyes so// des phywa ba chen kyi sengge myang bran chos ye/ skyi pho tshul 'phags/ khams pa lo tsA ba ston 'dum/ phag mo grub pa/ dus gsum mkhyen pa/
g.yor/ gnyan/ smog cog pa sogs mang po la/ rtsa ma'i sbyor drug rtsa 'grel/ sbyor phreng rtsa 'grel/ snying po gsum rtsa 'grel gyi sgo nas gdams pa gnang ste grol bar
mdzad do//bla ma zhang g.yu brag pa/bla ma zhang g.yu brag pa ni/ yul gung thang tsha ba gru/ yab zhang sna nam rdo rje sems dpa'/

yum ban de mo mang skyid kyi sras su chu mo yos kyi lo la sku bltams/ rngog mdo sde dang / sampu lo tsA ba las slob gnyer mdzad/ nyer drug pa la khams su byon/ dkon brtsegs
gzigs pas nges 'byung lhag par skyes nas dge slong chig rdzogs su mdzad/ mtshan brtson 'grus grags par btags/ sum pa rgya shod kyi lkog skye'u dgon par bzhugs dus/ dpal
chen po rgwa lo 'byon pa yod zer 'ur chen po byung bas bsil ba'i tshal du spyod pa la gshegs pa de yin nam byas pas yin zer/ gdams ngag ma gnang yang thub la 'changs pa rang
gis chog snyam nas drung du 'gro rtsis byas pas nga de zla ba gcig na sog tu 'byon zer bas/ de nas rim gyis nag shod drab mkhar du phyin pas/ bla ma khrom chen po dang
