bcas te byon/ zhang gis dung mkhan byas te yul mi rnams kyi bsu ba byas pas/ zhal mthong ma thag lus skyi bung song nas snang ba log gis 'gyur/ sems nyid nam mkha' lta
bur phyal gyis song / mi rnams klag cor zer yang rmi lam lta bur mthong / bde gsal gyi nyams myong ngo mtshar ba skyes te byin brlabs zhus/

de'i phyi de nub khrom rnams gyes pa dang / bla ma mjal te za 'og yul gcig dang mar tshud cig phul nas/ sangs rgyas thob par byed pa'i thabs khyed rang gi thugs nyams su bzhes
pa de thugs la gdags par zhu/ phyags phyir 'breng ba yin zhus pas/ nga la yi dam gyi lha kha mig rna ba can med/ stong ba nyid dang snying rje zung 'jug tu bsgom pa yin
pas khyod rang de bsgoms shig gdams ngag nges tshar ro// nge'i phyir 'breng na nga 'dag sbyar byed/ 'khor rnams la la sprad du 'gro/ la las par 'gyes pa yin/ khyod rang
ltogs te shi bar 'ongs gsung bas/ chos phyir 'chi nus na phyag phyir 'deng gsung bar go nas shin tu dga' nas yod tsam na/ bu ram la go snyod btab pa'i thang zhig gsol gyin
'dug pa gnang byung ba 'thungs/ phor pa sa la bzhag pas btsun pa zhig gis blangs nas lhag de byogs/ de la ster ba min gsung / de nas yang da mi lto gsung bas/ gsol ras
gnang ba de gdams ngag thun mong ma yin pa khyod la sbyin bya bar go/ mi ster ba yin bya ba de gzhan la bshad ma ran bya bar

go/ nga ma lto gsung ba de bshad kyi mi lto gsung bar go/ de nas phyag phyir 'brangs te rtag tu maNDal phul zhing gsol ba btab pas/ thog mar rlung la sems 'dzin pa'i man ngag
gnang / dbang bskur gcig gnang bar zhus pas/ nga'i dbang yon la ja sig bzhi bzhi dngul bre bzhi bzhir phab yod pa 'byor na bya gsung / grub thob yin pas brdas mdzad par
go nas/ de rnams yid kyis phul te phul zin lags zhus pas/ byar btub khyod kyi pha de yang de 'dra 'byor 'byor ba 'dug gsung / der bde mchog gi dbang bskur/ rtsa mi'i sems
sbyong rin po che'i phreng ba/ yi ge nyer gsum pa dang lhas skyes rnams gnang / spyir rdul tshon dang ras bris la brten pa'i dbang gnyis ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang bskur
gsum/ dbang gong ma yongs su rdzogs pa gcig rlung bum pa can/ gtum mo'i gdams pa gnang / de nas lkog skye'u dgon par mtshams bcad rlung bum pa can dang / lus spyod la 'bungs
pas nyams myong dang mthong snang gi bye brag mang po byung ste rlung nam gzung tsam na 'od kha dog sna tshogs pa dang / me sla nga tsam pa dang / lag pa nag po gnyis
kyis mgo nas mar bsdams

nas ma phrel ba dang / nag po bskor ling zhig gi dkyil na mi thod skam po rtsig ge ba dang / sbar gnag po'i dkyil na mig dmar rtse re sogs byung bas/ nag shod ri dpung du bla
ma la zhus pas/ 'od de rlung gi 'byung ba 'khrugs pa'i 'od yin/ thod pa de rtsa nang du rlung chud pa'i brtags yin/ mig dmar rtse re ba de la mdzu gu tshugs/ 'tsho ba
ngan pas lan pa yin gsung / mar khu dang thud yod tshad 'tshal ba yin te zhus pas/ des mi phan rab tu byung ba sha mi za yang sha dang rus pa phan/ ci ri ri za/ ci ri ri
sgom dgos pa yin/ khams sos pa dang 'phro chod gsung nas/ se khyims su sbyor ba yan lag drug gi khrid gnang / thams cad bor la 'bad 'bungs thon la bsgoms dang 'phro ma bcad
par byas pas nga gzong gsha' ma 'ong ba yin gsungs/ rtse gcig tu bsgoms pas nyams kyi klong rdol/ mgon po mgul khug ma dang mi g.yo ba dang chab gtor bA su ki gsan/ de
nas yab sras 'grogs te dbus su byon/ rang yul tsha ba gru ra gdan grangs nas bsnyen bskur

mthon po mdzad/ de dus bla mas zhal ras kyis nam mkha' khyab pa'i rdzu 'phrul bstan/ yer par byon dus spos kha dang 'brom dang glang ra rnams su sku'i bkod pa re re dus gcig
la bstan/ de nas sgo la la byon nas gsum phreng gi bar du bla ma'i phyag phyi mdzad/ yul du 'gro bar zhus pas/ bla mas skud cig gnang nas/ 'o 'di la lo gsum gyi sgom rgyags
kyis/ lo gsum na nga mgor 'dzod brag la bsdod dus shog gsungs nas bla ma 'bab rom du bzhud/ de nas yul du byon te bya mkhar sogs ri khrod 'grim zhing bsgoms pas/ sngar
bla ma thugs log 'dug snyam pa'i log rtogs lan cig byung ba'i rten 'brel gyis/ skabs zhig tu thig le'i gegs zhig byung ba/ mal yer ba la gegs sel zhus pas/ da res kyi
gegs 'di nA ro pa'i gdams ngag cig gis sel bar 'dug gtan du nam yang bla ma dpal chen po'i gdams ngag las lhag pa med pas de rang bsgom dgos so gsungs nas gtum mo dang gegs
sel gnang / lo gsum na mgor 'dzod la byon/ bla ma dang mjal bas shin tu

mnyes te ston chung nga'i zla la nyol gsungs nas bla ma'i 'dab tu nyal/ khyod do nub bsgoms shig gsung pa la thang chad pas mnal ba 'od gsal 'ba' zhig tu song / nam langs pa
dang / bla ma rnams gdams ngag so so yin kyang byin brlabs gcig tu 'ong / nyams la bogs shig thon 'dug gsungs/ bla ma khri'i steng na bzang po'i 'dug stangs mdzad/ spyan
gsum yod pa'i dbus ma'i spyan 'bras kham chil le ba chil le ba gcig gzigs/ de nas bla sku 'da' tshul ma bstan gyi bar du zhabs tog byas te gdams ngag lhag ma rnams zhus/
bya mkhar phug tu bsgoms pas drod la bsten nas zhabs la tsher ma zug pa yang bde bar lhang lhang song / lan cig rkyen ci yang med par snang ba thams cad nam mkha' sprin
dwangs pa bzhin bun gyis song / sems skye 'gag gnas gsum dang bral ba nam mkha' lta bur rtogs/ gdod ma nyid nas dngos po thams cad rtogs/ shes sogs mgur yang gsungs/ de
nas dwags po sgom tshul gyi drung du byon pas/ 'o khyod bla ma dpal chen po lta bu bsten nas thugs ma tshim mam

gsungs/ bla ma tshim pa min te/ dogs pa zhig gcod du 'ongs pa lags zhus pas/ phyag rgya chen po'i gdams ngag gcig gnang / bsam gtan gyi shes rab dang rtog dpyod kyi yan lag
mthar phyin/ rgya gar bai ro tsa na badzra dang / gshen dgon dkar ba dang / 'ol kha ba rnams la gdams pa mang du gsan/ de nas g.yu brag la sogs pa'i sgrub gnas lang bor
sgrub pa rtse gcig tu mdzad pas grub pa brnyes/ tshal gung thang btab/ gzhan don dpag tu med pa mdzad de don gnyis pa chu mo glang la sku gshegs so//sras lha phyug pa/de'i
thugs kyi sras lha phyug pa ni/ dol zhugs gyi na lung du yab sngags 'chang sangs rgyas skyabs/ yum mtshur mo shes rab skyid kyi sras su me pho stag la 'khrungs/ gdung ba
zig rngog mdo sde la kyai rdor gsan/ bcu drug pa la g.yu brag tu bla ma zhang la sems bskyed thob/ nyer bdun pa la nges 'byung skyes te gnyal du byon nas lo ro chu khyer
ba'i drung du byon/ de dus bla ma zhang shin tu dren pa byung te/ zla ba phyed tsam na tshur log nas zhang sgrags/ mda' na chos gsung ba'i dus su chu mo sbrul gyi lo

la mjal/ da lta rang sangs rgya bas chos cig zhu byas pas zhang mnyes nas de nyid du sngon 'gro'i gdams pa dang / ngar phug tu phyag chen gyi khrid tshar bar gnang / sum cu
pa la sha mi 'dul 'dzin gyis mkhan po zhang gi las slob mdzad nas lha sar bslab pa chig rdzogs mdzad/ zhang gi gsung nas nyi zla ltar sems can gyi don byed pa cig 'ong zhes
mtshan yang nyi zla 'od du btags/ mkhan po la 'dul ba gsan cing lag len byang la slab pa la gces spras che bar mdzad pas 'dul ba 'dzin par grags/ yab yum sku mched rnams
grongs pa dang yul zhing btsongs nas spong thag mdzad de bla ma zhang la ma lus par phul/ lto gos la gyong khur te/ zhang gi phyag phyir 'brengs nas/ rdul tshon dang
ras khris la brten pa'i dbang nyer lnga mchog dbang dang bcas pa thob/ dpal rgwa lo'i gdams pa ma lus pa thob nas/ mngon mtshan ci chung chung byas te/ gcig pur brtson 'grus
drag pos bsgoms pas nyams rtogs kyi 'ur rdol/ res spyis khungs la sogs pa ri khrod 'grims zhing / res

phyag phyir 'brengs te lo nyer gcig gi bar du bla ma zhang bsten/ zhang gi chos skor ma lus pa thob/ nga la bla ma zhang gcig pus chog chos kyang 'di'i chos gcig pus chog snyam
nas su la yang chos 'brel ma zhus ba yul dang ba lam mtha' brag dang 'ju phu chu bzang dpal rdzong la sogs pa'i ri khrod rnams su sgrub pa rtse gcig tu mdzad pas grub
pa brnyes/ ba lam phur lha phyug mkhar zhes pa'i dgon gnas btab nas slob ma skal  ldan mang du 'dus pa la bla ma zhang gi phyag len bzhin gdul bya thun mong ba la dpal
sgam po pa'i chos skor dang / thun mong ma yin pa la dpal rgwa lo'i chos skor gyis smin grol du mdzad cing / gung thang du'ang gdan sa lo lnga mdzad de bla ma'i 'phrin las
rgyas par mdzad do// des zur stengs pa/ des dol pa ye shes mgon po/ des kun spangs chen po la gnang ba nas rim par brgyud de tsa mi'i sbyor drug sde skor/ sbyor phreng
/ rlung sbyor bzhi pa/ rtsa mi'i sbyor drug rgyas pa/ 'bring po nor bu 'don pa'i dpes bstan pa/ 'khrul 'khor nyer lnga pa/ bsdus pa snying po gsum dang / don dam bzhir dbye
ba chu bo'i

dpes bstan pa/ bcud len/ gegs sel/ nyams rtogs bstan pa rnams la tsa mi lugs su grags/ rgwa lo'i sbyor drug gi man ngag de kho na nyid kyi man ngag rnal 'byor gyi de kho na
nyid kyi man ngag 'chi ba brtag pa/ 'pho ba'i man ngag rnams la rgwa lugs su grags/ zhang gi khrid skor rnams la tshal lugs su grags pa rnams byung ngo //yang bla ma zhang
/ khams pa ras tshang ba/ khams pa ras chen/ 'dag sbyar ba byang chub 'bum/ de la kun spangs chen pos tsa mi'i sbyor phreng gsan no//rong gling lo tsA ba/rong gling lo
tsA ba ni/ gnyal rong gling du 'khrungs/ rus rong po/ rten dge bsnyen/ mtshan rdo rje dbang phyug ma ga dhar byon nas a bha ya dang tsa mi la gtugs te gzhung gdams ngag
mang du gsan cing / khyad par du dus 'khor la mkhas par gyur nas bod du phebs te/ rong gling du sogs ka zhes pa'i gnas btab ste 'gro don mdzad do//steng lo tshul khrims 'byung
gnas/steng pa lo tsA ba tshul khrims 'byung gnas sbas pa ni/ gnyal

smad dge ri'i 'dab tu yab steng pa tog 'bar dang / yum mtha' mo bu skyid kyi sras su me mo phag la 'khrungs/ gdung rus ga rod/ dgung lo drug pa'i tshe gyang bug cig na phar
bltas pas mchod rten dang bcas pa'i yul khams mang po mthong / phyis rgya gar du byon dus de ka bzhin du 'dug gsung / mi g.yo ba la bsnyen pa dum re byas pas ngag nus che
bar byung / ma yar sdad pas lo bcu gsum pa la dwags por byon klog bslabs shing klog 'don byas pa'i rnyed pa pha'i khyim du bskyal bas pha yang 'bar/ skyo ba skyes nas dwags
por byon/ skan mo gnas brtan la skra bcad/ bco lnga la myang stod du rgya 'dul las rab tu byung / mchims thams cad mkhyen pa la spyod phyogs bslabs/ bcu dgu la rgyas
mkhan po/ gnyal ba dge 'dun skyabs kyis las slob/ skyi pho tshul 'phags kyis gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ nyi shu pa la rgya gar du 'byon bzhengs nas ding rir
phebs pa na spyan ras gzigs kyi mi zhig tu sprul nas lam gyi rgyus bshad/ de

nas ma ga dhar byon te tsa mi la gtugs nas sgra tshad sde snod mang po dang / khyad par du dus 'khor la mkhas par sbyangs/ de dus gcung chos 'bar gyis gser mang po khyer nas
bskyal/ de yang slob gnyer la btsud pas paNDi ta mkhas pa zhig byung ste tshangs pas grongs/ 'da' khar khyed kyis nga'i rus pa bod du skyel dgos zer mna' bkag pas sum cu
pa la bod du byon/ dge ri gnas su gcung gi gdung khang bzhengs/ slar rgya gar du byon te tsa mi mi bzhugs pas gdung la mchod pa phul/ lo lngar paN chen bcu gsum la mang
du gsan/ khyad par du bha ska ra gupta la dus 'khor gsan/ kha che spyan gsum pa'i brgyud pa a langka de wa dang / shrI la tsandra spyan drangs/ rgya dpe mi khur bcu bdun
bsnams/ dus 'khor rgyud 'grel/ gsang 'dus 'phags skor/ nyi khri gzhung 'grel/ 'dul ba rang 'grel/ skyes rabs/ sgrub thabs bsdus pa chen po sogs gzhi 'gyur dang 'gyur bcos
mang du

mdzad/ yang rgya gar du byon nas bye brag bshad mdzod chen mo 'bum gsum gyi yig tshogs yod pa lo gsum gyi bar du bslabs/ rten rang byung brgyad cu dang / srin pos ma hA bho
dhi la mchod pa byed pa'i bkod pa gzigs/ bsil ba tshal du gur mgon dang / na lan dar phyag bzhi pa dang / de wa ri Shir dbyangs can ma gzigs/ a langka de wa dang lhan cig
bod du byon nas bshad mdzod kyi 'gyur sum gnyis tsam grub pa na paN chen sku gshegs/ mdang du chos 'khor che ba zhig mdzad/ mchod rten bzhengs/ bal por byon nas rdo rje
gdan du mar me'i rgyu gser dang / kha cher gdung skal brdzangs/ slar dge ri dben tshar bzhugs bde mchog lha drug cu'i zhal gzigs/ gro lung ba chen po sogs mkhas pa che dgu'i
zhabs la gtugs/ bstan pa'i bdag por gyur nas gya bzhi pa lcags pho khyi la gshegs/ gdung las rten ring bsrel mang du byon/ slob ma yang chag lo dgra bcom dang po thams
cad mkhyen

pa dang / rong lo'i dbon po rgyal ba rnal 'byor dang / dben tsha ba sogs mang du byung ngo // khams pa she'u lo tsA ba/ a bha ya dang tsa mi gnyi ga la dbang rgyud bshad man
ngag dang bcas pa zhus/ de la rgya pho ba lung bas dbang yongs su rdzogs pa zhus/ de la snye mdo thams cad mkhyen pas dgung lo zhe gcig bzhes pa'i tshe zhus/ de nas snye
mdo kun dga' don grub/ karma pa rang byung rdo rje nas deng sang gi bar dbang rgyun ma chad par yod do//se lo tsA ba gzhon nu tshul khrims/se lo tsA ba gzhon nu tshul khrims
ni/ rgya gar du byon te rtsa mi chen po gtso bor bstan nas rgyud bshad tshar gnyis/ a bha ya la tshar gcig a bhi yugta ya tshar gcig bhAkSha ra guptal tshar gcig gsan/
dbang rgyuud man ngag mtha' dag la mnga' brnyes nas bod du phebs dus la stod byang gi gnyos ston 'od ma zhes pa bgres po zhig gis de lo gsum bsten nas rgyud 'grel gsan
zhing nan tan che bar mdzad/ se mo dbus su gshegs pa'i shul du mgo ba la dkar

bkus/ se lo yar byon dus dri gtugs mdzad pas the tshom med par legs par mkhyen/ dag bshad man ngag ma lus pa thob/ se lo ni rgya gar du gshegs so// 'od ma la slob ma dus 'khor
ba bkra shis rin chen dang / gnyos sgom gnyis las/ gnyos sgom ni sgom pas grub pa thob te sa 'og gi gtegs mthong ba sogs kyi yon tan dang ldan no// bkra shis rin chen
gyis 'od ma lo bcu gnyis kyi bar du bstan nas sbyangs pas bum pa gang byo yod pa'i steng du/ rwa 'bro gyi jo sogs kyi bka' yang gsan te rang las lhag pa mi 'dug gsung /
de la bstod byang gi dus 'khor ba sangs rgyas rdo rjes tshar sum cu rtsa gnyis mnyan pas bum pa gang byor mkhyen/o rgyan pa rin chen dpal/de la o rgyan pas gsan te/ de ni
yul la stod lho/ yab rus jo phan dang / yum sdug ge la sras bzhi'i gcen po che ba go lung pa mdo sde dpal rgyam mtshan/ gsum pa rje 'di yin te lcags pho stag la 'khrungs/
lo bdun pa la/ khu bo go lung pa jo btsun nam mkha' rgyal mtshan la/ bde dgyes ma phugs sogs gsan/ rgod tshang pa la dge

bsnyen mnos/ bcu drug pa bo dong er byon nas mngon grwa pa rin rtse la phar tshad mngon sum bslabs/ nyi shu pa la rin rtses mkhan po/ zhang bsam gling bas las slob/ bsod nams
'od zer bas gsang ston mdzad nas bsnyen par rdzogs/ mtshan rin chen dpal du gsol/ de nas lo bcu gnyis su sngor kar gdan gcig mdzad/ rin rtse la dus 'khor 'bro lugs gsan
pas/ rin rtse'i zhal nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi chos gzhan thams cad shes par bya yi/ dus 'khor zhog zer na nga mi byed gsung bas dad pa lhag par skyes/ gcen po go lung
pa mdo sde dpal rgyal mtshan la/ phar phyin 'dul ba/ rgyud sde mang po'i dbang rgyud man ngag gsan/ khyad par dus 'khor cha lugs legs par bslabs/ rtsis la sbyangs shing
mkhas par mkhyen/ khong gi gsung gis/ dus 'khor ba sangs rgyas rdo rje de tsa mi lugs la mkhas pas der nyon gsung bas/ la stod byang gi dgon pa rnal 'byor mangs su de'i
drung du byon/ zla ba bcu gcig gi bar du rgyud 'grel phran dang

bcas pa gsan/ der khong chos bcag nas/ ser chags la byon pa la/ thugs skyo nas dam pa sangs rgyas la gsol ba btab pas mnal lam du mjal zhing lung yang bstan/ bde chen stengs
su rgod tshang pa'i drung du byon pas phebs ma thag ro gcig gi rtogs pa 'khrungs/ bdag shambha lar dus 'khor gyi dka' phreng ma bde ba rnams gcod pa la 'gro zhus pas/ shambha
lar 'brel ba med u rgyan dang 'brel ba yod pas der byon/ ma bde ci 'dra yod gsung pa la/ dka' phreng 'ga' zhig zhus pas/ lan ji lta ba bzhin du gnang byung / dus 'khor
ni ma gsan 'di 'dra ba'i mkhas pa 'ong ba tsug lags zhus pas/ nga shrI rir bsdad dus rdo rje rnal 'byor mas po ti cig byin pa ming pa'i snang ba byung bas bod du 'gyur
ba'i chos la mi shes pa med gsungs/ 'o na bdag la dus 'khor gyi dbang cig zhu zhus pas/ gsol ba thob la rmi lam zungs shig gsungs/ gsol ba btab pas mnal lam du chos rje
nyid dus 'khor ba sangs rgyas rdo rje'i cha byad du mdzad nas dbang rgyas pa gcig gnang / sang de

drung du byon pas slob dpon jo btsun thugs tshim mam gsung / de nas u rgyan du 'gro bar zhus nas dang por byang mi med kyi ri la sgrub pa la byon nas zla ba dgu bzhugs pas
sngar gyi chos brjed pa thams cad sos/ de nas ti ser byon pas rten 'brel shar nas bstan bcos phyi nang gsal ba zhes pa mdzad/ de nas dpal ye dang 'grogs nas byon te 'jigs
pa'i phrang mang po bcad/ khyad par sog po'i rta ba bzhis skyigs brdungs pas rlung dbu mar chud/ de ma thag bzhengs te bka' bskyon drag po phab pas de rnams skrag te bros/
chu bo sindhi'i 'gram du gnam sa go log 'gyur ba'i nyams shar/ de nas u rgyan dhu ma tha lar phebs/ der rdo rje rnal 'byor ma smad 'tshong ma'i bu mo'i gzugs su byas pa
cig gis tshod ma phor ba gang byin zhing byin gyis brlabs pas las kyi sgrib pa'i lhag ma thams cad slong shing zad/ rdo rje gsum gyi don ji lta ba bzhin du thugs la 'khrungs/
rdo rje rnal 'byor ma nyid kyis sku sindhu ra'i mdog can dngos su bstan nas seng ge'i 'o ma lta bu sbyor ba yan lag drug gi gdams pa gnang /

rdo rje gsum gyi bsnyen bsgrub ces su btags/ sku lus zag med rdo rje'i skur gyur/ tshur lam kha cher byon dus paN chen bhU mi shrI la chos gsan/ kha che'i rgyal pos gsod mi
btang yang skrong ma nus/ mnga' ris su bla chen de khyim gyi gces phrug brgya dus gcig la phul ba rab tu byung / de nas rgod tshang pas lung bstan ltar zhe bzhi pa la rgya
gar la byon/ ti ra hu tir ram shing rgyal po brtul shugs kyis btul/ rdo rje gdan du nub sgo nas byon nas byang chub kyi shing gzigs ma thag dad pa drag pos sku lus brdabs
shing phyag btsal bas rlung sems dbu mar chud/ kun rdzob byang chub kyi sems bcos min du 'khrungs/ tshogs kyi bdag pos srog snying phul/ bsil ba tshal gyi zhing skyong
dam la btags/ de nas bod du byon te lam du chu la mi 'byings pa dang / stag la rengs pa'i sbyor ba mdzad/ rdo rje gsum gyi bsnyen bsgrub kyis skal ldan mang po smin grol
la bkod/ ngas khrid btab na lung pa grub thob kyis 'gengs par 'dug te rgod tshang pa'i khrid srol la gnod par 'dug gsungs nas bka' rgya gdams/ bde chen du bstan

ma bcu gnyis kyis stod hor bzlog par gsol ba btab/ dbyangs can ma'i pi wang gi sgra gsan/ bal bo rdzong gi shar phyogs gal por 'byung bo 'dul byed kyi zhal gzigs mang yul kos
kar phug tu rnal 'byor mas rdo rje gsum gyi bsnyen bsgrub yi ger 'god pa rdzas su gnang / slar yang rdo rje gdan du byon te ma hA bo dhi la mchod pa mdzad/ de na grub
chen man lungs pa lho phyogs be dharbha'i yul du 'byon pa'i rim gror ston pa'i tshems la sku khrus gsol zhing bzhugs 'dug pa la bstod pa mdzad/ rgyal bu thams cad sgrol gyi
bzhugs gnas a yi ga sarba ta gzigs de nas bod du byon dus kyi rong nags su bho paNDi ta la chang skyug pa'i sbyor ba mdzad/ ri bo shar gangs kyi mgul du bde mchog gi zhal
gzigs/ de nas dbus su byon nas mtshur phur karma pa shi la karma pa'i chos skor gsan/ dbu zhwa zhwa nag kyang gnang / nga gsum pa chu pho rta la bsam yas su bstan rtsis
mdzad/ de'i phyi lo la yar klungs mdo mkhar du snye mdo ba sku mched dang chag lo'i

dbon po sogs la dus 'khor gyi dbang mdzad pa'i tshe rdzu 'phrul mang du bstan/ de dang g.ya' bzang su rgyud bshad gnang / g.ye rong du yar lha sham pos bsu ba byas/ de nas
gnyal du byon te zom phud du chom rkun rjes su bzung / de nas gnyal smad lte'u rar byon te phyag rdzas tshan che ba yod pa rnams/ mkhan chen gtsang pa la gtad nas de'i zhig
gsos kyi rkyen la sbyar/ lo ro dang mtsho sna'i bar du byon nas gzhan don sa 'ur dang rdo 'ur du mdzad/ phyir hor rgyal lo go se las spyan drangs nas hor yul du byon/
rgyal po la rin po che 'ba' zhig gi rdul tshon gyi dus kyi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur/ rdul tshon rnams chu bor dor/ dngos po'i bzung ba khab tsam yang med par
phyir byon/ brgyad cu pa sa mo bya la gshegs so//de'i slob ma'i gtso bo ni/ rdo rje rnal 'byor mas lung bstan pa'i slob ma rin po che mkhar chu ba/ snye mdo kun dga' don
grub/ karma pa rang byung rdo rje/ bla ma dbu ma pa/ mkhan chen bsod nams 'od zer/ rtogs ldan zla ba sengge/ gser khang pa sogs

byung / mkhar chu ba chos bsam 'od ni/ g.ya' bzang gi gdan sa lo bco brgyad mdzad pa'i dus su/ o rgyan pa g.ya' bzang su gdan drangs/ dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud bshad/ khyad
par du bsnyen sgrub gsan nas lho brag mkhar chur rtse gcig tu bsgoms pas bsgrub pa brnyes so//snye mdo ba/snye mdo ba ni/ yab mes sngags rnying ma'i rgyud pa/ gdung rabs
nyi shu rtsa lnga'i bar du sngags rgyud zam ma chad par byang ba'i rigs can/ sngags 'chang bkra shis grags la sras gsum byung ba'i che ba rtse sgang pa/ bar pa zhig po nyi
seng / chung ba mkhas pa brtson seng dang gsum 'khrungs/ brtson seng snye mdor bzhugs pa la sras snye mdo thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams dpal byung / de dang yum sngags
skyes kyi rnal 'byor ma dbang phyug skyid la sras gsum 'khrungs pa'i che ba kun dga' bzang po rgod tshang pa'i skye ba yin/ yab dang o rgyan pa la dus 'khor gsan pas mkhas
par mkhyen/ bar pa kun dga' mgon po/ chung ba kun mkhyen kun dga' don grub pa ni/ sa pho 'brug la 'khrugs/ lo bcu

tshun yab kyi drung du dus 'khor sogs gsar rnying gi bka' lung phal cher gsan/ yab 'das nas gcen kun bzang ba la dus 'khor/ bde dgyes/ gsang 'dus mA yA gdan bzhi mdo sgyu sems
gsum gyi gzhung gdams ngag dang bcas pa dang / zhi byed rgyud pa gsum gsan/ yab kyi bu chen rnams las kyang slob gnyer mthar phyin par mdzad/ bco lnga pa la grub chen
o rgyan pa dang mjal/ de'i phyi lo la g.ya' bzang dang mdo mkhar du grub chen pa la dbang rgyud bshad tshar gnyis man ngag dang bcas pa rdzogs par gsan/ o rgyan pa'i bu
chen gzhon nu dpal la bde mchog snyan ngag dbyangs 'char sogs gsan/ bcu bdun pa la chad dmar ba la phreng bskor gsum/ rngog chos/ sa skya pa'i chos skor/ phyag chen gsan/
lo de nyid la gtsang du byon nas mkhan po khro phu ba bsod nams seng ge dang / brag ram gyi dbu ma pa shes rab 'bum gyi drung du rab tu byung / mkhan po la khro phu ba'i
chos skor dang / slob dpon la dbu ma gsan/ o rgyan pa'i gsung la brten nas grags pa snye mdor gdan drangs nas rgyud 'grel

man ngag dang bcas pa dang / dbang rdo rje phreng ba gsan/ gzhan yang thar lo/ g.yag sde lo tsA ba'i thugs sras dpen lung pa/ snar thang pa dpon mgon/ rgyal tsha lung mang
po/ bla ma so pa/ tshal yang dgon pa/ karma pa shi/ 'bri khung pa rdo rje rin chen bsten nas rig pa'i gnas lnga la mkhas par sbyangs/ sbyor drug dang / zhi phyag rdzogs gsum
gyi skor thams cad la rdo rus 'phrod par sgrub pa snying por mdzad pas mnyam rjes med pa'i thugs la 'khrungs/ yi dam gyi lha dpag tu med pa'i zhal gzigs/ chos rje rang
byung rdo rje/ gsang phu ba yon tan dpal/ snar thang pa sangs rgyas dpal/ la stod pa rin smon/ mdo smad pa ting 'dzin bzang po sogs mkhas btsun mang po la dus 'khor la
sogs pa'i 'phrin las bskyangs/ si ta rin chen grags pa dang / g.yu sbyin dang / du wen sha sogs dpon che dgu mang po smin par mdzad/ chos 'byung / bsdus rgyud kyi sa bcad/
Ti kA/ mngon dkyil/ khrid yig sogs bstan bcos mang du mdzad de re gcig pa sa pho 'brug

la me tog gi char dang bcas te mya ngan las 'das so//chos rje karma pa rang byung rdo rje/chos rje karma pa rang byung rdo rje ni/ rje btsun mi la'i 'khrungs yul la stod rtse'i
phur shing pho spre'u la 'khrungs/ dgung lo lnga na o rgyan pa dang mjal zhing / bdag gi zhwa nag khyer shog gsungs nas gung la bzhugs pa na/ khyod der bsdod pa ci yin
gsungs pas/ ming yongs su grags pas karma pa yin/ sems la dbang thob na'ang lus ma rdzogs pa'i re shig khyod kyi 'og tu bsdad do zhes gsungs/ rang byung rdo rje zhes pa'ang
karma pa shi'i gsang mtshan yin pas mtshan gzhan ma btags so// de nas o rgyan pa la bde dgyes ma phur rnams kyi dbang dang dus 'khor sgyu drwa 'byung bo 'dul byed kyi
rgyud rnams dang gdams pa mang du gsan/ bdun pa la mkhan po kun ldan shes rab las rab tu byung / de nas mtshur phur gnyan ras la karma pa'i chos rnams gsan/ bco brgyad
pa la mkhan chen gzhon byang pa dang / dge 'dun rin chen sogs las bsnyen par rdzogs/ gsang phu ba shAka gzhon la phar tshad mngon pa gsan/ mdo rgyud bstan

bcos mtha' dag la mkhas pa'i tshul bstan/ snyen mdo ba la rgyud bshad rgyas par gsan nas dus 'khor 'di la mchog tu rtsal 'don pa zhu zhes/ o rgyan pas gsol ba bzhin phyis snye
mdo kun mkhyen la dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa rgyas pa phran dang bcas pa/ sbyor drug rigs brgyad sogs gsan/ de'i tshe rigs ldan rgyud pa'i bla ma mkha'
'gro dang bcas pa byon nas byin gyis brlabs pas phyi nang gzhan sum gyi don cig tu dgongs/ khyung rdzong du o rgyan pa byon nas rdo rje gsum gyi bsnyen sgrub kyi gnad
ma lus par gnang / mtshur phu phyi nang gi gza' skar mthun par gzigs pas rtsis kyi bstan bcos mdzad/ bde chen steng su phyi nang gi rten 'brel dag par gzigs pas/ zab mo
nang don gyi bstan bcos mdzad/ hor rgyal po'i bla ma mdzad de hor bod kyi 'gro ba dpag tu med pa smin grol la bkod nas nga drug pa sa mo yos la rgya'i yul du zhi bar gshegs
te chos rje nyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi nang du bzhugs par bstan pas

rgyal po 'khor dang bcas pa dad par mdzad do//rgyal ba g.yung ston pa/'di'i slob ma rgyud bshad la mkhas pa g.yung ston pa dang / man ngag la mkhas pa mgon rgyal ba dang /
sha grags seng ba dang / g.yag sde paN chen dang / dar rgyal ba sogs byung ba las/ rgyal ba g.yung ston pa ni/ 'khrungs yul tshongs 'dus pa/ gdung glan/ shing pho spre'u
la 'khrungs/ gzhon dus nas mkhyen pa shin tu che/ sngags gsar rnying dang mngon pa kun las btus la mkhas/ zur byams pa seng ges shangs pa kShA 'bum la gshin rje'i skor gsan
pa'i phyag phyir byon nas bla ma dang lhan cig tu legs par bslabs pas/ 'khrul 'khor las sbyor sogs la shin tu mkhas shing mthu che/ gzhon dus su gong ma'i lung gi rgya
yul du byon/ 'chams la sogs pa'i rnam 'gyur dang / gong du 'bru 'dabs dgos pa'i mi sde mang pos than pa byung ba'i tshe/ gong ma la char 'beb pa rdzong bar zhu ba byas/
der khong rdzang pa na char che bar phebs pas gong ma dgyes te gnang sbyin mang po gnang / bod du phebs nas yo byed

thams cad yum gyi don du bla ma dang dge 'dun la phul/ bla ma mang po la lung man ngag gi gsan pa shin tu che/ khyad par du chos rje rang byung rdo rje la dus kyi 'khor lo'i
dbang rgyud man ngag mtha' dag gsan cing mkhas par sbyangs/ karma pa'i chos skor rnams kyang gsan/ bu ston rin po che'i drung du'ang dus 'khor gsan cing dogs pa chod par
mdzad/ mon pa gror thugs dam gyi rtsal chen po 'khrungs te/ mnyam med rgyal ba g.yung ston ngas/ zhes pa la sogs pa'i mgur yang gsungs/ phung po ri bo che dang ra dum brag
la sogs par bzhugs te bshad pas gzhan la phan pa chen po mdzad/ sngags kyi sangs rgyas dang mtshan nyid kyi sangs rgyas gnyis kyi khyad 'byed mdzad pa/ g.yag sde paN
chen gyis gzigs pas shin tu dad de/ dpon slob bco lnga ba phung po ri bo cher byon nas zhabs la gtugs/ sku tshe'i smad la tshogs pa chos lung ba las bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/
mtshan rdo rje 'bum zhes pa rdo rje dpal zhes par bsgyur/ rgod sgros

chu'i grong pa dum bur bcad kyang chu mi 'bo ba dang / lcags sregs blangs kyang mi 'tshigs pa dang / rtsig pa la rdo drug sbyor gyi zhal ba byas pas rtsig pa brag chen po cig
tu gyur pa la sogs pa'i rten 'brel mang po mdzad/ gya gnyis pa shing mo sbrul la zhi bar gshegs so//chos rje rol pa'i rdo rje/chos rje rol pa'i rdo rje ni/ yul rngod kyi
a la rong go chen spang khar gyi gnam rdzong du/ yab bsod nams don grub/ yum brtson 'grus rgyan gyi lhums su/ chos rje rang byung rdo rje nyid dga' ldan nas byon te bzhugs/
lcags pho 'brug la bltams/ la stod pa rtogs ldan mgon rgyal ba la sbyor drug dang zab mo nang don sogs karma pa'i chos skor rnams gsan/ mtshur phur phebs nas/ mkhan
chen don grub dpal pa dang slob dpon bsod nams 'bum las rab tu byung / mtshan dpal dharma kIrtir gsol/ dpal ldan bla ma la 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs gsan/ g.yung ston pa
la rdo rje phreng ba sogs gsang sngags gsar rnying gi dbang rgyud man ngag mang po dang / khyad par du dus 'khor rgyud 'grel phran

dang bcas pa gsan/ bco brgyad pa la sngar gyi mkhan slob dang / gsang ston gzhon nu dpal gyis mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ sha chang spu rtse tsam yang spyan lam du mi 'grim
pa/ bcu dgu pa la tho gan the mur gyis spyan drangs nas/ rim gyis byon te nyer gcig pa la pho brang du phebs/ rgyal po yab sras la dus 'khor gyi dbang khrid rgyud 'grel
cha lag dang bcas pa gnang / slar bod du phebs te 'gro phan rgya chen po mdzad nas zhe bzhi pa la byang phyogs kyi ri bo'i 'dabs su gshegs so//dpal mkha' spyod dbang po/'di'i
slob ma'i gtso bo sha grags seng ge ba'i sku'i skye ba dpal mkha' spyod dbang po ni/ yul gnam gyi bye ma lung du yab lha rgyal dang / yum 'brog mo'i sras su lcags pho
stag la 'khrungs/ mkhas grub dar rgyal bas mtshur phu'i gnas nang du gdan drangs/ dgung lo bdun la chos rje rol pa'i rdo rje la dge bsnyen mnos/ mkhan chen don grub dpal
ba dang / rje rol pa'i rdo rje las rab tu byung / bco brgyad pa la don grub dpal ba/ chos rdor ba/ gzhon nu dpal ba rnams las bsnyen par

rdzogs/ rje rol pa'i rdo rje dang / mkhas grub dar rgyal ba las dbang rgyud man ngag dpag tu med pa gsan cing / khyad par du dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud bshad man ngag dang bcas
pa gsan/ bde ba can pa 'jam rin pa la byams chos tshad ma 'dul ba rnams gsan/ mkhan chen kun dga' 'od zer las rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang sogs gsan/ tsa ri'i brag dkar
mor yang lo gsum thugs dam rtse gcig tu mdzad/ stag rtse dang / dga' ldan ma mo la sogs pa gnas mang du btab/ bka' 'bum po ti bdun tsam mdzad cing 'phrin las rgya cher bskyangs
nas nga drug pa shing mo bya la zhi bar gshegs so//lha gzigs rin chen rgyal mtshan/slob ma yang / chos rje de bzhin gshegs pa/ sog dbon rigs pa'i ral gri/ lha gzigs
rin chen rgyal mtshan/ 'khrul zhig bsod nams 'bum/ bla ma chos bzang pa sogs mang du byon pa las/ lha gzigs pa ni/ dang po 'bri khung pa'i gzims g.yog pa yin/ phyis mkha'
spyod pa'i zhabs la gtugs te gdams pa ma lus pa mnos nas gsung rnams la zin bris mdzad/ rtogs pa mchog tu gyur te sa stod smad thams cad du gzhan don rgya

cher bskyangs so// de'i slob ma mkhan chen lhag ru ba shAkya grags pa/ mtshan gzhan rin chen dpal bzang dang rang grol lhun grub ces grags pa des dang por mkha' spyod pa nyid
la thugs cing gdams pa'i zhib tshegs thams cad lha gzigs pa la sten nas gsan pas grub pa brnyes te/ dgung lo gya gnyis kyi bar du 'gro don bskyangs so// de la sems dpa'
chen po nam pa'i zhal snga nas gdams pa ma lus par gsan te bdag la dpal mkha' spyod pa'i lugs kyi sbyor drug legs par gnang ngo //'khrul zhig bsod nams 'bum/'khrul zhig
bsod nams 'bum ni/ gnas nang dang nye ba'i g.yu ma zhes par 'khrungs/ mkha' spyod pa la gdams pa ma lus pa gsan/ gsung zin bris su btab te bsnyen sgrub kyi khrid yig chen
mo sogs mdzad/ gnas nang gi gdan sar bzhugs nas 'phrin las bskyangs/ de la slob dpon rin po che bla ma rgyal mtshan pas gsan to// bla ma chos bzang pa ni/ 'khrungs yul
nags shod pa/ mkha' spyod pa la gdams pa

ma lus par mnos/ stag rtse dang ba yo'i gdan sa mdzad nas phrin las bskyangs so//chos rje de bzhin gshegs pa/rol pa'i rdo rje'i sku'i skye ba chos rje de bzhin gshegs pa ni/
yul nyang por yab sngags 'chang gu ru rin chen dang / yum lha mo skyid kyi sras su shing pho byi ba la me tog gi char dang bcas te sku bltams/ dgung lo gnyis pa la sgar
du phebs/ bzhi pa la dpal mkha' spyod pa dang mjal te stag rtser rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang / chos drug phyag chen sbyor drug sogs karma pa'i chos skor rnams gsan/ bdun pa
la rtse lha sgang du tshal min pa dang yon blo ba las rab tu byung / mtshan chos dpal bzang por gsol/ bco brgyad pa la mdo khams su thegs te karma dang ri bo che sogs su
chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor/ nyi shu pa la rtse lha sgang du sngar gyi mkhan slob las bsnyen par rdzogs/ khrid pa sgom ma nus pa zhig la kho'i khang thog tu byon
nas sku stod rib tsam dang dbu rib tsam mdzad nas gzigs pa'i rdzu 'phrul bstan pa dang / de 'jigs te bsgoms pas rtogs pa bskyed pa sogs slob ma grangs med pa grol

bar mdzad/ de nas gong ma ye dbang gis gdan drangs te lhas mtshur phu khams kyi sa'i cha rnams rims kyis brgyud nas phebs pa na/ rgya'i yul du nyin mtshan kun tu 'od kyis gang
ba dang / sprin gseb tu sangs rgyas byang sems mang po bzhugs pa dang / lha'i bu pho mo mang po mchod pa 'bul ba sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas brgya rtsa brgyad bstan pa
kun gyis mthong pas/ rgyal po 'khor bcas lhag par dad de rgyal po sogs sems can bgrang ba las 'das pa yang dag pa'i lam la bkod/ sku'i gzi brjid dang / tshangs pa'i dbyangs
dang / mngon shes dang rdzu 'phrul sogs kyis 'gro ba rnams smin par mdzad pas/ thub pa'i dbang po 'jig rten du byon pa 'dra zhes/ rgyal pos de bzhin gshegs pa zhes su
gsol/ slar bod du phebs te skye dgu'i tshogs mtha' yas pa gdams pa dang / zhal mthong ba tsam gyis byang chub la bkod nas so gnyis pa shing mo lug la/ ngas karma'i nye logs
su 'dun pa btang tshar bas der gsol ba thob ces lung bstan mdzad de lha sa po ta lar mya ngan las 'da'

ba'i tshul bstan to// rje 'di la sogs dbon rigs pa'i ral gri rin chen bzang po dang / sprul sku chos dpal ye shes pa dang / zur mangs pa sogs slob ma mkhas grub mang du byung
ngo //chos dpal ye shes pa/dpal mkha' spyod pa'i sku'i skye ba chos dpal ye shes pa ni/ yul nyang por yab khu bsam 'grub dang / yum bar gza' gnyis kyi sras su me pho khyi
la sku mdzes shing zhabs la rgyal zhes pa'i yi ges mtshan pa zhig 'khrungs/ dgung lo gnyis pa la stag rtse dang dga' ldan ma mo sogs su gdan drangs/ brag dang rtsig pa/
gang la yang thogs pa med par 'byon pa sogs rdzu 'phrul mang po bstan/ chos bzang ba la mkha' spyod bka' 'bum sogs lung dang dbang khrid mang po dang / grags rgyal ba
la bde mchog gsan/ brgyad pa la chos rje de bzhin gshegs pa dang mjal te stag rtser rje de las rab tu byung / chos sgrub bsnyen sgrub sbyor drug sogs dbang khrid mang du
gsan/ ta'i ming rgyal pos gnod sbyin bzang po phul/ 'ol khar tshal min pa las bsnyen par rdzogs/ rig pa'i ral gri la rang byung rdo rje'i bka' 'bum byams chos

dbu ma gsan/ mtshur ston chos kyi rin chen la mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang sogs chos mang po dang / khyad par sbyor drug gi khrid dang zab mo nang don gsan te 'di'i brgyud
pa ni/ rang byung rdo rje/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan dza ya badzra/ chos kyi rin chen zhes so// stag rtse sogs su chos rje mthong ba don ldan pa la chos rnams gtad/ rkong por
nyin lam bcu gnyis kyi bar kyi 'khrug pa zhi ba'i rgya bsdams/ rgya la dgongs pa rnams cho 'phrul du mas btul/ karmar mthong ba don ldan pa'i sku tshe'i bar chad bsal/
khams dbus kun tu 'gro ba'i don mdzad nas zhe bdun pa chu pho spre'u la dga' ldan ma mor me tog gi char dang bcas te sku'i bkod pa bsdus so//chos rje mthong ba don ldan/de
bzhin gshegs pa'i sku'i skye ba chos rje mthong ba don ldan pa ni/ karma dang nye ba'i sa cha dom du sngags 'chang gza' ma'i sras su me pho spre'u la 'khrungs/ mkhan chen
mgo blon pas sgar du gdan drangs te 'ol khar tshal min pa las rab tu byung / dka' bzhi pa rig pa'i ral gri/ sprul sku chos dpal ye shes/

rong chen pa sogs skyes bu dam pa mang du bstan nas gsan pa'i tshul rgya che bar mdzad/ khyad par chos dpal ye shes pa la sbyor drug gsan/ gangs can gyi 'gro ba smin cing grol
bar mdzad nas so brgyad pa chu mo bya la dben gnas bsa' phur gshegs/ de'i slob ma'i mchog mang du byung ba las gtso bor gyur pa ni/ ban dkar ba 'jam dpal bzang po dang
/ gu shrI dpal 'byor don grub gnyis so// mthong ba don ldan pa'i sku'i skye ba dpal karma pa chos grags rgya mtsho ni/ rngod kyi sa'i cha spyi nang du yab grags pa dpal
dang yum lha mo skyid kyi sras su shing pho khyi la sku bltams/ ban dkar ba dang / gu shrI dpal 'byor don grub gnyis las rab tu byung nas mang du gsan pa rgya mtsho lta
bu mdzad de/ mdo sngags kyi gzhung lugs mtha' dag la mchog tu mkhas pa'i tshul ston/ shin tu sgrin po'i mkhas pas kyang mkhyen pa'i mtha' mi mngon/ rgya rgyal pos lus bzang
po dang 'bul ba tshan chen po phul/ chos kyi rje spyan snga rin po ches sne gdong rtser spyan drangs nas gus pas bsten/ mkhas btsun mi chen dge 'dun tshogs stong

phrag mang po la chos kyi char phab/ 'phags yul dang rgya nag tshun 'phrin las kyi khyab/ dbus gtsang khams sum gyis sa'i cha kun tu zhabs kyis bcags te/gang du chos gsungs
pa'i sar lha rnams kyis me tog gi char 'bebs pa dang / rab tu gnas pa'i me tog rgyang ring po nas 'thor ba yul du ma bskal ba'i sar 'bab pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i cho 'phrul
dang / mngon par mkhyen pas dus gsum lung ston cing / gzhung bshad dang gdams pa stsol ba dang zhal ston pa dang phyag gis dbang bskur ba'i skye dgu'i tshogs dpag tu med
pa byang chub kyi lam la 'god par mdzad pa las/ bsam yas mchim phur phebs pa'i tshe bdag la rje rang byung pa'i khrid yig gi steng nas yan lag drug pa'i khrid bka' drin
gyis bstsal to//zhwa dmar chos grags ye shes dpal bzang /chos dpal ye shes pa'i sku'i skye ba chos kyi rje sprul ba'i sku zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa bzhi pa ni/ tre shod
mthil tu yab ldong dgon pa skyabs dang yum bsod nams sgrol ma'i sras su chu mo bya la sku bltams/ mtshan mi pham rdo rjer

gsol/ 'khrungs ma thag nas mkhyen pa'i gting mi dpogs pa'i tshul gyis thogs pa med par chos gsungs shing mngon par mkhyen pas dus gsum lung ston/ dgung lo bcu pa la gu shrI
dpal 'byor don grub las dge bsnyen mnos/ mtshan chos kyi grags pa ye shes dpal bzang por gsol/ de la dbang khrid lung mang du gsan/ bcu gcig pa la zur mangs dgon par karma
pa dang mjal/ gu shrI bas mkhan po/ ban dkar bas slob dpon mdzad de rab tu byung / ban dkar ba la gsang 'dus dang lnga tshan sogs gsan/ bcu gnyis pa la dga' ldan ma mor
phebs/ bco lnga pa la slob dpon  bla ma rgyal mtshan rkong por gdan drangs nas rdo rje phreng ba la sogs pa'i dbang khrid lung mang po dang / khyad par nag pa'i zla ba
la dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang mnos pa'i tshe mar me'i phreng ba zhag mang du 'bar ba byung / rgyud 'grel man ngag dang bcas pa gsan/ bco brgyad pa la slar yang mdo khams nas
zi ling mkhar gyi bar du thegs nas sems can grangs med pa 'khor ba mtha' can du mdzad/ de nas hor yul

du thegs nas hor rnams dul bar mdzad de a ram gyi sdig las chen po rgyun bcad/ chos bstan nas ban de la gus par byed du bcug te byang chub tu nges par mdzad/ slar khams dang
rkong po rim par brgyud de/ nyer bzhi pa la dbus phyogs su phebs/ chos kyi rje spyan snga rin po ches tshong 'dus yangs pa can du gdan drangs/ dbus phyogs kyi dge ba'i
bshes gnyen che dgu thams cad 'dus pa la so so'i 'dod pa bzhin chos mang du stsal/ thams cad mkhyen pa 'gos lo tsA ba la sha wa ri'i lugs kyi sbyor drug dang / rgyud gsum
gsang ba gsan/ rje des mkhan po/ mkhan chen rab 'byor bas las slob/ chos rje rin po che nam pas gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ nyer lnga pa la 'gos lo tsA ba las
sgra tshad sogs rig pa'i gnas dang mdo sngags kyi gzhung lugs rgya mtsho lta bu gsan cing sbyangs pa'i tshul mdzad/ khyad par dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel rwa 'bro'i bshad
pa/ dpal ldan bla ma'i TIka chen/ rgyud phyi ma/ rdo rje snying 'grel/ dbang mdor bstan/ lta 'dod mdor bstan/ do dam bsnyen

pa/ dpe med mtsho'i sbyor drug rtsa 'grel/ mtshan brjod 'grel pa bdud rtsi thigs pa/ dus zhabs snyan rgyud/ yu mo'i gsal sgron/ sgrom lde/ chos rje phyogs pa'i sbyor drug gi
khrid ngo sprod sogs cha lag dang bcas pa gsan/ rje lo chen pa la paN chen lugs kyi sbyor drug dang rngog chos sogs mang po dang / dpal karma pa dang stag lung pa la'ang
mang du gsan pa mdzad/ dbus gtsang lho bum thang tshun zhabs kyis bcags te mkhas btsun mi chen skye dgu'i tshogs bgrang ba las 'das pa theg pa chen por smin par mdzad/
dga' ldan ma mor btsug lag khang rten chen dang bcas pa ngo mtshar ba'i bkod pa can bzhengs/ dpal kun tu bzang po'i nags khrod du sengge'i khri la bzhugs te bstan pa'i sgron
me sbar bar mdzad do//rgyal ba 'di nyid kyi zhabs kyi padmo la bdag gis gus pas btud de rnal 'byor yan lag drug pa'i gdams pa dpal mkha' spyod pa'i lugs legs par thob
po/ grub chen o rgyan pa'i slob ma dbu ma pas rdo rje tshig la bshad pa dang man ngag lag len dang bcas

pa mdzad/ de la mkhas grub 'byung gnas bzang pos gsan te thugs nyams su bzhes pas grub pa brnyes nas/ mchims phur bzhugs te khrid yig gi snying po mdzad nas 'phrin las bskyangs
so//de nas yon rin pa/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ 'khrul zhig pa/ bdag gi bla ma dus 'khor zhabs so// mkhan chen bsod nams 'od zer bas rdo rje tshig gi rnam bshad chen mo
mdzad pa/ chos rje gangs pa nas rgyud nas dpal ldan bla'i bar du byung ngo // rtogs ldan zla bas ming bas/ rdo rje tshig gi rnams bshad/ khrid rim gegs sel ngo sprod la
sogs pa'i yig 'jog mang du mdzad cing / phreng skor du grags pa mdzad do// de nas spyid phu'i mkhan chen byang chub seng ge/ 'phags mchog bsod nams dpal/ rgod phrug grags
pa 'byung gnas/ 'gos lo tsA ba gzhon nu'i zhabs rnams rim par brgyud do//  yang zla seng ba/ rtogs ldan shes rin pa/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/
'khrul zhig pa/ bdag gi bla ma dus zhabs pa rnams so// gser khang pa gzhon nu 'bum/ grags

pa dpal/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston rin po che rnams rim par brgyud pa'i man ngag kyang byung ngo // o rgyan pa'i dngos slob 'di dag rgyud 'grel dang sbyar te khrid kyis
gdul bya rjes su 'dzin pa kho na'o// //5)paN chen shAkya shrI'i lugs/paN chen shAkya shrIlnga pa paN chen shAkya shrI'i lugs ni/ paN chen des dgung lo don brgyad bzhes
pa'i dus su paNDi ta bi bhU ti tsantra/ su ga ta shrI/ dza ya datta/ dA na shrI la/ sanggha shrI/ su ma ti sA ga ra/ kA la tsakri/ dzi na gupta/ ma hA bo dhi ste 'khor paNDi
ta dgu dang bcas pa dza gangda la gnas/ khro phu lo tsA bas gdan drangs te/ bo dur tshong 'dus/ gro mo/ phag ri/ 'bring mtshams/ rgyang ro rnams su rim kyis byon/ de
nas dpyal lo tsA bas khro bo che dang dam kha gnas su gdan drangs/ kyai rdo rje 'grel pa man ngag dang bcas pa gnang / de nas mgur mo dang / chu mig ring mor dge 'dun gyi
tshogs chen pos bskor bas khyim pa rnams kyis zhal yang blta dka' bar byung / der sa paN gyis kyang mjal/ de nas khro phur phebs/ shing pho byi ba lo'i dbyar gnas de nyid
du mdzad de tshul shing len

pa brgyad brgya byung / lho brag pa byang chub dpal bsnyen rdzogs gnang / brgyad stong pa a bha ya'i 'grel ba dang bcas pa dang so thar dang mdo sde rgyan gsungs/ de nas snar
gyi slas mo cher byon der thugs bag phebs pas sngar ma gzigs pas yi dam mang po'i zhal gzigs/ sum cu rtsa gsum dang dga' ldan pa'i mchod pa'i rnga sgra las chos kyi sgra
'byung ba gsan/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi bkod pa dus 'khor nas ji ltar bshad pa bzhin mngon sum du gzigs pas sngon (mngon )pa'i lugs de ma dag pa yin nam dgongs pa na/
sgrol ma'i zhal nas gdul bya'i blo dang bstun pas mi 'gal te sde pa bco brgyad lta bu yin/ yang dag par na 'jig rten rang yang med gsungs/ gtsang po ba bsod nams mdzes kyis
mjal te bdag bsnyen par rdzogs nas ltung ba byung ba ma dran pas/ tshul khrims bsrungs pa'i bde ba byang chub tu bsngo bar zhus pas/ dbu zhwa zul gyis phud phyag thal
mo sbyar nas/ bsngo rgyu bzang 'di lta bu rgya gar na yang dkon/ kho bo'i rtsar bsdod la mchod gnas gyis gsungs

ste bsngo ba gnang / der bsod snyoms 'dren pa shin tu mang bas gdan gcig gi dus su chos rje nyid la drangs pa'i gdugs tshogs kyis dge 'dun nyi brgya'i 'tsho ba sbyor/ chos
che phra mang du gsungs shing lam rim dang chos spyod rgyas pa brtsams/ paN chung rnams la sa sde dang / tshad ma sde bdun dang / dus 'khor rgyud 'grel gnang / glang lo'i
dbyar gnas kyang slas mo cher mdzad de mdo rtsa dang me tog phreng rgyud gsungs/ dgag dbye thon nas chu mig ring mor byon/ rin chen phreng ba dang dpe rgyan gsungs/ rgyan
gong gnas su rdo rje dpal la bsnyen rdzogs gnang / de nas srin po ri pas spyan drangs te/ gzhu snye dang mtshur phu nas brgyud lha sa mjal nas srin po rir phebs/ der phyag
lo dgra bcom gyis kyang mjal ba la byon/ stag lo'i dbyar gnas kyang srin po rir mdzad de mngon pa kun las btus dznyA na mi tra'i 'grel pa dang bcas pa/ spyi chos la mya
ngan med lung bstan pa dang / las rgya pa/ gzhan yang byams chos lnga dang rigs tshogs rnams gsungs/ srin po ri'i gdan sa ba la byams chos kyi khrid

rigs tshogs kyi khrid/ spyod phyogs kyi khrid rnams gnang / de nas lha zhi ba 'od kyi bsam yas su spyan drangs te chos mang du gsungs/ bsam yas kyi bkod pa la mnyes te bi kra
ma shrI la dang dus mtshungs su 'dug gsungs/ der sangs rgyas dbon ston gyis mjal te rgya ma rin chen sgang du gdan drangs/ slar srin po rir phebs/ chag lo dgra bcom gyis
gdan drangs te thang po che dang / rim gyis gnyal lte'u rar phebs/ yos lo'i dbyar gnas de nyid du mdzad/ dge slong tshul shing len pa bdun brgya byung / lo paN gnyis kyis
mdo sngags kyi chos mang du bsgyur zhing gsungs/ gser phye 'bum pa'i nub kyi chos khri la lo paN gnyis ga bzhugs nas sems bskyed dang lam rim gsungs/ zhang dang skyal
ba la bsnyen rdzogs gnang / rnam rgyal mchod rten bzhengs pas me tog gi char bab/ de nas thang po cher byon bstan rtsis mdzad/ spu bu ngor yang chos gsungs/ 'brug lo'i dbyar
gnas thang po cher mdzad nas/ 'on zangs ri g.ye gangs sar nas slar gnyal lte'u ra dang / de'i bu lag rong rtse dkar chun du thegs te zangs chen pa sogs mkhas btsun

mang po la lam rim gyi khrid dang / me tog phreng rgyud/ brgyad stong pa/ thub pa dgongs rgyan gsungs/ sa lha'i gnas su sgrol ma'i bris skus paN chen la chos gsungs/ bya nag
rin chen 'od sogs la spyod rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang gnang / lo ro mtsho sna/ lho brag/ gru shul rnams la'ang lo paN gnyis ka byon te chos mang du gsungs/ slar
yang lte'u ra/ thang po che/ srin po ri/ rgya ma rin chen sgang rnams su rim gyis byon te/ sbrul lo'i dbyar gnas rin chen sgang du mdzad/ chos bstan pas phyir mi ldog
pa'i sa thob pa brgyad cu lhag pa byung / ra sgreng du'ang byon/ 'bri khung pas gdan 'dren byung ba la ma thegs par chos skyes gnang / de nas rim gyis gtsang du byon nas
nyung chung du bzhugs pa na/ sa skya pas gdan drangs te rta lo'i dbyar gnas sa skyar mdzad/ chos rje sa paN la bsnyen rdzogs gnang / dka' chen bzhi sogs mang du gsungs shing
/ khyad par du dus 'khor rgyud 'grel phran dang bcas pa gnang / de nas shangs/ 'u yug/ nyang ro la sogs par byon/ lug lo'i dbyar gnas shangs lu

gu gdong du mdzad/ de mo than pa che bas char 'bebs mdzad pa na/ klu brgyad dngos su 'ongs nas char phul lha btsun gung thang pa la bsnyen rdzogs gnang / jo gdan sengge dpal
la khyed bod la gtad pa med/ rlung re bzung drod en tsam re byung ba dang grub thob tu re bar 'dug gsungs/ gzhan gyis phul ba'i yo byad yod do cog khro phu'i byams chen
la btang / spre'u lo'i dbyar gnas khro phur mdzad/ dbyar zla 'bring po la byams chen gyi rab gnas gnang nas rim gyis mnga' ris su thegs/ bod kyi dge slong rjes su 'brang
ba rnams gtsang po ba dang / byang rdor rnam gnyis la gtad nas stan gcig pa'i sde btsugs/ pu hrangs su chos kyi rgyal po stag tsha'i bla ma mdzad nas bya lo'i dbyar gnas
de nyid du mdzad/ de nas phag lo la kha cher phebs te thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gyis grub pa'i sgrol ma lha khang du gtso bor bzhugs te/ lo bcu dang zla ba drug gi bar
du bstan pa'i bya ba rgya cher mdzad nas/ dgu bcu go dgu pa shing mo bya'i lo dga' ldan du gshegs/

spur bzhu ba'i tshe nam mkha'i rol mo las sil snyan bdun pa zhes pa'i tshigs su bcad pa byung ba paNDi ta phyed dang nyis brgyas yi ger bkod pa yod do//dpyad lo tsA ba chos
kyi bzang po/paN chen 'di la bod kyi slob ma mang du byon pa las/ chos 'di pa'i sras kyi thu bo ni dpyal chags gsum gyi/ dpyal lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po ni/ dpyal lo tsA
ba kun dga' rdo rje'i sras kun dga' grags la sras lnga yod pa'i bar ba yin/ gzhon nus dus nas lha lung pa jo bzang kyi drung du dpyal ba'i chos skor la sbyangs/ phyag
na rdo rje bsgrub pas zhal gzigs/ 'bring mtshams pa zhang lo las lo tsA bslabs/ zhwa lu'i jo bo las lung bstan thob nas/ lha lung pas kyang bka' gnang ste/ grogs mchog dam
pa chag lo dgra bcom dang lhan cig rgya gar du byon/ thog mar ma hA bo dhi la mchod pa phul te gsol ba btab/ shrI na landar paN chen shAkya shrI las rab tu byung / byang
chub shing drung du A nantA ka ra las thugs bskyed/ rdo rje gdan du nikSha langka bde mchog gi dbang thob/ paN grub de rnams dang / mu ni shrI/ kShi ti garbha/ shrI lA

kA ra/ ma hA nirti rnams las sgra tshad sde snod rgyud sde mtha' dag la sbyangs pas mkhas par gyur/ 'bar ba'i phug go sam la/ o tantra/ phulla ha ri/ klu sgrub dang nag po
spyod pa'i sgrub khang rnams su sgrub pa mdzad pas 'jig rten dbang phyug gi zhal gzigs/ rgya gar shar nub kun tu byon te gnas khyad par can rnams mjal/ rdo rje gdan du ston
pa'i tshems la mchod pa phul/ na landar gaNdi brdungs te chos ston lan lnga mdzad/ lo bcu gnyis bzhugs nas mthar grub thob niShka langka spyan drangs nas bod du byon/
dam kha'i gnas dang gser gdings su bzhugs nas dbang gzhung man ngag gis 'gro phan che bar mdzad/ dben gnas thar pa gling du gtso bor bzhugs pa na/ paN chen shAkya shrI byon
pa mjal nas nA ro pa'i brtag gnyis 'grel chen gsan cing bsgyur/ de'i man ngag kyang gsan te sbyor drug rin po che'i sgrom gyi lde mig mdzad/ sbyor drug rdo rje tshig gi
snying po bsdus pa'ang bsgyur/ bde dgyes phag mo gsang 'dus gshed dmar

rnams kyi zhal gzigs/ glang lo ston 'bring gi tshes drug la gshegs so// de la de nyid kyi dbon po dpyal a mo ghas sbyor drug gi gdams pa gsan te kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer
la gnang ba nas rim par brgyud pa byung la/ yang a mo gha nas/ dpal gzhon nu ye shes/ thar lo/ bu ston zhabs nas rim par brgyud pa byung ngo //dpyal chos bzang gi slob ma
gnyal pa hrul po zhes pas sgrom lde'i 'grel pa mdzad de/ rim par brgyud nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa 'gos lo tsA ba/ sprul pa'i sku zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa'i zhal sngar
bdag gis nod do//chag lo dgra bcom pa/chag lo tsA ba dgra bcom pa ni/ chag yon tan rin chen gyi sras che ba/ shing pho khyi la 'khrungs/ gro lung pa chen po'i slob ma chag
rin tshul las rab tu byung / nyi shu pa la mdo sde phug tu stong 'dul gyi brgyud pa mkhan chen shud phu ba dar ma brtson 'grus la bsnyen par rdzogs/ steng pa lo tsA ba
las lo tsA dang dus 'khor bslabs/ bod du bla ma bco lnga bsten/ chos phal che ba mkhyen/

kharpas Nis lung bstan nas rgya gar la byon/ ganggA'i 'gram du shi skyid kyi jag pa byung yang bde bar rdo rje gdan du byon/ nyin re bzhin gser gyis nyos pa'i me tog gi phreng
ba zung 'thor bas ma hA bo dhi'i snyan gong gnyis su nges bar chags/ shAkya shrI/ buddha shrI/ mai tri tsantra/ niShka langka/ shrI lA kA ra/ A nantA kA ra gupta/ de
wa shrI/ karna Ta pa/ a mo gha ste paN chen dgu'i zhabs bsten pas yongs su rdzogs pa'i paNDi tar gyur/ tshad pas bsnyung pa na sgrol mas dngos su khrus gsol pas dengs shing
ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo du ma 'khrungs/ rgya gar gyi rten rang byung brgyad cu yang gzigs/ na landar bod mchog gi zhal gzigs te lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes mngon du gyur/
zhe bdun pa la bal yul nas paNDi ta buddha shrI gdan drangs te lcags mo bya la lo paN gnyis kyis chu mig mgur mo/ 'phan yul rgyal/ lhas/ thang po che la sogs pa'i gnas
rnams su bzhugs te chos gsungs/ de nas gnyal lte'u rar phebs nas mkhas btsun mang po la rgyal ba'i lam 'jug

mngon rtogs rgyan paN chen nyid kyi 'grel pa dang bcas pa/ dus 'khor gsang 'dus bde dgyes sogs gzhung gdams ngag dang bcas pa paNDi tas rgya skad dang / lo tsA bas bod du gsungs/
paN chen la gser srang sum brgyas gtsos pa'i 'bul nod rgya chen po mdzad pas shin tu dgyes/ chu pho khyi'i ston gnyal nas stag nas paN chen bal yul du ma phebs bar
gyi zhabs tog mdzad cing yar lam chu mig ring mor bstan rtsis mdzad/ nga gsum pa la paN chen shAkya shrI srin po ri nas bsus te thang po che dang lte'u ra sogs su gdan drangs/
paN chen de nyid dang / ratna shrI dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i dpal bzang po rnams las gzhung mang po'i 'gyur mdzad/ stan gcig chos gos gsum pa dbu rag zhabs rjen
rdo rje'i skyil dkrung sogs sbyangs pa'i yon tan dang ldan/ tshul khrims kyi dri ngad kyis sa rgyang por khyab/ paNDi ta dharma shrI sogs rgya gar ba'i slob ma mkhas pa'ang
mang du byung / re bzhi pa me mo glang la lte'u rar sprul ba'i sku'i bkod pa bsdus so// de nyid la chag lo tsA

ba chos rje dpal gyis sbyor drug gi khrid gsan to//chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/chos rje sa skya paNDi ta ni/ skye ba nyi shu lngar 'jam dpal gyis rjes su bzung bas mkhyen rabs
'gran zla dang bral/ bco lnga pa la rje btsun chen po las yab mes kyi chos thams cad thugs su chud/ mnal lam du dbyig gnyen mjal bas mngon pa bslab ma dgos par mkhyen/
nyer gsum pa la chu mig ring mor paN chen shrI dang mjal/ paN chen dbus su byon gyi bar/ bal po sanggha shrI dang / su ga ta shrI sa skyar spyan drangs nas sgra tshad snyan
ngag sdeb sbyor mngon brjod zlos gar sogs gsan cing / sngar ma 'gyur ba'i rnal 'byor gyi rgyud gsum la gcig 'gyur mdzad/ paN chen yar phebs nas/ nyer dgu pa la paN chen
gyis mkhan po/ spyi po lhas pas las slob/ don mo ri pas gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ paN chen la rnam 'grel sogs dka' chen bzhi/ dus 'khor rgyud 'grel cha lag
dang bcas pa gsang 'dus 'phags skor/ ye shes zhabs lugs/

bod mchog rnams kyi dbang gzhung bshad man ngag dang bcas pa/ khyad par sbyor drug srog rtsol snyan rgyud gsan/ yongs su rdzogs pa'i paNDi tar gyur/ yi dam gyi lha mang po'i
zhal gzigs/ skyi rong du 'phrog byed dga' bo sogs mu stegs kyi ston pa drug btul/ mkhas pa'i grags pas 'phags yul dang rgya nag tshun khyab/ bstan bcos mang du brtsams
te bstan pa ches gsal bar mdzad/ bo dong rin po che sogs gdul bya mang po la 'jam pa'i dbyangs dngos su bstan/ gsang ba'i gnas bltar mi mngon/ dbu gtsug tor dang ldan/ mdzod
spu dung ltar 'khyil/ re gsum pa la rgyal bu go tan gyis gdan drangs nas gong du byon/ sprul pa'i sder bzhugs nas rgya mtsho'i mtha' tshun thub pa'i bstan pas khyab par
mdzad/ rje btsun grags pa/ bi rU pa/ nag po spyod pa gsum gyis mngon par dga' ba'i zhing du rgyal ba dri ma med pa'i dpal zhes su 'tshang rgya bar lung bstan/ bdun cu
pa la ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dang bcas te gshegs so//

des srog rtsol rdo rje'i snyan rgyud rgyus pa gzhon nu sengge la gnang / des dol po ye shes mgon po/ des kun spangs chen po la gnang ste/ des srog rtsol gyi man ngag 'di nyid
la gtso bor mdzad do//6)chag lugs/chag lo tsA ba chos rje dpal/drug pa chag lugs ni/ rje sgra bsgyur gyi rgyal po chag lo tsA ba chos rje dpal zhes grags pa 'dis/ rgya
gar gyi paN chen rnams la gsan pa ste/ de ni gnyal smad chag grong du chag lo tsA ba dgra bcom pa'i gcung po slob dpon dar ma 'byung gnas dang / yum ngo rje mo chos 'bum
skyid kyi sras su sa pho rta la 'khrungs/ dbu gdugs ltar mdzes pa/ spyan mthon  mthing / tshems dkar mnyam bzhi bcu tshang ba/ ljags srab yangs/ sku 'tsham zhing mdzes pa/
tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang ldan pa/ dgung lo bdun nas lte'u rar khu bo chos rje lo tsA ba dgra bcom pa'i drung du/ rgya bod kyi yi ge 'dri klog dang / pi wa rta dang bkas
bcad dang / bri thig bslabs/ bcu gcig nas nyi shu'i bar zhabs drung rtag tu bsten/ bcu gsum pa dge bsnyen/ bco lnga la dge tshul mdzad

cing / sdom 'byung dang kun rig gi dbang dang sems bskyed/ sngags mtshan nyid theg pa che chung gi gdams pa mang po dang khyad par sbyor drug gsan/ lo tsA mkhas par mkhyen/
bcu gcig pa la/ paN chen shAkya shrI lte'u rar byon pa la/ sems bskyed/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin brlabs/ lam rim dang / paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i dpal la thub pa
dgongs rgyan gsan/ bco lnga pa la bkra shis lhun por mi g.yo ba'i zhal gzigs/ nyi shu pa la mon 'gar sdong po rtsa'i gtsug lag khang du/ chag lo gong mas mkhan po/ dge
rgyas pa stag 'dul ba 'dzin pa las slob/ 'gar lha sdings pas gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ nyer gcig pa la chos rje gong ma sku yar ba'i zhal chems ltar rdo rje
gdan ma mthong bar du ldog ri zhes dbu bsnyung bzhes nas bal yul du byon/ paN chen ratna rakShi ta 'phags pa shing kun na rten 'ga'i rab gnas mdzad khar phebs pas mnyes nas
bod ngo mtshar che gsungs/ der lo gcig bzhugs nas khams pa ston grags sogs drug dang lhan cig tu rdo rje phreng ba la sogs pa'i dbang

mang po dang / bde dgyes gsang gsum sogs kyi gdams pa gsan/ nyer gnyis pa la mnga' ris ngang gtsang du byon/ lha btsun gung thang pa mgon po dpal/ 'dzang yon tan shes rab/
sa skya paNDi ta/ khro phu lo tsA ba/ myang stod lo tsA ba/ go lung pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ yol ston padma rgyal mtshan/ snar thang pa gro chen po/ mchims blo brtan/ dga'
ba gdong pa dbyar nyi ma ko brag pa/ 'jad pa rin chen grags/ yol ba pa la sogs pa'i zhal sngar/ lo bzhi'i bar du sngags mtshan nyid theg pa che chung gi chos dpag tu
med pa gsan/ khyad par du yol ston pa la rtsis dang sbyor drug dang / dro chung zer sgom la'ang sbyor drug gsan/ nyer lnga pa la bal yul du byon nas/ dharma dha tu bi ha
rar paN chen rdo rje gdan pa re wenda'i spyan sngar lo gcig bzhugs te 'dus pa dang dus 'khor la sogs pa'i dbang bskur bcu gsum dang / 'dus pa gshed skor bde dgyes dus 'khor
sgyu thod gdan bzhi yo ga sogs kyi gzhung bshad man ngag gsan/ nyer drug pa la rgya gar du byon/ rdo rje gdan sogs gnas

chen rnams mjal/ na lendrar paN chen gnas brtan rA hu la shrI bha dra gtso bor bsten nas/ ka lA pa 'dul ba ting nge 'dzin rgyal po/ dus 'khor bde dgyes gsang 'dus sogs gsan/
ma ga dha rgyal po'i khab tu paN chen ya sho mi tra la sgra rtsis sman dpyad/ zlos gar/ grub snying skor gsan/ rdo rje gdan du bskor ba mdzad pa'i skabs su rgyal ba shAkya
thub pa'i g.yas g.yon tu byams pa 'jam dbyangs zhugs pa'i zhal gzigs/ de gsum zhal 'dzum pa'i 'od bkye bas phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing dpag tu med pa gzigs/ rdo
rje gdan gyi shar sgo'i 'gram gyi klu sgrub kyi sgom khang du 'phags pa yab sras dang bir wa pas dbang bskur byin gyis brlabs/ rgya gar du lo gnyis bzhugs nas/ nyer brgyad
pa la ti ra hu tir bsnyun drag pos 'dzin dus ye shes mgon po phyag bzhi pas bod kyi jo sras kyi rnam par sprul nas bsnyung g.yog byas te bsnyung dengs/ de nas bal yul
du phebs te/ paN chen re wentra pa la sngar gsan pa'i ngag thor dang slar yang gzhung gdams ngag mang du gsan/ rangga Na bi ha rar

bikra ma shI lA'i chos dpon paN chen dzi na rakShi ta dang / sthi bi ha rar bi bhU ti tsantra dang / ma Ni ka shrI dznyA na dang / dharma shrI dang / ma no ra tha gupta dang
/ gau ta ma shrI dznyA na rnams las/ rig pa'i gnas lnga sde snod gsum rgyud sde bzhi'i gzhung bshad dbang gdams ngag mang du gsan khyad par du/ dzi na rakShi ta la dus
'khor rgyud 'grel gsan cing 'gyur yang mdzad/ bi bhU ti la rgyud bshad dang / lhag par sha wa ra lugs kyi sbyor drug gsan/ so gsum pa la mang yul gung thang du nag tsho'i
gdan sa yang thog dang / ha ri man da sogs ma dang 'dra ba'i bu bzhi la sogs pa gnas gzhi brgyad cu tham pa rnams su lo bzhi bzhugs/ glo bo lo tsA ba dang g.yag sde lo tsA
ba dang / go lung pa mdo sde dpal rgyal mtshan dang / g.yung phug pa rgyal mtshan dge ba sogs sde snod 'dzin pa mang bo la/ 'phags skor bde dgyes dus 'khor gshed skor
sogs gnang / sa skya paNDi tas rje 'di'i mtshan brjod 'grel pa bdud rtsi thigs pa'i gzhi 'gyur gzigs pas shin tu

mnyes te/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i rting la khyed las mkhas pa ma byung nges pa yin/ nga yang rgya gar du ma btang pas yab mes gong ma rnams sku drin che la chung du byung
gsungs nas rnam pa kun tu bsngags pa cher mdzad pas mkhas pa'i grags pas hor yul tshun khyab/ 'phags pa rin po ches kyang rig pa'i gnas 'ga' zhig gsan/ so bdun pa la
lam du'ang dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang skye bo mang po'i don mdzad cing lte'u rar phebs/ phan phyin a bha ya lugs dang spyod phyogs dang / ting nge 'dzin rgyal po dang / 'phags
skor bde dgyes rnams dus chos su gnang zhing / gzhan yang dus 'khor sogs bshad grwa dang / dgon gdang zhes par thugs dam skyong zhing / rim lnga dang sbyor drug gi
khrid grwa btsugs/ gzhi 'gyur dang 'gyur bcos mang po mdzad de 'gro phan che bar mdzad do// de nas lo gnyis na khra 'brug tu chos 'khor bskor te mkhas btsun dpag med 'dus/
de nas bsam yang su lha bkra shis lnga pos sbyin bdag byas chos 'khor bskor/ lha sar jo bo rin po che la dkar me gser chab

'bul ba la thegs pa'i lam du paN chen dA na shI la yar klungs stag tshal du mjal bas khyod rgya gar du phyin pas mkhas pa chen po'i chen por 'dug nga bod du bsdad pas ba lang
du song zhes bsngags pa mdzad/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa dang / hor rgyal po go se la yon mchod kyis dpon shi sha tha spyan 'dren du btang byung na'ang ma byon/ slar
lte'u rar bzhugs pa'i skabs su dpon e leb gan dang 'jur na gnyis la 'ja' so bskur nas spyan 'dren du byung bas byang snying 'bru gsum bar du byon/ de nas zhabs bsnyung ste/
dpon zin shes rab skyabs la rnam thar yi ger bkod nas gnang nas gnyal du byon/ nye gnas gzhon nu rgyal mtshan gong du btang pa la 'ja' swa dngul yig sbyil ba dang bcas
pa gnang / nga lnga pa la bkra shis sgo mang zhes pa btab/ der rim lnga dang sbyor drug sgrub grwa btsugs pas thugs dam sgom sder grags/ re gcig pa la thang po cher bcom
ldan ral gris thog drangs mkhas btsun mang po la 'phags skor sogs sngags mtshan nyid kyi chos mang du gsungs/ thang du bla brang brtsigs/ bying o dkar brag tu'ang thugs
dam mdzad/ gdan sa thel

du bcu gnyis rin po ches spyan drangs bskur bsti cher mdzad/ ral gud du'ang chos gsungs/ yar klungs su lo lnga bzhugs/ de'i tshe hor rgyal po yon mchod kyi bka' lung bzhin
chu mo phag lo la chu mig tu chos 'khor btsugs pa'i tshogs dpon la gdan 'dren byung bas thegs/ bcom ldan rigs pa'i ral gri/ chu mig pa chen po/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ ye
shes rgyal mtshan/ dus 'khor ba ye shes rin chen sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen khri phrag mang po la so so'i skal ba bzhin chos gsungs/ chos rgyal 'phags pa'i bka' bzhin dpon
chen shAkya bzang pos sa skyar gdan drangs/ tshogs dung btags ste dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtsho la chos gsungs dus 'khor rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa yang gnang / re bdun pa
la lte'u rar phebs nas mkhas btsun dpag med 'dus pa la chos 'khor zla med pa bskor/ brin lhas su shangs pa tshul shes gtsos pa'i rdo rje slob ma mang po la rdo rje phreng
ba'i dbang gnang / shing pho byi ba lo'i mgo'i zla ba'i tshes dgu'i nyin khro bo bcu'i zhal gzigs/ tshes bcu'i nyin sa g.yo ba dang bcas pa'i cho 'phrul bstan

te zhi bar gshegs/ bla brang gi steng du 'ja' kha dog lnga pa rnam par bkra ba kun gyis mthong / lha'i spos dang sil snyan 'khrol ba byung zhing / rgyal zla'i tshes bco lnga
la gdung bzhu ba 'du ba'i rtse la 'ja' gdugs phub pa lta bu nub phyogs la 'gro ba byung / lha'i me tog dkar po dkar yol lta bu'i char bab/ zhag gsum gyi bar du chab rom
thams cad zhu/ gdung las dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po dang / rigs lnga'i phyag mtshan sogs byon/ dge bshes gur dang ston pa'i chos skyabs gnyis bal por btang ste/ bal po'i
bzo bo nyang ro hi zhes pas nang rten byang chub chen po bzhengs nas gdan drangs/ lte'u ra'i gtsug lag khang du bzhugs su bcug phyi rten mchod rten bzhengs te char che
lo legs pas bkra shis char 'babs su grags/ bcom ldan rig ral gyis dus 'khor 'di na/ zla ba shar du 'gro ba dang / rgya nag bod kyi byang na yod pa sogs dngon sum dang 'gal
ba mang du yod ces smra ba la/ phyis chos rje lo tsA ba la rgyud 'grel gsan pas mchog tu dus 'khor la mos shing mkhas par gyur/ slob ma'i tshogs la'ang

lan du mar gsungs/ go lung pa mdo sde dpal rgyal mtshan gyis chos rje mnga' ris na bzhugs pa'i skabs su dbang rgyud 'grel man ngag dang bcas pa gsan cing sbyangs/ rtsis la
shin tu mkhas slad mar shong longs sku mched/ go lung pa gzhon nu dpal/ grub chen u rgyan pa sogs la gsungs so//gtsang pa dbang phyug shes rab/lo tsA ba chen po'i thugs sras
mkhan chen gtsang pa ni gtsang nags phug pa/ mtshan dbang phyug shes rab/ nags phug pa chen po dang / khyad par du lo tsA ba 'di nyid kyi zhabs la gtugs pas/ sgra tshad
dang sde snod mtha' dag la mkhas/ rgyud sde rgya mtsho la dbang 'byor/ dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud bshad man ngag rnams kyang gsan cing mkhas par mkhyen/ chag lo las bsnyen
par rdzogs/ tshul khrims kyi dris kun tu khyab/ lo tsA ba'i gdan sar bzhugs te 'phrin las bskyangs so//dbon bstan 'dzin dpal bzang po/de la chag lo'i dbon po bstan 'dzin
dpal bzang pos gsan te/ de ni chag lo'i gcung slob dpon jo yes kyi sras su 'khrungs/ mkhan chen gtsang pa las bsnyen par rdzogs/ chag lugs kyi chos rnams

mkhas par mkhyen/ grub chen u rgyan pa la dus 'khor rgyud bshad dbang man ngag dang bcas pa gsan/ lte'u ra'i gdan sar 'gro phan cher mdzad do// de nas de nyid kyi dbon po chag
rin chen 'byung gnas dpal bzang po/ rje btsun dpal chen bzang po/ chos rje ye shes dpal bzang po yab sras te rgyud 'grel gyi lung rgyud do// chag lo/ shangs pa tshul
she/ bla brang ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ bla brang pa blo gros dpal/ bla brang ba bzang po dpal/ dpal chen bzang po/ ye shes dpal bzang po dbang rgyud do// chag lo/ grum
ston shes rab dpal/ grub thob legs ldan 'od/ dpal chen bzang po/ ye shes dpal bzang po ste khrid kyi rgyud pa'o// yang chag lo/ bla brang ba chen po/ bla brang ba blo gros
dpal/ bla brang ba bzang po dpal/ dpal chen bzang po/ ye shes dpal bzang po/ rgyal sras blo bzang dpal 'byor ba ste mtshan brjod kyi 'grel ba bdud rtsi thigs pa'i brgyud
pa'o//7)sha war dbang phyug gi man ngag lugs/grub chen sha war dbang phyugbdun pa sha war dbang phyug gi man ngag lugs khyad par du bshad pa la/ rdo rje 'chang ngam spyan

ras gzigs la grub chen sha war dbang phyug gis gsan te/ 'di ni grong khyer te te'i gar mkhan lo ki dang gu na gnyis kyi bu tsha rigs ngan glu gar gyis 'tsho ba'i ming sring
gsum yod pa/ slob dpon klu sgrub bhaM ga la'i ri bo na bzhugs pa la slong du phyin pas/ rigs ngan la rnam rtog ma mdzad par nang du bos kha zas mang po byin pa dang dad
pa thob ste byang sems blo gros rin chen gyi sku'i ras bris mthong nas 'di ci lags zhus pas/ byang sems lha'i bu tha mal pas mi mthong ba zhig yin gsungs/ bdag cag la bstan
par zhu zhus pas/ spyi gtsug na yod kyis ltos gsung / de mthong ba'i mi gcig zhu zhus pas/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i dkyil 'khor du bcug nas dbang bskur rgyud bshad gdams pa
gnang / de dag gis kyang nyams su blangs pas rgyud dag nas byang sems kyi zhal mthong ste/ bram ze chen po'i do ha glur blangs nas gar byas mchod pa phul bas/ khyod kyis
de'i don shes sam gsungs/ mi shes pas zhu zhus pas/ rgyud byin gyis brlabs te do ha'i snying po don gyi dgongs pa bstan pas de nyid du de

kho na nyid kyi rtog pa thob po/ der byang chub sems dpas rigs kyi bu khyod lho phyogs ldong ngar gyi ston pa sha wa ra dbang phyug bya ba yin pas/ 'dir ma bsdod par rngon
pa'i chas su zhugs la lho phyogs dpal gyi ri sems ngal gso ba'i ri/ yid pham par byed pa'i ri la song la dbang po yang rab rnams kyi don gyis shig ces lung bstan pa bzhin/
de rnams kyis kyang de bzhin du byas pas phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub brnyes te deng sang gi bar du yang bzhugs so// 'dis ma rig mun pa'i nags tshal du/ gzung
'dzin gnyis kyi ri dwags rgyu/ thabs shes gnyis kyi gzhu brdungs nas/ snying po don gyi mda' gcig 'phangs/ 'chi ni rnam par rtog pa 'chi/ sha ni gnyis su med par zos/ ro
ni bde ba chen por myong / 'bras bu phyag rgya chen po thob/ ces glu blangs so// 'di la bla ma rdo rje gdan pas kyang / gar mkhan dpal gyi ri la bzhugs/ lcam sring gnyis
kyis dngos grub brnyes/ sha wa ra zhes bya ba yi/ bla ma de la phyag 'tshal lo// zhes bstod do//paN chen bi bhU ti tsantra/de la paN chen bi bhU ti tsantras gsan te

de ni rgya gar shar phyogs ba rentra pa/ sgos dza gadha la pa yin/ rigs rgyal rigs/ mang pos bkur ba'i sde las rab tu byung rig pa'i gnas lnga mkhyen/ theg pa che chung gi
chos ma lus pa la sbyangs/ khyad par du gsang sngags la mkhas/ bi khya ta de ba dang / shAkya shrI dang / chos 'bangs las dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud bshad man ngag dang bcas
pa gsan cing mkhas par mkhyen nas rgyad 'grel gyi mtshan mdzad/ thog mar 'jam dbyangs dang / phyis bde mchog dang dus 'khor la sogs pa yi dam gyi lha mang po'i zhal mjal/
shAkya shrI'i phyag phyir bod du byon/ srin po rir bde mchog gi sku bzhengs/ rgya gar du thegs nas slar yang bod du phebs/ sdom gsum 'od phreng mdzad/ bod skad la shin
tu byang bas 'bring mtshams rgya btags gnas su nyi ma dpal ye shes kyi brjed byang la sogs pa rang 'gyur mang po bsgyur/ 'gro phan che bar mdzad nas bal por byon te/ yam
bu'i sthaM bi ha ra ka ba'i gtsug lag khang na bzhugs pa'i tshe/ rgya gar gyi rnal 'byor pa rba ba la kr-iShna sa ri'i rwa dung bcug pa/ de'i lpags pa'i smad dkris

can ras kyi 'ga' phyar ba rna bas pa lang tsho dar la bab pa zhig byon nas/ 'dir zhag 'ga' bsdod pa min gsungs/ der sgra slob pa'i brang khang gcig tu bzhugs su bcug pas sgra
slob pa ba de rnams na re/ rnal 'byor ba 'di ngo mtshar can cig 'od zer bla mas spyan drangs te/ chos kyi gsung gleng byas pas/ gang bris pa thams cad thogs pa med par
byung bas/ sha wa ra yin par dgongs te yin nam zhus pas min gsungs pa dang / tshogs kyi 'khor dang maNDal phul te/ mdo rgyud thams cad kyi bcud bsdus pa'i snying po cig
zhu zhes gsol bas/ sbyor ba yan lag drug gi man ngag 'di gnang nas nga 'gro gsungs/ gar gshegs zhus pas/ nub phyogs kha cher 'gro lan can gyi gdul bya yod/ de nas dpal gyi
ri la 'gro gsungs nas gshegs te/ lar sthaM bi ha rar zhag nyi shu rtsa gnyis bzhugs skad do// paN chen gyis kyang bsgoms pas dngos grub brnyes nas gzhung chung yi ger btab/
de'i dus 'khor bshad bka' dang khyad par man ngag gi bka' 'di dar ba

cig bya/ lhag par bod du phan thogs cher bar 'ong ba dgongs nas/ bod kyi bya bral ba rnams la/ bod na dge ba'i bshes gnyen su che dris pas/ ko brag pa grags pa che bar gsan
nas/ ko brag pa la ngas bod na dge ba'i bshes gnyen snyan pa dang grags pa su che mnyen shing dris pas ko brag pa khyed grub thob kyi grags pa che bar 'dug nged la dus kyi
'khor lo'i dbang bshad/ khyad par man ngag gi bka' mchog tu gyur pa yod pas sbyin gyi khyed bal por thag ring ba la ma rtsog par shog 'gro phan cher 'byung gsungs ba'i
gsung shog dang / de'i rten du thub pa'i rdo sku mdzad pa brgyad kyis bskor ba gcig bal po lugs kyi za 'og yug gcig ka ra'i glang po che gcig rnams paN chung gcig la bkur
te ko brag pa glang gor na bzhugs pa'i sar skyel du btang byung bas/ ko brag pas/ bla ma paN chen gyi gsung shog gnang sbyin dang bcas pa thugs la btags/ nged gcig pu bal
por 'ongs pas sems can la phan thogs che rgyu mi 'chi/ bla ma paN chen nyid bod du byon na/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gzhan phan

can mang po la phan thogs che bar mchi bas/ cis kyang bod du byon pa cig thugs la 'dogs par zhu zhes pa'i zhu yig dang / yi ge'i rten du paN chen la ber thul bzang ba gcig
paN chung rnams la bod kyi na bza' bzang ba re re/ tshur la 'byon pa'i chas ka dang bcas pa mi bdun la bkur te paN chen gdan 'dren du sthaM bi ha rar btang ngo // de nas
paN chen 'byon gyi yod ces pa gtam slab byung ba dang / ko brag pas skyi rong thug bsu ba la byon/ phyogs thams cad du'ang paN chen 'byon gyi yod ces pa'i grags pa sgrog
tu btang / paN chen rlangs 'khor du phebs pa dang / bod kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po yang 'dus/ de rnams la dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud bshad khrid dang bcas pa gnang /
khyad par du ko brag pa/ dpyal a mo gha/ nyog po chos ldan/ lho pa tshul gzhon/ mar ston g.yang 'bar/ g.yung phug pa rgyal mtshan dge ba/ gnyal ba mi mnyam bzang po ste
slob ma dam pa bdun pa sbyor drug gi gdams pa rdzogs par gnang / mi mnyam

bzang pos dpe med 'tsho'i sbyor drug bsgyur/ glang gor du dus 'khor gyi bka' rdzogs pa gsum mdzad pa'i rjes su/ paN chen la bsnyung drag po cig byung ba la ko brag pas gegs
sel mdzad pas/ paN chen mnyes te ko brag pa la yang paN chen gyis chos gsan/ lar paN chen gyis bod du lan gsum byon pa'i tha ma yin/ de res kyang srin po ra yan chad du
byon te/ gtsang rong du rje btsun rgwa lo dang / gtsang stod du kun mkhyen chos sku ba la sbyor drug gnang / rgyus pa gzhon seng dang zha sgom rin seng la ye shes spyan sgrub
sogs gdams pa mang po gnang / khrid kyi sgo nas gzhan phan che bar mdzad de slob ma grub thob mang du byon/ paN chen slar rgya gar la thegs te gnyis su med pa'i ye shes
kyi sku grub po//grub thob ko brag pa/slob ma'i thub po grub thob dum bu ko brag pa ni/ yul ding ri/ yab ldong rgyal g.yung dang / yum stod mo rje la gnyis kyi sras su
chu pho stag la sku bltams/ bris klog rtsol med du mkhyen/ se mig pa las dge bsnyen mdzad/ paN chen

shAkya shrI la blo sbyong gsan/ grum du bla ma rdo rje dpal ba la rig 'dzin bcu gsan/ gnyos sangs rgyas rin chen la/ lam 'bras gsan/ gyang rim dang kong mo'i ri la bsgoms pas
rtogs pa 'khrungs/ paN chen ratna rakShi ta la bde mchog gi dbang gsan/ de nas la phyi sogs su bzhugs/ nyer dgu pa la chos rje skos/ phya ru 'dul 'dzin/ slob dpon lo rnams
la mkhan slob zhus nas dge slong chig rdzogs mdzad/ mtshan bsod nams rgyal mtshan du gsol/ de nas ti ser byon lo lnga bzhugs dus grub pa brnyes/ rdo rje lus kyi gnas
lugs ji lta ba bzhin du gzigs pas gegs sel la mchog tu mkhas/ ma phang gi klus chu'i dngos grub phul/ phyis myang stod ko brag gi dgon pa btab pas sa skam po la chu mig
rdol/ ko brag pa zhes grags/ mkhas btsun thams cad kyis kyang zhabs la gtugs/ chos la'ang 'di mi mkhyen bya ba med/ bal po nas bi bhU ti tsandra ding rir spyan drangs/ sbyor
drug gi gdams pa gsan/ 'gro don rgya cher mdzad nas

brgyad cu pa lcags mo bya la mkha' spyod du gshegs so//'di'i slob ma/ lo tsA ba dpyal khro chag gsum lha btsun gung thang pa/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ dbyar nyi ma/ 'jam gsar
ba/ rgyang ro gzhon rin/ mnga' ris dgra bcom/ nyi ma dbral nag yang dgon pa/ dran ston sher seng / gtsang so ba/ 'ol gong pa sogs mang du byung ba las sbyor drug gi brgyud
pa 'dzin pa ni grub chen go lung pa gzhon dpal lo//dpyal a mo gha/dpyal a mo gha ni/ dpyal chos bzang gi gcen po slob dpon ba stag dang / yum bkra shis dge la sras gsum
byung ba'i che ba yin/ mtshan kun dga' snying por btags/ dgung lo dgu pa la grub thob niShka langka la kyai rdor gyi dbang zhus dus de nyid rdo rje 'chang dngos su gzigs/
de dang khu bo dpyal chos bzang gnyis la bde dgyes gshin rje gshed la sogs pa'i chos mang du gsan/ bcu bdun pa la rab tu byung / mtshan a mo gha shrI bha dra don yod
dpal bzang por btags/ paN chen shAkya shrI dang / chu mig lung pa dmar ce dang / ko brag pa

sogs las sngags mtshan nyid gzhung gdams ngag mang du gsan/ khyad par du paN chen bi bhU ti tsandra rgya btags nas thar par spyan drangs/ skad gnyis yi ge dang bcas pa legs
par bslabs/ chos mang du gsan/ phyis paN chen ko brag pas gdan drangs pa'i tshe sbyor drug lugs gnyis rdzogs par gsan cing bsgoms pas grub pa brnyes/ thar pa'i gdan sar
gdul bya dpag tu med pa smin grol la bkod nas/ re brgyad pa la rje btsun sengge sgras lung bstan pa ltar 'jig rten gyi khams padmo can du gshegs pas padmo can pa zhes grags
so//de la thar pa'i mkhan chen dpal gzhon nu ye shes kyis chos bum pa gang byor gsan/ de la thar los gsan to//nyeg po chos ldan/nyeg po chos ldan ni 'khrungs yul lho pa/
spyir bla ma mang po las sde snod la legs par sbyangs/ khyad par se mo che pa dang 'jam gsar pa yun ring du bsten nas dus 'khor 'bro lugs mkhas par mkhyen/ bi bhU ti la
khrid gsan cing bsgoms pas rdzogs rim gyi lha grub po//lho go lung pa gzhon nu dpal/

lho go lung pa gzhon nu dpal ni/ nyeg po chos ldan la dus 'khor 'bro lugs/ go lung pa mdo sde dpal rgyal mtshan la chag lugs/ lo mchog pa la'ang gsan cing sbyangs pas dus 'khor
la mchog tu mkhas/ ko brag pa dang / g.yung phyug pa dang / nyeg po chos ldan gsum la sbyor drug lugs gnyis po gsan pas nyams rtogs mthar phyin nas mkha' spyod du gshegs
so//thar lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan/de la thar pa lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos gsan te/ de ni dge slong ngur smrig 'dzin pa chen po/ gangs can gyi
bla ma rnams las sde snod dang rgyud sde mang du gsan cing sbyangs/ rong pa sher seng la dus 'khor rwa lugs dang / go lung pa la 'bro lugs kyi dbang rgyud bshad man ngag
dang / khyad par du dpe med 'tsho dang sha wa ra'i gdams pa 'di gtso bor gsan/ dpal gzhon nu ye shes la dus 'khor gyi man ngag dpyal lugs dang / shong blo brtan la yang
gsan pa cher mdzad/ bal por lo bcu gnyis su sbyangs/ rgya gar

du lan 'ga' byon te/ bi bhU ti'i slob ma bi dza ya rakShi ta/ gau ta ma shrI/ su ru Shotta ma/ ratna shrI sogs paN grub du ma bsten nas rig pa'i gnas lnga la sbyangs pas paNDi
ta chen por gyur/ khyad par du bi dza ya rakShi ta dang rgya gar nub phyogs ma la ba'i grub thob go si pa la dus 'khor gyi gdams pa mang du mnos/ bal por bzhugs dus shing
kun gyi nags gseb tu skyo bsangs la byon pas shing drung zhig na grub chen a tsa la nA thA spre'u mang po 'dus pa'i rna bar gling bu btsugs te 'bud kyin 'dug pa la sgra
rings kyi gdams pa gsan/ paNDi ta A nanta shrI bod du spyan drangs te ri'i kun dga' sogs mdo bcu gsum bsgyur zhing / gzhan yang gzhi 'gyur dang 'gyur bcos mang po mdzad/
phyi nang gi rgyud sde'i dgongs pa thugs su chud cing sbyor drug la rtse gcig tu bsgoms pas/ 'chi 'pho ba dang skye ba mngon par mkhyen rlung la dbang thob/ 'byung ba
gsum dang gnad gnyis sogs gdams pa

'di'i bstan bcos mang po mdzad cing thar ba'i mkhan sar bzhugs nas 'phrin las bskyangs so//de la bu ston thams cad mkhyen pas gsan pas mngon par shes pa lnga thob po/ yang
paN chen bi bhU ti tsantra dang / dpyal padmo can gnyis ga la/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer gyis gsan/ de la kun spangs chen pos gsan to//mar ston g.yang 'bar/bi bhU ti tsantra'i
slob ma mar ston g.yang 'bar ni/ bi bhU ti la sbyor drug zhus nas bsgoms pas rlung dbu mar chud/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing mang po gzigs/ bla ma yang shin tu mnyes/ phyis
gtsang sag thang gi so sor bzhugs/ stong gzugs kho na las 'das ma 'ongs mtha' dag gzigs pa'i mngon shes dang ldan no//rnal 'byor sengge 'bum/de la rnal 'byor sengge
'bum gyis gsan to// de ni spyir rgyud sde dang gdams ngag mang du gsan/ khyad par du mar ston g.yang 'bar la sbyor drug gsan te rtse gcig tu bsgoms pas rtogs pa'i yon tan
phul tu phyin/ stong gzugs kyi ka 'bum la sogs pa gang rung dang bsres pas stong gzugs dang sku lus gcig tu gyur te sna tshogs su sprul nus/

bde ba can la sogs pa gang 'dod pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing de mi shigs pa'i thig le'i nang du gzigs ma thag mngon du 'gyur/ spyir gnas nges pa med par ri khrod gang dben du
bzhugs shing / 'khyog dur gyi dgon par cung zad bzhugs pa mdzad do// de la kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus kyis gsan no//yang sha wa ra dbang phyug gis pha dam pa sangs
rgyas la sbyor ba yan lag drug rdo rje'i glur blangs nas gsungs/ de zhwa ma lo tsA ba sengge rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba rim par brgyud de dpal karma pa la bdag gis thob
la skungs lungs pa sangs rgyas dpal/ bdag gi bla ma dus 'khor zhabs las kyang byung ngo //paN chen nags kyi rin chen/grub chen sha wa ra dbang phyug gi sras paN chen nags
kyi rin chen ni/ rgya gar shar phyogs grong khyer dam pa zhes par rgyal po'i sras su sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo brgyad pa la ma hA tsai tya'i gtsug lag khang du mkhan po sangs
rgyas dbyangs dang slob dpon su dzA ta ratna las rab tu byung ste rig pa'i gnas mang po la sbyangs/ mkhan po las sems bskyed cing dpe med mtsho nas brgyud pa'i sbyor
drug dang dbang man

ngag mang du gsan/ nyi shu pa la mkhan slob de gnyis las bsnyen par rdzogs/ de nas singgha la'i gling du byon te lo drug bzhugs nas slob dpon chos kyi grags pa la 'dul ba lung
dang 'od ldan gsan/ gnas dang rten khyad par can rnams mjal zhing gtso bor thugs dam la bzhugs/ sangs rgyas gang chen mtsho'i zhal gzigs/ slar rgya gar lho phyogs ka
lingga'i yul du phebs/ paNDi ta chen po mi'i nyi mas bstod pa phul/ de nas dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi mchod rten du byon nas klu'i byang chub kyi gnas su bzhugs/ der dpal
sha wa ra dbang phyug dang thog mar mjal/ ma ga dhar byon te rdo rje gdan du byang chub chen po la gsol ba btab/ paNDi ta ha ri ha ra la ka lA pa gsan/ chu bo kan ka shrI
taM gyi logs su rnal 'byor yan lag drug la lo gsum phyogs gsum gyi nges pa mdzad de bzhugs/ a ru bA se'i gnas su bi rU pakSha dang / sA gha la dang mjal/ spyan ras gzigs
kyi rdo skus bod yul du songs shig rgyal po zhig la brten nas 'gro ba mang po la phan par

'gyur ro zhes lung bstan pas/ bal por phebs te paNDi ta shrI la sA ga ra la sems bskyed gsan/ me pho rta'i lo la byon/ lha sa yar klungs su yang yud tsam phebs te slar bal
bor 'phags pa shing kun gyi shATta pU ri'i gtsug lag khang du bzhugs pa na/ dang por bla ma sangs rgyas dbyangs byon/ de nas sha wa ra dbang phyug byon nas sprul ba'i sdom
pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur/ zab mo'i dbang phyi ma la brten nas mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'i bde ba brnyes/ slar yang si tu rab brtan pas spyan drangs te rgyang mkhar rtser
phebs/ rong ston smra ba'i seng ges zhabs la gtugs/ 'dul ba me tog phreng rgyud la 'gyur bcos mdzad/ srin po rir phebs pa na/ chos rgyal grags pa 'byung gnas pas sne
gdong rtser gdan drangs/ chos 'khor lo tsA ba manydzu shrIs lo tsA byas te chos kyi rgyal po nyid dang dpal kun bzang rtse pa la lu yi pa dang mi g.yo bla med kyi dbang gsan/
de nas mon spa gror thegs te padma saM bha ba dang mjal/ slar yang me pho 'brug lo la sne

gdong du phebs/ thams cad mkhyen pa 'gos lo tsA ba/ snar thang mkhan chen bsod nams mchog grub pa/ chen po grags bzang pa/ chen po blo rgyal ba/ mkhan chen kun rgyal ba/ dpal
chos kyi grags pa chos rje blo gros dbang phyug sogs sde snod 'dzin pa sum cu rtsa gnyis la dpe med 'tsho'i lugs kyi sbyor drug rdzogs par gnang / khrid thon rjes mi g.yo
bla med kyi dbang dang phag mo'i byin brlabs kyang gnang / sbrul lo la chos rgyal grags pa 'byung gnas dang / dpal kun bzang rtse pa la rdo rje phreng ba dkyil 'khor
zhe lnga ma'i dbang rdzogs par gnang / de'i rjes la dkyil 'khor de nyid du 'gos lo tsA ba sogs sde snod 'dzin pa mang pos kyang dbang tshang bar zhus/ bde dgyes dang grwa
lnga'i sgos bka'/ khyad par du dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang yongs su rdzogs par gnang / dbang mdor bstan sA dhu pu tra'i dka' 'grel dang bcas pa/ dpyid thig 'grel pa mi
g.yo bla med kyi rgyud rnams paN chen nyid dang 'gos lo tsA bas bsgyur te gsungs/ man ngag snye ma dang dpe med 'tsho'i sbyor drug rtsa 'grel yang gnang / de nas bal bor
byon nas sangs rgyas dbyangs
